TV_1.1.1–1.1.3^1	atha yoga anuśāsanam namāmi jagat utpatti hetave vṛṣaketave kleśa karma vipāka ādi rahitāya hitāya ca natvā patañjalim ṛṣim vedavyāsena bhāṣite saṃkṣipta spaṣṭa bahu arthā bhāṣye vyākhyā vidhāsyate iha hi bhagavān patañjaliḥ prāripsitasya śāstrasya saṃkṣepataḥ tātparyārtham prekṣāvat pravṛtti aṅgam śrotuḥ ca sukha avabodha artham ācikhyāsuḥ ādau idam sūtram racayām cakāra atha yoga anuśāsanam tatra prathama avayavam atha śabdam vyācaṣṭe atha iti ayam adhikāra arthaḥ atha eṣa jyotiḥ iti vat na tu ānantarya arthaḥ anuśāsanam iti hi śāstram āha anuśiṣyate anena iti vyutpattyā na ca asya śama dama ādi anantaram pravṛttiḥ api tu tattva jñāna cikhyā payiṣa anantaram jijāsā jñānayoḥ tu syāt yathāmnāyate tasmāt śāntaḥ dāntaḥ uparataḥ titikṣuḥ samāhitaḥ bhūtvā ātmani eva ātmānam paśyet iti 
TV_1.1.3^2	 śiṣya praśna tapaḥ caraṇa rasāyana ādi upayoga ānantaryasya ca saṃbhave api na abhidhānam śiṣya pratīti pravṛttyoḥ anupayogāt prāmāṇika tve yoga anuśāsanasya tad abhāve api upeya tvāt aprāmāṇika tve ca tad bhāve api heya tvāt etena tattva jñāna cikhyā apayiṣayoḥ ānantarya abhidhānam parāḥ tam adhikāra artha tve tu śāstreṇa adhikriyamāṇasya prastūyamānasya yogasya abhidhānāt sakala śāstra tātparya artha vyākhyānena śiṣyaḥ sukhena eva bodhitaḥ ca pravartitaḥ ca bhavati iti niḥśreyasasya hetuḥ samādhiḥ iti hi śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇeṣu prasiddham nanu kim sarva saṃdarbha gataḥ atha śabdaḥ adhikāra arthaḥ tathā sati atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti ādau api prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha ayam iti nanu 
TV_1.1.4–1.1.5^1	 hiraṇyagarbhaḥ yogasya vaktā na anyaḥ purātanaḥ iti yogi yājñavalkya smṛteḥ katham patañjaleḥ yoga śāstra kartṛ tvam iti āśaṅkya sūtrakāreṇa anuśāsanam iti uktam śiṣṭasya śāsanam anuśāsanam iti arthaḥ yadā ayam atha śabdaḥ adhikāra arthaḥ tadā eṣa vākya arthaḥ saṃpadyate iti āha yoga anuśāsanam śāstram adhikṛtam iti nanu vyutpādyamāna tayā yogaḥ atra adhikṛtaḥ na tu śāstram iti atas āha veditavyam iti satyam vyutpādyamāna tayā yogaḥ prastutaḥ sa tu tad viṣayeṇa śāstreṇa karaṇena vyutpādyaḥ karaṇa gocaraḥ ca vyutpādakasya vyāpāraḥ na karma gocaraḥ iti kartṛ vyā pāra vivakṣayā yoga viṣayasya śāstrasya adhikṛta tvam veditavyam 
TV_1.1.5^2	 śāstra vyāpāra gocara tayā tu yogaḥ eva adhikṛtaḥ iti bhāvaḥ adhikāra arthasya ca atha śabdasya anya artham nīyamāna uda kumbha darśanam iva śravaṇam maṅgalāya api kalpate iti mantavyam śabda saṃdeha nimittam artha saṃdeham apanayati yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti yuja samādhau iti asmāt vyutpannaḥ samādhi arthaḥ na tu yujiḥ yoge iti asmāt saṃyoga arthaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu samādhiḥ api vakṣyamāṇasya aṅginaḥ yogasya aṅgam na ca aṅgam eva aṅgī iti atas āha sa ca sārvabhaumaḥ 
TV_1.1.5^3	 caḥ tu arthaḥ aṅgāt aṅginam bhinatti bhūmayaḥ avasthā vakṣyamāṇā madhumatī madhupratīkāḥ viśokā saṃskāra śeṣāḥ tāḥ cittasya tāsu sarvāsu viditaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ citta vṛtti nirodha lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ tad aṅgam tu samādhiḥ na evaṃbhūtaḥ vyutpatti nimitta mātra abhidhānam ca etat yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti aṅga aṅginoḥ abheda vivakṣā mātreṇa pravṛtti nimittam tu yoga śabdasya citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ eva iti parama arthaḥ vṛttayaḥ jñānāni ātma āśrayāṇi atas tad nirodhaḥ api ātma āśrayaḥ eva iti ye paśyanti tat nirāsāya āha cittasya dharmaḥ iti 
TV_1.1.5^4	 citta śabdena antaḥkaraṇam buddhim upalakṣayati na hi kūṭastha nityā citi śaktiḥ apariṇāminī jñāna dharmā bhavitum arhati buddhiḥ tu bhavet iti bhāvaḥ syāt etat sārvabhaumaḥ ced yogaḥ hanta bhoḥ kṣita mūḍha vikṣiptāḥ api citta bhūmayaḥ asti ca paraspara apekṣayā vṛtti nirodhaḥ api āsu iti tatra api yoga tva prasaṅgaḥ iti āśaṅkya heya upādeya bhūmīḥ upanyasyati kṣiptam ityādi kṣiptam sadā eva rajasā teṣu teṣu viṣayeṣu kṣipyamāṇam atyantam asthiram mūḍham tu tamaḥ samudrekāt nidrā vṛttimat kṣiptāt viśiṣṭam vikṣiptam 
TV_1.1.5^5	 viśeṣaḥ asthema bahulasya kādācid kaḥ sthemā sā ca asya asthema bahula tā sāṃsiddhikī vā vakṣyamāṇa vyādhiḥ tyāna ādi antarāya janitāḥ vā ekāgram ekatānam niruddha sakala vṛttikam saṃskāra mātra śeṣam cittam niruddham tatra kṣipta mūḍhayoḥ sati api paraspara apekṣayā vṛtti nirodhe pāramparyeṇa api niḥśreyasa hetu bhāva abhāvāt tad upaghātaka tvāt ca yoga pakṣāt dūra utsārita tvam iti na tayoḥ yogtvam niṣiddham vikṣiptasya tu kādācid ka sat bhūta viṣaya sthema śālinaḥ saṃbhāvyeta yoga tvam iti niṣedhati 
TV_1.1.5^6	 tatra vikṣipte cetasi samādhiḥ kādācid ka sadbhūta viṣayasya cittasya sthemā na yoga pakṣe vartate kasmāt yatas tad vipakṣa vikṣepa upasarjanībhūtaḥ vipakṣa varga antargatasya hi svarūpam eva durlabham prāk eva kārya karaṇam na khalu dahana antargatam bījam tricaturākṣaṇa avasthitam uptam api aṅkurāya kalpate iti bhāvaḥ yadi vikṣepa upasarjanībhūtaḥ samādhiḥ na yogaḥ kaḥ tarhi iti atas āha yaḥ tu ekāgre cetasi iti bhūtam iti samāropitam artham nivartayati nidrā vṛttiḥ api sva ālambane tamasi bhūte bhavati ekāgra iti atas uktam sat iti 
TV_1.1.5^7	 śobhanam nitānta āvirbhūtam sattvam tamaḥ samudrekaḥ tu aśobhanaḥ tasya kleśa hetu tvāt iti dyotanam hi tattva jñānam āgamāt vā anumānāt vā bhavat api parokṣa rūpa tayā na sākṣātkāravatīm avidyām ucchinatti dvi candra diś moha ādiṣu anucchedaka tvāt atas āha preti prakāraḥ hi prakarṣam dyotayan sākṣātkāram sūcayati avidyā mūla tvāt asmitā ādīnām kleśānām vidyāyāḥ ca avidyā uccheda rūpa tvāt vidyā udaye ca avidyā ādi kleśa samucchedaḥ virodhi tvāt kāraṇa vināśāt ca iti āha kṣiṇoti ca iti atas eva karma rūpāṇi bandhanāni ślathayati 
TV_1.1.5^8	 karma ca atra apūrvam abhimatam kārye kāraṇa upacārāt ślathayati sva kāryāt avasādayati vakṣyati hi sati mūle tad vipākaḥ iti kim ca nirodham abhumukham karoti abhimukhīkaroti sa ca saṃprajñātaḥ catuṣprakāraḥ iti āha sa ca iti asaṃprajñātam āha sarva vṛtti iti rajaḥ tamaḥ mayī kila pramāṇa ādi vṛttiḥ sāttvikīm vṛttim upādāya saṃprajñāte niruddhāḥ asaṃprajñāte tu sarvāsām eva nirodhaḥ iti arthaḥ tat iha bhūmi dvaye samāptāḥ yāḥ madhumati ādayaḥ bhūmayaḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ tāsu viditaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ iti siddham 
TV_1.2.1–1.2.2^1	 yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ dvitīyam sūtram avatārayati tasya lakṣaṇa iti tasya iti pūrva sūtra upāttam dvividham yogam parāmṛśati yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ nirudhyante yasmin pramāṇa ādi vṛttayaḥ avasthā viśeṣe cittasya saḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ yogaḥ nanu saṃprajñātasya yogasya avyāpaka tvāt alakṣaṇam idam aniruddhā hi tatra sāttvikī citta vṛttiḥ iti atas āha sarva śabda agrahaṇāt iti yadi sarva citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti ucyeta bhavet avyāpakam saṃprajñātasya kleśa karma vipāka āśaya paripanthī citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ tu tam api saṃgṛhṇāti tatra api rājasa tāmasa citta vṛtti nirodhāt tasya ca tad bhāvāt iti arthaḥ kutas punar ekasya cittasya kṣipta ādi bhūmi saṃbandhaḥ kimartham ca evam avasthasya cittasya vṛttayaḥ niroddhavyāḥ iti āśaṅkya prathamam tāvat avasthā saṃbandhe hetum upanyasyati cittam hi iti 
TV_1.2.2^2	 prakhyā śīla tvāt sattva guṇam pravṛtti śīla tvāt rajaḥ guṇam sthiti śīla tvāt tamaḥ guṇam prakhyā grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham tena anye api sāttvikāḥ prasāda lāghava prīti ādayaḥ sūcyante pravṛttyā ca paritāpa śoka ādayāḥ rājasāḥ pravṛtti virodhī tamaḥ vṛtti dharmaḥ sthitiḥ sthiti grahaṇāt gaurava āvaraṇa dainya ādayaḥ upalakṣyante etat uktam bhavati ekam api cittam triguṇa nirmita tayā guṇānām ca vaiṣamyeṇa paraspara vimarda vaicitryāt vicitra pariṇāmam sat aneka avastham upapadyate iti kṣipta ādyāḥ eva cittasya bhūmīḥ yathāsaṃbhavam avāntara avasthā bhedavatīḥ ādarśayati prakhyā rūpam hi iti citta rūpeṇa pariṇatam sattvam citta sattvam 
TV_1.2.2^3	 tat evam prakhyā rūpatayā sattva prādhānyam cittasya darśitam tatra citte sattvāt kiṃcid ūne rajaḥ tamasī yadā mithas same ca bhavatas tat aiśvaryam ca viṣayāḥ ca śabda ādayaḥ tāni eva priyāṇi yasya tat tathā uktam sattva prādhānyāt khalu cittam tattve praṇidhitsat api tattvasya tamasā pihita tvāt aṇima ādikam aiśvaryam eva tattvam abhimanyamānam tat praṇidhitsati praṇidhatte ca kṣaṇam atha rajasā kṣipyamāṇam tatra api alabdha sthitim tad priya mātram bhavati śabda ādiṣu punar asya svarasa vāhī premāḥ nirūḍhaḥ eva tat anena vikṣiptam cittam uktam kṣiptam cittam darśayan mūḍham api sūcayati tat eva tamasā iti yadā hi tamaḥ rajaḥ vijitya prasṛtam tadā citta sattva āvaraka tamaḥ samutsāraṇe aśakta tvāt rajasaḥ tamaḥ sthagitam cittam adharma ādi upagacchati 
TV_1.2.2^4	 ajñānam ca viparyaya jñānam abhāva pratyaya ālambanam ca nidrā jñānam uktam tatas ca mūḍha avasthā api sūcitā iti anaiśvaryam sarvatra icchā pratīghātaḥ adharma ādi vyāptam cittam bhavati iti arthaḥ yadā tu tat eva citta sattvam āvirbhūta sattvam apagata tamaḥ paṭalam sa rajaskam bhavati tadā dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryāṇi upagacchati iti āha prakṣīṇa ityādi mohaḥ tamaḥ tat eva ca āvaraṇam prakarṣeṇa kṣīṇam yasya tat tathā uktam atas eva sarvatas viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātra aliṅga puruṣeṣu pradyotamānam tathā api na dharmāya aiśvaryāya ca kalpate pravṛtti abhāvāt iti atas āha anuviddham rajaḥ mātrayā rajasaḥ pravartaka tvāt asti dharma ādi pravṛttiḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.2.2^5	 tat anena saṃprajñāta samādhi saṃpannayoḥ madhu bhūmika prajñā jyotiṣoḥ madhyamayoḥ yoginoḥ citta sattvam saṃgṛhītam saṃprati atikrānta bhāvanīyasya dhyāyinaḥ caturthasya citta avasthām āha tat eva cittam rajaḥ leśāt malāt apetam atas eva svarūpa pratiṣṭham abhyāsa vairāgya puṭapāka prabandha vidhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ malasya hi buddhi sattva tapanīyasya svarūpa pratiṣṭhasya viṣaya indriya pratyāhṛtasya anavasita adhikāra tayā ca kārya kāriṇaḥ viveka khyātiḥ param kāryam avaśiṣyate iti āha sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātram cittam dharma megha dhyāna upagam bhavati dharma meghaḥ ca vakṣyate atra eva yogi jana prasiddhim āha tat iti sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātram cittam dharma megha paryantam param prasaṃkhyānam iti ācakṣate dhyāyinaḥ 
TV_1.2.2^6	 citta sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca dharma dharmiṇoḥ abheda vivakṣayā draṣṭavyam viveka khyāteḥ hāna hetum citi śakteḥ ca upādāna hetum nirodha samādhim avatārayitum citi śakteḥ sādhu tām asādhu tām ca viveka khyāteḥ darśayati citi śaktiḥ ityādi sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvam aśuddhiḥ sukha mohau api hi vivekinam duḥkha akurutaḥ atas duḥkha vat dheyau tathā ca ati sundaram api antavat dunoti tena tat api heyam eva vivekinaḥ sā iyam aśuddhiḥ antar ca citi śaktau puruṣe na staḥ iti uktam śuddhā ca anantā ca iti nanu sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka śabda ādīn iyam cetayamānā tad ākāra āpannā katham viśuddhā tad ākāra parigraha parivarjane ca kurvatī katham ananta iti atas uktam darśita viṣaya iti 
TV_1.2.2^7	 darśitaḥ viṣayaḥ śabda ādiḥ yasyai sā tathā uktā bhavet etat evam yadi buddhi vat citi śaktiḥ viṣaya ākāra tām āpadyeta kim tu buddhiḥ eva viṣaya ākāreṇa pariṇatā sati atadākārāyai citi śaktyai viṣayam ādarśayati tatas puruṣaḥ cetayate iti ucyate nanu viṣaya ākārām buddhim anārūḍhāyāḥ citi śakteḥ katham viṣaya vedanam viṣaya ārohe vā katham na tad ākāra āpattiḥ iti atas uktam apratisaṃkrama iti pratisaṃkramaḥ saṃcāraḥ sa citeḥ na asti iti arthaḥ saḥ eva kutas asyāḥ na asti iti atas uktam apariṇāminī iti na citeḥ trividhaḥ api dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā lakṣaṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ asti yena kriyā rūpeṇa pariṇatā satī buddhi saṃyogena pariṇameta citi śaktiḥ asaṃkrāntāyāḥ api viṣaya saṃvedanam upapādayiṣyate tat siddham citi śaktiḥ śobhanā iti 
TV_1.2.2^8	 viveka khyātiḥ tu buddhi sattva ātmikā śobhanā iti uktam atas citi śakteḥ viparītā iti yadā ca viveka khyātiḥ api heyā tadā kā eva kathāḥ vṛtti antarāṇām doṣa bahulānām iti bhāvaḥ tatas tad hetoḥ nirodha samādheḥ avatāraḥ yujyate iti āha atas tasyām iti jñāna prasāda mātreṇa hi pareṇa vairāgyeṇa viveka khyātim api niruṇaddhi iti arthaḥ atha niruddha aśeṣa vṛttim cittam kīdṛśam iti atas āha tad avastham ityādi sa nirodhaḥ avasthā yasya tat tathā uktam nirodhasya svarūpam āha sa nirbījaḥ iti kleśa sahitaḥ karma āśayaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga bījam tasmāt nirgataḥ iti nirbījaḥ asya eva yogi jana prasiddhām anvartha saṃjñām ādarśayati na tatra iti upasaṃharati dvividhaḥ sa yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti 
TV_1.3.1–1.3.2^1	 tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe avasthānam saṃprati uttara sūtram avatārayitum codayati tad avasthe cetasi iti kim ākṣepe tad tad ākāra pariṇata buddhi bodha ātmā khalu ayam puruṣaḥ sadā anubhūyate na tu buddhi bodha rahitaḥ atas asya puruṣasya buddhi bodhaḥ svabhāvaḥ savituḥ iva prakāśaḥ na ca saṃskāra śeṣe cetasi saḥ asti na ca svabhāvam apahāya bhāvaḥ vartitum arhati iti bhāvaḥ syāt etat saṃskāra śeṣām api buddhim kasmāt puruṣaḥ na budhyate iti atas āha viṣaya abhāvāt iti na buddhi mātram puruṣasya viṣayaḥ api tu puruṣa arthavatī buddhiḥ viveka khyāti viṣaya bhogau ca puruṣa arthau tau ca niruddha avasthāyām na staḥ iti siddhaḥ viṣaya abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ sūtreṇa pariharati tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe avasthānam svarūpaḥ iti āropitam śānta ghora mūḍha svarūpam nivartayati puruṣasya hi caitanyam sva rūpam anaupādhikam na tu buddhi bodhaḥ śānta ādi rūpaḥ aupādhikaḥ hi sa sphaṭikasya iva svabhāva svaccha dhavalasya japā kusuma saṃnidhāna upādhiḥ aruṇimā 
TV_1.3.2^2	 na ca upādhi nivṛttau upahita nivṛttiḥ atiprasaṅgāt iti bhāvaḥ svarūpasya ca abhede api bhedam vikalpya adhikaraṇa bhāvaḥ uktaḥ iti ayam eva arthaḥ bhāṣya kṛtā dyotyate svarūpa pratiṣṭhā iti tadānīm nirodha avasthāyām na vyutthāna avasthāyām iti bhāvaḥ syāt etat vyutthāna avasthāyām apratiṣṭhitā svarūpe citi śaktiḥ nirodha avasthāyām pratitiṣṭhantī pariṇāminī syāt vyutthāne vā svarūpa pratiṣṭhāne vyutthāna nirodhayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ iti atas āha vyutthāna citte tu iti na jātu kūṭastha nityā citi śaktiḥ svarūpāt cyavate tena yathā nirodhe tathā eva vyutthāne api na khalu śuktikāyāḥ pramāṇa viparyaya jñāna gocara tve api svarūpa udaya vyayau bhavataḥ pratipattā tu tathābhūtam api atathātvena abhimanyate nirodha samādhim apekṣya saṃprajñātaḥ api vyutthānam eva iti 
TV_1.4.1–1.4.2^1	 vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra sūtra antaram avatārayitum pṛcchati katham tarhi iti yadi tathā bhavantī na tathā kena tarhi prakāreṇa prakāśate iti arthaḥ hetu padam adhyāhṛtya sūtram paṭhati darśita viṣaya tvāt vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra itaratra vyutthāne yāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ śānta ghora mūḍhāḥ tāḥ eva aviśiṣṭāḥ abhinnāḥ vṛttayaḥ yasya puruṣasya sa tathā uktaḥ sārūpyam iti atra sa śabdaḥ eka paryāyaḥ etat uktam bhavati japā kusuma sphaṭikayoḥ iva buddhi puruṣayoḥ saṃnidhānāt abheda grahe buddhi vṛttīḥ puruṣe samāropya śāntaḥ asmi duḥkhitaḥ asmi mūḍhaḥ asmi iti adhyavasyati yathā maline darpaṇa tale pratibimbitam mukham malinam āropya śocati ātmānam malinaḥ asmi iti 
TV_1.4.2^2	 yadi api puruṣa samāropaḥ api śabda ādi vijñāna vat buddhi vṛttiḥ yadi api ca prākṛta tvena acit rūpa tayā anubhāvyaḥ tathā api buddheḥ puruṣa tvam āpādayan puruṣa vṛttiḥ iva anubhavaḥ iva avabhāsate tathā ca ayam aviparyayaḥ api ātmā viparyayavān iva abhoktā api bhoktā iva viveka khyāti rahitaḥ api tad sahitaḥ iva viveka khyātyā prakāśate etat ca citeḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ tad ākāra āpattau sva buddhi saṃvedanam iti atra sattva puruṣayoḥ atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ iti atra ca upapādayiṣyate etat ca mata antare api siddham iti āha tathā ca iti pañcaśikha ācāryasya sūtram ekam eva darśanam khyātiḥ eva darśanam iti nanu katham ekam darśanam yāvatā buddheḥ śabda ādi viṣayā viveka viṣayā ca vṛttiḥ prākṛta tayā jaḍa tvena anubhāvyāḥ darśanam tatas anyat puruṣasya caitanyam anubhavaḥ darśanam iti atas āha khyātiḥ eva darśanam iti 
TV_1.4.2^3	 udaya vyaya dharmiṇīm vṛttim khyātim laukikīm abhipretya etat uktam ekam eva iti caitanyam tu puruṣasya svabhāvaḥ na khyāteḥ tat tu na loka pratyakṣa gocaraḥ api tu āgama anumāna gocaraḥ iti arthaḥ tat anena vyutthāna avasthāyām mūla kāraṇam avidyām darśayatā tad hetukaḥ saṃyogaḥ bhoga hetuḥ sva svāmi bhāvaḥ api sūcitaḥ iti tam upapādayan āha cittam svam bhavati puruṣasya svāminaḥ iti saṃbandhaḥ nanu citta janitam upakāram bhajamānaḥ hi cetanaḥ cittasya īśitāḥ na ca asya tad janita upakāra saṃbhavaḥ tad asaṃbandhāt anupakārya tvāt tad saṃyoga tad upakāra bhāgi tve pariṇāma prasaṅgāt iti atas āha ayaskānta maṇi kalpam saṃnidhi mātra upakāri dṛśya tvena iti 
TV_1.4.2^4–1.4.3	 na puruṣa saṃyuktam cittam api tu tad saṃnihitam saṃnidhiḥ ca puruṣasya na deśataḥ kālataḥ vā tad asaṃyogāt kim tu yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ asti ca puruṣasya bhoktṛ śaktiḥ cittasya bhoga śaktiḥ tat uktam dṛśya tvena iti śabda ādi ākāra pariṇatasya bhogya tvena iti arthaḥ bhogaḥ ca yadi api śabda ādi ākārā vṛttiḥ cittasya dharmaḥ tathā api citta caitanyayoḥ abheda samāropāt vṛtti sārūpyāt puruṣasya iti uktam tasmāt cittena asaṃyoge api tad janita upakāra bhāgitā puruṣasya apariṇāmi tā ca iti siddham nanu sva svāmi saṃbandhaḥ bhoga hetuḥ avidyā nimittaḥ avidyā tu kiṃnimittā na khalu animittam kāryam utpadyate yathā āhuḥ svapna ādi vat avidyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tasya kiṃkṛtā iti śaṅkām upasaṃhāra vyājena uddharati tasmāt citta vṛtti bodhe śānta ghora mūḍha ākāra citta vṛtti upabhoge anādya vidyā nimitta tvāt anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ avidyā vāsanayoḥ ca saṃtānaḥ bīja aṅkura saṃtāna vat anādiḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.5.1–1.5.2^1	 vṛttayaḥ pañcatayyaḥ kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ syāt etat puruṣaḥ hi śakyaḥ upadiśyate na ca vṛtti nirodhaḥ vṛttīḥ avijñāya śakyaḥ na ca sahasreṇa api puruṣa āyuṣaiḥ alam imāḥ kaścid parigaṇayitum asaṃkhyātāḥ ca katham niroddhavyā iti āśaṅkya tāsām iyattā svarūpa pratipādana param sūtram avatārayati tāḥ punar niroddhavyāḥ bahu tve sati cittasya vṛttayaḥ pañcatayyaḥ kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ vṛtti rūpaḥ avayavi ekaḥ tasya pramāṇa ādayaḥ avayavāḥ pañca tatas tad avayavā pañcatayī pañca avayavā vṛttiḥ bhavati tāḥ ca vṛttayaḥ caitra maitra ādi citta bhedāt bahvyaḥ iti bahuvacanam upapannam etat uktam bhavati caitraḥ vā maitraḥ vā anyaḥ vā kaścid sarveṣām eva teṣām vṛttayaḥ pañcatayyaḥ eva na adhikāḥ iti cittasya iti ca eka vacanam jāti abhiprāyam 
TV_1.5.2^2	 cittānām iti tu draṣṭavyam tāsām avāntara viśeṣam anuṣṭhāna upayoginam darśayati kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ iti akliṣṭāḥ upādāya kliṣṭāḥ niroddhavyāḥ tāḥ api pareṇa vairāgyeṇa iti asya vyākhyānam kleśa hetukāḥ iti kleśāḥ asmitā ādayaḥ hetavaḥ pravṛtti kāraṇam yāsām vṛttīnām tāḥ tathā uktāḥ yat vā puruṣa artha pradhānasya rajaḥ tamaḥ mayīnām hi vṛttīnām kleśa kāraṇa tvena kleśāya eva pravṛttiḥ kleśaḥ kliṣṭam tat āsām asti iti kliṣṭāḥ iti yatas eva kleśa upārjana artham amūṣām pravṛttiḥ atas eva karma āśaya pracaye kṣetrībhūtāḥ pramāṇa ādinā khalu ayam pratipatta artham avasāya tatra saktaḥ dviṣṭaḥ vā karma āśayam ācinoti iti bhavanti dharma adharma pracaya prasava bhūmayaḥ vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭāḥ iti akliṣṭāḥ vyācaṣṭe khyāti viṣayāḥ iti 
TV_1.5.2^3	 vidhūta rajaḥ tamasaḥ buddhi sattvasya praśānta vāhinaḥ prajñā prasādaḥ khyātiḥ tayā viṣayiṇyā tad viṣayam sattva puruṣa vivekam upalakṣayati tena sattva puruṣa viveka viṣayāḥ yatas atas eva guṇa adhikāra virodhinyaḥ kārya ārambhaṇam hi guṇānām adhikāraḥ viveka khyāti paryavasānam ca tat iti carita adhikārāṇām guṇānām adhikāram virundhanti iti atas tāḥ akliṣṭāḥ pramāṇa prabhṛtayaḥ vṛttayaḥ syāt etat vīta rāga janma adarśanāt kliṣṭa vṛttayaḥ eva sarve prāṇabhṛtaḥ na ca kliṣṭa vṛtti pravāhe bhavitum arhanti akliṣṭāḥ vṛttayaḥ na ca amūṣām bhāve api kārya kāritā virodhim adhyapāti tvāt tasmāt kliṣṭānām akliṣṭābhiḥ nirodhaḥ tāsām ca vairāgyeṇa pareṇa iti manoratha mātram iti atas āha kliṣṭa pravāha iti 
TV_1.5.2^4	 āgama anumāna ācārya upadeśa pariśīlana labdha janmanī abhyāsa vairāgye kliṣṭa= chidram antarā tatra patitāḥ svayam akliṣṭāḥ eva yadi api kliṣṭa pravāha patitāḥ na khalu śālagrāme kirāta śata saṃkīrṇe prativasan api brāhmaṇaḥ kirātaḥ bhavati akliṣṭa= chidreṣu iti nidarśanam kliṣṭa antara varti tayā ca kliṣṭābhiḥ anabhibhūtāḥ akliṣṭāḥ sva saṃskāra paripāka krameṇa kliṣṭāḥ eva tāvat abhibhavanti iti āha tathājātīyakāḥ iti akliṣṭābhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ akliṣṭāḥ saṃskārāḥ iti arthaḥ tat idam vṛtti saṃskāra cakram aniśam āvartate ā nirodha samādheḥ tat evaṃbhūtam cittam nirodha avastham saṃskāra śeṣam bhūtvā ātma kalpena avatiṣṭhata iti āpātataḥ pralayam vā gacchati iti paramārthataḥ piṇḍīkṛtya sūtra artham āha tāḥ iti pañcadhā iti artha kathana mātram na tu śabda vṛtti vyākhyānam tayapaḥ prakāre asmaraṇāt 
TV_1.6.1–1.6.2	 pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa nidrā smṛtayaḥ tāḥ sva saṃjñābhiḥ uddiśati pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa nidrā smṛtayaḥ nirdeśe yathāvacanam vigrahaḥ ca arthe dvaṃdvaḥ samāse itaretara yoge yathā anitya aśuci duḥkha anātmasu nitya śuci sukha ātma khyātiḥ avidyā iti ukte api na diś moha alāta cakra ādi vibhramāḥ vyudasyanta evam iha api pramāṇa ādi abhidhāne api vṛtti antara sadbhāva śaṅkā na vyudasyata iti tat nirāsāya vaktavyam pañcatayyaḥ iti etāvatyaḥ eva vṛttayaḥ na aparāḥ santi iti darśitam bhavati 
TV_1.7.1–1.7.2^1	 pratyakṣa anumāna āgamāḥ pramāṇāni tatra pramāṇa vṛttim vibhajan sāmānya lakṣaṇam āha pratyakṣa anumāna āgamāḥ pramāṇāni anadhigata tattva bodhaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ vyavahāra hetuḥ pramā tad kāraṇam pramāṇam vibhāga vacanam ca nyūna adhika saṃkhyā vyavaccheda artham tatra sakala pramāṇa mūla tvāt prathamatas pratyakṣam lakṣayati indriya iti arthasya iti samāropita tvam niṣedhati tat viṣaya iti bāhya gocara tayā jñāna ākāra gocara tvam nivārayati citta vartinaḥ jñāna ākārasya bāhya jñeya saṃbandham darśayati bāhya vastu uparāgāt iti vyavahitasya tad uparāge hetum āha indriya praṇālikayā iti sāmānya mātram arthaḥ iti eke viśeṣāḥ eva iti anye sāmānya viśeṣa tadvat tā iti apare vādinaḥ pratipannāḥ tat nirāsāya āha sāmānya viśeṣa ātmanaḥ iti na tadvat tā kim tu tādātmyam arthasya etat ca ekāntānabhypagamaḥ iti atra pratipādayiṣyate 
TV_1.7.2^2	 anumāna āgama viṣayāt pratyakṣa viṣayam vyavacchinatti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhāna iti yadi api sāmānyam api pratyakṣe pratibhāsate tathā api viśeṣam pratyupasarjanībhūtam iti arthaḥ etat ca sākṣātkāra upalakṣaṇa param tathā ca viveka khyātiḥ api lakṣitā bhavati phala vipratipattim nirākaroti phalam pauruṣeyaḥ citta vṛtti bodhaḥ iti nanu puruṣa vartī bodhaḥ katham citta gatāyāḥ vṛtteḥ phalam na hi khadira gocara vyāpāreṇa paraśunā palāśe chidā kriyate iti atas āha aviśiṣṭaḥ iti na hi puruṣa gataḥ bodhaḥ janyate api tu caitanyam eva buddhi darpaṇa pratibimbitam buddhi vṛttyā artha ākārayā tad ākāra tām āpadyamānam phalam tat ca tathābhūtam buddheḥ aviśiṣṭam buddhi ātmakam vṛttiḥ ca buddhi ātmikā iti sāmānādhikaraṇyāt yuktaḥ pramāṇa phala bhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ etat ca upapādayiṣyāmaḥ iti āha pratisaṃvedī iti 
TV_1.7.2^3	 pratyakṣa anantaram pravṛtti ādi liṅgaka śrotṛ buddhi anumāna prabhava saṃbandha darśana samuttha tayā āgamasya anumāna ja tvāt anumitasya ca āgamena anvākhyānāt āgamāt prāk anumānam lakṣayati anumeyasya iti jijñāsita dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī anumeyaḥ tasya tulya jātīyāḥ sādhya dharma sāmānyena samāna arthāḥ sa pakṣāḥ teṣu anuvṛttaḥ iti anena viruddha tvam asādhāraṇa tvam ca sādhana dharmasya nirākaroti bhinna jātīyāḥ asapakṣāḥ te ca sa pakṣāt anye tad viruddhāḥ tad abhāvavantaḥ ca tebhyaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ tat anena sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tvam apākaroti saṃbadhyate iti saṃbandhaḥ liṅgam anena pakṣa dharma tām darśayan asiddha tām nivārayati tad viṣayā tad nibandhanā ṣin bandhane iti asmāt viṣaya pada vyutpatteḥ sāmānya avadhāraṇa iti pratyakṣa viṣayāt vyavacchinatti saṃbandha saṃvedana adhīna janma anumānam viśeṣeṣu saṃbandha grahaṇa abhāvena sāmānyam eva sukara saṃbandha grahaṇam gocarayati iti 
TV_1.7.2^4–1.7.4^1	 udāharaṇam āha yathā iti caḥ hetu arthe vindhyaḥ agatiḥ yatas tasmāt tasya aprāptiḥ atas gati nivṛttau prāpteḥ nivṛttiḥ deśa antara prāpteḥ gatimat candra tārakam caitra vat iti siddham āgamasya vṛtteḥ lakṣaṇam āha āptena iti tattva darśana kāruṇya karaṇa pāṭava abhisaṃbandhaḥ āptiḥ tayā vartate iti āptaḥ tena dṛṣṭaḥ anumitaḥ vā arthaḥ śrutasya pṛthak anupādānam tasya dṛṣṭa anumita mūla tvena tābhyām eva caritārtha tvāt āpta citta varti jñāna sadṛśasya jñānasya śrotṛ citte samutpādaḥ sva bodha saṃkrāntiḥ tasyai arthaḥ upadiśyate śrotṛ hita ahita prāpti parihāra upāya tayā prajñāpyate 
TV_1.7.2^4–1.7.4^2	 śeṣam sugamam yasya āgamasya aśraddheya arthaḥ vaktā yathā yāni eva daśa dāḍimāni tāni ṣaṭ apūpāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti na dṛṣṭa anumita arthaḥ yathā caityam vandeta svarga kāmaḥ iti saḥ āgamaḥ plavate nanu evam manu ādīnām api āgamaḥ plaveta na hi te api dṛṣṭa anumita arthāḥ yathā āhuḥ yaḥ kaścid kasyacid dharmaḥ manunā parikīrtitaḥ sa sarvaḥ abhihitaḥ vede sarva jñāna mayaḥ hi saḥ iti atas āha mūla vaktari tu iti mūla vaktā hi tatra īśvaraḥ dṛṣṭa anumita arthaḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.8.1–1.8.2^1^1	 viparyayaḥ mithyājñānam atad rūpa pratiṣṭham viparyayaḥ mithyājñānam atad rūpa pratiṣṭham viparyayaḥ iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ mithyājñānam ityādi lakṣaṇam yat jñāna pratibhāsi rūpam tad rūpā pratiṣṭham eva atad rūpa pratiṣṭham yathāśrāddha bhojī iti atas saṃśayaḥ api saṃgṛhītaḥ etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ tatra jñāna ārūḍhā eva apratiṣṭhatā dvi candra ādeḥ tu bādha jñānena nanu evam vikalpaḥ api tad rūpa apratiṣṭhānāt vicārataḥ viparyayaḥ prasajyeta iti atas āha mithyājñānam iti anena hi sarva janīna anubhava siddhaḥ bādhaḥ uktaḥ 
TV_1.8.1–1.8.2^1^2	 sa ca asti viparyaye na tu vikalpe tena vyavahārāt paṇḍita rūpāṇām eva tu vicārayatām tatra bādha buddheḥ iti codayati sa kasmāt na pramāṇam na uttareṇa upajāta virodhinā jñānena pūrvam bādhanīyam api tu pūrveṇa eva prathamam upajātena anupajāta virodhinā param iti bhāvaḥ pariharati yatas pramāṇena iti yatra hi pūrva apekṣā para utpattiḥ tatra evam iha tu sva kāraṇāt anyonya anapekṣe jñāne jāyete tena uttarasya pūrvam anupamṛdya udayam anāsādayataḥ tad apabādha ātmā eva udayaḥ na tu pūrvasya uttara bādha ātmā tasya tadānīm aprasakteḥ 
TV_1.8.2^2–1.8.3^1	 tasmāt anupajāta virodhitā bādhya tve hetuḥ upajāta virodhitā ca bādhaka tve tasmāt bhūta artha viṣaya tvāt pramāṇena apramāṇasya bādhanam siddham udāharaṇam āha tatra pramāṇena iti asya kutsita tvam hānāya darśayati sā iyam pañca iti avidyā sāmānyam avidyā smita ādiṣu pañcasu parvasu iti arthaḥ avyakta mahat ahaṃkāra pañca tanmātreṣu aṣṭasu anātmasu ātma buddhiḥ avidyā tamaḥ evam yoginām aṣṭasu aṇima ādikeṣu aiśvaryeṣu aśreyaḥsu śreyaḥ buddhiḥ aṣṭavidhaḥ mohaḥ pūrvasmāt jaghanyaḥ sa ca asmitā ucyate 
TV_1.8.2^2–1.8.3^2	 yathā yogena aṣṭavidham aiśvaryam upādāya siddhaḥ bhūtvā dṛṣṭa anuśravi kāñ śabda ādīn daśa viṣayān bhokṣyaḥ iti evam ātmikā pratipattiḥ mahāmohaḥ rāgaḥ evam etena eva abhisaṃdhinā pravartamānasya kenacid pratibaddha tvāt aṇima ādīnām anutpattau tad nibandhanasya dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya upabhogasya asiddheḥ pratibandhaka viṣayaḥ krodhaḥ sa tāmisra ākhyaḥ dveṣaḥ evam aṇima ādi guṇa saṃpattau dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya pratyupasthāne ca kalpa ante sarvam etat naṅkṣyati iti yaḥ trāsaḥ saḥ abhiniveśaḥ andhatāmisraḥ tat uktam bhedaḥ tamasaḥ aṣṭavidhaḥ mohasya ca daśavidhaḥ mahāmohaḥ tāmisraḥ aṣṭādaśadhā tathā bhavati andhatāmisraḥ iti 
TV_1.9.1–1.9.2^1	 śabda jñāna anupātī vastu śūnyaḥ vikalpaḥ śabda jñāna anupātī vastu śūnyaḥ vikalpaḥ nanu śabda jñāna anupātī ced āgama pramāṇa antargataḥ vikalpaḥ prasajyeta nirvastuka tve vā viparyayaḥ syāt iti atas āha sa na iti na pramāṇa viparyaya antargataḥ kasmāt yatas vastu śūnya tve api iti pramāṇa antargatim niṣedhati śabda jñāna māhātmya nibandhanaḥ iti viparyaya antar gatim etat uktam bhavati kvacid abhede bhedam āropayati kvacid punar bhinnānām abhedam tatas bhedasya abhedasya ca vastunaḥ abhāvāt tad ābhāsaḥ vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam na api viparyayaḥ vyavahāra avisaṃvādāt iti 
TV_1.9.2^2	 śāstra prasiddham udāharaṇam āha tat yathā iti kim viśeṣyam kena vyapadiśyate viśeṣyate nābhede viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ na hi gavā gauḥ viśeṣyate kim tu bhinnena eva caitreṇa tat idam āha bhavati ca vyapadeśe vṛttiḥ vyapadeśa vyapadeśyayoḥ bhāvaḥ vyapadeśaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ iti yāvat tasmin vṛttiḥ vākyasya yathā caitrasya gauḥ iti śāstrīyam eva udāharaṇa antaram samuccinoti tathā iti pratiṣiddhaḥ vastunaḥ pṛthivī ādeḥ dharmaḥ parispandaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ kaḥ asau niṣkriyaḥ puruṣaḥ 
TV_1.9.2^3	 na khalu sāṃkhyīye rāddha ante abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid asti vastu dharmaḥ yena puruṣaḥ viśeṣyeta iti arthaḥ kvacid pāṭhaḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ vastu dharmā iti tasya arthaḥ pratiṣedha vyāptāḥ pratiṣiddhā na vastu dharmāṇām tad vyāpya tāḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ asaṃbandhāt atha ca tathā pratītiḥ iti laukikam udāharaṇam āha tiṣṭhati bāṇaḥ iti yathā hi pacati bhinatti iti atra pūrva aparībhūtaḥ karma kṣaṇa pracayaḥ eka phala avacchinnaḥ pratīyate evam tiṣṭhati iti atra api pūrvāparībhāvam eva āha sthāsyati sthitaḥ iti 
TV_1.9.2^4	 nanu bhavatu pāka vat pūrva aparībhūtayā avasthāna kriyayā bāṇāt bhinnayā bāṇasya vyapadeśaḥ iti atas āha gati nivṛttau dhātu artha mātram gamyate gati nivṛttiḥ eva tāvat kalpitā tasyāḥ api bhāva rūpa tvam tatra api pūrvāparībhāvaḥ iti aho kalpanā paramparā iti arthaḥ abhāvaḥ kalpitaḥ bhāvaḥ iva ca anugataḥ iva ca sarva puruṣeṣu gamyate na punar puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ dharmaḥ kaścid iti udāharaṇa antaram āha tathā anutpatti dharmā iti pramāṇa viparyayābhyām anyā na vikalpa vṛttiḥ iti vādinaḥ bahavaḥ pratipedire tad pratibodhanāya udāharaṇa prapañcaḥ iti mantavyam 
TV_1.10.1–1.10.2^1	 abhāva pratyaya ālambanā vṛttiḥ nidrā abhāva pratyaya ālambanā vṛttiḥ nidrā adhikṛtam hi vṛtti padam anuvādakam pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa smṛtīnām vṛtti tvam prati parīkṣakāṇām avipratipatteḥ atas tat anūdyate viśeṣa vidhānāya nidrāyāḥ tu vṛtti tve parīkṣakāṇām asti vipratipattiḥ iti vṛtti tvam vidheyam na ca prakṛtam anuvādakam vidhānāya kalpate iti punar vṛtti grahaṇam jāgrat svapna vṛttīnām abhāvaḥ tasya pratyayaḥ kāraṇam buddhi sattvāt chādakam tamaḥ tat eva ālambanam viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā vṛttiḥ nidrā buddhi sattve hi triguṇe yadā sattva rajasī abhibhūya samasta karaṇa avarakam āvirasti tamaḥ tadā buddheḥ viṣaya ākāra pariṇāma abhāvāt udbhūta tamaḥ mayīm buddhim avabudhyamānaḥ puruṣaḥ suṣuptaḥ antar saṃjñaḥ iti ucyate kasmāt punar niruddha kaivalyayoḥ iva vṛtti abhāvaḥ eva na nidrā iti atas āha sā ca saṃprabodhe pratyavamarśāt sa upapattikāt smaraṇāt pratyaya viśeṣaḥ 
TV_1.10.2^2	 katham yadā hi sattva sacivam tamaḥ āvirasti tad ā īdṛśaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ supta utthitasya bhavati sukham aham asvāpsam prasannam me manaḥ prajñām me viśāradīkaroti svat chīkaroti iti yadā tu rajaḥ sacivam tamaḥ āvirasti tad ā īdṛśaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ iti āha duḥkham aham asvāpsam styānam akarmaṇyam me manaḥ kasmāt yatas bhramati anavasthitam nitānta abhibhūta rajaḥ sattve tamaḥ samullāse svāpe prabuddhasya pratyavamarśam āha gāḍham mūḍhaḥ aham asvāpsam gurūṇi me gātrāṇi klāntam me cittam alasam muṣitam iva tiṣṭhati iti sādhya vyatireke hetu vyatirekam āha na khalu ayam iti prabuddhasya prabuddha mātrasya tad āśritāḥ ca iti bodha kāle pratyaya anubhave vṛtti abhāva kāraṇa anubhavaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu pramāṇa ādayaḥ vyutthāna citta adhikaraṇāḥ nirudhyantām samādhi pratipakṣa tvān nidrāyāḥ tu ekāgra vṛtti tulyāyāḥ katham samādhi pratipakṣata iti atas āha sā ca samādhau iti ekāgra tulyā api tāmasatvena nidrā sa bīja nirbīja samādhi pratipakṣā iti sā api niroddhavyā iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.11.1–1.11.2^1	 anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ pramāṇa ādibhiḥ anubhūte viṣaye yaḥ asaṃpramoṣaḥ asteyam sā smṛtiḥ saṃskāra mātra jasya hi jñānasya saṃskāra kāraṇa anubhava avabhāsitaḥ viṣayaḥ ātmīyaḥ tad adhika viṣaya parigrahaḥ tu saṃpramoṣaḥ steyam kasmāt sādṛśyāt muṣa steye iti asmāt pramoṣa pada vyutpatteḥ etat uktam bhavati sarve pramāṇa ādayaḥ anadhigatam artham sāmānyatas prakārataḥ vā adhigamayanti smṛtiḥ punar na pūrva anubhava maryādām atikrāmati tad viṣayā tad ūna viṣayāḥ vā na tu tad adhika viṣayā saḥ ayam vṛtti antarāt viśeṣaḥ smṛteḥ iti vimṛśati kim pratyayasya iti 
TV_1.11.2^2	 grāhya pravaṇa tvāt anubhavasya sva anubhava abhāvāt tad jaḥ saṃskāraḥ grāhyam eva smārayati iti pratibhāti anubhava mātra janita tvāt ca anubhavam eva iti vimṛśya upapattitaḥ ubhaya smaraṇam avadhārayati grāhya pravaṇa tayā grāhya uparaktaḥ paramārthataḥ tu grāhya grahaṇe eva ubhayam tayoḥ ākāram svarūpam nirbhāsayati prakāśayati sva vyañjakam kāraṇam añjanam ākāraḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ sva kāraṇa ākāraḥ iti arthaḥ vyañjakam udbodhakam tena añjanam phala abhimukhīkaraṇam yasya iti vā iti arthaḥ nanu yadi kāraṇa vicāreṇa buddhi smaraṇayoḥ sārūpyam kaḥ tarhi bhedaḥ iti atas āha tatra grahaṇa iti 
TV_1.11.2^3	 grahaṇam upādānam na ca gṛhītasya upāttasya upādānam saṃbhavati tat anena anadhigata bodhanam buddhiḥ iti uktam grahaṇa ākāraḥ grahaṇa rūpam pūrvam pradhānam yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā vikalpitaḥ ca ayam abhede api guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ iti grāhya ākāraḥ pūrvaḥ prathamaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā idam eva ca grāhya ākārasya grāhyasya pūrva tvam yat vṛtti antara viṣayīkṛta tvam arthasya tat anena vṛtti antara viṣayīkṛta gocarā smṛtiḥ iti uktam bhavati saḥ ayam asaṃpramoṣaḥ iti nanu asti smṛteḥ api saṃpramoṣaḥ darśayati hi pitṛ ādeḥ atītasya deśa kāla antara anubhūtasya ananubhūta cara deśa kāla antara saṃbandhaḥ svapnaḥ iti atas āha sā ca dvayī iti 
TV_1.11.2^4–1.12.2	 bhāvitaḥ kalpitaḥ smartavyaḥ yayā sā tathā uktā abhāvitaḥ akalpitaḥ pāramārthikaḥ iti yāvat na iyam smṛtiḥ api tu viparyayaḥ tad lakṣaṇa upapanna tvāt smṛtya ābhāsa tayā tu smṛtiḥ uktāḥ pramāṇa ābhāsam iva pramāṇam iti bhāvaḥ kasmāt punar ante smṛteḥ upanyāsaḥ iti atas āha sarvāḥ smṛtayaḥ iti anubhavaḥ prāptiḥ prāpti pūrvā vṛttiḥ smṛtiḥ tatas smṛtīnām upajanaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu ye puruṣam kliśnanti te niroddhavyāḥ prekṣāvatā kleśāḥ ca tathā na ca vṛttayaḥ tat kimartham āsām nirodhaḥ iti atas āha sarvāḥ ca etāḥ iti sugamam abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ nirodha upāyam pṛcchati atha iti sūtreṇa uttaram āha abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ abhyāsa vairāgyayoḥ nirodhe janayitavye avāntara vyāpāra bhedena samuccayaḥ na tu vikalpaḥ iti āha citta nadī iti prāgbhāraḥ prabandhaḥ nimna tā gambhīra tā agādhata iti yāvat 
TV_1.13.1–1.13.2	 tatra sthitau yatnaḥ abhyāsaḥ tatra abhyāsasya svarūpa prayojanābhyām lakṣaṇam āha tatra sthitau yatnaḥ abhyāsaḥ tat vyācaṣṭe cittasya āvṛttikasya rājasa tāmasa vṛtti rahitasya praśānta vāhi tā vimala tā sāttvika vṛtti vāhitā ekāgra tā sthitiḥ tad arthaḥ iti sthitau iti nimitta saptamī vyākhyātāḥ yathā carmaṇi dvīpinam hanti iti prayatnam eva paryāyābhyām viśadayati vīryam utsāhaḥ iti tasya icchā yonitām āha tad saṃpipādayiṣayā tat iti sthitim parāmṛśati prayatnasya viṣayam āha tad sādhana iti sthiti sādhanāni antaraṅga bahis aṅgāṇi yama niyama ādīni sādhana gocaraḥ kartṛ vyāpāraḥ na phala gocaraḥ iti 
TV_1.14.1–1.14.2	 sa tu dīrgha kāla nairantarya satkāra āsevitaḥ dṛḍha bhūmiḥ nanu vyutthāna saṃskāreṇa anādinā paripanthinā pratibaddhaḥ abhyāsaḥ katham sthityai kalpate iti atas āha sa tu dīrgha kāla nairantarya satkāra āsevitaḥ dṛḍha bhūmiḥ saḥ ayam abhyāsaḥ viśeṣaṇa traya saṃpannaḥ san dṛḍha avasthaḥ na sahasā vyutthāna saṃskāraiḥ abhibhūta sthiti rūpa viṣayaḥ bhavati yadi punar evaṃbhūtam api abhyāsam kṛtvā uparamet tatas kāla parivāsena abhibhūyeta tasmāt na uparantavyam iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.15.1–1.15.2^1	 dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya vaśīkāra saṃjñā vairāgyam vairāgyam āha dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya vaśīkāra saṃjñā vairāgyam cetana acetaneṣu dṛṣṭa viṣayeṣu vitṛṣṇatām āha striyaḥ iti aiśvaryam ādhipatyam anuśravaḥ vedaḥ tatas adhigatāḥ ānuśravikāḥ svarga ādayaḥ tatra api vaitṛṣṇyam āha svarga iti deha rahitāḥ videhāḥ karaṇeṣu līnāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ vaidehyam anye tu prakṛtim eva ātmānam abhimanyamānāḥ prakṛti upāsakāḥ prakṛtau sa adhikārāyām eva līnāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ prakṛti laya tvam tad prāpti viṣaye ānuśravika viṣaye vitṛṣṇasya anuśravika viṣaye vitṛṣṇaḥ hi svarga ādi prāpti viṣaye vitṛṣṇaḥ iti ucyate nanu yadi vaitṛṣṇya mātram vairāgyam hanta viṣaya aprāptau api tat asti iti vairāgyam syāt iti atas āha divya ādivya iti na vaitṛṣṇya mātram vairāgyam api tu divya ādivya viṣai saṃprayoge api cittasya anābhoga ātmikā tām eva spaṣṭayati heya upādeya śūnyā āsaṅga dveṣa rahita upekṣā buddhiḥ vaśīkāra saṃjñā 
TV_1.15.2^2	 kutas punar iyam iti atra āha prasaṃkhyāna balāt iti tāpa traya parīta tā viṣayāṇām doṣaḥ tad paribhāvanayā tad sākṣātkāraḥ prasaṃkhyānam tat balāt iti arthaḥ yatamāna saṃjñā vyatireka saṃjñā eka indriya saṃjñā vaśīkāra saṃjñā ca iti catasraḥ saṃjñā iti āgaminaḥ rāga ādayaḥ khalu kaṣāyāḥ citta vartinaḥ taiḥ indriyāṇi yathāsvam viṣayeṣu pravartante tat mā pravartiṣata indriyāṇi tad tad viṣayeṣu iti tad paripācanāya ārambhaḥ prayatnaḥ sā yatamāna saṃjñā tad ārambhe sati kecid kaṣāyāḥ pakvāḥ pacyante pakṣyante ca kecid tatra pakṣyamāṇebhyaḥ pakvānām vyatirekeṇa avadhāraṇam vyatireka saṃjñā indriya pravartanā samartha tayā pakvānām autsukya mātreṇa manasi vyavasthānam eka indriya saṃjñā autsukya mātrasya api nivṛttiḥ upasthiteṣu api divya ādivya viṣayeṣu upekṣā buddhiḥ saṃjñā trayāt parā vaśīkāra saṃjñā etayā eva ca pūrvāsām caritārtha tvāt na tāḥ pṛthak uktāḥ iti sarvam avadātam 
TV_1.16.1–1.16.2^1	 tat param puruṣa khyāteḥ guṇa vaitṛṣṇyam aparam vairāgyam uktvā param āha tat param puruṣa khyāteḥ guṇa vaitṛṣṇyam apara vairāgyasya param vairāgyam prati kāraṇa tvam tatra ca dvāram ādarśayati dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya doṣa darśī viraktaḥ iti anena aparam vairāgyam darśitam puruṣa darśana abhyāsāt āgama anumāna ācārya upadeśa samadhigatasya puruṣasya darśanam tasya abhyāsaḥ paunaḥpunyena niṣevaṇam tasmāt tasya darśanasya śuddhiḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ parihāṇyā sattva eka tāna tā tayā yaḥ guṇa puruṣayoḥ prakarṣeṇa vivekaḥ puruṣaḥ śuddhaḥ anantaḥ tad viparītāḥ guṇāḥ iti tena āpyāyitā buddhiḥ yasya yoginaḥ sa tathā uktaḥ tat anena dharma megha ākhyaḥ samādhiḥ uktaḥ 
TV_1.16.2^2	 sa tathābhūtaḥ yogī guṇebhyaḥ vyakta avyakta dharmakebhyaḥ sarvathā viraktaḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyātau api guṇa ātmikāyām yāvat viraktaḥ iti tat tasmāt dvayam vairāgyam pūrvam hi vairāgyam sattva samudreka vidhūta tamasi rajaḥ kaṇa kalaṅka saṃpṛkte citta sattve tat ca tauṣṭikānām api samānam te hi tena eva prakṛti layāḥ babhūvuḥ yathā uktam vairāgyāt prakṛti layaḥ iti tatra tayoḥ dvayoḥ madhye yat uttaram tad jñāna prasāda mātram mātra grahaṇena nirviṣayatām sūcayati tat eva hi tādṛśam citta sattvam rajaḥ leśa malena api aparāmṛṣṭam asya āśrayaḥ atas eva jñāna prasādaḥ iti ucyate citta sattvam hi prasāda svabhāvam api rajaḥ tamaḥ saṃparkāt malina tām anubhavati 
TV_1.16.2^3	 vairāgya abhyāsa vimala vāri dhārā dhauta samasta rajaḥ tamaḥ malam tu ati prasannam jñāna prasāda mātra pariśeṣam bhavati tasya guṇān upādeya tvāya darśayati yasya udaye sati yogī pratyudita khyātiḥ khyāti viśeṣe sati vartamāna khyātimān iti arthaḥ prāpaṇīyam kaivalyam prāptam yathā vakṣyati jīvan eva vidvān muktaḥ bhavati saṃskāra mātrasya cchinna mūlasya siddha tvāt iti bhāvaḥ kutas prāptam yatas kṣīṇāḥ kṣetavyāḥ kleśāḥ avidyā ādayaḥ sa vāsanāḥ nanu asti dharma adharma samūhaḥ bhavasya janma maraṇa prabandhasya saṃkramaḥ prāṇinām tat kutas kaivalyam iti atas āha chinnaḥ iti śliṣṭāni niḥsaṃdhīni parvāṇi yasya sa tathā uktaḥ 
TV_1.16.2^4	 dharma adharma samūhasya samūhinaḥ parvāṇi tāni śliṣṭāni na hi jātu jantuḥ maraṇa janma prabandhena tyakṣyate saḥ ayam bhava saṃkramaḥ kleśa kṣaye chinnaḥ yathā vakṣyati kleśa mūlaḥ karma āśayaḥ sati mūle tad vipākaḥ iti nanu prasaṃkhyāna paripākam dharma megham ca nirodham antarā kim tat asti yat jñāna prasāda mātram iti atas āha jñānasya eva iti dharma megha bhedaḥ eva param vairāgyam na anyat yathā vakṣyati prasaṃkhyāne api akusīdasya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharma meghaḥ samādhiḥ tadā sarva āvaraṇa mala apetasya jñānasya ānantyāt jñeyam alpam iti ca tasmāt etasya hi na antarīyakam avinābhāvi kaivalyam iti 
TV_1.17.1–1.17.2^1	 vitarka vicāra ānanda asmitā rūpa anugamāt saṃprajñātaḥ upāyam abhidhāya sa prakāra upeya kathanāya pṛcchati atha upāya dvayena iti vitarka vicāra ānanda asmitā rūpa anugamāt saṃprajñātaḥ saṃprajñāta pūrvaka tvāt asaṃprajñātasya prathamam saṃprajñāta upavarṇanam saṃprajñāta sāmānyam vitarka vicāra ānanda asmitānām rūpaiḥ svarūpaiḥ anugamāt pratipattavyam vitarkam vivṛṇoti cittasya iti svarūpa sākṣāt kāravatī prajñā bhogaḥ sa ca sthūla viṣaya tvāt sthūlaḥ yathā hi prāthamikaḥ dhānuṣkaḥ sthūlam eva lakṣyam vidhyati atha sūkṣmam evam prāthamikaḥ yogī sthūlam eva pāñcabhautikam catur bhuja ādi dhyeyam sākṣātkaroti atha sūkṣmam iti evam cittasya ālambane sūkṣmaḥ ābhogaḥ sthūla kāraṇa bhūta sūkṣma pañca tanmātra liṅga āliṅga viṣayaḥ vicāraḥ tat evam grāhya viṣayam darśayitvā grahaṇa viṣayam darśayati ānandaḥ iti 
TV_1.17.2^2	 indriye sthūlaḥ ālambane cittasya ābhogaḥ hlādaḥ ānandaḥ prakāśa śīla tayām khalu sattva pradhānāt ahaṃkārāt indriyāṇi utpannāni sattvam sukham iti tāni api sukhāni iti tasmin ābhogaḥ hlādaḥ iti grahītṛ viṣayam saṃprajñātam āha eka ātmikā saṃvid iti asmitā prabhavāni indriyāṇi tena eṣām asmitā sūkṣmam rūpam sā ca ātmanā grahītrā saha buddhiḥ eka ātmikā saṃvid tasyām ca grahītuḥ antarbhāvāt bhavati grahītṛ viṣayaḥ saṃprajñātaḥ iti caturṇām aparam api avāntara viśeṣam āha tatra prathamaḥ iti kāryam kāraṇa anupraviṣṭam na kāraṇam kāryeṇa tat ayam sthūlaḥ ābhogaḥ sthūla sūkṣma indriya asmitā kāraṇa catuṣṭaya anugataḥ bhavati uttare tu tri dvi eka kāraṇakāḥ tri dvi eka rūpāḥ bhavanti asaṃprajñātāt bhinatti sarve ete iti 
TV_1.18.1–1.18.2^1	 virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ saṃskāra śeṣaḥ anyaḥ krama prāptam asaṃprajñātam avatārayitum pṛcchati atha iti virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ saṃskāra śeṣaḥ anyaḥ pūrva padena upāya kathanam uttarābhyām ca svarūpa kathanam madhyamam padam vivṛṇoti sarva vṛtti iti prathamam padam vyācaṣṭe tasya param iti virāmaḥ vṛttīnām abhāvaḥ tasya pratyayaḥ kāraṇam tasya abhyāsaḥ tad anuṣṭhānam paunaḥpunyam tat eva pūrvam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ atha aparam vairāgyam nirodha kāraṇam kasmāt na bhavati iti atas āha sa ālambanaḥ hi iti kārya sarūpam kāraṇam yujyate na virūpam 
TV_1.18.2^2	 virūpam ca aparam vairāgyam sa ālambanam nirālambana samādhinā kāryeṇa tasmāt nirālambanāt eva jñāna prasāda mātrāt tasya utpattiḥ yuktāḥ dharma megha samādhiḥ eva hi nitānta vigalita rajaḥ tamaḥ malāt buddhi sattvāt upajātaḥ tad tad viṣaya atikrameṇa pravartamānaḥ anantaḥ viṣaya avadya darśī samasta viṣaya parityāgāt ca svarūpa pratiṣṭhaḥ san nirālambanaḥ saṃskāra mātra śeṣasya nirālambanasya samādheḥ kāraṇam upapadyate sārūpyāt iti ālambanīkaraṇam āśrayaṇam abhāva prāptam iva vṛtti rūpa kārya akaraṇāt nirbījaḥ nirālambanaḥ athavā bījam kleśa karma āśayāḥ te niṣkrāntāḥ yasmāt sa tathā 
TV_1.19.1–1.19.2^1	 bhava pratyayaḥ videha prakṛti layānām nirodha samādheḥ avāntara bhedam hāna upādāna aṅgam ādarśayati sa khalu ayam nirodha samādhiḥ dvividhaḥ upāya pratyayaḥ bhava pratyayaḥ ca upāyaḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ śraddhā ādiḥ pratyayaḥ kāraṇam yasya nirodha samādheḥ sa tathā uktaḥ bhavanti jāyante asyām jantavaḥ iti bhavaḥ avidyā bhūta indriyeṣu vā vikāreṣu prakṛtiṣu vā avyakta mahat ahaṃkāra pañca tanmātreṣu anātmasu ātma khyātiḥ tauṣṭikānām vairāgya saṃpannānām sa khalu ayam bhavaḥ pratyayaḥ kāraṇam yasya nirodha samādheḥ sa bhava pratyayaḥ tatra tayoḥ madhye upāya pratyayaḥ yoginām mokṣyamāṇānām bhavati viśeṣa vidhānena śeṣasya mumukṣu saṃbandham niṣedhati keṣām tarhi bhava pratyayaḥ iti atra sūtreṇa uttaram āha bhava pratyayaḥ videha prakṛti layānām 
TV_1.19.2^2	 videhāḥ ca prakṛti layāḥ ca teṣām iti arthaḥ tat vyācaṣṭe videhānām devānām bhava pratyayaḥ bhūta indriyāṇām anyatamat ātma tvena pratipannāḥ tad upāsanayā tad vāsanā vāsita antaḥkaraṇāḥ piṇḍa pāta anantaram indriyeṣu bhūteṣu vā līnāḥ saṃskāra mātra a= aśeṣa manasaḥ ṣāṣ kauśika śarīra rahitāḥ videhāḥ te hi sva saṃskāra mātra upayogena cittena kaivalya padam iva anubhavantaḥ prāpnuvantaḥ videhāḥ avṛttika tvam ca kaivalyena sārūpyam sādhikāra saṃskāra śeṣa tā ca vairūpyam saṃskāra mātra upabhogena iti kvacid pāṭhaḥ tasya arthaḥ saṃskāra mātram eva upabhogaḥ yasya na tu citta vṛttiḥ iti arthaḥ prāptau= adhayaḥ sva saṃskāra vipākam tathājātīyakam ativāhayanti atikrāmanti punar api saṃsāre viśanti tathā ca vāyu proktam 
TV_1.19.3–1.19.6	 daśa manvantarāṇi iha tiṣṭhanti indriya cintakāḥ bhautikāḥ tu śatam pūrṇam iti tathā prakṛti layāḥ ca avyakta mahat ahaṃkāra pañca tanmātreṣu anyatamat ātma tvena pratipannāḥ tad upāsanayā tad vāsanā vāsita antaḥkaraṇāḥ piṇḍa pāta anantaram avyakta ādīnām anyatamasmin līnāḥ sa adhikāre acarita arthe evam hi caritārtham cetaḥ syāt yadi viveka khyātim api janayet ajanita sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyāteḥ tu cetasaḥ acarita arthasya asti sa adhikāra tā iti sa adhikāre cetasi prakṛti līne kaivalya padam iva anubhavanti yāvat na punar āvartate adhikāra vaśāt cittam iti prakṛti sāmyam upagatam api avadhim prāpya punar api prādurbhavati tatas vivicyate yathā varṣā atipāte mṛd bhāvam upagataḥ maṇḍūka dehaḥ punar ambhoda vāridhārā vasekāt maṇḍūka deha bhāvam anubhavati iti tathā ca vāyu proktam sahasram tu ābhimānikāḥ bauddhāḥ daśa sahasrāṇi tiṣṭhanti vigata jvarāḥ pūrṇam śata sahasram tu tiṣṭhanti avyakta cintakāḥ puruṣam nirguṇam prāpya kāla saṃkhyā na vidyate iti taḥ asya punarbhava prāpti hetu tayā heya tvam siddham 
TV_1.20.1–1.20.2^1	 śraddhā vīrya smṛti samādhi prajñā pūrvakaḥ itareṣām yoginām tu samādheḥ upāya kramam āha śraddhā vīrya smṛti samādhi prajñā pūrvakaḥ itareṣām nanu indriya ādi cintakāḥ api śraddhāvantaḥ eva iti atas āha śraddhā cetasaḥ saṃprasādaḥ sa ca āgama anumāna ācārya upadeśa samadhigata tattva viṣayaḥ bhavati hi cetasaḥ saṃprasādaḥ abhiruciḥ ati icchā śraddhā na indriya ādiṣu ātma abhimāninām abhiruciḥ asaṃprasādaḥ hi sa vyāmoha mūla tvāt iti arthaḥ kutas asau eva śraddhā iti atas āha sā hi jananī iva kalyāṇī yoginam pāti vimārga pāta janmanaḥ anarthāt saḥ ayam icchā viśeṣaḥ iṣyamāṇa viṣayam prayatnam prasūtaḥ iti āha tasya hi śraddadhānasya 
TV_1.20.2^2	 tasya vivaraṇam viveka arthinaḥ vīryam upajāyate smṛtiḥ dhyānam anākulam avikṣiptam samādhīyate yoga aṅga samādhi yuktam bhavati yama niyama ādinā āntarīyaka samādhi upanyāsena ca yama niyama ādayaḥ api sūcitāḥ tat evam akhila yoga aṅga saṃpannasya saṃprajñātaḥ jāyate iti āha samāhita cittasya iti prajñāyāḥ vivekaḥ prakarṣaḥ upajāyate saṃprajñāta pūrvam asaṃprajñāta utpādam āha tad abhyāsāt tatra eva tad tad bhūmi prāptau tad tad viṣayāt ca vairāgyāt asaṃprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ bhavati sa hi kaivalya hetuḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyāti pūrvaḥ hi nirodhaḥ cittam akhila kārya karaṇena caritārtham adhikārāt avasādayati 
TV_1.21.1–1.21.2	 tīvra saṃvegānām āsannaḥ nanu śraddhā ādayaḥ ced yoga upāyāḥ tarhi sarveṣām aviśeṣeṇa samādhi tad phale syātām dṛśyate tu kasyacid siddhiḥ kasyacid asiddhiḥ kasyacid cireṇa siddhiḥ kasyacid ciratareṇa kasyacid kṣipram iti atas āha te khalu nava yoginaḥ iti upāyāḥ śraddhā ādayaḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātrāḥ prāc bhavīya saṃskāra adṛṣṭa vaśāt yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ saṃvegaḥ vairāgyam tasya api mṛdu madhyatīvra tā prāc bhavīya vāsana adṛṣṭa vaśāt eva iti teṣu yādṛśām kṣepīyasī siddhiḥ tān darśayati sūtreṇa tīvra saṃvegānām āsannaḥ iti sūtram śeṣam bhāṣyam samādheḥ saṃprajñātasya phalam asaṃprajñātaḥ tasya api kaivalyam 
TV_1.22.1–1.23.2	 mṛdu madhya adhimātra tvāt tatas api viśeṣaḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātra tvāt tatas api viśeṣaḥ nigada vyākhyātena bhāṣyeṇa vyākhyātam iti īśvara praṇidhānāt vā sūtra antaram pātayitum vimṛśati kim etasmāt eva iti na vā śabdaḥ saṃśaya nivartakaḥ īśvara praṇidhānāt vā vyācaṣṭe praṇidhānāt bhakti viśeṣāt mānasāt vācikāt kāyikāt vā avarjitaḥ abhimukhīkṛtaḥ tam anugṛhṇāti abhidhyānam anāgata artha icchā idam asya abhimatam astu iti tanmātreṇa na vyāpāra antareṇa śeṣam sugamam 
TV_1.24.1–1.24.2^1	 kleśa karma vipāka āśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ nanu cetna acetanābhyām eva vyūḍham na anyena viśvam īśvaraḥ ced acetanaḥ tarhi pradhānam pradhāna vikārāṇām api pradhānam adhyapātāt tathā ca na tasya āvarjanam acetana tvāt atha cetanaḥ tathā api citi śakteḥ audāsīnyāt asaṃsāritayā ca asmita ādi virahāt kutas āvarjanam kutas ca abhidhyānam iti āśayavān āha atha pradhāna iti atra sūtreṇa uttaram āha kleśa karma vipāka āśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ kliśnanti khalu amī puruṣam sāṃsārikam vividha duḥkha prahāreṇa iti kuśala akuśalāni iti dharma adharmāḥ teṣām ca karma ja tvāt upacārāt karma tvam vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ vipāka anuguṇāḥ vāsanāḥ tāḥ citta bhūmau āśeratas iti āśayāḥ na hi karabhaja ati nirvartakam karma prāc bhavīya karabha bhoga bhāvitām bhāvanām na yāvat abhivyanakti tāvat kara bha ucitāya bhogāya kalpate 
TV_1.24.2^2	 tasmāt bhavati karabhaja ati anubhava janmā bhāvanā karabha vipāka anuguṇa iti nanu amī kleśa ādayaḥ buddhi dharmāḥ na kathaṃcid api puruṣam parāmṛśanti tasmāt puruṣa grahaṇāt eva tad aparāmarśa siddheḥ kṛtam kleśa karma ityādinā iti atas āha te ca manasi vartamānāḥ sāṃsārike puruṣe vyapadiśyante kasmāt sa hi tad phalasya bhoktā cetayitā iti tasmāt puruṣa tvāt īśvarasya api tad saṃbandhaḥ prāptaḥ iti tad pratiṣedhaḥ upapadyate iti āha yaḥ hi anena buddhi sthena api puruṣa mātra sādhāraṇena bhogena aparāmṛṣṭaḥ sa puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ viśiṣyate iti viśeṣaḥ puruṣa antarāt vyavacchidyate viśeṣa padasya vyāvartyam darśayitu kāmaḥ paricodanā pūrvam pariharati kaivalyam prāptāḥ tarhi iti prakṛti layānām prākṛtaḥ bandhaḥ vaikārikaḥ bandhaḥ videhānām dakṣiṇa ādi bandhaḥ divya ādivya viṣaya bhoga bhājām tāni amūni trīṇi bandhanāni 
TV_1.24.2^3	 prakṛti bhāvanā saṃskṛta manasaḥ hi deha pāta anantaram eva prakṛti layatām āpannāḥ iti itareṣām pūrvā bandha koṭiḥ prajñāyate tena uttara koṭi vidhāna mātram iha tu pūrva apara koṭi niṣedhaḥ iti saṃkṣipya viśeṣam darśayati sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvaraḥ iti jñāna kriyā śakti saṃpad aiśvaryam atra pṛcchati yaḥ asau iti jñāna kriye hi na cicchakteḥ apariṇāminyāḥ saṃbhavate iti rajaḥ tamaḥ rahita viśuddha citta sattva āśraye vaktavye na ca īśvarasya sadā muktasya avidyā prabhava citta sattva samutkarṣeṇa saha sva svāmi bhāvaḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati iti atas uktam prakṛṣṭa sattva upādānāt iti na īśvarasya pṛthagjanasya iva avidyā nibandhanaḥ citta sattvena sva svāmi bhāvaḥ kim tu tāpa traya parītān pretyabhāva mahā arṇavāt jantūn uddhariṣyāmi jñāna dharma upadeśena na ca jñāna kriyā sāmarthya atiśaya saṃpattim antareṇa tad upadeśaḥ 
TV_1.24.2^4	 na ca iyam apahata rajaḥ tamaḥ mala viśuddha sattva upādānam vinā iti ālocya sattva prakarṣam upādatte bhagavān aparāmṛṣṭaḥ api avidyayā avidyā abhimānī ca avidyāyāḥ tattvam avidvān bhavati na punar avidyām avidyā tvena sevamānaḥ na khalu śailūṣaḥ rāma tvam āropya tāḥ tāḥ ceṣṭāḥ darśayan bhrāntaḥ bhavati tat idam āhāryam asya rūpam na tāttvikam iti syāt etat uddidhīrṣayā bhagavatā sattvam upādeyam tad upādānena ca tad uddidhīrṣā asyāḥ api prākṛta tvāt tathā ca anyonya āśrayaḥ iti atas uktam śāśvatikaḥ iti bhavet etat evam yadi idaṃprathama tā sargasya bhavet anādau tu sarga saṃhāra prabandhe sarga antara samutpanna saṃjihīrṣā vadhi samaye pūrṇe mayā sattva prakarṣaḥ upādeyaḥ iti praṇidhānam kṛtvā bhagavān jagat saṃjahāra tadā ca īśvara citta sattvam praṇidhāna vāsitam pradhāna sāmyam upagatam api paripūrṇaḥ mahāpralaya avadhau praṇidhāna vāsanā vaśāt tathā eva īśvara citta sattva bhāvena pariṇamate 
TV_1.24.2^5	 yathā caitraḥ śvas prātar eva utthātavyam mayā iti praṇidhāya suptaḥ tadā eva uttiṣṭhati praṇidhāna saṃskārāt tasmāt anādi tvāt īśvara praṇidhāna sattva upādānayoḥ śāśvatika tvena na anyonya āśrayaḥ na ca īśvarasya citta sattvam mahāpralaye api na prakṛti sāmyam upaiti iti vācyam yasya hi na kadācid api pradhāna sāmyam na tat prādhānikam na api citi śaktiḥ ajña tvāt iti artha antaram aprāmāṇikam āpadyeta tat ca ayuktam prakṛti puruṣa vyatirekeṇa artha antara abhāvāt saḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ īśvarasya śāśvatikaḥ utkarṣaḥ sa kim sa nimittaḥ sa pramāṇakaḥ āhosvit nirnimittaḥ niṣpramāṇakaḥ iti uttaram tasya śāstram nimittam śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇāni śāstram codayati śāstram punar kiṃnimittam pratyakṣa anumāna pūrvam hi śāstram na ca īśvarasya sattva prakarṣe kasyacid pratyakṣam anumānam vā asti na ca īśvara pratyakṣa prabhavam śāstram iti yuktam 
TV_1.24.2^6	 kalpayitvā api hi ayam brūyāt ātma aiśvarya prakāśanāya iti bhāvaḥ pariharati prakṛṣṭa sattva nimittam ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ mantra āyurvedeṣu tāvat īśvara praṇīteṣu pravṛtti sāmarthyāt artha avyabhicāra viniścayāt prāmāṇyam siddham na ca oṣadhi bhedānām tad saṃyoga viśeṣāṇām ca mantrāṇām ca tad tad varṇa avāpa uddhāreṇa sahasreṇa api puruṣa āyuṣaiḥ laukika pramāṇa vyavahārī śaktaḥ kartum anvaya vyatirekau na ca āgamāt anvaya vyatirekau tābhyām ca āgamaḥ tad saṃtānayoḥ anādi tvāt iti pratipādayitum yuktam mahāpralaye tad saṃtānayoḥ vicchedāt na ca tad bhāve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ abhinnam pradhāna vikāraḥ jagat iti hi pratipādayiṣyate sadṛśa pariṇāmasya ca visadṛśa pariṇāma tā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā kṣīra ikṣu rasa ādeḥ dadhi guḍa ādi rūpam visadṛśa pariṇāmasya pūrvam sadṛśa pariṇāma tā ca dṛṣṭāḥ tat iha pradhānena api mahat ahaṃkāra ādi rūpa visadṛśa pariṇāmena satā bhāvyam kadācid sadṛśa pariṇāmena api 
TV_1.24.2^7	 sadṛśa pariṇāmaḥ ca asya sāmya avasthā sa ca mahāpralayaḥ tasmāt mantra āyurveda praṇayanāt tāvat bhagavataḥ vigalita rajaḥ tamaḥ mala āvaraṇa tayā paritas pradyotamānam buddhi sattvam āstheyam tathā ca abhyudaya niḥśreyasa upadeśa paraḥ api veda rāśiḥ īśvara praṇītaḥ tad buddhi sattva prakarṣāt eva bhavitum arhati na ca sattva utkarṣe rajaḥ tamaḥ prabhavau vibhrama vipralambhau saṃbhavataḥ tat siddham prakṛṣṭa sattva nimittam śāstram iti syāt etat prakarṣa kārya tayā prakarṣam bodhayat śāstram śeṣavat anumānam bhavet na tu āgamaḥ iti atas āha etayoḥ iti na kāryatvena bodhayati api tu anādi vācya vācaka bhāva saṃbandhena bodhayati iti arthaḥ īśvarasya hi buddhi sattve prakarṣaḥ vartate śāstram api tad vācaka tvena tatra vartate iti upasaṃharati etasmāt īśvara buddhi sattva prakarṣa vācakāt śāstrāt etat bhavati jñāyate viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ lakṣaṇāt sadā eva īśvaraḥ sadā eva muktaḥ iti 
TV_1.24.2^8–1.25.1	 tat evam puruṣa antarāt vyavacchidya īśvara antarāt api vyavacchinatti tat ca tasya iti atiśaya vinirmuktim āha na tāvat iti kutas yat eva iti kasmāt sarva atiśaya vinirmuktam tat aiśvaryam iti atas āha tasmāt yatra iti atiśaya niṣṭhām aprāptānām aupacārikam aiśvaryam iti arthaḥ sāmya vinirmuktim āha na ca tad samānam iti prākāmyam avihata icchatā tad vighātān ūna tvam anūna tve vā dvayoḥ api prākāmya vighātaḥ kārya anutpatteḥ utpattau vā viruddha dharma samāliṅgitam ekadā kāryam upalabhyeta iti āśayavān āha dvayoḥ ca iti aviruddha abhiprāya tve vā pratyekam īśvara tve kṛtam anyaiḥ ekena eva īśanāyāḥ kṛta tvāt saṃbhūyakāri tve vā na kaścid īśvaraḥ pariṣadvan nitya īśanā yoginām ca paryāya ayogāt kalpanā gaurava prasaṅgāt ca iti draṣṭavyam tasmāt sarvam avadātam tatra niratiśayam sarvajña bījam 
TV_1.25.2^1	 evam asya kriyā jñāna śaktau śāstram pramāṇam abhidhāya jñāna śaktau anumānam pramāṇayati kim ca tatra niratiśayam sarvajña bījam vyācaṣṭe yat idam iti buddhi sattva āvaraka tama upagama tāratamyena yat idam atīta anāgata pratyutpannānām pratyekam ca samuccayena ca vartamānānām atīndriyāṇām grahaṇam tasya viśeṣaṇam alpam bahu iti sarvajña bījam kāraṇam kaścid kiṃcid eva atīta ādi gṛhṇāti kaścid bahu kaścid bahutaram kaścid bahutamam iti grāhya apekṣayā grahaṇasya alpa tvam bahu tvam kṛtam etat vivardhamānam yatra niṣkrāntam atiśayāt sa sarvajñaḥ iti tat anena prameya mātram kathitam atra pramāṇayati asti kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ sarvajña bījasya iti sādhya nirdeśaḥ niratiśaya tvam kāṣṭhā yatas param atiśaya vat tā na asti iti tena na avadhi mātreṇa siddha sādhanam sa atiśaya tvāt iti hetuḥ yat yat sa atiśayam tat tat sarvam niratiśayam yathā kuvala āmalaka bilveṣu sa atiśayam mahat tvam ātmani niratiśayam iti vyāptim darśayati parimāṇa vat 
TV_1.25.2^2	 na ca garima ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ iti sāṃpratam na khalu avayava garimā atiśayī garimauvayavinaḥ kim tvā paramāṇubhyaḥ āntya avayavibhyo yāvantaḥ kecana teṣām pratyeka vartinaḥ garimṇaḥ samāhṛtya garimāḥ vardhamāna abhimānaḥ jñānam tu na pratijñā iyam samāpyate iti eka dvi bahu viṣaya tayā yuktam sa atiśayam iti na vyabhicāraḥ upasaṃharati yatra kāṣṭhā iti nanu santi bahavaḥ tīrthakarāḥ buddha arhatakapila ṛṣi prabhṛtayaḥ tat kasmāt te eva sarva jñāḥ na bhavanti asmāt anumānāt iti atas āha sāmānyā iti kutas tarhi tad viśeṣa pratipattiḥ iti atas āha tasya iti buddha ādi praṇītaḥ āgama ābhāsaḥ na tu āgamaḥ sarva pramāṇa bādhi ta kṣaṇika nairātmya ādi mārga upadeśaka tvena vipralambhaka tvāt iti bhāvaḥ tena śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇa lakṣaṇāt āgamataḥ āgacchanti buddhim ārohanti asmāt abhyudaya niḥśreyasa upāyāḥ iti āgamaḥ tasmāt saṃjñā ādi viśeṣa pratipattiḥ saṃjñā viśeṣaḥ śiveśvara ādiḥ śruti ādiṣu prasiddhaḥ ādipadena ṣaṣ aṅga tādaśa avyayate saṃgṛhīte yathā uktam vāyupurāṇe 
TV_1.25.3–1.25.6^1^1	 sarvajña tā tṛptiḥ anādi bodhaḥ svatantra tā nityam alupta śaktiḥ ananta śaktiḥ ca vibhoḥ vidhi jñāḥ ṣaṭ āhuḥ aṅgāni maheśvarasya tathā jñānam vairāgyam aiśvaryam tapaḥ satyam kṣamā dhṛtiḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam ātma saṃbodhaḥ hi adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam eva ca avyayāni daśa etāni nityam tiṣṭhanti śaṃkare iti syāt etat nitya tṛptasya bhagavataḥ vairāgya atiśaya saṃpannasya sva arthe tṛṣṇā saṃbhavāt kāruṇikasya ca sukha eka tāna jana sarjana parasya duḥkha bahula jīva loka janana anupapatteḥ aprayojanasya ca prekṣāvataḥ pravṛtti anupapatteḥ kriyāśakti śālinaḥ api na jagatkriyā iti atas āha tasya ātma anugraha abhāve api iti 
TV_1.25.3–1.25.6^1^2	 bhūtānām prāṇinām anugrahaḥ prayojanam śabda ādi upabhoga viveka khyāti rūpa kārya karaṇāt kila caritārtham cittam nivartate tatas puruṣaḥ kevalī bhavati atas tad prayojanāya kāruṇikaḥ viveka khyāti upāyam kathayati tena ācarita artha tvāt cittasya jantūn i īśvaraḥ puṇya apuṇya sahāyaḥ sukha duḥkhe bhāvayan api na akāruṇikaḥ viveka khyāti upāya kathanāya bhūta anugraham dvāram āha jñāna dharma upadeśena iti jñānam ca dharmaḥ ca jñāna dharmau tayoḥ upadeśena jñāna dharma samuccayāl labdha viveka khyāti paripākāt kalpa pralaye brahmaṇaḥ dina avasāne yatra satya loka varjam jagat astam eti 
TV_1.25.6^2	 mahāpralaye sa satya lokasya brahmaṇaḥ api nidhane saṃsāriṇaḥ sva kāraṇa gāminaḥ atas tadā maraṇa duḥkha bhājaḥ kalpa iti upalakṣaṇam anyadā api sva arjita karma pāka vaśena janma maraṇa ādi bhājaḥ puruṣān uddhariṣyāmi iti kaivalyam prāpya puruṣāḥ uddhṛtāḥ bhavanti iti arthaḥ etat ca karuṇā prayuktasya jñāna dharma upadeśanam kāpilānām api siddham iti āha tathā ca uktam pañcaśikha ācāryeṇa ādi vidvān kapilaḥ iti ādi vidvān iti pañcaśikha ācārya vacanam ādi mukta sva saṃtāna ādi guru viṣayam na tu anādi mukta parama guru viṣayam ādi mukteṣu kadācid mukteṣu vidvatsu kapilaḥ asmākam ādi vidvān muktaḥ saḥ eva ca guruḥ iti kapilasya api jāyamānasya maheśvara anugrahāt eva jñāna prāptiḥ śrūyate iti kapilaḥ nāma viṣṇoḥ avatāra viśeṣaḥ prasiddhaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ tu hiraṇyagarbhaḥ tasya api sāṃkhya yoga prāptiḥ vede śrūyate iti saḥ eva īśvaraḥ ādi vidvān kapilaḥ viṣṇuḥ na svayaṃbhūḥ iti bhāvaḥ svāyaṃbhuvānām tu īśvaraḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.26.1–1.26.2	 pūrveṣām api guruḥ kālena anavacchedāt saṃprati bhagavataḥ brahma ādibhyaḥ viśeṣam āha saḥ eṣaḥ iti pātanikā saḥ eṣaḥ iti sūtram pūrveṣām api guruḥ kālena anavacchedāt vyācaṣṭe pūrve hi iti kālaḥ tu śata varṣa ādiḥ avaccheda arthena avacchedena prayojanena na upāvartate na vartate prakarṣasya gatiḥ prāptiḥ pratyetavyaḥ āgamāt 
TV_1.27.1–1.27.2^1	 tasya vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ tat anena prabandhena bhagavān īśvaraḥ darśitaḥ saṃprati tad praṇidhānam darśayitum tasya vācakam āha tasya vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ vyācaṣṭe vācyaḥ iti tatra pareṣām matam vimarśa dvāreṇa upanyasyati kim asya iti vācaka tvam pratipādaka tvam iti arthaḥ pare hi paśyanti yadi svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃketena asmāt śabdāt ayam arthaḥ pratyetavya iti evam ātmakena abhivyajyeta tatas yatra na asti sa saṃbandhaḥ tatra saṃketa śatena api na vyajyeta na hi pradīpa vyaṅgyaḥ ghaṭaḥ yatra na asti tatra pradīpa sahasreṇa api śakyaḥ vyaṅktum kṛta saṃketaḥ tu karabha śabdaḥ vāraṇe vāraṇa pratipādakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tatas saṃketa kṛtam eva vācaka tvam iti vimṛśya abhimatam avadhārayati sthitaḥ asya iti ayam abhiprāyaḥ sarve eva śabdāḥ sarva ākāra artha abhidhāna samarthāḥ iti sthitaḥ eva eṣām sarva ākāraiḥ arthaiḥ svābhāvikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ īśvara saṃketaḥ tu prakāśakaḥ ca niyāmakaḥ ca 
TV_1.27.2^2	 tasya īśvara saṃketā saṃketa kṛtaḥ ca asya vācaka apabhraṃśa vibhāgaḥ tat idam āha saṃketaḥ tu īśvarasya iti nidarśanam āha yathā iti nanu śabdasya prādhānikasya mahāpralaya samaye pradhāna bhāvam upagatasya śaktiḥ api pralīnā tatas mahat ādi krameṇa utpannasya avācakasya eva māheśvareṇa saṃketena na śakyā vācaka śaktiḥ abhivyañjayitum vinaṣṭa śakti tvāt iti atas āha sarga antareṣu api iti yadi api saha śaktyā pradhāna sāmyam upagataḥ śabdaḥ tathā api punar āvirbhavan tad śakti yukta eva āvirbhavati varṣa atipāta samadhi gata mṛd bhāvaḥ iva udbhijjaḥ megha visṛṣṭa vāridhārā avasekāt tena pūrva saṃbandha saṃketa anusāreṇa saṃketaḥ kriyate bhagavatā iti tasmāt saṃpratipatteḥ sadṛśa vyavahāra paramparāyāḥ nitya tayā nityaḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ na kūṭastha nityaḥ iti āgamikāḥ pratijānate na punar āgama nirapekṣāḥ sarga antareṣu api tādṛśaḥ eva saṃketaḥ iti pratipattum īśate iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.28.1–1.28.2	 tad japaḥ tad artha bhāvanam vācakam ākhyāya praṇidhānam āha tad japaḥ tad artha bhāvanam vyācaṣṭe praṇavasya iti bhāvanam punar punar citte niveśanam tatas kim sidhyati iti atas āha praṇavam iti ekasmin bhagavati āramati cittam atra eva vaiyāsikīm gāthām udāharati tathā ca iti tatas īśvaraḥ samādhi tad phala lābhena tam anugṛhṇāti 
TV_1.29.1–1.29.2^1	 tatas pratyak cetanā adhigamaḥ api antarāya abhāvaḥ ca kim ca aparam asmāt tatas pratyak cetanā adhigamaḥ api antarāya abhāvaḥ ca pratīpam viparītam añcati vijānāti iti pratyak sa ca asau cetanaḥ ca iti pratyak cetanaḥ avidyāvān puruṣaḥ tat anena īśvarāt śāśvatika sattva utkarṣa saṃpannāt vidyāvataḥ nivartayati pratīcaḥ cetanasya adhigamaḥ jñānam svarūpataḥ asya bhavati antarāyāḥ vakṣyamāṇāḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca asya vivaraṇam ye tāvat iti svam ātmā tasya rūpam rūpa grahaṇena avidyā samāropitān dharmān niṣedhati nanu īśvara praṇidhānam īśvara viṣayam katham iva pratyak cetanam sākṣātkaroti atiprasaṅgāt iti atas āha yathā eva īśvaraḥ iti 
TV_1.29.2^2	 śuddhaḥ kūṭastha nityatayā udaya vyaya rahitaḥ prasannaḥ kleśa varjitaḥ kevalaḥ dharma adharma apetaḥ atas eva anupasargaḥ upasargāḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ sādṛśyasya kiṃcid bheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt īśvarāt bhinatti buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī iti tat anena pratyak grahaṇam vyākhyātam atyanta vidharmiṇoḥ anyatara artha anucintanam na tad itarasya sākṣātkārāya kalpate sadṛśa artha anucintanam tu sadṛśa antara sākṣātkāra upayogi tām anubhavati eka śāstra abhyāsaḥ iva tad sadṛśa artha śāstra antara jñāna upayogi tām pratyāsattiḥ tu sva ātmani sākṣātkāra hetuḥ na parātmani iti sarvam avadātam 
TV_1.30.1–1.30.2^1	 vyādhiḥ tyāna saṃśaya pramāda ālasya āvirati bhrānti darśana alabdha bhūmika tva anavasthita tvāni citta vikṣepāḥ te antarāyāḥ pṛcchati atha kaḥ iti sāmānyena uttaram yaḥ iti viśeṣa saṃkhye pṛcchati kaḥ iti uttaram vyādhi ityādi sūtram antarāyāḥ nava etāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ yoga antarāyāḥ yoga virodhinaḥ cittasya vikṣepa kāś cittam khalu amī vyādhi ādayaḥ yogāt vikṣipanti apanayanti iti vikṣepāḥ yoga pratipakṣa tve hetum āha saha etaḥ iti saṃśaya bhrānti darśane tāvat vṛtti tayā vṛtti nirodha pratipakṣau ye api na vṛttayaḥ vyādhi prabhṛtayaḥ te api vṛtti sāhacaryāt tad pratipakṣāḥ iti arthaḥ padārthān vyācaṣṭe vyādhiḥ iti dhātavaḥ vāta pitta śleṣmāṇaḥ śarīra dhāraṇāt aśita pīta āhāra pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ rasaḥ 
TV_1.30.2^2	 karaṇāni indriyāṇi teṣām vaiṣamyam nyūna adhika bhāvaḥ iti akarmaṇya tā karma anarhatā saṃśayaḥ ubhaya koṭi spṛś vijñānam sati api atad rūpa pratiṣṭha tvena saṃśaya viparyāsayoḥ abhede ubhaya koṭi sparśa asparśa rūpa avāntara viśeṣa vivakṣayā atra bhedena upanyāsaḥ abhāvanam akaraṇam tatra aprayatnaḥ iti yāvat kāyasya guru tvam kapha ādinā cittasya guru tvam tamasā gardhaḥ tṛṣṇā madhumati ādayaḥ samādhi bhūmayaḥ labdha bhūmeḥ yadi tāvatā eva susthitaṃmanyasya samādhi bhreṣaḥ syāt tatas tasyāḥ api bhūmeḥ apāyaḥ syāt yasmāt samādhi pratilambhe tad avasthitam syāt tasmāt tatra prayatitavyam iti 
TV_1.31.1–1.31.2	 duḥkha daurmanasya aṅgamejayatva śvāsa praśvāsāḥ vikṣepa sahabhuvaḥ na kevalam nava antarāyāḥ duḥkha ādayaḥ api asya tad sahabhuvaḥ bhavanti iti āha duḥkha ityādi pratikūla vedanīyam duḥkham ādhyātmikam śārīram vyādhi vaśāt mānasam ca kāma ādi vaśāt ādhibhautikam vyāghra ādi janitam ādhidaivikam graha pīḍā ādi janitam tat ca idam duḥkham prāṇi mātrasya pratikūla vedanīya tayā heyam iti āha yena abhihatāḥ iti anicchataḥ prāṇaḥ yat bāhyam vāyum ācāmati pibati praveśayati iti yāvat sa śvāsaḥ samādhi aṅga recaka virodhī anicchataḥ api prāṇaḥ yat kauṣṭhyam vāyum niścārayati niḥsārayati sa praśvāsaḥ samādhi aṅga pūraka virodhī 
TV_1.32.1–1.32.2^1	 tad pratiṣedha artham eka tattva abhyāsaḥ ukta artha upasaṃhāra sūtram avatārayati atha ete iti atha ukta artha anantaram upasaṃharan idam sūtram āha iti saṃbandhaḥ niroddhavya tve hetuḥ uktaḥ samādhi pratipakṣāḥ iti yadi api īśvara praṇidhānāt iti abhyāsa mātram uktam tathā api vairāgyam iha tad sahakāritayā grāhyam iti āha tābhyām ukta lakṣaṇābhyām eva abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām niroddhavyāḥ tatra tayoḥ abhyāsa vairāgyayoḥ madhye abhyāsasya anantara uktasya iti tad pratiṣedha artham ityādi ekam tattvam īśvaraḥ prakṛta tvāt iti vaināśikānām tat sarvam ekāgram eva cittam na asti kiṃcid vikṣiptam iti tad upadeśānām tad arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam iti āha yasya tu iti 
TV_1.32.2^2	 yasya mate pratyarthe arpyamāṇaḥ ekasmin anekasmin vā niyatam yāvat artha avabhāsam utpannam tatra eva samāptam ananya gāmi artha antaram tāvat prathamam gṛhītvā artha antaram api paścāt kasmāt na gṛhṇāti iti atas āha kṣaṇikam ca kṣaṇasya abhedya tvena pūrva paścāt bhāvasya api abhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ asmad mate tu akṣaṇikam cittam sva viṣayaḥ ekasmin anekasmin vā anavasthitam pratikṣaṇam tad tad viṣaya upādāna parityāgābhyām viṣaya aniyatam vikṣiptam atas vikṣepa pariṇāmam apanīya śakya ekāgra tādhātum iti tad upadeśa pravṛttyoḥ na anarthaka tvam iti āha yadi punar idam iti upasaṃharati atas na iti vaināśikam utthāpayati yaḥ api iti 
TV_1.32.2^3	 mā bhūt ekasmin kṣaṇike cittaḥ ekāgra tā ādhāna prayatnaḥ citta saṃtāne tu anādau akṣaṇike vikṣepam apanīya ekāgra tā dhāsyate iti arthaḥ tat etat vikalpya dūṣayati tasya iti tasya darśanaḥ ekāgra tā yadi pravāha cittasya citta saṃtānasya vā dharmaḥ tatra ekam krama vat utpādeṣu pratyayeṣu anugatam na asti pravāha cittam kutas yat yāvat asti tasya sarvasya kṣaṇika tvāt akṣaṇikasya ca asattvāt bhavatām darśanaḥ iti bhāvaḥ dvitīyam kalpam gṛhṇāti atha iti sāṃvṛtasya pravāhasya aṃśaḥ pratyayaḥ parama artha san tasya pratyayasya ekāgra tā prayatna sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ dūṣayati sa sarvaḥ sāṃvṛta pravāha apekṣayā sadṛśa pratyaya pravāhī vā visadṛśa pratyaya pravāhī vā 
TV_1.32.2^4	 atas parama artha sattā rūpeṇa pratyartha niyata tvāt yad artha avabhāsa utpannaḥ tatra samāpta tvāt ekāgre eva iti vikṣipta citta anupapattiḥ yat apanayena ekāgra tā adhīyate iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti itas api cittam ekam aneka artham avasthitam ca iti āha yadi ca iti yathā hi maitreṇa adhītasya śāstrasya na caitraḥ smarati yathā vā maitreṇa apacitasya puṇyasya pāpasya vā karma āśayasya phalam tad asaṃbandhī caitraḥ na bhuṅkte evam pratyaya antara dṛṣṭasya pratyaya antaram na smaret pratyaya antara upacitasya vā karma āśayasya phalam ca na pratyaya antaram upabhuñjīta iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.32.2^5	 nanu na ati prasajyete kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati iti viśeṣaṇāt śrāddha vaiśvān arīya iṣṭi ādau akartṛ mātṛ pitṛ putra ādi gāmi phala darśanān madhura rasa bhāvitānām vāmra bīja ādīnām paramparayā phala mādhurya niyamāt iti atas āha samādhīyamānam api etat iti ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ kaḥ khalu eka saṃtāna vartinām pratyayānām saṃtāna antara vartibhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ yena eka saṃtāna vartinā pratyayena anubhūtasya upacitasya ca karma āśayasya tad saṃtāna vartī eva pratyayaḥ smartā bhoktā ca syāt na anya saṃtāna vartī na hi saṃtānaḥ nāma kaścid asti vastu san yaḥ enam saṃtānam saṃtāna antara vartibhyaḥ bhindyāt 
TV_1.32.2^6	 na ca kālpanikaḥ bhedaḥ kriyāyām upapadyate na khalu kalpita agni bhāvaḥ māṇavakaḥ pacati na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva saṃbandhaḥ api vāstavaḥ sahabhuvoḥ savya itara viṣāṇayoḥ iva abhāvāt asaha bhuvoḥ api pratyutpanna āśraya tva ayogāt na hi atīta anāgatau vyāsajjya pratyutpannam vartitum arhataḥ tasmāt saṃtānena vā kārya kāraṇa bhāvena vā svābhāvikena anupahitāḥ parama artha santaḥ pratyayāḥ paraspara asaṃsparśi tvena sva saṃtāna vartibhyaḥ para saṃtāna vartibhyaḥ vā pratyaya antarebhyaḥ na bhidyante saḥ ayam gomayam ca pāyasam ca adhikṛtya pravṛttaḥ nyāyaḥ gomayam pāyasam gavya tvāt ubhaya siddha pāyasa vat iti 
TV_1.32.2^7	 tam ākṣipati nyāya ābhāsa tvena tatas api adhika tvāt iti na ca atra kṛta nāśa akṛta abhyāgamam ca udyam yatas cittam eva karmaṇām kartṛ tat eva tad janitābhyām sukha duḥkhābhyām yujyate sukha duḥkhe ca citi= chāyā āpannam cittam bhuṅkte iti puruṣe bhoga abhimānaḥ citi cittayoḥ abheda grahāt iti sva pratyayam pratītya samutpannānām svabhāvaḥ eva eṣām tādṛśaḥ yat te eva smaranti phalam ca upabhuñjate na tu anye na ca svabhāvāḥ niyoga paryanuyogau arhanti evam bhavata mā evam bhūta iti vā kasmāt na evam iti ca iti yaḥ pūrva ukte na parituṣyati tam pratyāha kim ca sva ātmā iti 
TV_1.32.2^8	 udaya vyaya dharmāṇām anubhavānām anubhava smṛtīnām ca nānātve api tad āśrayam abhinnam cittam aham iti pratyayaḥ pratisaṃdadhānaḥ katham atyanta bhinnān pratyayān ālambeta nanu grahaṇa smaraṇa rūpa kāraṇa bhedāt pārokṣya apārokṣya rūpa viruddha dharma saṃsargāt vā na pratyabhijñānam nāma ekaḥ pratyayaḥ yatas pratyayinaḥ cittasya ekatā syāt iti atas āha sva anubhava iti nanu kāraṇa bheda viruddha dharma saṃsargau eva atra bādhakau uktau iti atas āha na ca pratyakṣasya iti pratyakṣa anusārataḥ eva sāmagrya bhedaḥ pārokṣya apārokṣya dharma avirodhaḥ ca upapāditaḥ nyāya kaṇikāyām akṣaṇikasya ca artha kriyā nyāya kaṇikā brahma tattva samīkṣābhyām upapāditā iti sarvam avadātam 
TV_1.33.1–1.33.2	 maitrī karuṇām udita upekṣāṇām sukha duḥkha puṇya apuṇya viṣayāṇām bhāvanātaḥ citta prasādanam aparikarmita manasaḥ asūyā ādimataḥ samādhi tad upāya saṃpatti anutpādāt citta prasādana upāyān asūyā ādi virodhinaḥ pratipādayitum upakramate yasya cittasya avasthitasya idam iti maitrī karuṇā ityādi prasādana antam sukhiteṣu maitrīm sauhārdam bhāvayataḥ īrṣyā kāluṣyam nivartate cittasya duḥkhiteṣu ca karuṇām ātmani iva parasmin duḥkha prahāṇa icchām bhāvayataḥ para apakāra cikīrṣā kāluṣyam cetasaḥ nivartate puṇya śīleṣu prāṇiṣu muditām harṣam bhāvayataḥ asūyā kāluṣyam cetasaḥ nivartate apuṇya śīleṣu ca upekṣām mādhyasthyam bhāvayataḥ amarṣa kāluṣyam cetasaḥ nivartate tatas ca asya rājasa tāmasa dharma nivṛttau sāttvikaḥ śuklaḥ dharmaḥ upajāyate sattva utkarṣa saṃpannaḥ saṃbhavati vṛtti nirodha pakṣe tasya prasāda svābhāvyāt cittam prasīdati prasannam ca vakṣyamāṇebhyaḥ upāyebhyaḥ ekāgram sthiti padam labhate asatyām punar maitrī ādi bhāvanāyām na te upāyāḥ sthityai kalpante iti 
TV_1.34.1–1.34.2	 pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vā prāṇasya tān idānīm sthiti upāyān āha pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vā prāṇasya vā śabdaḥ vakṣyamāṇa upāya antara apekṣaḥ vikalpa arthaḥ na maitrī ādi bhāvanā apekṣayā tayā saha samuccayāt pracchardanam vivṛṇoti kauṣṭhyasya iti prayatna viśeṣāt yoga śāstra vihitāt yena kauṣṭhyaḥ vāyuḥ nāsikā puṭābhyām śanais recyate vidhāraṇam vivṛṇoti vidhāraṇam prāṇāyāmaḥ recitasya prāṇasya kauṣṭhyasya vāyoḥ yat āyāmaḥ bahis eva sthāpanam na tu sahasā praveśanam tat etābhyām pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vāyoḥ laghu kṛta śarīrasya manaḥ sthiti padam labhate atra ca uttara sūtra gatāt sthiti nibandha nīti padāt sthiti grahaṇam ākṛṣya saṃpādayet iti artha prāptena saṃbandhanīyam 
TV_1.35.1–1.35.2	 viṣayavatī vā pravṛttiḥ utpannā manasaḥ sthiti nibandhanī sthiti upāya antaram āha viṣayavatī vā pravṛttiḥ utpannā manasaḥ sthiti nibandhanī vyācaṣṭe nāsikā agre dhārayate iti dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhīn kurvataḥ tad jaya ādyāḥ divya gandha saṃvid tad sākṣātkāraḥ evam anyāsu api pravṛttiṣu yojyam etat ca āgamāt pratyetavyam na upapattitaḥ syāt etat kim etādṛgbhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ kaivalyam pratyanupayoginībhiḥ iti atas āha etāḥ vṛttayaḥ alpena eva kālena utpannāḥ cittam īśvara viṣayāyām vā viveka khyāti viṣayāyām vā sthitau nibadhnanti nanu anya viṣayā vṛttiḥ katham anyatra sthitim nibadhnāti iti atas āha saṃśayam vidhamanti apasārayanti atas eva samādhi prajñāyām iti vṛtti antarāṇām api āgama siddhānām viṣayavat tvam atidiśati etena iti nanu āgama ādibhiḥ avagateṣu artheṣu kutas saṃśayaḥ iti atas āha yadi api hi iti śraddhā mūlaḥ hi yogaḥ upadiṣṭa artha eka deśa pratyakṣīkaraṇe ca śraddhā atiśayaḥ jāyate tad mūlāḥ ca dhyāna ādayaḥ asya apratyūham bhavanti iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.36.1–1.36.2^1	 viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī vigata śokā duḥkha rahitā jyotiṣmatī jyotiḥ asyāḥ asti iti jyotiṣmatī prakāśa rūpāḥ hṛdaya puṇḍarīkaḥ iti udara urasoḥ madhye yat padmam adhomukham tiṣṭhati aṣṭa dalam recaka prāṇāyāmena tat ūrdhva mukham kṛtvā tatra cittam dhārayet tad madhye sūrya maṇḍalam akāraḥ jāgarita sthānam tasya upari candra maṇḍalam ukāraḥ svapna sthānam tasya upari vahni maṇḍalam makāraḥ suṣupti sthānam tasya upari para vyoma ātmakam brahma nādam turīya sthānam ardha mātram udāharanti brahma vādinaḥ tatra karṇikāyām ūrdhva mukhī sūrya ādi maṇḍala madhya gāḥ brahma nāḍī tatas api ūrdhvam pravṛttā suṣumnā nāma nāḍī tayā khalu bāhyāni api sūrya ādīni maṇḍalāni protāni sa hi citta sthānam tasyām dhārayataḥ yoginaḥ citta saṃvid upajāyate upapatti pūrvakam buddhi saṃvidaḥ ākāram ādarśayati buddhi sattvam hi iti ākāśa kalpam iti vyāpitām āha 
TV_1.36.2^2	 sūrya ādīnām prabhāḥ tāsām rūpam tad ākāreṇa vikalpate nānā rūpā bhavati manaḥ ca atra buddhiḥ abhimatam na tu mahat tattvam tasya ca suṣumnā sthasya vaikārika ahaṃkāra janmanaḥ sattva bahula tayā jyotīrūpa tā vivakṣitā tad tad viṣaya gocara tayā ca vyāpi tvam api siddham asmitā kārye manasi samāpattim darśayitvā asmitā samāpatteḥ svarūpam āha tathā iti śāntam apagata rajaḥ tamaḥ taraṅgam anantam vyāpi asmitā mātram na punar nānā prabhā rūpam āgama antareṇa sva matam samīkaroti yatra idam uktam pañcaśikhena tam aṇum duradhigama tvāt ātmānam ahaṃkāra āspadam anuvidyā anucintya asmi iti evam tāvat saṃjānīta iti syāt etat nānā prabhā rūpā bhavatu jyotiṣmatī katham asmitā mātra rūpā jyotiṣmatī iti atas āha eṣā dvayī iti vidhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ mala asmitā eva sattva mayī jyotiḥ iti bhāvaḥ dvividhāyāḥ api jyotiṣmatyāḥ phalam āha yayā iti 
TV_1.37.1–1.38.2	 vīta rāga viṣayam vā cittam vīta rāga viṣayam vā cittam vīta rāgāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyana prabhṛtayaḥ teṣām cittam tat eva ālambanam tena uparaktam iti svapna nidrā jñāna ālambanam vā svapna nidrā jñāna ālambanam vā yadā khalu ayam svapne vivikta vana saṃniveśa vartinīm utkīrṇām iva candra maṇḍalāt komala mṛṇāla śakala anukāribhiḥ aṅga pratyaṅgaiḥ upapannām abhijāta candrakānta maṇi mayīm ati surabhi mālatī mallikā mālā hāriṇīm manoharām bhagavataḥ maheśvarasya pratimām ārādhayan eva prabuddhaḥ prasanna manāḥ tadā tām eva svapna jñāna ālambanībhūtām anucintayataḥ tasya tad eka ākāra manasaḥ tatra eva cittam sthiti padam labhate nidrā ca iha sāttvikī grahītavyā yasyāḥ prabuddhasya sukham aham asvāpsam iti pratyavamarśaḥ bhavati ekāgram hi tasyām manaḥ bhavati tāvat mātreṇa ca uktam etat eva brahma vidaḥ brahmaṇaḥ rūpam udāharanti supta avasthā iti jñānam ca jñeya rahitam na śakyam gocarayitum iti jñeyam api gocarīkriyate 
TV_1.39.1–1.40.2	 yathā abhimata dhyānāt vā yathā abhimata dhyānāt vā kim bahunā yat eva abhimatam tat tat devatā rūpam iti paramāṇu parama mahat tva antaḥ asya vaśīkāraḥ katham punar sthiti pada sā ātmībhāvaḥ avagantavyaḥ iti atas āha paramāṇu parama mahat tva antaḥ asya vaśīkāraḥ vyācaṣṭe sūkṣmaḥ iti uktam artham piṇḍīkṛtya vaśīkāra padārtham āha evam tām ubhayīm iti vaśīkārasya avantara phalam āha tad vaśīkārāt iti 
TV_1.41.1–1.41.2^1	 kṣīṇa vṛtteḥ abhijātasya iva maṇeḥ grahītṛ grahaṇa grāhyeṣu tad sthatad añjana tā samāpattiḥ tat evam citta sthiteḥ upāyāḥ darśitāḥ labdha sthitikasya cittasya vaśīkāraḥ api darśitaḥ saṃprati labdha sthitikasya cetasaḥ kiṃviṣayaḥ kiṃrūpaḥ ca saṃprajñātaḥ bhavati iti pṛcchati atha iti atra uttaram sūtram avatārayati tat ucyate iti sūtram paṭhati kṣīṇa vṛtteḥ ityādi samāpatti antam tat vyācaṣṭe kṣīṇa iti abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām kṣīṇa rājasa tāmasa pramāṇa ādi vṛtteḥ cittasya tasya vyākhyānam pratyasta mita pratyayasya iti tat anena citta sattvasya svabhāva svacchasya rajaḥ tamobhyām anabhibhavaḥ uktaḥ 
TV_1.41.2^2	 dṛṣṭāntam spaṣṭayati yathā iti upāśrayaḥ upādhiḥ japā kusuma ādiḥ uparaktaḥ tad chāyā āpannaḥ upāśrayasya yat ātmīyam rūpam lohita nīla ādi tat eva ākāraḥ tena lakṣitaḥ nirbhāsate dārṣṭa antike yojayati tathā grāhyā iti grāhyam ca tad ālambanam ca tena uparaktam tad anuviddham tat anena grahītṛ grahaṇābhyām vyavacchinatti ātmīyam antaḥkaraṇa rūpam apidhāya grāhya samāpannam grāhyatām iva prāptam iti yāvat atas grāhya svarūpa ākāreṇa nirbhāsate grāhya uparāgam eva sūkṣma sthūla tābhyām vibhajate bhūta sūkṣmā iti 
TV_1.41.2^3	 viśvabhedaḥ cetana acetana svabhāvaḥ gavādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ ca draṣṭavyaḥ tat anena vitarka vicāra anugatau samādhī darśitau tathā grahaṇeṣu api indriyeṣu iti gṛhyante ebhiḥ arthāḥ iti grahaṇāni indriyāṇi etat eva spaṣṭayati grahaṇa ālambanā iti grahaṇam ca ālambanam ca tat iti grahaṇa ālambanam tena uparaktam anuviddham ātmīyam antaḥkaraṇa rūpam apidhāya grahaṇam iva bahiṣkaraṇam iva āpannam iti tat anena ānanda anugatam uktvā asmita anugatam āha tathā grahītṛ puruṣa iti asmitā āspadam hi grahītā puruṣaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.41.2^4	 puruṣa tva aviśeṣāt anena eva muktaḥ api puruṣaḥ śuka prahlāda ādiḥ samādhi viṣaya tayā saṃgrahītavyaḥ iti āha tathā muktā iti upasaṃharan tad sthatad añjana tā padam vyācaṣṭe tat evam iti teṣu grahītṛ grahaṇa grāhyeṣu sthitasya dhāritasya dhyāna paripāka vaśāt apahata rajaḥ tamaḥ malasya citta sattvasya yā tad sthatad añjana tā tad ākāra tā sā samāpattiḥ saṃprajñāta lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ ucyate tatra ca grahītṛ grahaṇa grāhyeṣu iti sautraḥ pāṭha kramaḥ artha krama virodhāt na adartavyaḥ evam bhāṣye api prathamam bhūta sūkṣma upanyāsaḥ api anādaraṇīyaḥ iti sarvam ramaṇīyam 
TV_1.42.1–1.42.2^1	 tatra śabda artha jñāna vikalpaiḥ saṃkīrṇā sa vitarkā samāpattiḥ sāmānyatas samāpattiḥ uktā sā iyam avāntara bhedāt caturvidhā bhavati tat yathā savitarkā nirvitarkā sa vicārā nirvicārā ca iti tatra sa vitarkāyāḥ samāpatteḥ lakṣaṇam āha tatra ityādi tāsu samāpattiṣu madhye sa vitarkā samāpattiḥ pratipattavyā kīdṛśī śabdaḥ ca arthaḥ ca jñānam ca teṣām vikalpāḥ vastutas bhinnānām api śabda ādīnām itaretara adhyāsāt vikalpaḥ api ekasmin bhedam ādarśayati bhinneṣu ca abhedam tena śabda artha jñāna vikalpaiḥ saṃkīrṇā vyāmiśra iti arthaḥ tat yathā gauḥ iti śabdaḥ iti gauḥ iti upāttayoḥ artha jñānayoḥ śabda abheda vikalpaḥ darśitaḥ gauḥ iti arthaḥ iti gauḥ iti upāttayoḥ śabda jñānayoḥ artha abheda vikalpaḥ 
TV_1.42.2^2	 gauḥ iti jñānam iti gauḥ iti upāttayoḥ śabda arthayoḥ jñāna abheda vikalpaḥ tat evam avinirbhāgeṇa vibhaktānām api śabda artha jñānānām grahaṇam loke dṛṣṭam draṣṭavyam yadi avibhāgena grahaṇam kutas tarhi vibhāgaḥ iti atas āha vibhajyamānāḥ ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām parīkṣakaiḥ anye śabda dharmā dhvani pariṇāma mātrasya śabdasya udātta ādayaḥ dharmāḥ anye arthasya jaḍa tva mūrta tva ādayaḥ anye prakāśa mūrti viraha ādayaḥ jñānasya dharmāḥ iti tasmāt eteṣām vibhaktaḥ panthāḥ sva rūpa bheda unnayana mārgaḥ tatra vikalpate gavā ādi arthe samāpannasya iti tat anena yoginaḥ aparam pratyakṣam uktam śeṣam sugamam 
TV_1.43.1–1.43.2^1	 smṛti pariśuddhau svarūpa śūnyā iva artha mātra nirbhāsā nirvitarkā sūtram yojayitum prathamatas tāvat nirvitarkām vyācaṣṭe yadā punar iti pariśuddhiḥ apanayaḥ śabda saṃketa smaraṇa pūrve khalu āgama anumāne pravartete saṃketaḥ ca ayam gauḥ iti śabda artha jñānānām itaretara adhyāsa ātmā tatas ca āgama anumāna jñāna vikalpau bhavataḥ tena tat pūrvā samādhi prajñā sa vitarkā yadā punar artha mātra pravaṇena cetasā artha mātrāt ṛtena tad abhyāsāt na antarīyaka tām upagatā saṃketa smṛtiḥ tyaktāḥ tad tyāge ca śruta anumāna jñāna vikalpau tad mūlau tyaktau tadā tat śūnyāyām samādhi prajñāyām sva rūpa mātreṇa avasthitaḥ arthaḥ tad svarūpa mātra tayā eva na tu vikalpitena ākāreṇa paricchidyate sā nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ iti tat yoginām param pratyakṣam asadāra upagandhasya api abhāvāt syāt etat pareṇa pratyakṣeṇa artha tattvam gṛhītvā yoginaḥ upadiśanti upapādayanti ca 
TV_1.43.2^2	 katham ca ātad viṣayābhyām āgama para artha anumānābhyām saḥ arthaḥ upadiśyate upapādyate ca tasmāt āgama anumāne tad viṣaye te ca vikalpau iti param api pratyakṣam vikalpaḥ eva iti atas āha tat ca śrutā iti yadi hi sa vitarkam iva śruta anumāna saha bhūtam tat anuṣaktam syāt bhavet saṃkīrṇam tayoḥ tu bījam eva etat tatas hi śruta anumāne prabhavataḥ na ca yat yasya kāraṇam tat tad viṣayam bhavati na hi dhūma jñānam vahni jñāna kāraṇam iti vahni viṣayam tasmāt avikalpena pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā vikalpya upadiśanti ca upapādayanti ca upasaṃharati tasmāt iti vyākhyeyam sūtram yojayati nirvitarkāyāḥ iti smṛti pariśuddhau ityādi sūtram śabda saṃketaḥ ca śrutam ca anumānam ca teṣām jñānam eva vikalpaḥ tasmāt smṛtiḥ tasyāḥ pariśuddhiḥ apagamaḥ tasyām
