TV_1.43.2^3	 tatra ca saṃketa smṛti pariśuddhiḥ hetuḥ śruta anumāna smṛti pariśuddhiḥ ca hetumatī anumāna śabdaḥ ca karma sādhanaḥ anumeya vācakaḥ svam iva iti ivakāraḥ bhinnakramaḥ tyaktvā iti pada anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ viṣaya vipratipattim nirākaroti tasyāḥ ekā iti ekām buddhim upakramataḥ ārabhate iti ekabuddhi upakramaḥ tat anena paramāṇavaḥ nānā ātmānaḥ na nirvitarka viṣayāḥ iti uktam bhavati yogya tve api teṣām parama sūkṣmāṇām nānā bhūtānām mahattva eka artha samaveta eka tva nirbhāsa pratyaya viṣaya tva ayogāt astu tarhi parama artha satsu paramāṇuṣu sāṃvṛtaḥ pratibhāsa dharmaḥ sthaulyam iti atas āha artha ātmā iti na asati bādhake sthūlam anubhava siddham śakya apahnavam iti bhāvaḥ tatra ye paśyanti dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa go ghaṭa ādayaḥ upajāyante iti tān pratyāha aṇu pracaya iti 
TV_1.43.2^4	 aṇūnām pracayaḥ sthūla rūpa pariṇāmaḥ sa ca viśiṣyate anyasmāt pariṇāma antarāt saḥ eva ātmā svarūpam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ gavādiḥ bhoga āyatanam ghaṭa ādiḥ viṣayaḥ tat ca etat ubhayam api lokyate iti lokaḥ nanu eṣa bhūta sūkṣmebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā syāt bhinnaḥ ced katham tad āśrayaḥ katham ca tad ākāraḥ na hi ghaṭaḥ paṭāt anyaḥ tad ākāraḥ tad āśrayaḥ vā abhinnaḥ ced tadvat eva sūkṣmaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ ca syāt atas āha sa ca iti ayam abhiprāyaḥ na ekāntataḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ bhinnaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ abhinnaḥ vā bhinna tve gavāśva vat dharma dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ abhinna tve dharmi rūpavat eva tad anupapatteḥ tasmāt kathaṃcid bhinnaḥ kathaṃcid abhinnaḥ ca āstheyaḥ tathā ca sarvam upapadyate bhūta sūkṣmāṇām iti ṣaṣṭhyā kathaṃcid bhedam sūcayati ātma bhūtaḥ iti ca abhedam 
TV_1.43.2^5	 phalena vyaktena tad anubhava lakṣaṇena tad vyavahāra lakṣaṇena ca vyaktena vipratipannam pratyanumāpitaḥ kāraṇa abhede ca kāraṇa ākāratā upapannā iti āha sva vyañjaka añjanaḥ iti sa kim tad ātma bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ nityaḥ na iti āha dharma antarasya kapāla ādeḥ udayaḥ iti tasya avayavinaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ vyāvṛttam rūpam ādarśayati saḥ eṣaḥ iti paramāṇu sādhyāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ anyā kriyā madhu udaka ādi dhāraṇa lakṣaṇā tad dharmakaḥ iti na kevalam anubhavāt api tu vyavahārataḥ api tad nibandhana tvāt lokayātrāyāḥ iti āha tena iti syāt etat asati bādhake anubhavaḥ avayavinam vyavasthāpayet asti ca bādhakam yat sat tat sarvam anavayavam yathā vijñānam sat ca go ghaṭa ādi iti svabhāva hetuḥ sattvam hi viruddha dharma saṃsarga rahita tvena vyāptam tad viruddhaḥ ca viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ sa avayavaḥ upalabhyamānaḥ vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhyā sattvam api nivartayati 
TV_1.43.2^6	 asti ca avayavini tad deśa tva ātad deśa tva āvṛta tva at āvṛta tva rakta tva ārakta tva cala tva acala tva lakṣaṇaḥ viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ iti atas āha yasya punar iti ayam abhiprāyaḥ anubhava siddham sattvam hetuḥ kriyate yat kila pāṃśula pādukaḥ hālikaḥ api pratipadyate anyat vā anubhava siddhāt tatra anyat asiddha tvāt ahetuḥ anubhava siddham tu ghaṭa ādīnām sattvam artha kriyā kāritva rūpam na sthūlāt anyat saḥ ayam hetuḥ sthūla tvam apākurvan ātmānam eva vyāhanti nanu na sthūla tvam eva sattvam api tu asataḥ vyāvṛttiḥ asthaulya vyāvṛttiḥ ca sthaulyam vyāvartya bhedāt ca vyāvṛttayaḥ bhidyante atas sthaulya abhāve api na sattva vyāhatiḥ anya tvāt bhavatu vā vyāvṛtti bhedāt avasāya viṣaya bhedaḥ 
TV_1.43.2^7	 yat pūrvakāḥ tu avasāyāḥ tasya anubhavasya avikalpasya pramāṇasya kaḥ viṣayaḥ iti nirūpayatu bhavān rūpa paramāṇavaḥ nirantara utpādāḥ agṛhīta parama sūkṣma tattvāḥ iti ced hantā ete gandha rasa sparśa paramāṇubhiḥ antaritāḥ na nirantarāḥ tasmāt antarāla āgrahaḥ eka ghana vana pratyaya vat paramāṇu ālambanaḥ san ayam vikalpaḥ mithyā iti tad prabhava vikalpā na pāramparyeṇa api vastu pratibaddhāḥ iti kutas tad avasitasya sattvasya anavayava tva sādhaka tvam tasmāt avikalpasya pratyakṣasya prāmāṇyam icchatā tad anubhūyamāna sthaulyasya eva sattvam avikalpa avaseyam akāmena api abhyupeyam tathā ca tat bādha mānam sattvam ātmānam eva apabādheta parama sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ vijātīya paramāṇu anantaritāḥ anubhava viṣayāḥ iti vyāhatam aṅgīkaraṇam tat idam uktam yasya punar avastukaḥ sa pracaya viśeṣaḥ nirvikalpa viṣayaḥ 
TV_1.43.2^8	 santu tarhi sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ nirvikalpa viṣayāḥ iti atas āha sūkṣmam ca kāraṇam anupalabhyam avikalpasya iti tasya avayavi abhāvāt dhetoḥ atad rūpa pratiṣṭham mithyājñānam iti lakṣaṇena sarvam evam prāptam mithyājñānam yat sthaulya ālambanam yat ca tad adhiṣṭhāna sattva ālambanam iti arthaḥ nanu etāvatā api na jñānam ātmani mithyā bhavati tasya avayavi tvena aprakāśāt iti atas āha prāyeṇa iti nanu kim etāvatā api iti atas āha tadā ca iti sattva ādi jñānam ced mithyā tadā sattva ādi hetukam anavayavi tva ādi jñānam api mithyā eva tasya api hi nirvikalpa gocara sthūlam eva avaseya tayā viṣayaḥ sa ca na asti iti tātparya arthaḥ viṣaya abhāvaḥ eva kutas iti atas āha yat yat iti virodhaḥ ca pariṇāma vaicitryeṇa bheda abhedena ca ukta upapatti anusāreṇa uddhartavyaḥ iti sarvam ramaṇīyam 
TV_1.44.1–1.44.2^1^1	 etayā eva sa vicārā nirvicārā ca sūkṣma viṣayā vyākhyātāḥ etayā eva sa vicārā nirvicārā ca sūkṣma viṣayā vyākhyātāḥ abhivyaktaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ dharmaḥ yaiḥ te tathā uktāḥ ghaṭa ādi dharma upagṛhītāḥ iti yāvat deśaḥ upari adhas pārśva ādiḥ kālaḥ vartamānaḥ nimittam pārthivasya paramāṇoḥ gandha tanmātra pradhānebhyaḥ pañca tanmātrebhyaḥ utpattiḥ evam āpyasya paramāṇoḥ gandha tanmātra varjitebhyaḥ rasa tanmātra pradhānebhyaḥ caturbhyaḥ evam taijasasya gandha rasa tanmātra rahitebhyaḥ rūpa tanmātra pradhānebhyaḥ tribhyaḥ 
TV_1.44.1–1.44.2^1^2	 evam vāyavīyasya gandha ādi tanmātra rahitābhyām sparśa pradhānābhyām sparśa śabda tanmātrābhyām evam nābhasasya śabdaṇām eteṣām deśa kāla nimittānām anubhavaḥ tena avacchinneṣu na ananubhūta viśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiḥ upajāyate iti arthaḥ nanu sa vitarkayā saha kim sārūpyam sa vicārāyāḥ iti atas āha tat na api iti pārthivaḥ hi paramāṇuḥ pañca tanmātra pracaya ātmā eka buddhi nirgrāhyaḥ evam āpya ādayaḥ api catur tri dvi eka tanmātra ātmānaḥ eka buddhi nirgrāhyāḥ vedvyatavyāḥ uditaḥ vartamānaḥ dharmaḥ tena viśiṣṭam etāvatā ca atra saṃketa smṛti āgama anumāna vikalpa anuvedhaḥ sūcitaḥ 
TV_1.44.2^2	 na hi pratyakṣeṇa sthūle dṛśyamāne paramāṇavaḥ prakāśante api tu āgama anumānābhyām tasmāt upapannam asyāḥ saṃkīrṇa tvam iti nirvicārām āha yā punar iti sarvathā sarveṇa nīla pīta ādinā prakāreṇa sarvatas iti sārvavibhaktikaḥ tasiḥ sarvaiḥ deśa kāla nimitta anubhavaiḥ iti arthaḥ tat anena sva rūpeṇa kāla anavacchedaḥ paramāṇūnām iti darśitam na api tadārabdha dharma dvāreṇa iti āha śāntāḥ atītāḥ uditāḥ vartamānāḥ avyapadeśyāḥ bhaviṣyantaḥ dharmāḥ taiḥ anavacchinneṣu 
TV_1.44.2^3	 anavacchinnāḥ dharmaiḥ paramāṇavaḥ kim asaṃbaddhāḥ eva taiḥ iti atas āha sarva dharma anupātiṣu iti katamena saṃbandhena dharmān anupatanti paramāṇavaḥ iti atas āha sarva dharma ātmakeṣu kathaṃcid bhedaḥ kathaṃcid abhedaḥ dharmāṇām paramāṇubhyaḥ iti arthaḥ kasmāt punar iyam samāpattiḥ etat viṣaya iti atas āha evaṃsvarūpam hi iti vastu tattva grāhiṇī na atattve pravartate iti arthaḥ viṣayam abhidhāya asyāḥ svarūpam āha prajñā ca iti saṃkalayya svarūpa bheda upayogi viṣayam āha tatra iti upasaṃharati evam iti ubhayoḥ ātmanaḥ ca nirvicārāyāḥ ca iti 
TV_1.45.1–1.45.2	 sūkṣma viṣaya tvam ca aliṅga paryavasānam kim bhūta sūkṣmaḥ eva grāhya viṣayā samāpattiḥ samāpyate na kim tu sūkṣma viṣaya tvam ca aliṅga paryavasānam pārthivasya paramāṇoḥ saṃbandhinī yā gandha tanmātra tā sā samāpatteḥ sūkṣmaḥ viṣayaḥ evam uttaratra api yojyam liṅga mātram mahat tattvam tat dhi layam gacchati pradhānaḥ iti aliṅgam pradhānam tat dhi na kvacid layam gacchati iti arthaḥ aliṅga paryavasāna tvam āha na ca aliṅgāt param iti codayati nanu puruṣaḥ api sūkṣmaḥ na aliṅgam eva iti arthaḥ pariharati satyam iti upādāna tayā saukṣmyam aliṅgaḥ eva na anyatra iti arthaḥ tatra puruṣa artha nimitta tvāt mahat ahaṃkāra ādeḥ puruṣaḥ api kāraṇam aliṅga vat iti kutas evaṃlakṣaṇam aliṅgasya eva saukṣmyam iti āśayavān pṛcchati kim tu iti uttaram āha liṅgasya iti satyam kāraṇam na tu upādānam yathā hi pradhānam mahat ādi bhāvena pariṇamate na tathā puruṣaḥ tad hetuḥ api iti arthaḥ upasaṃharati atas pradhānaḥ eva saukṣmyam niratiśayam vyākhyātam 
TV_1.46.1–1.46.2	 tāḥ eva sa bījaḥ samādhiḥ catasṛṇām api samāpattīnām grāhya viṣayāṇām saṃprajñāta tvam āha tāḥ eva sa bījaḥ samādhiḥ eva kāraḥ bhinnakramaḥ sa bījaḥ iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ tatas catasraḥ samāpattayaḥ grāhya viṣayāḥ sa bīja tayā niyamyante sa bīja tā tu aniyatā grahītṛ grahaṇa gocarāyām api samāpattau vikalpa avikalpa bhedena aniṣiddhā vyavatiṣṭhate tena grāhye catasraḥ samāpattayaḥ grahītṛ grahaṇayoḥ catasraḥ iti aṣṭau siddhāḥ bhavanti iti nigada vyākhyātam bhāṣyam 
TV_1.47.1–1.47.2	 nirvicāra vaiśāradye adhyātma prasādaḥ catasṛṣu api samāpattiṣu grāhya viṣayāsu nirvicārāyāḥ śobhana tvam āha nirvicāra vaiśāradye adhyātma prasādaḥ vaiśāradya padārtham āha aśuddhi iti rajaḥ tamasoḥ upacayaḥ aśuddhiḥ sā eva āvaraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ malaḥ tasmāt apetasya prakāśa ātmanaḥ prakāśa svabhāvasya buddhi sattvasya atas eva anabhibhūtaḥ iti syāt etat grāhya viṣayā ced samāpattiḥ katham ātma viṣayaḥ prasādaḥ iti atas āha bhūta artha viṣayaḥ iti na ātma viṣayaḥ kim tu tad ādhāraḥ iti arthaḥ kramān anurodhī yugapad iti arthaḥ atra eva pāramarṣīm gāthām udāharati tathā ca iti jñāna āloka prakarṣeṇa ātmānam sarveṣām upari paśyan duḥkha traya parītān śocataḥ janān jānāti 
TV_1.48.1–1.48.2	 ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā atra eva yogi jana prasiddhān vartha saṃjñā kathanena yogi saṃmatim āha ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā sugamam bhāṣyam āgamena iti veda vihitam śravaṇam uktam anumānena iti mananam dhyānam cintā tatra abhyāsaḥ paunaḥpunyena anuṣṭhānam tasmin rasaḥ ādaraḥ tat anena nididhi āsanam uktam 
TV_1.49.1–1.49.2^1	 śruta anumāna prajñābhyām anya viṣayāḥ viśeṣa artha tvāt syāt etat āgama anumāna gṛhīta artha viṣayā bhāvanā prakarṣa labdha janmā nirvicāra āgama anumāna viṣayam eva gocarayet na khalu anya viṣaya anubhava janmā saṃskāraḥ śaktaḥ anyatra jñānam janayitum atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt nirvicārā ced ṛtaṃbhara āgama anumānayoḥ api tad prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha śruta anumāna ityādi buddhi sattvam hi prakāśa svabhāvam sarva artha darśana samartham api tamasā āvṛtam yatra eva rajasā udghāṭyate tatra eva gṛhṇāti yadā tu abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām apāsta rajaḥ tamaḥ malam anavadya vaiśāradyam udyotate tadā asya ati patita samasta māna meya sīmnaḥ prakāśa ānantye sati kim nāma yat na gocaraḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_1.49.2^2	 vyācaṣṭe śrutam āgama jñānam tad sāmānya viṣayam kasmāt na hi āgamena śakyaḥ viśeṣaḥ abhidhātum kutas yasmāt ānantyāt vyabhicārāt ca na viśeṣeṇa kṛta saṃketaḥ śabdaḥ yasmāt asya viśeṣeṇa saha vācya vācaka saṃbandhaḥ pratīyeta na ca vākya arthaḥ api īdṛśaḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhavati anumāne api liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha grahaṇa adhīna janmani gatiḥ eṣā eva iti āha tathā anumānam iti yatra prāptiḥ iti atra yatra tatra śabdayoḥ sthāna parivartanena vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ avagamayitavyaḥ atas atra anumānena sāmānyena upasaṃhāraḥ 
TV_1.49.2^3	 upasaṃharati tasmāt iti astu tarhi saṃbandha graha anapekṣam loka pratyakṣam na tad sāmānya viṣayam iti atas āha na ca asya ityādi mā bhūt saṃbandha graha adhīnam loka pratyakṣam indriya adhīnam tu bhavati eva na ca indriyāṇām asmin asti yogyatā iti arthaḥ nanu ca yadi āgama anumāna pratyakṣa agocaraḥ viśeṣaḥ tarhi na asti pramāṇa virahāt iti atas āha na ca iti na hi pramāṇam vyāpakam kāraṇam vā prameyasya yena tad nivṛttau nivarteta no khalu kalāvataḥ candrasya para bhāga varti hariṇa sadbhāvam prati na saṃdihate prāmāṇikāḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.49.2^4	 iti tasmāt samādhi prajñā nirgrāhyaḥ eva iti atra ca vivāda adhyāsitāḥ paramāṇavaḥ ātmānaḥ ca prātisvika viśeṣa śālinaḥ dravya tve sati parasparam vyāvartamāna tvāt ye dravya tve sati parasparam vyāvartante te prātisvika viśeṣa śālinaḥ yathā khaṇḍa muṇḍa ādayaḥ iti anumānena āgamena ca ṛtaṃbhara prajñā upadeśa pareṇa yadi api viśeṣaḥ nirūpyate tad anirūpaṇe saṃśayaḥ syāt nyāya prāpta tvāt tathā api adūra viprakarṣeṇa tat sattvam kathaṃcid gocarayataḥ śruta anumāne na tu sākṣāt ca artham iva samuccaya ādi padāni liṅga saṃkhyā yogi tayā tasmāt siddham śruta anumāna prajñābhyām anya viṣaya iti 
TV_1.50.1–1.50.3	 tad jaḥ saṃskāraḥ anya saṃskāra pratibandhī syāt etat bhavatu parama artha viṣayaḥ saṃprajñātaḥ yathā ukta upāya abhyāsāt anādinā tu vyutthāna saṃskāreṇa nirūḍha nibiḍa tayā pratibandhanīyā samādhi prajñā sā vā ati āvarta madhya varti pradīpa paramāṇuḥ iva iti śaṅkām apanetum sūtram avatārayati samādhi prajñā iti sūtram paṭhati tad jaḥ saṃskāraḥ anya saṃskāra pratibandhī tat iti nirvicārām samāpattim parāmṛśati anyā iti vyutthānam āha bhūta artha pakṣapātaḥ hi dhiyām svabhāvaḥ tāvat eva iyam anavasthitāḥ bhrāmyati na yāvat tattvam pratilabhate tad pratilambhe tatra sthita padā satī saṃskāra buddhiḥ saṃskāra buddhi cakra krameṇa āvartamānān ādim api atattva saṃskāra buddhi kramam bādhataḥ eva iti tathā ca bāhyāḥ api āhuḥ nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhaḥ anādimattve api buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātataḥ iti 
TV_1.50.4	 syāt etat samādhi prajñātaḥ astu vyutthāna jasya saṃskārasya nirodhaḥ samādhi jaḥ tu saṃskāra atiśayaḥ samādhi prajñā prasava hetuḥ asti avikalaḥ iti tad avasthā eva cittasya sa adhikāra tā iti codayati katham asau iti pariharati na te iti cittasya hi kārya dvayam śabda ādi upabhha ugaḥ viveka khyātiḥ ca iti tatra kleśa karma āśaya sahitam śabda ādi upabhoge vartate prajñā prabhava saṃskāra unmūlita nikhila kleśa karma āśayasya tu cetasaḥ a vasita prāya adhikāra bhāvasya viveka khyāti mātram avaśiṣyate kāryam tasmāt samādhi saṃskārāḥ cittasya na bhoga adhikāra hetavaḥ pratyuta tad paripanthinaḥ iti sva kāryāt bhoga lakṣaṇāt avasādayanti asamartham kurvanti iti arthaḥ kasmāt khyāti paryavasānam hi citta ceṣṭitam tāvat vibhogāya cittam ceṣṭate na yāvat viveka khyātim anubhavati saṃjāta viveka khyātinaḥ tu kleśa nivṛttau na bhoga adhikāraḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_1.51.1–1.51.2^1	 tasya api nirodhe sarva nirodhāt nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ tat atra bhoga adhikāra praśāntiḥ prayojanam prajñā saṃskārāṇām iti uktam pṛcchati kim ca iti kim ca asya bhavati prajñā saṃskāra vat cittam prajñā saṃskāra pravāha janakatayā tathā eva sa adhikāram iti adhikāra apanuttaye anyat api kiṃcid apekṣaṇīyam asti iti arthaḥ sūtreṇa uttaram āha tasya api nirodhe sarva nirodhāt nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ pareṇa vairāgyeṇa jñāna prasāda mātra lakṣaṇena saṃskāra upajanana dvārā tasya api prajñā kṛta saṃskārasya nirodhe na kevalam prajñāyāḥ iti api śabda arthaḥ sarvasya utpadyamānasya saṃskāra prajñā pravāhasya nirodhāt kāraṇa abhāvena kārya anutpādāt saḥ ayam nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ bhavati 
TV_1.51.2^2	 vyācaṣṭe sa nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ samādhi prajñā virodhinaḥ parasmāt vairāgyāt upajāyamānaḥ sva kāraṇa dvāreṇa na kevalam samādhi prajñā virodhī prajñā kṛtānām api asau saṃskārāṇām paripanthī bhavati nanu vairāgya jam vijñānam sat vijñānam prajñāmātram bādhatām saṃskāram tu avijñāna rūpam katham bādhate dṛṣṭā hi jāgrataḥ api svapna dṛṣṭa artha smṛtiḥ iti āśayavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti uttaram nirodha jaḥ iti nirudhyate anena prajñā iti nirodhaḥ param vairāgyam tatas jātaḥ nirodha jaḥ saṃskāraḥ saṃskārāt eva dīrgha kāla nairantarya satkāra āsevita para vairāgya janmanaḥ prajñā saṃskāra bādhaḥ na tu vijñānāt iti arthaḥ syāt etat nirodha ja saṃskāra sadbhāve kim pramāṇam sa hi pratyakṣeṇa vā anubhūyeta smṛtyā vā kāryeṇa anumīyeta 
TV_1.51.2^3	 na ca sarva vṛtti nirodhe pratyakṣam asti yoginaḥ na api smṛtiḥ tasya vṛtti mātra nirodha tayā smṛti janaka tva asaṃbhavāt iti atas āha nirodha iti nirodhe sthitiḥ cittasya niruddha avasthā iti arthaḥ tasyāḥ kāla kramaḥ muhūrta ardha yā āmayāmāhorātra ādiḥ tad anubhavena etat uktam bhavati vairāgya abhyāsa prakarṣa anurodhī nirodha prakarṣaḥ muhūrta ardhayāmādi vyāpitayā anubhūyate yoginā na ca vairāgya kṣaṇāḥ krama niyata tayā parasparam asaṃbhavantaḥ tad tad kāla vyāpitayā sa atiśayam nirodham kartum īśate iti tad tad vairāgya kṣaṇa pracaya janyaḥ sthāyī saṃskāra pracayaḥ eṣitavyaḥ iti bhāvaḥ nanu ucchidyantām prajñā saṃskārāḥ nirodha saṃskārāḥ tu kutas samucchidyante 
TV_1.51.2^4–1.51.3	 anucchede vā sa adhikāra tvam eva iti atas āha vyutthāna iti vyutthānam ca tasya nirodha samādhiḥ ca saṃprajñātaḥ tad prabhavāḥ saṃskārāḥ kaivalya bhāgīyāḥ nirodha jāḥ saṃskārāḥ iti arthaḥ vyutthāna prajñā saṃskārāḥ citte pralīnāḥ iti bhavati cittam vyutthāna prajñā saṃskāra vat nirodha saṃskāraḥ tu pratyuditaḥ eva āste citte nirodha saṃskāre sati api cittam anadhikāra vat puruṣa artha janakam cittam hi sādhikāram śabda ādi upabhoga viveka khyātī ca tathā puruṣa arthaḥ saṃskāra śeṣa tāyām tu na buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī puruṣaḥ iti na asau puruṣa arthaḥ videha prakṛti layānām na nirodha bhāgi tayā sa adhikāram cittam api tu kleśa vāsita tayā iti āśayavān āha yasmāt iti śeṣam sugamam yogasya uddeśa nirdeśau tad artham vṛtti lakṣaṇam yoga upāyāḥ prabhedāḥ ca pāde asmin upavarṇitāḥ 
TV_2.1.1–2.1.2	 tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni kriyā yogaḥ nanu prathama pādena eva sa upāyaḥ sāvāntara prabhedaḥ saphalaḥ yogaḥ uktaḥ tat kim aparam avaśiṣyate yad artham dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ prārabhyeta iti atas āha uddiṣṭaḥ iti abhyāsa vairāgye hi yoga upāyau prathame pādaḥ uktau na ca tau vyutthita cittasya drāk iti eva saṃbhavate iti dvitīya pāda upadeśyān upāyān apekṣate sattva śuddhi artham tatas hi viśuddha sattvaḥ kṛta rakṣā saṃvidhānaḥ abhyāsa vairāgye pratyaham bhāvayati samāhita tvam avikṣipta tvam katham vyutthāna cittaḥ api upadekṣyamāṇaiḥ upāyaiḥ yuktaḥ san yogī syāt iti arthaḥ tatra vakṣyamāṇeṣu niyameṣu ākṛṣya prāthamikam pratyupayuktatara tayā prathamatas kriyā yogam upadiśati sūtrakāraḥ tapaḥ svādhyāya ityādi kriyā eva yogaḥ kriyā yogaḥ yoga sādhana tvāt atas eva viṣṇupurāṇe khāṇḍikya keśi dhvaja saṃvāde 
TV_2.1.3–2.1.7^1	 yoga yuj prathamam yogī yuñjamānaḥ abhidhīyate iti upakramya tapaḥ svādhyāya ādayaḥ darśitāḥ vyatireka mukhena tapasaḥ upāya tvam āha na atapasvinaḥ iti tapasaḥ avāntara vyāpāram upāya topayoginam darśayati anādi iti anādibhyām karma kleśa vāsanābhyām citrātaḥ eva pratyupasthitam upanatam viṣaya jālam yasyām sā tathā uktā aśuddhiḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ samudrekaḥ na antareṇa tapaḥ saṃbhedam āpadyate sāndrasya nitānta virala tā saṃbhedaḥ nanūpādīyamānam api tapaḥ dhātu vaiṣamya hetu tayā yoga pratipakṣaḥ iti katham tad upāyaḥ iti atas āha tat ca iti 
TV_2.1.3–2.1.7^2	 tāvat mātram eva tapaḥ caraṇīyam na yāvatā dhātu vaiṣamyam āpadyate iti arthaḥ praṇava ādayaḥ puruṣa sūkta rudra maṇḍala brāhmaṇa ādayaḥ vaidikāḥ paurāṇikāḥ ca brahma pārāyaṇa ādayaḥ parama guruḥ bhagavān īśvaraḥ tasmin yatra idam uktam kāmataḥ akāmatas vā api yat karomi śubha aśubham tat sarvam tvayi saṃnyastam tvad prayuktaḥ karomi aham iti tad phala saṃnyāsaḥ vā phalān abhisaṃdhānena kārya karaṇam yatra idam uktam karmaṇi eva adhikāraḥ te mā phaleṣu kadācana mā karma phala hetuḥ bhūḥ mā te saṅgaḥ astu akarmaṇi 
TV_2.2.1–2.2.2^1	 samādhi bhāvanā arthaḥ kleśa tanūkaraṇa arthaḥ ca tasya prayojana abhidhānāya sūtram avatārayati sa hi iti sūtram samādhi bhāvanā arthaḥ kleśa tanūkaraṇa arthaḥ ca nanu kriyā yogaḥ eva ced kleśān pratanūkaroti kṛtam tarhi prasaṃkhyānena iti atas āha pratanūkṛtān iti kriyā yogasya pratanūkaraṇa mātre vyāpāraḥ na tu vandhya tve kleśānām prasaṃkhyānasya tu tad vandhya tve dagdha bīja kalpān iti vandhya tvena dagdha kalama bīja sārūpyam uktam syāt etat prasaṃkhyānam eva ced kleśān aprasava dharmiṇaḥ kariṣyati kṛtam eṣām pratanūkaraṇena iti atas āha teṣām iti 
TV_2.2.2^2	 kleśānām atānave hi balavat virodhi grastā sattva puruṣa anya tā khyātiḥ udetum eva na utsahate prāk eva tad vandhya bhāvam kartum praviralīkṛteṣu tu kleśeṣu durbaleṣu tad virodhinī api vairāgya abhyāsābhyām upajāyate upajātā ca taiḥ aparāmṛṣṭa an abhibhūtā na eva yāvat parāmṛśyate iti sattva puruṣa anya tā mātra khyātiḥ sūkṣmā prajñā ati indriya tayā sūkṣmaḥ asyāḥ viṣayaḥ iti sūkṣmā prajñā pratiprasavāya pravilayāya kalpiṣyate kutas samāpta adhikārāḥ yatas samāptaḥ adhikāraḥ kārya ārambhaṇam guṇānām yayā hetu bhūtayā sā tathā uktā iti 
TV_2.3.1–2.3.2	 avidyā smitā rāga dveṣa abhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ pṛcchati atha iti avidyā iti sūtreṇa parihāraḥ avidyā smitā rāga dveṣa abhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ vyācaṣṭe pañca viparyayāḥ iti avidyā tāvat viparyayaḥ eva asmitā ādayaḥ api avidyā upādānāḥ tad avinirbhāga vartinaḥ iti viparyayāḥ tatas ca avidyā samucchede teṣām api samucchedaḥ yuktaḥ iti bhāvaḥ teṣām ucchettavya tā hetum saṃsāra kāraṇa tvam āha te spandamānāḥ samudācarantaḥ guṇānām adhikāram draḍhayanti balavantam kurvanti atas eva pariṇāmam avasthāpayanti avyakta mahat ahaṃkāra paramparayā hi kārya kāraṇa srotaḥ unnamayanti udbhāvayanti yad artham sarvam etat kurvanti tat darśayati paraspara iti karmaṇām vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga lakṣaṇaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ tam amī kleśāḥ abhinirharanti niṣpādayanti kim pratyekam na iti āha paraspara anugraha iti karmabhiḥ kleśāḥ kleśaiḥ ca karmāṇi iti 
TV_2.4.1–2.4.2^1	 avidyā kṣetram uttareṣām prasupta tanu vicchinna udārāṇām heyānām kleśānām avidyā mūla tvam darśayati avidyā kṣetram uttareṣām prasupta tanu vicchinna udārāṇām tatra kā prasuptiḥ iti sva ucitām artha kriyām akurvatām kleśānām sadbhāve na pramāṇam asti iti abhiprāyaḥ pṛcchataḥ uttaram cetasi iti mā nāma artha kriyām kārṣuḥ kleśāḥ videha prakṛti layānām bīja bhāvam prāptāḥ tu te śakti mātreṇa santi kṣīraḥ iva dadhi na hi viveka khyāteḥ anyat asti kāraṇam tad vandhyatāyām atas videha prakṛti layāḥ viveka khyāti virahiṇaḥ prasupta kleśāḥ na yāvat tad avadhi kālam prāpnuvanti tad prāptau tu punarāvṛttāḥ santaḥ kleśāḥ teṣu teṣu viṣayeṣu saṃmukhībhavanti śakti mātreṇa pratiṣṭhā yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ tat anena utpatti śaktiḥ uktāḥ 
TV_2.4.2^2	 bīja bhāva upagamaḥ iti ca kārya śaktiḥ iti nanu viveka khyātimataḥ api kleśāḥ kasmāt na prasuptāḥ iti atas āha prasaṃkhyānavataḥ iti carama dehaḥ na tasya deha antaram utpatsyate yat apekṣayā asya dehaḥ pūrvaḥ iti arthaḥ na anyatra videha ādiṣu iti arthaḥ nanu sataḥ na atyanta vināśaḥ iti kim iti tadīya yoga ṛddhi balena viṣaya saṃmukhībhāve na kleśāḥ prabudhyante iti atas āha satām iti santu kleśāḥ dagdhaḥ tu eṣām prasaṃkhyāna agninā bīja bhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ kleśa pratipakṣaḥ kriyā yogaḥ tasya bhāvanam anuṣṭhānam tena upahatāḥ tanavaḥ athavā samyak jñānam avidyāyāḥ pratipakṣaḥ bheda darśanam asmitāyāḥ mādhyasthyam rāga dveṣayoḥ anubandha buddhi nivṛttiḥ abhiniveśasya iti 
TV_2.4.2^3	 vicchittim āha tathā iti kleśānām anyatamena samudācaratā abhibhavāt vā atyanta viṣaya sevayā vā vicchidya vicchidya tena tena ātmanā samudācaranti āvirbhavanti vājīkaraṇa ādi upayogena vā abhibhāvaka daurbalyena vā iti vīpsayā viccheda samudācārayoḥ paunaḥpunyam darśayatā yathā uktāt prasuptāt bhedaḥ uktaḥ rāgeṇa vā samudācaratā vijātīyaḥ krodhaḥ abhibhūyate sajātīyena vā viṣaya antara vartinā rāgeṇa eva viṣaya antara vartī rāgaḥ abhibhūyate iti āha rāga iti bhaviṣyat vṛtteḥ trayī gatiḥ yathāyogam veditavyā iti āha sa hi iti bhaviṣyat vṛtti kleśa mātra parāmarśi sarvanāma na caitra rāga parāmarśi tasya vicchinna tvāt eva iti udāram āha viṣayaḥ iti 
TV_2.4.2^4–2.4.3	 nanūdāraḥ eva puruṣān kliśnāti iti bhavatu kleśaḥ anye tu akliśnantaḥ katham kleśāḥ iti atas āha sarve eva ete iti kleśa viṣaya tvam kleśa pada vācya tvam na atikrāmanti udāra tām āpadyamānāḥ atas eva te api heyāḥ iti bhāvaḥ kleśa tvena ekatām manyamānaḥ codayati kaḥ tarhi iti kleśa tvena samāna tve api yathā ukta avasthā bhedāt viśeṣaḥ iti pariharati ucyate satyam iti syāt etat avidyātaḥ bhavantu kleśāḥ tathā api avidyā nivṛttau kasmāt nivartante na khalu paṭaḥ kuvinda nivṛttau nivartate iti atas āha sarve eva iti bhedāḥ iva bhedāḥ tad avinirbhāga vartinaḥ iti yāvat pṛcchati kasmāt uttaram sarveṣu iti tat eva sphuṭayati yat iti ākāryate samāropyate śeṣam sugamam prasuptāḥ tattva līnānām tanu avasthāḥ ca yoginām vicchinna udāra rūpāḥ ca kleśāḥ viṣaya saṅginām iti saṃgrahaḥ 
TV_2.5.1–2.5.2^1	 anitya aśuci duḥkha anātmasu nitya śuci sukha ātma khyātiḥ avidyā anitya aśuci duḥkha anātmasu nitya śuci sukha ātma khyātiḥ avidyā anitya tva upayogi viśeṣaṇam kāryaḥ iti kecid kila bhūtāni nitya tvena abhimanyamānāḥ tad rūpam abhīpsavaḥ tāni eva upāsate evam dhūma ādi mārgān upāsate candra sūrya tāraka ādyu lokān nityān abhimanyamānāḥ tad prāptaye evam divaukasaḥ devān amṛtān abhimanyamānāḥ tabhāvāya somam pibanti āmnāyate hi apāma somam amṛtāḥ abhūmaḥ iti sā iyam anityeṣu nitya khyātiḥ avidyā tathā aśucau parama bībhatse kāye ardha uktaḥ eva kāya bībhatsatāyām vaiyāsikīm gāthām paṭhati sthānāt iti mātuḥ udaram mūtra ādi upahatam sthānam pitroḥ lohita retasīm bījam aśita pīta āhāra rasa ādi bhāvaḥ upaṣṭambhaḥ tena śarīram dhāryate niḥsyandaḥ prasvedaḥ nidhanam ca śrotriya śarīram api apavitrayati tad sparśe snāna vidhānāt nanu yadi śarīram aśuci kṛtam tarhi mṛd jala ādi kṣālanena iti atas āha ādheya śauca tvāt iti 
TV_2.5.2^2	 svabhāvena aśuceḥ api śarīrasya śaucam ādheyam sugandhitā iva kāminīnām aṅgarāga ādibhiḥ ardha uktam pūrayati iti uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ aśucau śarīraḥ iti śuci khyātim āha nava iti hāvaḥ śṛṅgāra jāḥ līlā kasya strī kāyasya parama bībhatsasya kena mandatama sādṛśyena śaśāṅka lekhā ādinā saṃbandhaḥ etena aśucau strī kāye śuci khyāti pradarśanena apuṇye hiṃsā ādau saṃsāra mocaka ādīnām puṇya pratyayaḥ evam arjana rakṣaṇa ādi duḥkha bahula tayā anarthe dhana ādau artha pratyayāḥ vyākhyātāḥ sarveṣām jugupsita tvena aśuci tvāt tathā duḥkhaḥ iti sugamam tathā anātmani iti sugamam tathā etat atra uktam pañcaśikhena vyaktam cetanam putra dāra paśu ādi avyaktam acetanam śayyāsana aśana ādi sa sarvaḥ apratibuddhaḥ mūḍhaḥ catvāri padāni sthānāni asyāḥ iti catuṣpadā nanu anyā api diś moha alāta cakra ādi viṣaya ananta pada avidyā tat kim ucyate catuṣpada iti atas āha mūlam asya iti 
TV_2.5.2^3	 santu nāma anyāḥ api avidyāḥ saṃsāra bījam tu catuṣpadā eva iti nanu avidyā iti nañsamāsaḥ pūrva padārtha pradhānaḥ vā syāt yathā makṣikam iti uttara padārtha pradhānaḥ vā yathārāja puruṣaḥ iti anya padārtha pradhānaḥ vā yathā makṣikaḥ deśaḥ iti tatra pūrva padārtha pradhāna tve vidyāyāḥ prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ gamyeta na ca asyāḥ kleśa ādi kāraṇa tvam uttara padārtha pradhāna tve vā vidyā eva kasyacid abhāvena viśiṣṭāḥ gamyeta sā ca kleśa ādi paripanthinī na tu tat bījam na hi pradhāna upaghātī pradhāna guṇaḥ yuktaḥ tad anupaghātāya guṇe tu anyāyi a kalpanā tasmāt vidyā svarūpa anupaghātāya nañaḥ anyathā karaṇam api āhāraḥ vā niṣedhyasya iti anya padārtha pradhāna tve tu avidyamāna vidyā buddhiḥ vaktavyā na ca asau vidyāyāḥ abhāva mātreṇa kleśa ādi bījam viveka khyāti pūrvaka nirodha saṃpannāyāḥ api tathā tva prasaṅgāt 
TV_2.5.2^4	 tasmāt sarvathā eva avidyāyāḥ na kleśa ādi mūlatā iti atas āha tasyāḥ ca iti vastunaḥ bhāvaḥ vastu sa tattvam vastu tvam iti yāvat tat anena na prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ na api vidyā eva avidyā na tad abhāva viśiṣṭā buddhiḥ api tu vidyā viruddham viparyaya jñānam avidyā iti uktam loka adhīna avadhāraṇaḥ hi śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ loke ca uttara padārtha pradhānasya api nañaḥ uttara pada abhidheya upamardakasya tad lakṣita tad viruddha para tayā tatra tatra upalabdheḥ iha api tad viruddhe vṛttiḥ iti bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭāntam vibhajate yathā na amitraḥ iti na mitra abhāvaḥ na api mitra mātram iti asya anantaram vastu antaram kim tu tad viruddhaḥ sapatnaḥ iti vaktavyam tathāgoṣpadam iti na goṣpada abhāvaḥ na goṣpada mātram kim tu deśaḥ eva vipulaḥ goṣpada viruddhaḥ tābhyām abhāva goṣpadābhyām anyat vastu antaram dārṣṭa antike yojayati evam iti 
TV_2.6.1–2.6.2^1	 dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ eka ātma tā iva asmitā avidyām uktvā tasyāḥ kāryam asmitām rāga ādi vārṣiṣṭhām āha dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ eka ātma tā iva asmitā dṛś ca darśanam ca te eva śaktī tayoḥ ātmānātmanoḥ anātmani ātma jñāna lakṣaṇa avidyā pāditā yā eka ātma tā iva na tu paramārthataḥ eka ātma tā sa asmitā dṛś darśanayoḥ iti vaktavye tayoḥ bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ yogya tā lakṣaṇam saṃbandham darśayitum śakti grahaṇam sūtram vivṛṇoti puruṣaḥ iti nanu anayoḥ abheda pratīteḥ abhedaḥ eva kasmāt na bhavati kutas ca eka tvam kliśnāti puruṣam iti atas āha bhoktṛ bhogyā iti bhogya śaktiḥ buddhiḥ bhoktṛ śaktiḥ puruṣaḥ tayoḥ atyanta vibhaktayoḥ kutas atyanta vibhakta tvam iti atas āha atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ 
TV_2.6.2^2	 apariṇāmi tva ādi dharmakaḥ puruṣaḥ pariṇāmi tva ādi dharmikā buddhiḥ iti asaṃkīrṇa tā tat anena pratīyamānaḥ api abhedaḥ na pāramārthikaḥ iti uktam avibhāga iti kleśa tvam uktam anvayam darśayitvā vyatirekam āha svarūpa iti pratilambhaḥ viveka khyātiḥ parasya api etat saṃmatam iti āha tat uktam pañcaśikhena buddhitaḥ iti ākāraḥ svarūpam sadā viśuddhiḥ śīlam audāsīnyam vidyā caitanyam buddhiḥ aviśuddhān udāsīnā jaḍā ca iti tatra ātma buddhiḥ avidyā mohaḥ pūrva avidyā janitaḥ saṃskāraḥ tamaḥ vā avidyāyāḥ tāmasa tvāt iti 
TV_2.7.1–2.7.2	 sukha anuśayī rāgaḥ viveka darśane rāga ādīnām vinivṛtteḥ avidyā pādita asmitā rāga ādīnām nidānam iti asmitā anantaram rāga ādīn lakṣayati sukha anuśayī rāgaḥ anabhijñasya smṛteḥ abhāvāt sukha abhijñasya iti uktam smaryamāṇe sukhe rāgaḥ sukha anusmṛti pūrvakaḥ anubhūyamāne tu sukhe na anusmṛtim apekṣate tad sādhane tu smaryamāṇe dṛśyamāne vā sukha anusmṛti pūrvaḥ eva rāgaḥ dṛśyamānam api hi sukha sādhanam tad jātīyasya sukha hetu tām smṛtvā tad jātīya tayā vā asya sukha hetu tvam anumāya icchati anuśayi padārtham āha yaḥ iti 
TV_2.8.1–2.9.2^1	 duḥkha anuśayī dveṣaḥ duḥkha anuśayī dveṣaḥ duḥkha abhijñasya iti pūrvavat vyākhyeyam anuśayi padārtham āha yaḥ pratighaḥ iti pratihanti iti pratighaḥ etat eva paryāyaiḥ vivṛṇoti manyuḥ iti svarasa vāhī viduṣaḥ api tathā rūḍhaḥ abhiniveśaḥ svarasa vāhī viduṣaḥ api tathā rūḍhaḥ abhiniveśaḥ abhiniveśa padārtham vyācaṣṭe sarvasya pāṇinaḥ iti iyam ātma āśīḥ ātmani prārthanā mā na bhūvam mābhāvī bhūvam bhūyāsam jīvyāsam iti na ca ananubhūta maraṇa dharmakasya ananubhūtaḥ maraṇa dharmaḥ yena jantunā na tasya eṣā bhavati ātma āśīḥ abhiniveśaḥ maraṇa bhayam prasaṅgataḥ janma antaram pratyācakṣāṇam nāstikam nirākaroti etayā ca iti pratyuditasya śarīrasya dhriyamāṇa tvāt pūrva janma anubhavaḥ pratīyate 
TV_2.9.2^2	 nikāya viśiṣṭābhiḥ apūrvābhiḥ deha indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ abhisaṃbandhaḥ janma tasya anubhavaḥ prāptiḥ sā pratīyate katham iti atas āha sa ca ayam abhiniveśaḥ ardha uktau eva asya kleśa tvam āha kleśaḥ iti ayam ahita karma ādinā jantūn kliśnāti duḥkha akaroti iti kleśaḥ vaktum upakrāntam parisamāpayati svarasa vāhī iti svabhāvena vāsanā rūpeṇa vahana śīlaḥ na punar āgantukaḥ kṛmeḥ api jāta mātrasya duḥkha bahulasya nikṛṣṭatama caitanyasya anāgantuka tve hetum āha pratyakṣa anumāna āgamaiḥ pratyudite janmani asaṃbhāvitaḥ asaṃpāditaḥ maraṇa trāsa uccheda dṛṣṭi ātmakaḥ pūrva janma anubhūtam maraṇa duḥkham anumāpayati 
TV_2.9.2^3	 ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ jāta mātre eva hi bālakaḥ māraka vastu darśanāt vepamānaḥ kampa viśeṣāt anumita maraṇa pratyāsattiḥ tatas bibhyat upalabhyate duḥkhāt duḥkha hetoḥ ca bhayam dṛṣṭam na ca asmin janmani anena maraṇam anubhūtam anumitam śrutam vā prāk eva asya duḥkha tvam tad hetu tvam vā avagamyeta tasmāt tasya tathābhūtasya smṛtiḥ pariśiṣyate na ca iyam saṃskārāt ṛte na ca ayam saṃskāraḥ anubhavam vinā na ca asmin janmani anubhavaḥ iti prāc bhavīyaḥ pariśiṣyate iti āsīt pūrva janma saṃbandhaḥ iti tathā āpadam yathāpadam ākāṅkṣati iti artha prāpte yathāpade sati yādṛśaḥ vākya arthaḥ bhavati tādṛśam darśayati yathā ca ayam iti 
TV_2.9.2^4	 atyanta mūḍheṣu mandatama caitanyeṣu vidvattām darśayati vijñāta pūrva apara antasya antar koṭiḥ puruṣasya hi pūrvā koṭiḥ saṃsāraḥ uttarā ca kaivalyam sā eva vijñātā śruta anumānābhyām yena sa tathā uktaḥ saḥ ayam maraṇa trāsaḥ ā kṛmeḥ ā ca viduṣaḥ rūḍhaḥ prasiddhaḥ iti nanu aviduṣaḥ bhavatu maraṇa trāsaḥ viduṣaḥ tu na saṃbhavati vidyayā unmūlita tvāt anunmūlane vā syāt atyanta sattvam iti āśayavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti uttaram āha samānā hi iti na saṃprajñātavān vidvān api tu śruta anumita vivekaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_2.10.1–2.10.2	 te pratiprasava heyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ tat evam kleśāḥ lakṣitāḥ teṣām ca heyānām prasupta tanu vicchinna udāra rūpa tayā catasraḥ avasthāḥ darśitāḥ kasmāt punar pañcamī kleśa avasthā dagdha bīja bhāva tayā sūkṣmā na sūtrakāreṇa kathitā iti atas āha te pratiprasava heyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ yat kila puruṣa prayatna gocaraḥ tat upadiśyate na ca sūkṣma avasthā āhānam prayatna gocaraḥ kim tu pratiprasavena kāryasya cittasya asmitā lakṣaṇa kāraṇa bhāva āpattyā hātavya iti vyācaṣṭe te iti sugamam 
TV_2.11.1–2.11.2	 dhyāna heyāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ atha kriyā yoga tanūkṛtānām kleśānām kiṃviṣayāt puruṣa prayatnāt dhānam iti atas āha sthitānām tu bīja bhāva upagatānām iti vandhyebhyaḥ vyavacchinatti sūtram paṭhati dhyāna heyāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ vyācaṣṭe kleśānām iti kriyā yoga tanūkṛtāḥ api hi pratiprasava hetu bhāvena kāryataḥ sva rūpataḥ ca śakyāḥ ucchettum iti sthūlāḥ uktāḥ puruṣa prayatnasya prasaṃkhyāna gocarasya avadhim āha yāvat iti sūkṣmīkṛtāḥ iti vivṛṇoti dagdhā iti atra eva dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā vastrāṇām iti yatnena kṣālana ādinā upāyena kṣāra saṃyoga ādinā sthūla sūkṣma mātra tayā dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ sāmyam na punar prayatna apaneya tayā pratiprasava heyeṣu tad asaṃbhavāt su alpaḥ pratipakṣaḥ uccheda hetuḥ yāsām tāḥ tathā uktāḥ mahān pratipakṣaḥ uccheda hetuḥ yāsām tāḥ tathā uktāḥ pratiprasavasya ca adhastāt prasaṃkhyānam iti avaratayā su alpa tvam uktam 
TV_2.12.1–2.12.2^1	 kleśa mūlaḥ karma āśayaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ syāt etat jāti āyuḥ bhoga hetavaḥ puruṣam kliśnantaḥ kleśāḥ karma āśayaḥ ca tathā na tu avidyā ādayaḥ tat katham avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ iti atas āha kleśa mūlaḥ karma āśayaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ kleśāḥ mūlam yasya utpāde ca kārya karaṇe ca sa tathā uktaḥ etat uktam bhavati avidyā ādi mūlaḥ hi karma āśayaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga hetuḥ iti avidyā ādayaḥ api tad hetavaḥ atas kleśāḥ iti vyācaṣṭe tatra iti āśerate sāṃsārikāḥ puruṣāḥ asmin iti āśayaḥ karmaṇām āśayaḥ dharma adharmau kāmāt kāmya karma pravṛttau svarga ādi hetuḥ dharmaḥ bhavati evam lobhāt para dravya apahāra ādau adharmaḥ mohāt adharme hiṃsā ādau dharma buddheḥ pravartamānasya adharmaḥ eva na tu asti moha jaḥ dharmaḥ 
TV_2.12.2^2	 asti krodha jaḥ dharmaḥ tat yathā dhruvasya jana ka apamāna janmanaḥ krodhāt tad jigīṣayā cittena karma āśayena puṇyena antarikṣa loka vāsinām upari sthānam adharmaḥ tu krodha jaḥ brahma vadha ādi janmā prasiddhaḥ eva bhūtānām tasya dvaividhyam āha sa dṛṣṭa janma iti dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyam āha tīvra saṃvegena iti yathāsaṃkhyam dṛṣṭāntau āha yathā nandīśvaraḥ iti tatra nārakāṇām iti yena karma āśayena kumbhīpāka ādayaḥ naraka bhedāḥ prāpyante tad kāriṇaḥ nārakāḥ teṣām na asti dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ karma āśayaḥ na hi manuṣya śarīreṇa tad pariṇāma bhedena vā sā tādṛśī vatsara sahasra ādi nirantarā upabhogyā vedanā saṃbhavati iti śeṣam sugamam 
TV_2.13.1–2.13.2^1^1	 sati mūle tad vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ syāt etat avidyā mūla tve karma āśayasya vidyā utpāde sati avidyā vināśāt mā nāma karma āśaya antaram ca eṣīt prācām tu karma āśayānām anādi bhava paramparā saṃcitānām asaṃkhyātānām aniyata vipāka kālānām bhogena kṣapayitum aśakya tvāt aśakyocchedaḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt iti atas āha sati mūle tad vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ etat uktam bhavati sukha duḥkha phalaḥ hi karma āśayaḥ tādarthyena tat na antarīyaka tayā janma āyuṣī api prasūte sukha duḥkhe ca rāga dveṣa anuṣakte tad avinirbhāga vartinī tad abhāve na bhavataḥ 
TV_2.13.1–2.13.2^1^2	 na ca asti saṃbhavaḥ na ca tatra yaḥ tuṣyati vā udvijate vā tat ca tasya sukham vā duḥkham vā iti tat iyam ātma bhūmiḥ kleśa salila avasiktā karma phala prasava kṣetram iti asti kleśānām phala upajanane api karma āśaya sahakāritā iti kleśa samucchede saha kāri vaikalyāt san api anantaḥ api aniyata vipāka kālaḥ api prasaṃkhyāna dagdha bīja bhāvaḥ na phalāya kalpate iti uktam artham bhāṣyam eva dyotayati satsu iti atra eva dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā tuṣa iti sa tuṣāḥ api dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ sveda ādibhiḥ dārṣṭa antike yojayati tathā iti 
TV_2.13.2^2	 nanu na kleśāḥ śakyāḥ apanetum na hi satām apanayaḥ iti atas āha na prasaṃkhyāna dagdha kleśa bīja bhāvaḥ iti vipākasya traividhyam āha sa ca iti vipacyate sādhyate karmabhiḥ iti vipākaḥ karma eka tvam dhruvam kṛtvā janma ekatva aneka tva gocarā prathamā vicāraṇā dvitīyā tu karma aneka tvam dhruvam kṛtvā janma ekatva aneka tva gocarā tat evam catvāraḥ vikalpāḥ tatra prathamam vikalpam apākaroti na tāvat ekam karma ekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam pṛcchati kasmāt iti uttaram anādi kāla ekaika janma pracitasya atas eva asaṃkhyeyasya ekaika janma kṣapitāt ekaikasmāt karmaṇaḥ avaśiṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ sāṃpratikasya ca phala krama anigamāt anāśvāsaḥ lokasya prasaktaḥ sa ca aniṣṭaḥ iti etat uktam bhavati karma kṣayasya virala tvāt tad utpatti bāhulyāt ca anyonya saṃpīḍitāḥ karma āśayāḥ nirantara utpattayaḥ nirucchvāsāḥ sva vipākam prati iti na phala kramaḥ śakyaḥ avadhārayitum prekṣāvatā iti anāśvāsaḥ puṇya anuṣṭhānam prati prasaktaḥ iti dvitīyam vikalpam nirākaroti na ca ekam karma anekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam pṛcchati kasmāt iti 
TV_2.13.2^3	 uttaram anekasmin janmani āhitam ekaikam eva karma anekasya janma lakṣaṇasya vipākasya nimittam iti avaśiṣṭasya vipāka kāla abhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ sa ca api aniṣṭaḥ karma vaiphalyena tad ananuṣṭhāna prasaṅgāt yadā eka janma samucchedye karmaṇi ekasmin phala krama aniyamāt anāśvāsaḥ tadā kā eva kathā bahu janma samuccedye karmaṇi ekasmin tatra hi avasara abhāvāt vipāka kāla abhāvaḥ eva sāṃpratikasya iti bhāvaḥ tṛtīyam vikalpam nirākaroti na ca anekam karma anekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam tatra hetum āha tat anekam janma yugapad na saṃbhavati ayoginaḥ iti krameṇa vācyam yadi hi karma sahasram yugapad janma sahasram prasuvīta tatas eva karma sahasra prakṣayāt avaśiṣṭasya vipāka kālaḥ phala krama niyamaḥ ca syātām na hi asti janmanām yaugapadyam evam eva prathama pakṣa uktam dūṣaṇam iti arthaḥ tat evam pakṣa traye nirākṛte pāriśeṣyāt anekam karma ekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam iti pakṣaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate iti āha tasmāt janma iti 
TV_2.13.2^4	 janma ca prāyaṇam ca janma prāyaṇe tayoḥ antaram madhyam tasmin vicitra sukha duḥkha phala upahāreṇa vicitraḥ yat atyantam udbhūtam anantaram eva phalam dāsyati tat pradhānam yat tu kiṃcid vilambena tat upasarjanam prāyaṇam maraṇam tena abhivyaktaḥ sva kārya ārambhaṇa abhimukham upanītaḥ eka praghaṭṭakena yugapad saṃmūrchitaḥ janma ādi lakṣaṇe kārye kartavyaḥ ekalolībhāvam āpannaḥ ekam eva janma karoti na anekam tat ca janma manuṣya ādi bhāvaḥ tena eva karmaṇā labdha āyuṣkam kāla bhedāt niyata jīvitam bhavati 
TV_2.13.2^5	 tasmin āyuṣi tena eva karmaṇā bhogaḥ sukha duḥkha sākṣātkāraḥ sva saṃbandhi tayā saṃpadyate iti tasmāt asau karma āśayaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga hetu tvāt tri vipākaḥ abhidhīyate autsargikam upasaṃharati atas eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ uktaḥ iti ekaḥ bhavaḥ eka bhavaḥ pūrva kālaḥ ityādinā samāsaḥ eka bhavaḥ asya asti iti matvarthīyaḥ ṭhan kvacid pāṭhaḥ aikabhavikaḥ iti tatra eka bhava śabdāt bhava arthe ṭhak pratyayaḥ eka janma avacchinnam asya bhavanam iti arthaḥ tat evam autsargikasya eka bhavikasya tri vipāka tvam uktvā dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya aihikasya karmaṇaḥ tri vipāka tvam vyavacchinatti dṛṣṭā iti 
TV_2.13.2^6	 nandīśvarasya khalu aṣṭa varṣa avacchinna āyuṣaḥ manuṣya janmanaḥ tīvra saṃvega adhimātra upāya janmā puṇya bhedaḥ āyuḥ bhoga hetutvāt dvi pākaḥ nahuṣasya tu pārṣṇi prahāra virodhina agastyasya indra pada prāpti hetunā eva karmaṇā āyuṣaḥ vihita tvāt apuṇya bhedaḥ bhoga mātra hetuḥ nanu yathā eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ tathā kim kleśa vāsanāḥ bhoga anukūlāḥ ca karma vipāka anubhava vāsanās tathā ca manuṣyaḥ tiryagyonim āpannaḥ na tat jātīya ucitam bhuñjīta iti atas āha kleśa iti saṃmūrchitam ekalolībhāvam āpannam dharma adharmābhyām vyavacchettum vāsanāyāḥ svarūpam āha ye saṃskārāḥ iti autsargikam eka bhavika tvam kvacid apavaditum bhūmikām āracayati yaḥ tu asau iti tuśabdena vāsanātaḥ vyavacchinatti dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya niyata vipākasya eva ayam eka bhavika tva niyamaḥ na tu adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya kiṃbhūtasya aniyata vipākasya iti hetum pṛcchati kasmāt iti hetum āha yaḥ hi iti ekām tāvat gatim āha kṛtasya iti dvitīyām āha pradhāna iti tṛtīyām āha niyata iti tatra prathamām vibhajate tatra kṛtasya iti 
TV_2.13.2^7	 saṃnyāsi karmabhyaḥ aśukla akṛṣṇebhyaḥ anyāni trīṇi eva karmāṇi kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa śukla śuklāni tat iha tapaḥ svādhyāya ādi sādhyaḥ śuklaḥ karma āśayaḥ uditaḥ eva adatta phalasya kṛṣṇasya nāśakaḥ aviśeṣāt ca śabalasya api kṛṣṇa bhāga yogāt iti mantavyam atra eva bhagavān āmnāyam udāharati yatra idam iti dve dve ha vai karmaṇī kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa śukle apahanti iti saṃbandhaḥ vīpsayā bhūyiṣṭhatā sūcitā kasya iti atas āha pāpakasya puṃsaḥ kaḥ asau apahanti iti atas āha ekaḥ rāśiḥ puṇya kṛtaḥ samūhasya samūhi sādhya tvāt tat anena śuklaḥ karma āśayaḥ tṛtīyaḥ uktaḥ 
TV_2.13.2^8	 etat uktam bhavati īdṛśaḥ nāma ayam para pīḍā ādi rahita sādhana sādhyaḥ śuklaḥ karma āśayaḥ yat ekaḥ api san kṛṣṇān kṛṣṇa śuklān ca atyanta virodhinaḥ karma āśayān bhūyasaḥ api apahanti tat tasmāt icchasva iti cchānda satvāt ātmanepadam śeṣam sugamam atra ca śukla karma udayasya eva sa kaḥ api mahimā yatas itareṣām abhāvaḥ na tu svādhyāya ādi janmanaḥ duḥkhāt na hi duḥkha mātra virodhya dharmaḥ api tu sva kārya duḥkha virodhī na ca svādhyāya ādi janyam duḥkham tasya kāryam tad kārya tve svādhyāya ādi vidhāna ānarthakyāt tad balāt eva tad utpatteḥ 
TV_2.13.2^9	 anutpattau vā kumbhī pāka ādi api vidhīyeta avidhāne tu tad anutpatteḥ iti sarvam catur asram dvitīyām gatim vibhajate pradhāne karmaṇi jyotiṣṭoma ādike tad aṅgasya paśu hiṃsā ādeḥ āvāpa gamanam dve khalu hiṃsā ādeḥ kārye pradhāna aṅga tvena vidhānāt tad upakāraḥ na hiṃsyāt sarvāḥ bhūtāni iti hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣiddha tvāt anarthaḥ ca tatra pradhāna aṅga tvena anuṣṭhānāt apradhāna tā eva iti atas na drāk iti eva pradhāna nirapekṣā satī sva phalam anartham prasotum arhati kim tu ārabdha vipāke pradhāne sāhāyakam ācarantī vyavatiṣṭhate 
TV_2.13.2^10	 pradhāna sāhāyakam ācarantyāḥ ca sva kārye bīja mātra tayā avasthānam pradhāne karmaṇi āvāpa gamanam yatra idam uktam pañcaśikhena su alpaḥ saṃkaraḥ jyotiṣṭoma ādi janmanaḥ pradhāna apūrvasya paśu hiṃsā ādi janmanā anartha hetunā apūrveṇa sa parihāraḥ śakyaḥ hi kiyatā prāyaścittena parihartum atha pramādataḥ prāyaścittam api na ācaritam pradhāna karma vipāka samaye ca vipacyeta tathā api yāvat tam asau anartham prasūte tāvān sa pratyavamarṣaḥ mṛṣyante hi puṇya saṃbhāra upanīta sukha sudhā mahā hrada avagāhinaḥ kuśalāḥ pāpa mātra upapāditām duḥkha vahni kaṇikām 
TV_2.13.2^11	 atas kuśalasya su mahataḥ puṇyasya na apakarṣāya prakṣayāya paryāptaḥ pṛcchati kasmāt puṇyavataḥ uttaram kuśalam hi me bahu anyat asti pradhāna karma parikaratayā vyavasthitam dīkṣaṇīya ādi dakṣiṇa antam yatra ayam saṃkaraḥ su alpaḥ svarge api asya phale saṃkīrṇa puṇya labdha janmanaḥ svargāt sarvathā duḥkhena aparāmṛṣṭāt apakarṣam alpam alpa duḥkha saṃbhedam kariṣyati iti tṛtīyām gatim vibhajate niyata iti balīyaḥ tvena iha prādhānyam abhimatam na tu aṅgitayā balīyaḥ tvam ca niyata vipāka tvena anya dānava kāśa tvāt aniyata vipākasya tu durbala tvam anyadā sa avakāśa tvāt ciram avasthānam bīja bhāva mātreṇa na punar pradhāna upakāri tayā tasya svatantra tvāt nanu prāyaṇena ekadā eva karma āśayaḥ abhivyajyate iti uktam idānīm ca cira avasthānam ucyate tat katham param pūrveṇa na virudhyate iti āśayavān pṛcchati katham iti uttaram adṛṣṭā iti jāti abhiprāyam eka vacanam tad itarasya gatim uktām avadhārayati yat tu adṛṣṭā iti śeṣam sugamam 
TV_2.14.1–2.14.2	 te hlāda paritāpa phalāḥ puṇya apuṇya hetu tvāt uktam kleśa mūla tvam karmaṇām karma mūla tvam ca vipākānām atha vipākāḥ kasya mūlam yena amī tyaktavyāḥ iti atas āha te hlāda paritāpa phalāḥ puṇya apuṇya hetu tvāt vyācaṣṭe te janma āyuḥ bhogāḥ iti yadi api janma āyuṣoḥ eva hlāda paritāpa pūrva bhāvitayā tad phala tvam na tu bhogasya hlāda paritāpa udayā anantara bhāvinaḥ tad anubhava ātmanaḥ tathā api anubhāvya tayā bhogya tayā bhoga karma tā mātreṇa bhoga phala tvam iti mantavyam nanu apuṇya hetukāḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ paritāpa phalāḥ bhavantu heyāḥ pratikūla vedanīya tvāt kasmāt punar puṇya hetavaḥ tyajyante sukha phalāḥ anukūla vedanīya tvāt na ca eṣām pratyātma vedanīya anukūla tā śakyā sahasreṇa api anumāna āgamaiḥ apākartum na ca hlāda paritāpau paraspara avinābhūtau yatas hlādaḥ upādīyamāne paritāpe api avarjanīya tayā patet tayoḥ bhinna hetuka tvāt bhinna rūpa tvāt ca iti atas āha yathā ca idam iti 
TV_2.15.1–2.15.2^1	 pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca duḥkham eva sarvam vivekinaḥ yadi api na pṛthagjanaiḥ pratikūla ātma tayā viṣaya sukha kāle saṃvedyate duḥkham tathā api saṃvedyate yogibhiḥ iti praśna pūrvakam tad upapādanāya sūtram avatārayati katham tat upapadyate iti pariṇāma ityādi sūtram pariṇāmaḥ ca tāpaḥ ca saṃskāraḥ ca etāni eva duḥkhāni taiḥ iti pariṇāma duḥkha tayā viṣaya sukhasya duḥkha tām āha sarvasya ayam iti na khalu sukham rāga anuvedham antareṇa saṃbhavati na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ na tatra tuṣyati tat ca tasya sukham iti rāgasya ca pravṛtti hetu tvāt pravṛtteḥ ca puṇya apuṇya upacaya hetu tvāt tatra asti rāga jaḥ karma āśayaḥ asataḥ anupajananāt 
TV_2.15.2^2	 tadā ca sukham bhuñjānaḥ tatra saktaḥ api vicchinna avasthena dveṣeṇa dveṣṭi duḥkha sādhanāni tāni parihartum aśaktaḥ muhyati ca iti dveṣa moha kṛtaḥ api asti karma āśayaḥ dveṣa vat mohasya api viparyaya apara nāmnaḥ karma āśaya hetu tvam aviruddham nanu katham raktaḥ dveṣṭi muhyati vā rāga samaye dveṣa mohayoḥ adarśanāt iti atas āha tathā ca uktam vicchinna avasthān kleśān upapādayadbhiḥ asmābhiḥ tat anena vāc manasa pravṛtti janmanī puṇya apuṇye darśite rāga ādi janmanaḥ kartavyam idam iti mānasasya saṃkalpasya sa abhilāṣa tvena vācanika tvasya api aviśeṣāt yathā āhuḥ 
TV_2.15.3–2.15.5	 sa abhilāṣaḥ ca saṃkalpaḥ vācya arthān na atiricyate iti śārīram api karma āśayam darśayati na anupahatya iti atas eva dharma śāstra kārāḥ pañca sūnāḥ gṛhasthasya iti āhuḥ syāt etat na pratyātma vedanīyasya viṣaya sukhasya pratyākhyānam ucitam yoginām anubhava virodhāt iti atas āha viṣaya sukham ca avidyā iti uktam caturvidha viparyāsa lakṣaṇām avidyām darśayadbhiḥ iti na āpāta mātram ādriyante vṛddhāḥ asti khalu āpātatas madhu viṣa saṃpṛktān na upabhoge api sukha anubhavaḥ pratyātma vedanīyaḥ kim tu āyatyām asukham iyam ca darśitā bhagavatā eva viṣaya indriya saṃyogāt yat tat agre amṛta upamam pariṇāme viṣam iva tat sukham rājasam smṛtam iti 
TV_2.15.6–2.15.7	 codayati yā bhogeṣu iti na vayam viṣaya hlādam sukham ātiṣṭhāmahe kim tu tṛpyatām puṃsām tad tad viṣaya prārthanā parikliṣṭa cetasām tṛṣṇā eva mahat duḥkham na ca iyam upabhogam antareṇa śāmyati na ca asyāḥ praśamaḥ rāga ādi anuviddhaḥ iti na asya pariṇāma duḥkha tā iti bhāvaḥ tṛpteḥ tṛṣṇā kṣayāt dhetoḥ indriyāṇām upaśāntiḥ apravartanam viṣayeṣu iti arthaḥ etat eva vyatireka mukhena spaṣṭayati yā laulyāt iti pariharati na ca indriyāṇām iti hetau anoḥ prayogaḥ satyam tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ sukham anavadyam tasya tu na bhoga abhyāsaḥ hetuḥ api tu tṛṣṇāyāḥ eva tad virodhinyāḥ yathā āhuḥ na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate iti 
TV_2.15.8^1	 śeṣam ati rohitam tāpa duḥkha tām pṛcchati atha kā iti uttaram sarvasya iti sarva jana prasiddha tvena tad svarūpa prapañcam akṛtvā tāpa duḥkha tā api pariṇāma duḥkha tā samatayā prapañcitā iti saṃskāra duḥkha tām pṛcchati kā iti uttaram sukha iti sukha anubhavaḥ hi saṃskāram ādhatte sa ca sukha smaraṇam tat ca rāgam sa ca manaḥ kāya vacana ceṣṭām sā ca puṇya apuṇye tatas vipāka anubhavaḥ tatas vāsanā iti evam anāditā iti atra ca sukha duḥkha saṃskāra atiśayāt tad smaraṇam tasmāt ca rāga dveṣau tābhyām karmāṇi karmabhyaḥ vipākaḥ iti yojanā tat evam duḥkha srotaḥ prasṛtam yoginam eva kliśnāti na itaram pṛthagjanam iti āha evam idam anādi iti itaram tu tri parvāṇaḥ tāpāḥ anuplavantaḥ iti saṃbandhaḥ ādhibhautika ādhidaivikayoḥ tāpayoḥ bāhya tvena ekatvam vivakṣitam 
TV_2.15.8^2	 citte vṛttiḥ asyāḥ iti avidyā citta vṛttiḥ tayā hātavyaḥ eva buddhīndriya śarīra ādau dāra apatya ādau ca ahaṃkāram amakāra anupātinam iti tat atra na samyak darśanāt anyat paritrāṇam asti iti āha tat evam iti tat evam aupādhikam viṣaya sukhasya pariṇāmataḥ saṃskārataḥ tāpa saṃyogāt ca duḥkha tvam abhidhāya svābhāvikam ādarśayati guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca iti vyācaṣṭe prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti rūpāḥ buddhi rūpeṇa pariṇatāḥ guṇāḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi paraspara anugraha tantrāḥ śāntam sukha ātmakam ghoram duḥkha ātmakam mūḍham viṣāda ātmakam eva pratyayam sukha upabhoga rūpam api triguṇam ārabhante na ca saḥ api tādṛśa pratyaya rūpaḥ asya pariṇāmaḥ sthiraḥ iti āha calam ca guṇa vṛttam iti kṣipra pariṇāmi cittam uktam nanu ekaḥ pratyayaḥ katham paraspara viruddha śānta ghora mūḍha tvāni ekadā pratipadyate iti atas āha rūpa atiśayāḥ vṛtti atiśayāḥ ca paraspareṇa virudhyante 
TV_2.15.8^3	 rūpāṇi aṣṭau bhāvāḥ dharma ādayaḥ vṛttayaḥ sukha ādyāḥ tat iha dharmeṇa vipacyamānena adharmaḥ tādṛśaḥ virudhyate evam jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryaiḥ sukha ādibhiḥ ca tādṛśāni eva tad viparītāni virudhyante sāmānyāni tu asamudācara drupāṇi atiśayaiḥ samudācaradbhiḥ saha avirodhāt pravartante iti nanu gṛhṇīmaḥ etat tathā api viṣaya sukhasya kutas svābhāvikī duḥkha tā iti atas āha evam ete iti upādāna abhedāt upādāna ātmaka tvāt ca upādeyasya api abhedaḥ iti arthaḥ tat kim idānīm ātyantikam eva tādātmyam tathā ca buddhi vyapadeśa bhedau na kalpete iti atas āha guṇa pradhāna iti sāmānya ātmanā guṇa bhāvaḥ atiśaya ātmanā ca prādhānyam tasmāt upādhitaḥ svabhāvataḥ ca duḥkham eva sarvam vivekinaḥ iti duḥkham ca heyam prekṣāvatā 
TV_2.15.8^4–2.15.9	 na ca tad nidāna hānam antareṇa tat dheyam bhavitum arhati na ca aparijñātam nidānam śakyam hātum iti mūla nidānam asya darśayati tat asya iti duḥkha samudāyasya prabhavaḥ utpattiḥ yatas tad bījam iti arthaḥ tad uccheda hetum darśayati tasyāḥ ca iti idānīm asya śāstrasya sarva anugraha artham pravṛttasya tadvidhena eva śāstreṇa sādṛśyam darśayati yathā iti catvāraḥ vyūhāḥ saṃkṣipta avayava racanā yasya tat tathā uktam nanu duḥkham heyam uktvā saṃsāram heyam abhidadhataḥ kutas na virodhaḥ iti atas āha tatra duḥkha bahulaḥ iti yat kṛtvā avidyā saṃsāram karoti tat asyāḥ avāntara vyāpāram saṃsāra hetum āha pradhāna puruṣayoḥ iti mokṣa svarūpam āha saṃyogasya iti mokṣa upāyam āha hāna upāyaḥ iti kecid paśyanti hātuḥ svarūpa ucchedaḥ eva mokṣaḥ yathā āhuḥ pradīpasya iva nirvāṇam vimokṣaḥ tasya cetasaḥ iti 
TV_2.15.10	 anye tu sa vāsana kleśa samucchedāt viśuddha vijñāna utpādaḥ eva mokṣaḥ iti ācakṣate tān pratyāha tatra iti tatra hānam tāvat dūṣayati hāne tasya iti na hi prekṣāvān kaścid ātma ucchedāya yatate nanu dṛśyante tīvra gada unmūlita sakala sukhām duḥkha mayīm iva mūrtim udvahantaḥ sva ucchedāya yatamānāḥ satyam kecid eva te na tu evam saṃsāriṇaḥ vividha vicitra deva ādi ānanda bhoga bhāginaḥ te api ca mokṣamāṇā dṛśyante tasmāt apuruṣa artha tva prasakteḥ na hātuḥ svarūpa ucchedaḥ mokṣaḥ abhyupeyaḥ astu tarhi hātuḥ sva rūpam upādeyam iti atas āha upādāne ca hetuvādaḥ upādāne hi kāryatvena anitya tve sati mokṣa tvāt eva cyaveta amṛta tvam hi mokṣaḥ na api viśuddhaḥ vijñāna saṃtānaḥ bhavati amṛtaḥ saṃtānibhyaḥ vyatiriktasya saṃtānasya vastu sataḥ abhāvāt saṃtāninām ca anitya tvāt tasmāt tathā yatitavyam yathā śāśvata vādaḥ bhavati tathā ca puruṣa artha tāpa vargasya iti āha ubhaya pratyākhyānaḥ iti tasmāt svarūpa avasthānam eva ātmanaḥ mokṣaḥ iti etat eva samyak darśanam 
TV_2.16.1–2.17.2^1	 heyam duḥkham anāgatam tat etat śāstram catur vyūham iti abhidhīyate heyam duḥkham anāgatam anāgatam iti atīta vartamāne vyavacchinne tatra upapattim āha duḥkham atītam iti nanu vartamānam upabhujyamānam na bhogena ativāhitam iti kasmāt na heyam iti atas āha vartamānam ca iti sugamam draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ heyam uktam tasya nidānam ucyate draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ draṣṭuḥ svarūpam āha draṣṭā iti citi= chāyā āpattiḥ eva buddheḥ buddhi pratisaṃvedi tvam udāsīnasya api puṃsaḥ nanu etāvatā api buddhiḥ eva anena dṛśyeta na dṛśyeran śabda ādayaḥ atyanta vyavahitāḥ iti atas āha dṛśyā buddhi sattva iti indriya praṇālikayā buddhau śabda ādi ākāreṇa pariṇatāyām dṛśyāyām bhavanti śabda ādayaḥ api dharmāḥ dṛśyāḥ iti arthaḥ nanu tad ākāra āpattyā buddhiḥ śabda ādi ākārā bhavatu puṃsaḥ tu buddhi saṃbandhe abhyupagamyamāne pariṇāmi tvam asaṃbandhe vā katham teṣām buddhi sattva upārūḍhānām api śabda ādīnām dṛśya tvam 
TV_2.17.2^2	 na hi dṛśinā saṃspṛṣṭam dṛśyam dṛṣṭam iti atas āha tat etat dṛśyam iti prapañcitam idam asmābhiḥ prathama pādaḥ eva yathā cityā saṃpṛktam api buddhi sattvam atyanta svaccha tayā citi bimba udgrāhitayā samāpanna caitanyam iva śabda ādi anubhavati iti atas eva ca śabda ādi ākāra pariṇata buddhi sattva upanītān śabda ādīn bhuñjānaḥ svāmī bhavati draṣṭā tādṛśam ca asya buddhi sattvam svam bhavati tat etat buddhi sattvam śabda ādi ākāra vat dṛśyam ayaskānta maṇi kalpam puruṣasya svam bhavati dṛśi rūpasya svāminaḥ 
TV_2.17.2^3	 kasmāt anubhava karma viṣaya tām āpannam yatas anubhavaḥ bhogaḥ puruṣasya karma kriyā tat viṣaya tām bhujyamāna tām āpannam yasmāt atas svam bhavati nanu svayaṃprakāśam buddhi sattvam katham anubhava viṣayaḥ iti atas āha anya svarūpeṇa iti yadi hi caitanya rūpam vastutas buddhi sattvam syāt bhavet svayaṃprakāśam kim tu svam caitanyāt anyat jaḍa rūpam tena pratilabdha ātmakam tasmāt tad anubhava viṣayaḥ nanu yasya hi yatra kiṃcid āyatate tat tad adhīnam na ca buddhi sattvasya puruṣam udāsīnam prati kiṃcid āyatate iti katham tat tantram 
TV_2.17.2^4–2.17.3	 tathā ca na tasya karma iti atas āha svatantram api para artha tvāt puruṣa artha tvāt paratantram puruṣa tantram nanu ayam dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ saṃbandhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ vā syāt naimittikaḥ vā svābhāvika tve saṃbandhinoḥ nitya tvāt aśakyocchedaḥ saṃbandhaḥ tathā ca saṃsāra nitya tvam naimittika tve tu kleśa karma tadvāsanānām antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti tayā sati antaḥkaraṇe bhāvāt antaḥkaraṇasya ca tad nimitta tve paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt anādi tvasya ca sarga ādau asaṃbhavāt anutpādaḥ eva saṃsārasya syāt yathā uktam pumān akartā yeṣām tu teṣām api guṇaiḥ kriyā katham ādau bhavet tatra karma tāvat na vidyate mithyājñānam na tatra asti rāga dveṣa ādayaḥ api vā manaḥ vṛttiḥ hi sarveṣām na ca utpannam manaḥ tadā 
TV_2.17.4^1	 iti śaṅkām apanayati tayoḥ dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ anādiḥ artha kṛtaḥ saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ satyam na svābhāvikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ naimittikaḥ tu na ca evam ādimān anādi nimitta prabhava tayā tasya api anādi tvāt kleśa karma tadvāsanā saṃtānaḥ ca ayam anādiḥ pratisarga avasthāyām ca saha antaḥkaraṇena pradhāna sāmyam upagataḥ api sarga ādau punar tādṛś eva prādurbhavati varṣa apāyaḥ iva udbhijja bhedaḥ mṛd bhāvam upagataḥ api punar varṣāsu pūrva rūpaḥ iti asakṛt āveditam prāc bhāvitayā saṃyogasya avidyā kāraṇam sthiti hetu tayā puruṣa arthaḥ kāraṇam tad vaśena tasya sthiteḥ tat idam uktam artha kṛtaḥ iti tathā ca uktam pañcaśikhena tad saṃyogaḥ buddhi saṃyogaḥ saḥ eva hetuḥ duḥkhasya tasya vivarjanāt syāt ayam ātyantikaḥ duḥkha pratīkāraḥ arthāt tad aparivarjane duḥkham iti uktam bhavati tatra eva atyanta prasiddham nidarśanam āha tat yathā iti 
TV_2.17.4^2	 pāda trāṇam upānat syāt etat guṇa saṃyogaḥ tāpa hetuḥ iti ucyamāne guṇānām tāpaka tvam abhyupetam na ca tapikriyāyāḥ asti ādeḥ iva kartṛ sthaḥ bhāvaḥ yena tapyam anyat na apekṣeta na ca asyāḥ tapyatayā puruṣaḥ karma tasya apariṇāmi tayā kriyā janita phala śāli tva ayogāt tasmāt tapeḥ tapya vyāptasya tad nivṛttau nivṛttim avagacchāmaḥ jvalana viraheṇa iva dhūma abhāvam iti atas āha atra api tāpakasya iti guṇānām eva tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ tatra mṛdu tvāt pāda tala vat sattvam tapyam rajaḥ tu tīvra tayā tāpakam pṛcchati kasmāt sattvam eva tapyam na tu puruṣaḥ uttaram tapikriyāyāḥ iti tat kim idānīm puruṣaḥ na tapyate tathā ca acetanasya astu sattvasya tāpaḥ kim naḥ chinnam iti atas āha darśita viṣaya tvāt sattve tu tapyamāne tad ākāra anurodhī puruṣaḥ api anutapyate iti darśita viṣaya tvam anutāpa hetuḥ tat ca prāk vyākhyātam 
TV_2.18.1–2.18.3	 prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīlam bhūta indriya ātmakam bhoga apavarga artham dṛśyam prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīlam bhūta indriya ātmakam bhoga apavarga artham dṛśyam vyācaṣṭe prakāśa iti sattvasya hi bhāgaḥ prakāśaḥ tāmasena bhāgena dainyena vā rājasena vā duḥkhena anurajyate evam rāja sa ādiṣu api draṣṭavyam tat idam uktam paraspara uparakta pravibhāgāḥ iti puruṣeṇa saha saṃyoga viyoga dharmāṇaḥ yathāmnāyate ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām bahvīḥ prajāḥ sṛjamānām sarūpāḥ ajaḥ hi ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ anyaḥ iti 
TV_2.18.4^1	 itaretara upāśrayeṇa upārjitā mūrtiḥ pṛthivī ādi rūpāḥ yaiḥ te tathā uktāḥ syāt etat sattvena śānta pratyaye janayitavye rajaḥ tamasoḥ api sattva aṅga tvena tatra hetu bhāvāt asti sāmarthyam iti yadā api ca rajaḥ tamasoḥ aṅgi tvam tadā api śāntaḥ eva pratyayaḥ udīyeta na ghoraḥ mūḍhaḥ vā sattva prādhānyaḥ iva iti atas āha paraspara aṅga aṅgi tve api asaṃbhinna śakti pravibhāgāḥ bhavatu śānte pratyaye janayitavye rajaḥ tamasoḥ aṅga bhāvaḥ tathā api na eṣām śaktayaḥ saṃkīryante kārya asaṃkara unneyaḥ hi śaktīnām asaṃkaraḥ 
TV_2.18.4^2	 asaṃkīrṇena ca samudācaratā rūpeṇa śānta ghora mūḍha rūpāṇi kāryāṇi dṛśyante iti siddham śaktīnām asaṃbhedaḥ iti syāt etat asaṃbhedaḥ ced śaktīnām na saṃbhūyakāri tvam guṇānām na jātu bhinna śaktīnām saṃbhūyakāri tvam dṛṣṭam na hi tantu mṛd piṇḍa vīraṇa ādīni ghaṭa ādīn saṃbhūya kurvataḥ iti atas āha tulya jātīya atulya jātīya śakti bheda anupātinaḥ yadi api tulya jātīyaḥ upādāna śaktiḥ na anyatra sahakāri śaktiḥ tu atulya jātīye paṭe tu janayitavye na vīraṇānām asti sahakāri śaktiḥ api iti na taiḥ tantūnām saṃbhūyakāritā iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_2.18.4^3	 tulya jātīya atulya jātīyeṣu śakyeṣu ye śakti bhedāḥ tān anupatitum śīlam yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ pradhāna velāyām iti divya śarīre janayitavye sattva guṇaḥ pradhānam aṅge rajaḥ tamasī evam manuṣya śarīre janayitavye rajaḥ pradhānam aṅge sattva tamasī evam tiryak śarīre janayitavye tamaḥ pradhānam aṅge sattva rajasī tena ete guṇāḥ pradhāna tva velāyām upadarśita saṃnidhānāḥ kārya upajananam pratyudbhūta vṛttayaḥ iti arthaḥ pradhāna śabdaḥ ca bhāva pradhānaḥ yathā dvi ekayoḥ dvivacana eka vacane iti atra dvi tva eka tvayoḥ iti anyathā dvi ekeṣu iti syāt nanu tadā pradhānam udbhūta tayā śakyam asti iti vaktum anudbhūtānām tu tad aṅgānām sadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti atas āha guṇa tve api ca iti yadi api na udbhūtāḥ tathā api guṇānām aviveki tvāt saṃbhūyakāri tvāt ca vyāpāra mātreṇa sahakāritayā pradhāne antarṇītam sat anumitam astitvam yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ nanu santu guṇāḥ saṃbhūyakāriṇaḥ samarthāḥ kasmāt punar kurvanti na hi samartham iti eva kāryam janayati 
TV_2.18.4^4	 mā bhūt asya kārya upajananam prati virāmaḥ iti atas āha puruṣa artha kartavyatayā iti tatas nirvartita nikhila puruṣa arthānām guṇānām uparamaḥ kārya anārambhaṇam iti uktam bhavati nanu puruṣasya anupakurvataḥ katham puruṣa arthena prayujyate iti atas āha saṃnidhi mātrā iti nanu dharma adharma lakṣaṇam eva nimittam prayojakam guṇānām tat kim ucyate puruṣa artha prayuktāḥ iti atas āha pratyayam antareṇa iti ekatamasya sattvasya rajasaḥ tamasaḥ vā pradhānasya sva kārye pravṛttasya vṛttim itare pratyayam nimittam dharma ādikam vinā eva anuvartamānāḥ 
TV_2.18.4^5	 yathā ca vakṣyati nimittam aprayojakam prakṛtīnām varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas kṣetrika vat iti ete guṇāḥ pradhāna śabda vācyāḥ bhavanti iti saṃbandhaḥ pradhīyate ādhīyate viśvam kāryam ebhiḥ iti vyutpattya etat dṛśyam ucyate tat evam guṇānām śīlam abhidhāya tasya kāryam āha tat etat iti satkārya vāda siddhau yat yad ātmakam tat tena rūpeṇa pariṇamate iti bhūta indriya ātmaka tvam dīpayati bhūta bhāvena ityādinā bhoga apavarga artham iti sūtra avayavam avatārayati tat tu na aprayojanam api tu prayojanam urarīkṛtya pravartate 
TV_2.18.4^6	 bhogam vivṛṇoti tatra iti sukha duḥkhe hi triguṇāyāḥ buddheḥ svarūpe tasyāḥ tathā tvena pariṇāmāt tathā api guṇa gatatayā avadhāraṇe na bhogaḥ iti atas āha avibhāga āpannam iti etat ca asakṛt vivecitam apavargam vivṛṇoti bhoktuḥ iti apavṛjyate anena iti apavargaḥ prayojana antarasya abhāvam āha dvayoḥ iti tathā ca uktam pañcaśikhena  ayam tu khalu iti nanu vastutas bhoga apavargau buddhi kṛtau buddhi vartinau ca katham tat akāraṇe tad andhi karaṇe ca puruṣe vyapadiśyete iti atas āha tau etau iti bhoktṛ tvam ca puruṣasya upapāditam agre ca vakṣyate paramārthataḥ tu buddheḥ eva puruṣa artha aparisamāptiḥ iti etena bhoga apavargayoḥ puruṣa saṃbandhi tva kathana mārgeṇa grahaṇa ādayaḥ api puruṣa saṃbandhinaḥ veditavyāḥ tatra sva rūpa mātreṇa artha jñānam grahaṇam tatra smṛtiḥ dhāraṇam tad gatānām viśeṣāṇām ūhanam ūhaḥ samāropitānām ca yuktyā apanayaḥ apohaḥ tābhyām eva ūha apohābhyām tad avadhāraṇam tattva jñānam tattva avadhāraṇa pūrvam hāna upādāna jñānam abhiniveśaḥ 
TV_2.19.1–2.19.2^1	 viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātra aliṅgāni guṇa parvāṇi dṛśyānām guṇānām svarūpa bheda avadhāraṇa artham idam ārabhyate viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātra aliṅgāni guṇa parvāṇi yeṣām aviśeṣāṇām śānta ghora mūḍha lakṣaṇa viśeṣa rahitānām ye viśeṣāḥ vikārāḥ eva na tu tattva antara prakṛtayaḥ teṣām tān āha tatra ākāśa iti utpāda krama anurūpaḥ eva upanyāsa kramaḥ asmitā lakṣaṇasya aviśeṣasya sattva pradhānasya buddhīndriyāṇi viśeṣāḥ rājasasya karmendiyāṇi manaḥ tu ubhaya ātmakam ubhaya pradhānasya iti mantavyam atra ca pañca tanmātrāṇi buddhi kāraṇakāni aviśeṣa tvāt asmitā vat iti vikāra hetu tvam ca aviśeṣa tvam tanmātreṣu ca asmitāyām ca aviśiṣṭam 
TV_2.19.2^2	 saṃkalayya viśeṣān parigaṇayati guṇānām eṣaḥ iti aviśeṣān api gaṇayati ṣaṣ iti saṃkalayya udāharati tat yathā iti viśiṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa iti gandhaḥ ātmanā pañca lakṣaṇaḥ rasaḥ ātmanā catur lakṣaṇaḥ rūpam ātmanā tri lakṣaṇam sparśaḥ ātmanā dvi lakṣaṇaḥ śabdaḥ śabda lakṣaṇaḥ eva iti kasya punar amī ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ kāryam iti atas āha ete sattā mātrasya ātmanaḥ iti puruṣa artha kriyā kṣamam sat tasya bhāvaḥ sattā tanmātram tat mahat tattvam yāvatī kācid puruṣa artha kriyā śabda ādi bhoga lakṣaṇā sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti lakṣaṇā vā asti sā sarvāḥ mahati buddhau samāpyate iti arthaḥ 
TV_2.19.2^3	 ātmanaḥ iti svarūpa upadarśanena tuccha tvam niṣedhati prakṛteḥ ayam ādyaḥ pariṇāmaḥ vāstavaḥ na tu tad vivarte iti yāvat yat tat param viprakṛṣṭa kālam aviśeṣebhyaḥ tad apekṣayā saṃnikṛṣṭa kālebhyaḥ liṅga mātram mahat tattvam tasmin ete ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ sattā mātre mahati ātmani avasthāya satkārya vāda siddheḥ vivṛddhi kāṣṭhām anubhavanti prāpnuvanti ye punar aviśeṣāṇām viśeṣa pariṇāmāḥ teṣām ca dharma lakṣaṇa avasthāḥ pariṇāmāḥ iti sā iyam eṣām vivṛddhi kāṣṭhā pariṇāma kāṣṭha iti 
TV_2.19.2^4	 tat evam utpatti kramam abhidhāya pralaya kramam āha pratisaṃsṛjyamānāḥ pralīyamānāḥ sva ātmani līna viśeṣāḥ aviśeṣāḥ tasmin eva sattā mātre mahati ātmani avasthāya vilīya saha eva mahatā te aviśeṣāḥ avyaktam anyatra layam na gacchati iti aliṅgam pratiyanti tasya eva viśeṣaṇam niḥsattā sattam sattā puruṣa artha kriyā kṣama tvam asattā tucchatā niṣkrāntam sattāyāḥ asattāyāḥ ca yat tat tathā uktam etat uktam bhavati sattva rajaḥ tamasām sāmya avasthā na kvacid puruṣa arthaḥ upayujyate iti na satī na api gagana kamalinī iva tuccha svabhāvā tena na asati api iti syāt etat 
TV_2.19.2^5	 avyakta avasthāyām api asti mahat ādi tad ātmanā na hi sataḥ vināśaḥ vināśe vā na punar utpādaḥ na hi asataḥ utpādaḥ iti mahat ādi sadbhāvāt puruṣa artha kriyā pravarteta tat katham niḥsattvam avyaktam iti atas āha niḥsadasat iti niṣkrāntam kāraṇam sataḥ kāryāt yadi api kāraṇa avasthāyām sat eva śakti ātmanā kāryam tathā api sva ucitām artha kriyām akurvat asat iti uktam na ca etat kāraṇam śaśa viṣāṇāyamāna kāryam iti āha nirasat iti niṣkrāntam asataḥ tuccha rūpāt kāryāt tathā sati hi vyoma aravindam iva asmān na kāryam utpadyeta iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_2.19.2^6	 pratisargam uktam upasaṃharati eṣa teṣām iti eṣaḥ iti anantara uktāt pūrvasya parāmarśaḥ liṅga mātra ādi avasthāḥ puruṣa artha kṛta tvāt anityā aliṅga avasthā tu puruṣa arthena akṛta tvāt nitya iti atra hetum āha aliṅga avasthāyām iti kasmāt punar na puruṣa arthaḥ hetuḥ iti atas āha na āliṅga avasthāyām iti bhavatinā viṣayeṇa viṣayi jñānam upalakṣayati etat uktam bhavati evam hi puruṣa artha tā kāraṇam aliṅga avasthāyām jñāyeta yadi aliṅga avasthā śabda ādi upabhogam vā sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyātim vā puruṣa artham nirvartayet tad nirvartane hi na sāmya avasthā syāt 
TV_2.19.2^7	 tasmāt puruṣa artha kāraṇa tvam asyām na jñāyate iti na asyāḥ puruṣa artha tāḥ hetuḥ upasaṃharati na asau iti itiḥ tasmāt arthe anityām avasthām āha trayāṇām liṅga mātrā viśeṣa viśeṣāṇām iti parva svarūpam darśayitvā guṇa svarūpam āha guṇāḥ tu iti nidarśanam āha yathā devadattaḥ iti yatra atyanta bhinnānām gavām upacaya apacayau devadatta upacaya apacaya hetū tatra kā eva kathā guṇebhyaḥ bhinna abhinnānām vyaktīnām upajana apāyayoḥ iti arthaḥ nanu sarga kramaḥ kim aniyataḥ na iti āha liṅga mātram iti 
TV_2.19.2^8	 na khalu nyagrodhadhānāḥ ahnāya eva nyagrodha śākhinam sāndra śādvala dala jaṭila śākhā kāṇḍa nipīta mārtaṇḍa caṇḍa ātapa maṇḍalam ārabhante kim tu kṣiti salila tejaḥ saṃparkāt paramparayā upajāyamāna aṅkura patra kāṇḍa nāla ādi krameṇa evam iha api yukti āgama siddhaḥ kramaḥ āstheya iti katham bhūta indriyāṇi aviśeṣa saṃsṛṣṭāni iti atas āha tathā ca uktam purastāt idam eva sūtram prathamam vyācakṣāṇaiḥ atha viśeṣāṇām kasmāt na tattva antara pariṇāmaḥ uktaḥ iti atas āha na viśeṣebhyaḥ iti tat kim idānīm apariṇāminaḥ eva viśeṣāḥ tathā ca nityāḥ prasajyeran iti atas āha teṣām tu iti 
TV_2.20.1–2.20.2^1	 draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhaḥ api pratyaya anupaśyaḥ vyākhyātam dṛśyam draṣṭuḥ svarūpa avadhāraṇa artham idam ārabhyate draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhaḥ api pratyaya anupaśyaḥ vyācaṣṭe dṛśi mātraḥ iti viśeṣaṇāni dharmāḥ taiḥ aparāmṛṣṭāḥ tat anena mātra grahaṇasya tātparyam darśitam syāt etat yadi sarva viśeṣaṇa rahitā dṛś śaktiḥ na tarhi śabda ādayaḥ dṛśyeran na hi dṛśinā saṃspṛṣṭam dṛśyam bhavati iti atas āha sa puruṣaḥ iti buddhi darpaṇe puruṣa pratibimba saṃkrāntiḥ eva buddhi pratisaṃvedi tvam puṃsaḥ tathā ca dṛśi= chāyā āpannayāḥ buddhyā saṃsṛṣṭāḥ śabda ādayaḥ bhavanti dṛśyāḥ iti arthaḥ syāt etat pāramārthikam eva buddhi caitanyayoḥ kasmāt aikyam na upeyate kim anayā tad chāyā āpattyā iti atas āha sa buddheḥ na sarūpaḥ iti tathā asarūpasya tad chāyā āpattiḥ api durghaṭa iti atas āha na atyantam virūpaḥ iti tatra sārūpyam niṣedhati na tāvat iti 
TV_2.20.2^2	 hetum pṛcchati kasmāt sa hetukam vairūpye hetum āha jñātā iti pariṇāminī buddhiḥ yasmāt tasmāt virūpāḥ yadā khalu iyam śabda ādi ākārā bhavati tadā jñātaḥ asyāḥ śabda ādi lakṣaṇaḥ bhavati viṣaya s tad anākāra tve tu ajñātaḥ tathā ca kadācid eva tat ākāra tām dadhatī pariṇāminī iti prayogaḥ ca bhavati buddhiḥ pariṇāminī jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvāt śrotra ādi vat iti tad vaidharmyam puruṣasya tad viparītāt dhetoḥ sidhyati iti āha sadā iti syāt etat sadā ajñāta viṣayaḥ ced puruṣaḥ na tarhi kevalī syāt iti āśayavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti uttaram na hi buddhiḥ ca nāma iti buddhi agrahaṇayoḥ asti saha saṃbhavaḥ nirodha avasthāyām atas ukta virodha sūcanāya puruṣa viṣayaḥ ca iti tena ādyaḥ cakāraḥ buddhim viṣaya tvena samuccinoti pariśiṣṭau tu virodha dyotakau cakārau iti 
TV_2.20.2^3	 prayogaḥ tu puruṣaḥ apariṇāmī sadā asaṃprajñāta vyutthāna avasthayoḥ jñāta viṣaya tvāt yaḥ tu pariṇāmī na asau sadā ajñāta viṣayaḥ yathā śrotra ādiḥ iti vyatirekī hetuḥ aparam api vaidharmyam āha kim ca parārtha iti buddhiḥ khalu kleśa karma vāsanā ādibhiḥ viṣaya indriya ādibhiḥ ca saṃhatya puruṣa artham abhinirvartayantī para arthāḥ prayogaḥ ca para arthā buddhiḥ saṃhatyakāri tvāt śayana āsana abhyaṅga vat iti puruṣaḥ tu na tathā iti āha sva arthaḥ puruṣaḥ iti sarvam puruṣāya kalpate puruṣaḥ tu na kasmaicid iti arthaḥ vaidharmya antaram āha sarva iti sarvān arthān śānta ghora mūḍhān tad ākāra pariṇatā buddhiḥ adhyavasyati sattva rajaḥ tamasām ca ete pariṇāmāḥ iti siddhā triguṇā buddhiḥ iti na ca evam puruṣaḥ iti āha guṇānām iti tad pratibimbitaḥ paśyati na tu tad ākāra pariṇataḥ iti arthaḥ upasaṃharati atas iti 
TV_2.20.2^4	 astu tarhi virūpaḥ iti na atyantam virūpaḥ kasmāt yatas śuddhaḥ api pratyaya anupaśyaḥ yathā ca etat tathā uktam vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra iti atra tathā ca uktam pañcaśikhena apariṇāminī hi bhoktṛ śaktiḥ ātmā atas eva buddhau apratisaṃkramā ca pariṇāmini buddhi rūpe arthe saṃkrāntā iva tad vṛttim buddhi vṛttim anupatati nanu asaṃkrāntā katham saṃkrāntā iva katham vā vṛttim vinā anupatati iti atas āha tasyāḥ ca iti prāptaḥ caitanya upagrahaḥ uparāgaḥ yena rūpeṇa tat tathā prāpta caitanya upagraham rūpam yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā etat uktam bhavati yathā nirmale jale asaṃkrāntaḥ api candramāḥ saṃkrānta pratibimba tayā saṃkrāntaḥ iva evam atra api asaṃkrāntā api saṃkrānta pratibimbā citi śaktiḥ saṃkrāntā iva tena buddhi ātma tvam āpannā buddhi vṛttim anupatati iti tat anena anupaśyaḥ iti vyākhyātam tām anukāreṇa paśyati iti anupaśyaḥ iti 
TV_2.21.1–2.21.2^1	 tad arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ svarūpam uktvā sva svāmi lakṣaṇa saṃbandha aṅgam dṛśyasya draṣṭṛ artha tvam āha tad arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā vyācaṣṭe dṛśi rūpasya puruṣasya bhoktuḥ karma rūpa tām bhogya tām āpannam dṛśyam iti tasmāt tad arthaḥ eva draṣṭṛ arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā bhavati na tu dṛśya arthaḥ nanu na ātma ātmā arthaḥ iti atas āha svarūpam bhavati iti etat uktam bhavati sukha duḥkha ātmakam dṛśyam bhogyam sukha duḥkhe ca anukūlayitṛ pratikūlayitṛṇī tattvena tad arthe eva vyavatiṣṭhete viṣayāḥ api hi śabda ādayaḥ tādātmyāt eva ca anukūlayitāraḥ pratikūlayitāraḥ ca na ca ātmā eva eṣām anukūlanīyaḥ pratikūlanīyaḥ ca sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt atas pāriśeṣyāt citi śaktiḥ eva anukūlanīyā pratikūlanīyā ca 
TV_2.21.2^2	 tasmāt tad artham eva dṛśyam na tu dṛśya artham atas ca tad arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā na dṛśya arthaḥ yat sva rūpam asya yāvat puruṣa artham anuvartate nirvartite ca puruṣa arthe nivartate iti āha sva rūpam iti svarūpam tu dṛśyasya jaḍam para rūpeṇa ātma rūpeṇa caitanyena pratilabdha ātmakam anubhūta svarūpam bhoga apavarga artha tāyām kṛtāyām puruṣeṇa na dṛśyate bhogaḥ sukha ādi ākāraḥ śabda ādi anubhavaḥ apavargaḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā anubhavaḥ tat ca etat ubhayam api ājānataḥ jaḍāyāḥ buddheḥ puruṣa= chāyāpattyā iti puruṣasya eva tathā ca puruṣa bhoga apavargayoḥ kṛtayoḥ dṛśyasya bhoga apavarga artha tā samāpyate iti bhoga apavarga artha tāyām kṛtāyām iti uktam atra antare codayati svarūpa hānāt iti pariharati na tu vinaśyati iti 
TV_2.22.1–2.22.2^1	 kṛtārtham prati naṣṭam api anaṣṭam tad anya sādhāraṇa tvāt nanu atyantān upalabhyam katham na vinaśyati iti āśayavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti sūtreṇa uttaram āha kṛtārtham prati naṣṭam api anaṣṭam tad anya sādhāraṇa tvāt kṛtaḥ arthaḥ yasya puruṣasya sa tathā tam prati naṣṭam api anaṣṭam tat dṛśyam kutas sarvān puruṣān kuśalān akuśalān prati sādhāraṇa tvāt vyācaṣṭe kṛtārtham ekam iti nāśaḥ adarśanam anaṣṭam tu dṛśyam anya puruṣa sādhāraṇa tvāt 
TV_2.22.1–2.22.2^2	 tasmāt dṛśyāt parasya ātmanaḥ caitanyam rūpam tena tat iha śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇa prasiddham avyaktam anavayavam ekam anāśrayam vyāpi nityam viśva kārya śaktimat yadi api kuśalena tam prati kṛta kāryam na dṛśyate tathā api akuśalena dṛśyamānam na na asti na hi rūpam andhena na dṛśyate iti cakṣuṣmatā api dṛśyamānam abhāva prāptam bhavati na ca pradhāna vat ekaḥ eva puruṣaḥ tad nānātvasya janma maraṇa sukha duḥkha upabhoga mukti saṃsāra vyavasthayā siddheḥ eka tva śrutīnām ca pramāṇa antara virodhāt kathaṃcid deśa kāla vibhāga abhāvena bhaktyā api upapatteḥ prakṛti ekatva puruṣa nānā tvayoḥ ca śrutyā eva sākṣāt pratipādanāt 
TV_2.22.3–2.22.4	 ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām bahvīḥ prajāḥ sṛjamānām sarūpāḥ ajaḥ hi ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ anyaḥ iti śrutiḥ asyāḥ eva śruteḥ ca anena sūtreṇa arthaḥ anūditaḥ iti yatas dṛśyam naṣṭam api anaṣṭam puruṣa antaram prati asti atas dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ nitya tvāt anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ vyākhyātaḥ atra eva āgaminām anumatim āha tathā ca uktam iti dharmiṇām guṇānām ātmabhiḥ anādi saṃyogāt dharma mātrāṇām mahat ādīnām api anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ iti ekaikasya mahat ādeḥ saṃyogaḥ anādiḥ api anityaḥ eva yadi api tathā api sarveṣām mahat ādīnām nityaḥ puruṣa antarāṇām sādhāraṇa tvāt atas uktam dharma mātrāṇām iti mātra grahaṇena vyāptim gamayati atas etat bhavati yadi api ekasya mahataḥ saṃyogaḥ atītatām āpannaḥ tathā api mahat antarasya puruṣa antareṇa saṃyogaḥ na atītaḥ iti nityaḥ uktaḥ 
TV_2.23.1–2.23.2^1	 sva svāmi śaktyoḥ svarūpa upalabdhi hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ tat evam tādarthye saṃyoga kāraṇaḥ ukte prāsaṅgike pradhāna nitya tve saṃyoga sāmānya nitya tve hetau ca ukte saṃyogasya yat sva rūpam asādhāraṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti yāvat tad abhidhitsayā idam sūtram pravavṛte sva svāmi śaktyoḥ svarūpa upalabdhi hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ yatas dṛśyam tad artham atas tat janitam upakāram bhajamānaḥ puruṣaḥ tasya svāmī bhavati bhavati ca tat dṛśyam asya svam sa ca anayoḥ saṃyogaḥ śakti mātreṇa vyavasthitaḥ tad svarūpa upalabdhi hetuḥ tat etat bhāṣyam avadyotayati puruṣaḥ svāmī yogya tā mātreṇa dṛśyena svena yogya tayā eva darśana artham saṃyuktaḥ śeṣam sugamam syāt etat 
TV_2.23.2^2	 draṣṭuḥ svarūpa upalabdhiḥ apavṛjyate anena iti apavargaḥ uktaḥ na ca mokṣaḥ sādhanavān tathā sati ayam mokṣa tvāt eva cyaveta iti atas āha darśana kārya avasānaḥ buddhi viśeṣeṇa saha puruṣa viśeṣasya saṃyogaḥ iti darśanam viyoga kāraṇam uktam katham punar darśana kārya avasāna tvam saṃyogasya iti atas āha darśanam iti tatas kim iti atas āha adarśanam avidyā saṃyoga nimittam iti uktam uktam artham spaṣṭayati na atra iti nanu darśanam adarśanam virodhi nivartayatu bandhasya kutas nivṛttiḥ iti atas āha darśanasya iti buddhi ādi viviktasya ātmanaḥ svarūpa avasthānam mokṣaḥ uktaḥ na tasya sādhanam darśanam api tu adarśana nivṛtteḥ iti arthaḥ asādhāraṇam saṃyoga hetum adarśana viśeṣam grahītum adarśana mātram vikalpayati kim ca idam iti 
TV_2.23.2^3	 paryudāsam gṛhītvā āha kim guṇānām adhikāraḥ kārya ārambhaṇa sāmarthyam tatas hi saṃyogaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ upajāyate prasajya pratiṣedham gṛhītvā dvitīyam vikalpam āha āhosvit iti darśitaḥ viṣayaḥ śabda ādiḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā ca yena cittena tasya tad viṣayasya anutpādaḥ etat eva sphorayati svasmin dṛśye śabda ādau sattva puruṣa anyatāyām ca iti tāvat eva pradhānam viceṣṭate na yāvat dvividham darśanam abhinirvartayati niṣpādita ubhaya darśanam tu nivartate iti paryudāsaḥ eva tṛtīyam vikalpam āha kim arthavat tā guṇānām satkārya vāda siddhau hi bhāvinau api bhoga apavarga arthau avyapadeśya tayā staḥ iti arthaḥ paryudāsaḥ eva caturtham vikalpam āha atha avidyā pratisarga kāle sva cittena saha niruddhā pradhāna sāmyam āgatāḥ vāsanā rūpeṇa sva citta utpatti bījam 
TV_2.23.2^4	 tena darśanāt anya avidyā vāsanā eva adarśanam uktāḥ paryudāsaḥ eva pañcamam vikalpam āha kim sthiti saṃskārasya pradhāna vartinaḥ sāmya pariṇāma paramparā vahinaḥ kṣaye gatiḥ mahat ādi vikāra ārambhaḥ tad hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ pradhānasya gati saṃskāraḥ tasya abhivyaktiḥ kārya unmukha tvam tad ubhaya saṃskāra sadbhāve mata antara anumatim āha yatra idam uktam aikāntika tvam vyāsedhadbhiḥ pradhīyate janyate vikāra jātam anena iti pradhānam tat ced sthityā eva varteta na kadācid gatyā tatas vikāra akaraṇāt na pradhīyate tena kiṃcid iti apradhānam syāt atha gatyā eva varteta na kadācid api sthityā tatra āha tathā gatyā eva iti kvacid pāṭhaḥ sthityai gatyai iti 
TV_2.23.2^5	 tādarthye caturthī eva kāraḥ ca draṣṭavyaḥ sthityai ced na varteta na kvacid vikāraḥ vinaśyet tathā ca bhāvasya sataḥ avināśinaḥ na utpattiḥ api iti vikāra tvāt eva cyaveta evam ca na pradhīyate atra kiṃcid iti apradhānam syāt tat ubhayathā sthityā gatyā ca asya vṛttiḥ pradhāna vyavahāram labhate na anyathā ekānta abhyupagame na kevalam pradhāne kāraṇa antareṣu api para brahma tanmāyā paramāṇu ādiṣu kalpiteṣu samānaḥ ca rcaḥ vicāraḥ tāni api hi sthityā eva vartamānāni vikāra akaraṇāt akāraṇāni syuḥ gatyā eva vartamānāni vikāra nitya tvāt akāraṇāni syuḥ iti ca paryudāsaḥ eva ṣaṣṭham vikalpam āha darśana śaktiḥ eva iti 
TV_2.23.2^6	 yathā prajāpativrate na īkṣeta udyantam ādityam iti anīkṣaṇa pratyāsannaḥ saṃkalpaḥ gṛhyate evam iha api darśana niṣedhe tad pratyāsannā tad mūlā śaktiḥ ucyate sā ca darśanam bhoga ādi lakṣaṇam prasotum draṣṭāram dṛśyena yojayati iti atra eva śrutim āha pradhānasya iti syāt etat ātma khyāpana artham pradhānam pravartate iti śrutiḥ āha na tu ātma darśana śakteḥ pravartate iti atas āha sarva bodhya bodha samarthaḥ iti prāk pravṛtteḥ pradhānasya na ātma khyāpana mātram pravṛttau prayojakam asāmarthye tad ayogāt tasmāt sāmarthyam pravṛtteḥ prayojakam iti śrutyā arthāt uktam iti arthaḥ darśana śaktiḥ pradhāna āśraya iti aṅgīkṛtya ṣaṣṭhaḥ kalpaḥ imām eva ubhaya āśrayām āsthāya saptamam vikalpam āha ubhayasya puruṣasya ca dṛśyasya ca adarśanam darśana śaktiḥ dharmaḥ iti eke 
TV_2.23.2^7	 syāt etat mṛṣyāmahe dṛśyasya iti tasya sarva śakti āśraya tvāt na draṣṭuḥ iti punar mṛṣyāmaḥ na hi tad ādhārā jñānaśaktiḥ tatra jñānasya asamavāyāt anyathā pariṇāma āpattiḥ iti atas āha tatra idam iti bhavatu dṛśya ātmakam tathā api tasya jaḍa tvena tad gata śakti kāryam darśanam api jaḍam iti na śakyam tad dharma tvena vijñātum jaḍasya svayam aprakāśa tvāt atas dṛśeḥ ātmanaḥ pratyayam caitanya= chāyā āpattim apekṣya darśanam tad dharma tvena bhavati jñāyate viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ lakṣaṇāt nanu etāvatā api dṛśya dharma tvam asya jñānasya bhavati na tu puruṣa dharma tvam api iti atas āha tathā puruṣasya iti 
TV_2.23.2^8	 satyam puruṣasya anātma bhūtam eva tathā api dṛśya buddhi sattvasya yaḥ pratyayaś caitanya= chāyā āpattiḥ tam apekṣya puruṣa dharma tvena iva na tu puruṣa dharma tvena etat uktam bhavati caitanya bimba udgrāhi tayā buddhi caitanyayoḥ abhedāt buddhi dharmāḥ caitanya dharmāḥ iva cakāsati iti aṣṭamam vikalpam āha darśanam jñānam eva śabda ādīnām adarśanam na tu sattva puruṣa anyatāyāḥ iti kecid yathā cakṣuḥ rūpe pramāṇam api rasa ādau apramāṇam ucyate etat uktam bhavati sukha ādi a ākāra śabda ādi jñānāni sva siddhi anuguṇa tayā draṣṭṛ dṛśya saṃyogam ākṣipanti iti tat evam vikalpya caturtham vikalpam svīkartum itareṣām vikalpānām sāṃkhya śāstra gatānām sarva puruṣa sādhāraṇyena bhoga vaicitrya abhāva prasaṅgena dūṣayati iti ete śāstra gatāḥ iti 
TV_2.24.1–2.24.2^1	 tasya hetuḥ avidyā caturtham vikalpam nirdhārayitum sūtram avatārayati yaḥ tu pratyak cetanasya sva buddhi saṃyogaḥ iti pratīpam añcati prāpnoti iti pratyak asādhāraṇaḥ tu saṃyogaḥ ekaikasya puruṣasya ekaikayā buddhyā vaicitrya hetuḥ sūtram paṭhati tasya iti nanu avidyā viparyaya jñānam tasya bhoga apavargayoḥ iva sva buddhi saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ asaṃyuktāyām buddhau tad anutpatteḥ tat katham avidyā saṃyoga bhedasya hetuḥ iti atas āha viparyaya jñāna vāsanā iti sarga antarīyāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ sva cittena saha niruddhāyāḥ api pradhāne asti vāsanā tad vāsanā vāsitam ca pradhānam tad tad puruṣa saṃyoginīm tādṛśīm eva buddhim sṛjati evam pūrva pūrva sargeṣu iti anādi tvāt adoṣaḥ atas eva pratisarga avasthāyām na puruṣaḥ mucyate iti āha viparyaya jñāna iti 
TV_2.24.2^2–2.24.3	 yadā puruṣa khyātim kārya niṣṭhām prāptā tadā viparyaya jñāna vāsanāyāḥ bandha kāraṇasya abhāvāt na punar āvartate iti āha sā tu iti atra kaścid nāstikaḥ kaivalyam paṇḍaka upākhyānena upahasati paṇḍaka upākhyānam āha mugdhayā iti kimartham iti artha śabdaḥ nimittam upalakṣayati prayojanasya api nimitta tvāt paṇḍaka upākhyānena sāmyam āpādayati tathā idam vidyamānam guṇa puruṣa anya tā jñānam citta nivṛttim na karoti para vairāgyeṇa jñāna prasāda mātreṇa sa saṃskāram niruddham vinaṣṭam kariṣyati iti kā pratyāśā yasmin sati eva yat bhavati tat tasya kāryam na tu yasmin asatī iti bhāvaḥ atra eka deśimatena parihāram āha tatra iti īṣat aparisamāptaḥ ācāryaḥ ācārya deśīyaḥ ācāryaḥ tu vāyu prokte kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ ācinoti ca śāstra artham ācāre sthāpayati api svayam ācarate yasmāt ācāryaḥ tena ca ucyate iti 
TV_2.24.4	 bhoga viveka khyāti rūpa pariṇata buddhi nivṛttiḥ eva mokṣaḥ na ca buddhi svarūpa nivṛttiḥ sā ca dharma megha anta viveka khyāti pratiṣṭhāyāḥ anantaram eva bhavati sati api buddhi svarūpa mātra avasthānaḥ iti arthaḥ etat eva sphorayati adarśanasya bandha kāraṇasya abhāvāt buddhi nivṛttiḥ tat ca adarśanam bandha kāraṇam darśanāt nivartate darśana nivṛttiḥ tu para vairāgya sādhyāḥ sati api buddhi svarūpa avasthāne mokṣaḥ iti bhāvaḥ eka deśi matam upanyasya sva matam āha tatra citta nivṛttiḥ eva mokṣaḥ nanu uktam darśane nivṛtte acirāt citta svarūpa nivṛttiḥ bhavati iti katham darśana kārya iti atas āha kimartham asthāne mati vibhramaḥ iti ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ yadi darśanasya sākṣāt citta nivṛttau kāraṇa bhāvam aṅgīkurvīmahi tatas evam upālabhyemahi kim tu viveka darśanam prakarṣa kāṣṭhām prāptam nirodha samādhi bhāvanā prakarṣa krameṇa citta nivṛttimat puruṣa svarūpa avasthāna upayogī iti ātiṣṭhāmahe tat katham upālabhyemahi iti 
TV_2.25.1–2.25.2	 tad abhāvāt saṃyoga abhāvaḥ hānam tat dṛśeḥ kaivalyam tat evam vyūha dvayam uktvā tṛtīya vyūha abhidhānāya sūtram avatārayti heyam duḥkham iti tad abhāvāt saṃyoga abhāvaḥ hānam tat dṛśeḥ kaivalyam vyācaṣṭe tasya iti asti hi mahāpralaye api saṃyoga abhāvaḥ atas uktam ātyantikaḥ iti duḥkha uparamaḥ hānam iti puruṣa artha tā darśitāḥ śeṣam ati rohitam
