TV_2.26.1–2.26.2	 viveka khyātiḥ aviplavāḥ hāna upāyaḥ hāna upāya lakṣaṇam caturtham vyūham ākhyātum sūtram avatārayati atha iti viveka khyātiḥ aviplavāḥ hāna upāyaḥ āgama anumānābhyām api viveka khyātiḥ asti na ca asau vyutthānam tad saṃskāram vā nivartayati tadvataḥ api tad anuvṛtteḥ iti tad nivṛtti artham aviplava iti viplavaḥ mithyājñānam tat rahitā etat uktam bhavati śruta mayena jñānena vivekam gṛhītvā yukti mayena ca vyavasthāpya dīrgha kāla nairantarya satkāra āsevitāyāḥ bhāvanāyāḥ prakarṣa paryantam samadhigatā sākṣātkāravatī viveka khyātiḥ nivartita savāsana mithyā jñānāḥ nirviplavāḥ hāna upāyaḥ iti śeṣam sugamam bhāṣyam 
TV_2.27.1–2.27.2^1	 tasya saptadhā prānta bhūmiḥ prajñā viveka khyāti niṣṭhāyāḥ svarūpam āha sūtreṇa tasya saptadhā prānta bhūmiḥ prajñā vyācaṣṭe tasya iti pratyudita khyāteḥ vartamāna khyāteḥ yoginaḥ pratyāmnāyaḥ parāmarśaḥ aśuddhiḥ eva āvaraṇam citta sattvasya tat eva malam tasya apagamāt cittasya pratyaya antara anutpāde tāmasa rāja sa vyutthāna pratyaya anutpāde nirviplava viveka khyāti niṣṭhām āpannasya sapta prakāra eva prajñā vivekinaḥ bhavati viṣaya bhedāt prajñā bhedaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ antaḥ yāsām bhūmīnām avasthānām tāḥ tathā uktāḥ yatas param na asti sa prakarṣaḥ prāntāḥ bhūmayaḥ yasyāḥ prajñāyāḥ viveka khyāteḥ sā tathā uktā tāḥ eva sapta prakārāḥ prānta bhūmīḥ udāharati tat yathā iti tatra puruṣa prayatna niṣpādyāsu catasṛṣu bhūmiṣu prathamām udāharati parijñātam heyam yāvat kila prādhānikam tat sarvam pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāraiḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāt duḥkham eva iti heyam tat parijñātam prānta tām darśayati na asya punar kiṃcid aparijñātam parijñeyam asti dvitīyām āha kṣīṇāḥ iti 
TV_2.27.2^2	 prānta tām āha na punar iti tṛtīyām āha sākṣātkṛtam pratyakṣeṇa niścitam mayā saṃprajñāta avasthāyām eva nirodha samādhi sādhyam hānam na punar asyāḥ param niścetavyam asti iti śeṣaḥ caturthīm āha bhāvitaḥ niṣpāditaḥ viveka khyāti rūpaḥ hāna upāyaḥ na asyāḥ param bhāvanīyam asti iti śeṣaḥ eṣā catuṣṭayī kāryā vimuktiḥ samāptiḥ kārya tayā prayatna vyāpya tā darśitāḥ kvacid pāṭhaḥ kārya vimuktiḥ iti kārya antareṇa vimuktiḥ prajñāyāḥ iti arthaḥ prayatna niṣpādya anuniṣpādanīyām aprayatna sādhyām citta vimuktim āha citta vimuktiḥ tu trayī prathamām āha carita adhikārā buddhiḥ kṛta bhoga apavarga kārya iti arthaḥ dvitīyām āha guṇāḥ iti prānta tām āha na ca eṣām iti tṛtīyām āha etasyām avasthāyām iti etasyām avasthāyām jīvan eva puruṣaḥ kuśalaḥ muktaḥ iti ucyate carama deha tvāt iti āha etām iti anaupacārikam muktam āha pratiprasave pradhāna laye api cittasya muktaḥ kuśalaḥ iti eva bhavati guṇa atīta tvāt iti 
TV_2.28.1–2.28.2^1	 yoga aṅga anuṣṭhānāt aśuddhi kṣaye jñāna dīptiḥ ā viveka khyāteḥ tat evam caturaḥ vyūhān uktvā tad madhya patitasya hāna upāyasya viveka khyāteḥ go dohana ādi vat prāc asiddheḥ asiddhasya ca upāyatva abhāvāt siddhi upāyān vaktum ārabhate iti āha siddhā iti tatra abhidhāsyamānānām sādhanānām yena prakāreṇa viveka khyāti upāya tvam tat darśayati sūtreṇa yoga aṅga anuṣṭhāṇāt aśuddhi kṣaye jñāna dīptiḥ ā viveka khyāteḥ yoga aṅgāni hi yathāyogam dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa dvāreṇa aśuddhim kṣiṇvanti pañcaparvaṇaḥ viparyayasya iti upalakṣaṇam puṇya apuṇyayoḥ api jāti āyuḥ bhoga hetu tvena aśuddhi rūpa tvāt iti śeṣam sugamam nānāvidhasya kāraṇa bhāvasya darśanāt yoga aṅga anuṣṭhānasya kīdṛśam kāraṇa tvam iti atas āha yoga aṅga anuṣṭhānam iti 
TV_2.28.2^2	 aśuddhyā viyojayati buddhi sattvam iti aśuddheḥ viyoga kāraṇam dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā paraśuḥ iti paraśuḥ chedyam vṛkṣam mūlena viyojayati aśuddhyā viyojayat buddhi sattvam viveka khyātim prāpayati yathā dharmaḥ sukham tathā yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam viveka khyāteḥ prāpti kāraṇam na anyena prakāreṇa iti āha viveka khyāteḥ tu iti na anyathā iti pratiṣedha śravaṇāt pṛcchati kati ca etāni iti uttaram navā eva iti tāni darśayati kārikayā tat yathā utpatti iti atra udāharaṇāni āha tatra utpatti kāraṇam iti manaḥ hi vijñānam avyapadeśya avasthātaḥ apanīya vartamāna avasthām āpādayat utpatti kāraṇam vijñānasya sthiti kāraṇam manasaḥ puruṣa artha tā 
TV_2.28.2^3	 asmitāyāḥ utpannam manaḥ tāvat avatiṣṭhate na yāvat dvividham puruṣa artham abhinirvartayati atha nirvartita puruṣa artha dvayam sthiteḥ apaiti tasmāt sva kāraṇāt utpannasya manasaḥ anāgata puruṣa artha tā sthiti kāraṇam dṛṣṭāntam āha śarīrasya iva iti pratyakṣa jñāna nimittam indriya dvārā vā svatas vā viṣayasya saṃskriya abhivyaktiḥ tasyāḥ kāraṇam yathā rūpasya ālokaḥ vikāra kāraṇam manasaḥ viṣaya antaram yathā hi mṛkaṇḍoḥ samāhita manasaḥ vallakī vipañcyamāna pañcama svara śravaṇa samanantaram unmīlita akṣasya svarūpa lāvaṇya yauvana saṃpannām apsarasam pramlocām īkṣamāṇasya samādhim apahāya tasyām saktam manaḥ babhūva iti 
TV_2.28.2^4	 atra eva nidarśanam āha yathā agniḥ pākyasya taṇḍula ādeḥ kaṭhina avayava saṃniveśasya praśithila avayava saṃyoga lakṣaṇasya vikārasya kāraṇam sataḥ eva viṣayasya pratyaya kāraṇam dhūma jñānam agni jñānasya iti jñāyate iti jñānam agniḥ ca asau jñānam ca iti agni jñānam tasya etat uktam bhavati vartamānasya eva agneḥ jñeyasya pratyaya kāraṇa tayā kāraṇam iti autsargikī nirapekṣāṇām kāraṇānām kārya kriyā prāptiḥ tasyāḥ kutaścid apavādaḥ aprāptiḥ yathā nimna upasarpaṇa svabhāvānām apām pratibandhaḥ setunā tathā iha api buddhi sattvasya sukha prakāśa śīlasya svābhāvikī sukha viveka khyāti janaka tā prāptiḥ sā kutaścid adharmāt tamasaḥ vā pratibandhāt na bhavati 
TV_2.28.2^5	 dharmāt yoga aṅga anuṣṭhānāt vā tad apanaye tad apratibaddha vṛtti svabhāvataḥ eva tad janakatayā tat āpnoti yathā vakṣyati nimittam aprayojakam prakṛtīnām varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas kṣetrika vat iti tat evam viveka khyāti lakṣaṇa kārya apekṣayā prāpti kāraṇam uktam avāntara kārya apekṣayā tu tat eva viyoga kāraṇam iti āha viyoga kāraṇam iti anya tva kāraṇam āha anya tva kāraṇam yathā suvarṇakāraḥ suvarṇasya kaṭaka kuṇḍala keyūra ādibhyaḥ bhinna abhinnasya bheda vivakṣayā kaṭaka ādi bhinnasya abheda vivakṣayā kaṭaka ādi abhinnasya suvarṇasya kuṇḍalāt anya tvam tathā ca kaṭaka kārī suvarṇakāraḥ kuṇḍalāt abhinnāt suvarṇāt anyat kurvan anya tva kāraṇam 
TV_2.28.2^6	 agniḥ api pākyasya anyatva kāraṇam yadi api tathā api dharmiṇaḥ dharmayoḥ pulāka tva taṇḍula tvayoḥ bheda avivakṣayāḥ dharmayoḥ upajana apāye api dharmī anuvartate iti na tasya anya tvam śakyam vaktum iti vikāra mātra kāraṇa tvam uktam iti na saṃkaraḥ na ca saṃsthāna bhedaḥ dharmiṇaḥ anya tva kāraṇam iti vyākhyeyam suvarṇakāraḥ iti asya asaṃgateḥ bāhyam anya tva kāraṇam upanyasya ādhyātmikam udāharati evam ekasya iti avidyā kamanīyā iyam kanyakā ityādi jñānam tad moha yogāt saḥ eva strī pratyayaḥ mūḍhaḥ viṣaṇṇaḥ bhavati caitrasya maitrasya puṇyavataḥ bata kalatra ratnam etat na tu mama bhāgya hīnasya iti evam sapatnī janasya tasyām dveṣaḥ strī pratyayasya duḥkha tve 
TV_2.28.2^7	 evam maitrasya tasyāḥ bhartuḥ rāgaḥ tasya eva strī pratyayasya sukha tve tattva jñānam tvac māṃsa medaḥ asthi majjā samūhaḥ strī kāyaḥ sthāna bīja ādibhiḥ aśuciḥ iti vivekinām mādhyasthye vairāgye kāraṇam iti dhṛti kāraṇam śarīram indriyāṇām vidhārakam indriyāṇi ca śarīrasya sāmānyā karaṇa vṛttiḥ hi prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca tad abhāve śarīra pātāt evam māṃsa ādikāya aṅgānām api paraspara vidhārya vidhāraka tvam evam mahābhūtāni pṛthivī ādīni manuṣya varuṇa sūrya gandha vaha śaśi loka nivāsinām śarīrāṇām tāni ca parasparam pṛthivyām hi gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabda guṇāyām pañca mahābhūtāni parasparam vidhārya vidhāraka bhāvena avasthitāni apsu catvāri tejasi trīṇi dve ca mātariśvanī iti 
TV_2.28.2^8	 tairyagyauna mānuṣa daivata ādīni ca vidhārya vidhāraka bhāvena avasthitāni nanu ādhāra ādheya bhāva rahitānām kutas tattvam iti atas āha paraspara artha tvāt iti manuṣya śarīram hi paśu pakṣi mṛga sarīsṛpa sthāvara śarīra upayogena dhriyate evam vyāghra ādi śarīram api manuṣya paśu mṛga ādi śarīra upayogena evam paśu mṛga ādi śarīram api sthāvara ādi upayogena evam daiva śarīram api manuṣya upahṛta= chāga mṛga kapiñjala māṃsa ājya puroḍāśa sahakāra śākhā prastara ādibhiḥ ijyamānam tad upayogena evam devatā api vara dāna vṛṣṭi ādibhiḥ manuṣya ādīni dhārayati iti asti paraspara artha tvam iti arthaḥ śeṣam sugamam 
TV_2.29.1–2.29.2	 yama niyama āsana prāṇāyāma pratyāhāra dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhayaḥ aṣṭau aṅgāni saṃprati nyūna adhika saṃkhyā vyavaccheda artham yoga aṅgāni avadhārayati tatra yoga aṅgāni avadhāryante iti yama niyama āsana prāṇāyāma pratyāhāra dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhayaḥ aṣṭau aṅgāni abhyāsa vairāgya śraddhā vīrya ādayaḥ api yathāyogam eteṣu eva svarūpataḥ na antarīyaka tayā ca antar bhāvayitavyāḥ 
TV_2.30.1–2.30.2^1	 ahiṃsā satya asteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ yamāḥ yama niyama ādi aṅgāni uddiśya yama nirdeśakam sūtram avatārayati tatra iti ahiṃsā satya asteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ yamāḥ yogāṅgam ahiṃsām āha sarvathā iti īdṛśīm ahiṃsām stauti uttare ca iti tad mūlāḥ iti ahiṃsām aparipālya kṛtā api akṛta kalpā niṣphala tvāt iti arthaḥ tad siddhi para tayā eva anuṣṭhānam ahiṃsā ced mūlam uttareṣām katham te ahiṃsā siddhi parā iti atas āha tad pratipādanāya iti siddhiḥ jñānam na utpattiḥ iti arthaḥ syāt etat ahiṃsā jñāna arthāḥ yadi uttare kṛtam taiḥ anyatas eva tad avagamāt iti atas āha tad avadātā iti yadi uttare na anuṣṭhīyeran ahiṃsā malinā syāt asati a ādibhiḥ iti arthaḥ atra eva āgamikānām saṃmatim āha tathā ca iti sugamam 
TV_2.30.2^2	 satya lakṣaṇam āha yathā arthe vāc manase iti yathāśabdam sa ākāṅkṣam pūrayati yathā dṛṣṭam iti pratisaṃbandhinam tathāśabdam pratikṣipati tathā vāc manaḥ ca vivakṣāyām kartavyāyām iti anyathā tu na satyam etat sa upapattikam āha paratra puruṣe sva bodha saṃkrāntaye sva bodha sadṛśa bodha jananāya vāc ukta uccāritāḥ atas sā yadi na vañcitā vañcikāḥ yathā droṇa ācāryeṇa sva tanaya aśvatthāma maraṇam āyuṣman satya dhana aśvatthāmā hataḥ iti pṛṣṭasya yudhiṣṭhirasya prativacanam hastinam abhisaṃdhāya satyam hataḥ aśvatthāmā iti tat idam uktasya uttaram na yudhiṣṭhirasya sva bodham saṃkrāmayati sva bodhaḥ hi asya hasti hanana viṣayaḥ indriya janmā na ca asau saṃkrāntaḥ kim tu anyaḥ eva tasya tanaya vadha bodhaḥ jātaḥ iti 
TV_2.30.2^3	 bhrāntāḥ vā bhrānti jāḥ vā bhrāntiḥ ca vivakṣā samaye vā jñeya artha avadhāraṇa samaye vā pratipattyā vandhyā pratipatti vandhyā yathārthān prati mleccha bhāṣā pratipatti vandhyā niṣprayojanā vā syāt iti yathā anapekṣita abhidhānā vāc tatra hi paratra sva bodhasya saṃkrāntiḥ api asaṃkrāntiḥ eva niṣprayojana tvāt iti evaṃlakṣaṇam api satyam para apakāra phalam satya ābhāsam na tu satyam iti āha eṣā iti tat yathā satya tapasaḥ taskaraiḥ sārtha gamanam pṛṣṭasya sārtha gamana abhidhānam iti abhidhīyamāna uccāryamāṇāḥ śeṣam sugamam abhāvasya bhāva adhīna nirūpaṇa tayā steya lakṣaṇam āha steyam aśāstra pūrvakam iti viśeṣeṇa sāmānyam lakṣyate iti arthaḥ 
TV_2.30.2^4	 mānasa vyāpāra pūrvaka tvāt vācanika kāyika vyāpārayoḥ prādhānyāt manaḥ vyāpāraḥ uktaḥ aspṛhā rūpam iti brahmacarya svarūpam āha guptā iti saṃyata upasthaḥ api hi strī prekṣaṇa tad ālāpa kandarpa āyatana tad aṅga sparśana saktaḥ na brahmacaryavān iti tad nirāsāya uktam gupta indriyasya iti indriya antarāṇi api tatra lolupāni rakṣaṇīyāni iti aparigraha svarūpam āha viṣayāṇām iti tatra saṅga doṣaḥ uktaḥ bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇām iti hiṃsā lakṣaṇaḥ ca doṣaḥ na anupahatya bhūtāni upabhogaḥ saṃbhavati iti aśāstrīyāṇām ayatna upanatānām api viṣayāṇām nindita pratigraha ādi rūpa arjana doṣa darśanāt chāstrīyāṇām api upārjitānām ca rakṣaṇa ādi doṣa darśanāt asvīkaraṇam aparigrahaḥ 
TV_2.31.1–2.31.2	 jāti deśa kāla samayān avacchinnāḥ sārvabhaumāḥ mahā vratam sāmānyatas uktāḥ yādṛśāḥ punar yoginām upādeyāḥ tādṛśān vaktum sūtram avatārayati te tu iti jāti deśa kāla samayān avacchinnāḥ sārvabhaumāḥ mahā vratam sarvāsu jāti ādi lakṣaṇāsu bhūmiṣu viditāḥ sārvabhaumāḥ ahiṃsā ādayaḥ iti anyatra api avacchedaḥ ūhanīyaḥ sugamam bhāṣyam 
TV_2.32.1–2.32.3^1	 śauca saṃtoṣa tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni niyamāḥ śauca ādi niyamān ācaṣṭe śauca saṃtoṣa tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni niyamāḥ vyācaṣṭe śaucam iti ādi śabdena gomaya ādayaḥ gṛhyante go mūtra yāvaka ādi medhyam tasya abhyavaharaṇa ādi ādi śabdāt grāsa parimāṇa saṃkhyā niyama ādayaḥ grāhyāḥ medhya abhyavaharaṇa ādi janitam iti vaktavye medhya abhyavaharaṇa ādi ca iti uktam kārye kāraṇa upacārāt citta malāḥ madamāna asūyādayaḥ tad apanayaḥ manaḥ śaucam prāṇa trāṇa mātra hetoḥ abhyadhikasya anupāditsā saṃtoṣaḥ prāk eva svīkaraṇa parityāgāt iti śeṣaḥ 
TV_2.32.1–2.32.3^2–2.33.2	 kāṣṭha maunam iṅgitena api sva abhiprāya aprakāśanam avacana mātram ākāra maunam parikṣīṇa vitarka jālaḥ iti vitarkaḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ saṃśaya viparyayau vā iti etāvatā śuddhaḥ abhisaṃdhiḥ uktaḥ ete ca yama niyamāḥ viṣṇupurāṇe uktāḥ brahmacaryam ahiṃsām ca satya āsteya aparigrahān seveta yogī niṣkāmaḥ yogyatām sva manaḥ nayan svādhyāya śauca saṃtoṣa tapāṃsi niyata ātmavān kurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasmin pravaṇam manaḥ ete yamāḥ sa niyamāḥ pañca pañca prakīrtitāḥ viśiṣṭa phala dāḥ kāmyāḥ niṣkāmānām vimukti dāḥ iti vitarka bādhane pratipakṣa bhāvanam śreyāṃsi bahu vighnāni iti eṣām apavāda saṃbhave tad pratīkāra upadeśa param sūtram avatārayati eteṣām yama niyamānām iti sūtram vitarka bādhane pratipakṣa bhāvanam vitarkāṇām bhāṣye na asti tirohitam iva kiṃcana 
TV_2.34.1–2.34.2	 vitarkāḥ hiṃsā ādayaḥ kṛta kārita anumoditāḥ lobha krodha moha pūrvakāḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātrāḥ duḥkha ajñāna ananta phalāḥ iti pratipakṣa bhāvanam tatra vitarkāṇām svarūpa prakāra kāraṇa dharma phala bhedān pratipakṣa bhāvān āviṣayān pratipakṣa bhāvanā svarūpa abhidhitsayā sūtreṇa āha vitarkāḥ hiṃsā ādayaḥ kṛta kārita anumoditāḥ lobha krodha moha pūrvakāḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātrāḥ duḥkha ajñāna ananta phalāḥ iti pratipakṣa bhāvanam vyācaṣṭe tatra hiṃsā iti prāṇabhṛt bhedasya aparisaṃkhyeya tvāt niyama vikalpa samuccayāḥ saṃbhavinaḥ hiṃsā ādiṣu tatra adharmataḥ tamaḥ samudreke sati caturvidha viparyaya lakṣaṇasya ajñānasya api udayaḥ iti ajñāna phala tvam api eteṣām iti duḥkha ajñāna ananta phala tvam eva hi pratipakṣa bhāvanam tad vaśāt ebhyaḥ nivṛtteḥ iti tat eva pratipakṣa bhāvanam sphorayati vadhyasya paśu ādeḥ vīryam prayatnam kāya vyāpāra hetum prathamam ākṣipati yūpa niyojanena tena hi paśoḥ aprāgalbhyam bhavati śeṣam ati sphuṭam 
TV_2.35.1–2.35.2	 ahiṃsā pratiṣṭhāyām tad saṃnidhau vaira tyāgaḥ uktāḥ yama niyamāḥ tad apavādakānām ca vitarkāṇām pratipakṣa bhāvanātaḥ hāniḥ uktā saṃprati apratyūham yama niyama abhyāsāt tad siddhi parijñāna sūcakāni cihnāni upanyasyati yat parijñānāt yogī tatra tatra kṛtakṛtyaḥ kartavyeṣu pravartate iti āha yadā iti ahiṃsā pratiṣṭhāyām tad saṃnidhau vaira tyāgaḥ śāśvatika virodhāḥ api aśva mahiṣa mūṣaka mārjārāhi nakula ādayaḥ api bhagavataḥ pratiṣṭhita ahiṃsasya saṃnidhānāt tad citta anukāriṇaḥ vairam parityajanti iti 
TV_2.36.1–2.36.2	 satya pratiṣṭhāyām kriyā phala āśraya tvam satya pratiṣṭhāyām kriyā phala āśraya tvam kriyā asādhyau dharma adharmau kriyā tad phalam ca svarga naraka ādi te eva āśrayati iti āśrayaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tat asya bhagavataḥ vācaḥ bhavati iti kriyā āśraya tvam āha dhārmikaḥ iti phala āśraya tvam āha svargam iti amogha apratihatā 
TV_2.37.1–2.38.2	 asteya pratiṣṭhāyām sarva ratna upasthānam asteya pratiṣṭhāyām sarva ratna upasthānam su bodham brahmacarya pratiṣṭhāyām vīrya lābhaḥ brahmacarya pratiṣṭhāyām vīrya lābhaḥ vīryam sāmarthyam yasya lābhāt apratighān apratighātān guṇān aṇima ādīn utkarṣayati upacinoti siddhaḥ ca tāra ādibhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ siddhibhiḥ ūhā ādi a para nāmabhiḥ upetaḥ vineyeṣu śiṣyeṣu jñānam yoga tad aṅga viṣayam ādhātum samarthaḥ bhavati iti 
TV_2.39.1–2.39.2	 aparigraha sthaiḥ ye janma kathaṃtā saṃbodhaḥ aparigraha sthaiḥ ye janma kathaṃtā saṃbodhaḥ nikāya viśiṣṭaiḥ deha indriya ādibhiḥ abhisaṃbandhaḥ janma tasya kathaṃtā kiṃprakāra tā tasyāḥ saṃbodhaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ sa prakāra ati indriya śānta udita avyapadeśya janma parijñānam iti yāvat atītam jijñāsate kaḥ aham āsam iti tasya eva prakāra bhedam utpāde sthitau ca jijñāsate katham aham āsam iti vartamānasya janmanaḥ svarūpam jijñāsate kim svid iti śarīram bhautikam kim bhūtānām samūha mātram āhosvit tebhyaḥ anyat iti atra api katham svid iti anuṣañjanīyam kvacid tu paṭhyatas eva anāgatam jijñāsate ke vā bhaviṣyāmaḥ iti atra api katham svid iti anuṣaṅgaḥ evam asya iti pūrva antaḥ atītaḥ kālaḥ parāntaḥ bhaviṣyan madhyaḥ vartamānaḥ teṣu ātmanaḥ bhāvaḥ śarīra ādi saṃbandhaḥ tasmin jijñāsā tatas ca jñānam yaḥ hi yat icchati sa tat karoti iti nyāyāt 
TV_2.40.1–2.41.2	 śaucāt sva aṅga jugupsā paraiḥ asaṃsargaḥ śaucāt sva aṅga jugupsā paraiḥ asaṃsargaḥ anena bāhya śauca siddhi sūcakam kathitam sattva śuddhi saumanasya ekāgrya indriya jaya ātma darśana yogya tvāni ca āntara śauca siddhi sūcakam āha kim ca iti sattva śuddhi saumanasya ekāgrya indriya jaya ātma darśana yogya tvāni ca citta malānām ākṣālane citta sattvam amalam prādurbhavati vaimalyāt saumanasyam svaccha tā svaccham tad ekāgram tatas manaḥ tantrāṇām indriyāṇām tad jayāt jayaḥ tatas ātma darśana yogya tvam buddhi sattvasya bhavati iti 
TV_2.42.1–2.42.4	 saṃtoṣāt anuttamaḥ sukha lābhaḥ saṃtoṣāt anuttamaḥ sukha lābhaḥ na vidyate asmāt uttamaḥ iti anuttmaḥ yathā ca uktam yayātinā pūrau yauvanam arpayatā yā dustyajā durmatibhiḥ yā na jīryati jīryatām tām tṛṣṇām saṃtyajan prājñaḥ sukhena eva abhipūryate iti tat etat darśayati yat ca kāma sukham lokaḥ ityādinā 
TV_2.43.1–2.44.2	 kāya indriya siddhiḥ aśuddhi kṣayāt tapasaḥ tapaḥ siddhi sūcakam āha kāya indriya siddhiḥ aśuddhi kṣayāt tapasaḥ aśuddhi lakṣaṇam āvaraṇam tāmasam adharma ādi aṇima ādyāḥ mahimā laghimā prāptiḥ ca sugamam svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā saṃprayogaḥ svādhyāya siddhi sūcakam āha svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā saṃprayogaḥ sugamam 
TV_2.45.1–2.45.2	 samādhi siddhiḥ īśvara praṇidhānāt samādhi siddhiḥ īśvara praṇidhānāt na ca vācyam īśvara praṇidhānāt eva ced saṃprajñātasya samādheḥ aṅginaḥ siddhiḥ kṛtam saptabhiḥ aṅgaiḥ iti īśvara praṇidhāna siddhau dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭau āntara vyāpāreṇa teṣām upayogāt saṃprajñāta siddhau ca saṃyoga pṛthaktvena dadhnaḥ iva kratu artha tā puruṣa artha tā ca na ca evam anantaraṅga tā dhāraṇā dhyāna sama adhīnām saṃprajñāta siddhau saṃprajñāta samāna gocara tayā aṅga antarebhyaḥ atad gocarebhyaḥ asya antaraṅga tva pratīteḥ īśvara praṇidhānam api īśvara gocaram na saṃprajñeya gocaram iti bahis aṅgam iti sarvam avadātam prajānāti iti prajñāpada vyutpattiḥ darśitāḥ 
TV_2.46.1–2.46.2^1	 sthira sukham āsanam uttara sūtram avatārayati uktāḥ saha siddhibhiḥ yama niyamāḥ āsana ādīni vakṣyāmaḥ tatra sthira sukham āsanam sthiram niścalam yat sukham sukha āvaham tat āsanam iti sūtra arthaḥ āsyate āste vā anena iti āsanam tasya prabhedān āha tat yathā iti padmāsanam prasiddham sthitasya ekataraḥ pādaḥ bhūnyaste ekataraḥ ca ākuñcita jānoḥ upari nyastaḥ iti etat vīrāsanam pāda tale vṛṣaṇa samīpe saṃpuṭīkṛtya tasya upari pāṇikacchapikām kuryāt tat bhadrāsanam savyam ākuñcitam caraṇam dakṣiṇa jaṅghoḥ vantare dakṣiṇam ca ākuñcitam vāma jaṅghoru antare nikṣipet etat svastikam 
TV_2.46.2^2	 upaviśya śliṣṭa aṅgulikau śliṣṭa gulphau bhūmi śliṣṭa jaṅghā ūḥ upādau prasārya daṇḍāsanam abhyaset yoga paṭṭaka yogāt sa upāśrayam jānu prasārita bāhoḥ śayanam paryaṅkaḥ krauñca niṣadana ādīni krauñca ādīnām niṣaṇṇānām saṃsthāna darśanāt pratyetavyāni pārṣṇī agra pādābhyām dvayoḥ ākuñcitayoḥ anyonya saṃpīḍanam sama saṃsthānam yena saṃsthānena avasthitasya sthairyam sukham ca sidhyati tat āsanam sthira sukham tat etat bhagavataḥ sūtrakārasya saṃmatam tasya vivaraṇam yathāsukham ca iti 
TV_2.47.1–2.47.2	 prayatna śaithilya ananta samāpattibhyām āsana svarūpam uktvā tad sādhanam āha prayatna śaithilya ananta samāpattibhyām sāṃsiddhikaḥ hi prayatnaḥ śarīra dhārakaḥ na yoga aṅgasya upadeṣṭa vyāsanasya kāraṇam tasya tad kāraṇatvaḥ upadeśa vaiyarthyāt svarasataḥ eva tad siddheḥ tasmāt upadeṣṭavyasya āsanasya ayam asādhakaḥ virodhī ca svābhāvikaḥ prayatnaḥ tasya ca yādṛt chikā āsana hetu tayā āsana niyama upahantṛ tvāt tasmāt upadiṣṭa niyama āsanam abhyasyatā svābhāvika prayatna śaithilyāya prayatnaḥ āstheyaḥ na anyathā upadiṣṭam āsanam sidhyati iti svābhāvika prayatna śaithilyam āsana siddhi hetuḥ anante vā nāganāyake sthiratara phaṇā sahasra vidhṛta viśvaṃbharā maṇḍale samāpannam cittam āsanam nirvartayati iti 
TV_2.48.1–2.49.2	 tatas dvaṃdva anabhighātaḥ āsana vijaya sūcakam āha tatas dvaṃdva anabhighātaḥ nigada vyākhyātam bhāṣyam āsanam api uktam viṣṇupurāṇe evam bhadrāsana ādīnām samāsthāya guṇaiḥ yutam iti tasmin sati śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ āsana anantaram tat pūrvaka tām prāṇāyāmasya darśayan tad lakṣaṇam āha tasmin sati śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ recaka pūraka kumbhakeṣu asti śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ iti prāṇāyāma sāmānya lakṣaṇam etat iti tathā hi yatra bāhyaḥ vāyuḥ ācamya antar dhāryate pūrake tatra asti śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ yatra api kauṣṭhyaḥ vāyuḥ virecya bahis dhāryate recake tatra asti śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ evam kumbhake api iti tat etat bhāṣyeṇa ucyate sati āsana iti 
TV_2.50.1–2.50.2^1	 bāhya abhyantara stambha vṛttiḥ deśa kāla saṃkhyābhiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ prāṇāyāma viśeṣa traya lakṣaṇa param sūtram avatārayati sa tu iti bāhya abhyantara stambha vṛttiḥ deśa kāla saṃkhyābhiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ vṛtti śabdaḥ pratyekam saṃbadhyate recakam āha yatra praśvāsa iti pūrakam āha yatra śvāsa iti kumbhakam āha tṛtīyaḥ iti tat eva sphuṭayati yatra ubhayoḥ śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ sakṛt eva vidhārakāt prayatnāt abhāvaḥ bhavati na punar pūrvavat āpūraṇa prayatna ogha vidhāraka prayatnaḥ na api recaka prayatna ogha vidhāraka prayatnaḥ apekṣyate kim tu yathā tapte upale nihitam jalam pariśuṣyat sarvatas saṃkocam āpadyate evam ayam api mārutaḥ vahana śīlaḥ balavat vidhāraka prayatna niruddha kriyaḥ śarīraḥ eva sūkṣmībhūtaḥ avatiṣṭhate na tu pūrayati yena pūrakaḥ na tu recayati yena recakaḥ iti iyān asya deśaḥ viṣayaḥ prādeśa vitasti hasta ādi parimitaḥ nivāta pradeśaḥ īśīkā tūla ādi kriyā anumitaḥ bāhyaḥ evam āntaraḥ api āpāda talam āmastakam pipīlikā sparśa sadṛśena anumitaḥ sparśena 
TV_2.50.2^2	 nimeṣa kriyā avacchinnasya kālasya caturthaḥ bhāgaḥ kṣaṇaḥ teṣām iyattā avadhāraṇena avacchinnaḥ sva jānu maṇḍalam pāṇinā tris parāmṛśya cśoṭikā avacchinnaḥ kālaḥ mātrā tābhiḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatā mātrābhiḥ parimitaḥ prathamaḥ udghātaḥ mṛduḥ saḥ eva dvi guṇīkṛtaḥ dvitīyaḥ madhyamaḥ saḥ eva triguṇīkṛtaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tīvraḥ tam imam saṃkhyā paridṛṣṭam prāṇāyāmam āha saṃkhyābhiḥ iti svasthasya hi puṃsaḥ śvāsa praśvāsa kriyā avacchinnena kālena yathā ukta= śoṭikā kālaḥ samānaḥ prathama udghāta karma tām nītaḥ udghātaḥ vijitaḥ vaśīkṛtaḥ nigṛhītaḥ kṣaṇānām iyattā kālaḥ vivakṣitaḥ śvāsa praśvāseyattā saṃkhyā iti kathaṃcid bhedaḥ sa khalu ayam pratyaham abhyastaḥ divasa pakṣa māsa ādi krameṇa deśa kāla pracaya vyāpitayā dīrghaḥ parama naipuṇya samadhi gamanīya tayā ca sūkṣmaḥ na tu manda tayā 
TV_2.51.1–2.51.2	 bāhya abhyantara viṣaya ākṣepī caturthaḥ evam trayaḥ viśeṣāḥ lakṣitāḥ caturtham lakṣayati bāhya abhyantara viṣaya ākṣepī caturthaḥ vyācaṣṭe deśa kāla saṃkhyābhiḥ iti ākṣiptaḥ abhyāsa vaśīkṛtāt rūpāt avaropitaḥ saḥ api dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ eva tad pūrvakaḥ bāhya abhyantara viṣaya prāṇāyāmaḥ deśa kāla saṃkhyā darśana pūrvakaḥ na ca asau caturthaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iva sakṛt prayatnāt ahnāya jāyate kim tu abhyasyamāna s tām tām avasthām āpannaḥ tad tad avasthā vijayā anukrameṇa bhavati iti āha bhūmi jayāt iti nanu ubhayoḥ gati abhāvaḥ stambha vṛttau api asti iti kaḥ asmāt asya viśeṣaḥ iti atas āha tṛtīyaḥ iti anālocana pūrvaḥ sakṛt prayatna nirvartitaḥ tṛtīyaḥ caturthaḥ tu ālocana pūrvaḥ bahu prayatna nirvartanīyaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ tayoḥ pūraka recakayoḥ viṣayaḥ anālocitaḥ ayam tu deśa kāla saṃkhyābhiḥ ālocitaḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_2.52.1–2.52.5^1	 tatas kṣīyate prakāśa āvaraṇam prāṇāyāmasya avāntara prayojanam āha tatas kṣīyate prakāśa āvaraṇam āvriyate anena buddhi sattva prakāśaḥ iti āvaraṇam kleśaḥ pāpmā ca vyācaṣṭe prāṇāyāmān iti jñāyate anena iti jñānam buddhi sattva prakāśaḥ vivekasya jñānam viveka jñānam viveka jñānam āvṛṇoti iti viveka jñāna āvaraṇīyam bhavya geya pravacanīya ādīnām kartari nipātanasya pradarśana artha tvāt kopanīya rañjanīya vat atra api kartari kṛtya pratyayaḥ karma śabdena tat janyam apuṇyam tat kāraṇam kleśam lakṣayati atra eva āgaminām anumatim āha yat tat ācakṣate iti 
TV_2.52.1–2.52.5^2	 mahāmohaḥ rāgaḥ tad avinirbhāga vartinī avidyā api tad grahaṇena gṛhyate akāryam adharmaḥ nanu prāṇāyāmaḥ eva ced pāpmānam kṣiṇoti kṛtam tarhi tapasā iti atas āha durbalam bhavati iti na tu sarvathā kṣīyate atas tad prakṣayāya tapaḥ apekṣyate iti atra api āgaminām anumatim āha tathā ca uktam iti manuḥ api āha prāṇa āyamaiḥ dahet doṣān iti prāṇāyāmasya yoga aṅga tā viṣṇupurāṇa uktā prāṇa ākhyam anilam vaśyam abhyāsāt kurute tu yaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa bījaḥ abījaḥ eva ca paraspareṇa abhibhavam prāṇa apānau yadā anilau kurutaḥ tad vidhānena tṛtīyam saṃyamāt tayoḥ iti 
TV_2.53.1–2.54.1–2.54.5^1	 dhāraṇāsu ca yogyatā manasaḥ kim ca dhāraṇāsu ca yogyatā manasaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ hi manaḥ sthirīkurvan dhāraṇāsu yogyam karoti sva viṣaya asaṃprayoge citta svarūpa anukāraḥ iva indriyāṇām pratyāhāraḥ tat evam yama ādibhiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ saṃyamāya pratyāhāram ārabhate tasya lakṣaṇa sūtram avatārayitum pṛcchati atha iti sva viṣaya asaṃprayoge citta svarūpa anukāraḥ iva indriyāṇām pratyāhāraḥ cittam api mohanīya rañjanīya kopanīyaiḥ śabda ādibhiḥ viṣayaiḥ na saṃprayujyate tad asaṃprayogāc cakṣuḥ ādīni api na saṃprayujyante iti saḥ ayam indriyāṇām citta svarūpa anukāraḥ yat punar tattvam cittam abhiniviśate na tad indriyāṇi bāhya viṣayāṇi iti ananukāraḥ api atas uktam anukāraḥ iva iti 
TV_2.54.1–2.54.5^2	 sva viṣaya asaṃprayogasya sādhāraṇasya dharmasya citta anukāra nimitta tvam saptamyāḥ darśayati sva iti anukāram vivṛṇoti citta nirodhaḥ iti dvayoḥ nirodha hetuḥ ca prayatnaḥ tulyaḥ iti sādṛśyam atra eva dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā madhukara rājam iti dārṣṭa antike yojayati tathā iti atra api viṣṇu purāṇa vākyam śabda ādiṣu anuṣaktāni nigṛhya akṣāṇi yoga vid kuryāt citta anukārīṇi pratyāhāra parāyaṇaḥ tasya prayojanam tatra eva darśitam vaśya tā paramā tena jāyate niścala ātmanām indriyāṇām avaśyaiḥ taiḥ na yoga sādhakaḥ iti 
TV_2.55.1–2.55.2^1	 tatas paramā vaśyatā indriyāṇām asya anuvādakam sūtram tatas paramā vaśyatā indriyāṇām nanu santi kim anyāḥ aparamāḥ indriyāṇām vaśya tā yāḥ apekṣya paramā iyam ucyate addhā tāḥ darśayati śabda ādiṣu iti etat eva vivṛṇoti saktī rāgaḥ vyasanam kayā vyupattyai vyasyati kṣipati nirasyati enam śreyasaḥ iti tad abhāvaḥ avyasanam vaśya tā aparām api vaśya tām āha aviruddhā śruti ādi aviruddha śabda ādi sevanam tad viruddheṣu apravṛttiḥ sā eva nyāyyā nyāyāt anapetāḥ yatas aparām api vaśya tām āha śabda ādi saṃprayogaḥ iti śabda ādiṣu indriyāṇām saṃprayogaḥ sva icchayā bhogyeṣu khalu ayam svatantraḥ na bhogya tantraḥ iti arthaḥ aparām api vaśya tām āha rāga dveṣa abhāve sukha duḥkha śūnyam mādhyasthyena śabda ādi jñānam iti eke 
TV_2.55.2^2–2.55.3	 sūtra kāra abhimatām vaśya tām parama ṛṣi saṃmatām āha cittasya ekāgryāt saha indriyaiḥ apravṛttiḥ eva śabda ādiṣu iti jaigīṣavyaḥ asyāḥ parama tām āha paramā tu iti tuśabdaḥ vaśya tā antarebhyaḥ viśinaṣṭi vaśya tā antarāṇi hi viṣaya āśīviṣa saṃprayoga śāli tayā kleśa viṣa saṃparka śaṅkām na apakrāmanti na hi viṣa vidyā vid prakṛṣṭaḥ api vaśīkṛta bhujaṃgamaḥ bhujaṃgamam aṅke nidhāya svapiti viśrabdhaḥ iyam tu vaśya tā vidūrīkṛta nikhila viṣaya vyatiṣaṅgāḥ nirāśaṅka tayā parama iti ucyate na itara indriya jaya vat iti yathā yatamāna saṃjñāyām eka indriya jaye api indriya antara jayāya prayatna antaram apekṣante na ca evam citta nirodhe bāhya indriya nirodhāya prayatna antara apekṣā iti arthaḥ kriyā yogam jagau kleśān vipākān karmaṇām iha tad duḥkha tvam tathā vyūhān pāde yogasya pañcakam iti 
TV_3.1.1–3.1.4	 deśa bandhaḥ cittasya dhāraṇā prathama dvitīya pādābhyām samādhiḥ tad sādhanam ca uktam tṛtīya pāde tad pravṛtti anuguṇāḥ śraddhā utpāda hetavaḥ vibhūtayaḥ vaktavyāḥ tāḥ ca saṃyama sādhyāḥ saṃyamaḥ ca dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi samudāyaḥ iti vibhūti sādhana tayā pañcabhyaḥ ca yoga aṅgebhyaḥ bahis aṅgebhyaḥ asya aṅga trayasya antaraṅga tayā viśeṣa jñāpana artham atra trayasya upanyāsaḥ tatra api ca dhāraṇā dhyāna sama adhīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāvena niyata paurvāparya tvāt tad anurodhena upanyāse kramaḥ iti prathamam dhāraṇā lakṣaṇīyā iti āha uktāni iti deśa bandhaḥ cittasya dhāraṇā ādhyātmika deśam āha nābhi cakraḥ iti ādi śabdena tālvādayaḥ grāhyāḥ bandhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ bāhya deśam āha bāhyaḥ iti bāhye ca na svarūpeṇa cittasya saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati iti uktam vṛtti mātreṇa jñāna mātreṇa iti atra api purāṇam prāṇāyāmena pavanam pratyāhāreṇa ca indriyam vaśīkṛtya tatas kuryāt citta sthānam śubha āśraye śubha āśrayāḥ bāhyāḥ hiraṇyagarbha vāsava prajāpati prabhṛtayaḥ idam ca tatra uktam 
TV_3.1.5	 mūrtam bhagavataḥ rūpam sarva upāśraya niḥspṛham eṣā vai dhāraṇā jñeyā yat cittam tatra dhāryate tat ca mūrtam hare rūpam yat vicintyam narādhipa tat śrūyatām anādhārā dhāraṇā na upapadyate prasanna vadanam cāru padma patra nibha īkṣaṇam su kapolam su vistīrṇa lalāṭa phalaka ujjvalam sama karṇa anta vinyasta cāru kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇam kambu grīvam su vistīrṇa śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasam valī vibhaṅginā magna nābhinā ca udareṇa ca pralamba aṣṭa bhujam viṣṇum athavā api catur bhujam sama sthita ūru jaṅgham ca svastika aṅghri vara ambujam cintayet brahma bhūtam tam pīta nirmala vāsasam kirīṭa cāru keyūra kaṭaka ādi vibhūṣitam śārṅga cakra gadā khaḍga śaṅkha akṣa valaya anvitam cintayet tad mayaḥ yogī samādhāya ātma mānasam tāvat yāvat dṛḍhībhūtā tatra eva nṛpa dhāraṇā etat ātiṣṭhataḥ anyat vā sva icchayā karma kurvataḥ na apayāti yadā cittam siddhām manyeta tām tadā iti 
TV_3.2.1–3.3.2	 tatra pratyaya eka tāna tā dhyānam dhāraṇa asādhyam dhyānam lakṣayati tatra pratyaya eka tāna tā dhyānam ekatā ānatā eka agra tā sugamam bhāṣyam atra api purāṇam tad rūpa pratyaya ekāgrya saṃtatiḥ ca anya niḥspṛhā tat dhyānam prathamaiḥ aṅgaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ niṣpādyate nṛpaḥ iti tat eva artha mātra nirbhāsam svarūpa śūnyam iva samādhiḥ dhyāna sādhyam samādhim lakṣayati tat eva artha mātra nirbhāsam svarūpa śūnyam iva samādhiḥ vyācaṣṭe dhyānam eva iti dhyeya ākāra nirbhāsam iti dhyeya ākārasya eva nirbhāsaḥ na dhyāna ākārasya iti atas eva āha śūnyam iti nanu śūnyam ced katham dhyeyam prakāśeta iti atas āha iva iti atra eva hetum āha dhyeya svabhāva āveśāt iti atra api purāṇam 
TV_3.3.3–3.3.5	 tasya eva kalpanā hīnam svarūpa grahaṇam hi yat manasā dhyāna niṣpādyam samādhiḥ saḥ abhidhīyate iti dhyeyāt dhyānasya bhedaḥ kalpanā tat hīnam iti arthaḥ aṣṭāṅga yogam uktvā khāṇḍikyāya keśidhvajaḥ upasaṃjahāraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ karaṇī jñānam karaṇam tat acetanam niṣpādya mukti kāryam vai kṛtakṛtyam nivartate iti 
TV_3.4.1–3.5.2	 trayam ekatra saṃyamaḥ dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhiḥ iti etat trayasya tatra tatra niyujyamānasya prātisvika saṃjñā uccāraṇe gauravam syāt iti lāghava artham paribhāṣā sūtram avatārayati trayam ekatra saṃyamaḥ vyācaṣṭe eka viṣayāṇi iti vācaka tva śaṅkām apanayati tat asya iti tantryate vyutpādyate yogaḥ yena śāstreṇa tat tantram tat bhavā tāntrikī saṃyama pradeśāḥ pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt iti evamādayaḥ tad jayāt prajñā lokaḥ saṃyama vijayasya abhyāsa sādhanasya phalam āha tad jayāt prajñā lokaḥ pratyaya antara anabhibhūtasya nirmala pravāhe avasthānam ālokaḥ prajñāyāḥ sugamam bhāṣyam 
TV_3.6.1–3.6.3	 tasya bhūmiṣu viniyogaḥ kva punar viniyuktasya saṃyamasya phalam etat iti atas āha tasya bhūmiṣu viniyogaḥ bhūmim viśeṣayati bhāṣya kāraḥ tasya iti jitāyāḥ bhūmeḥ yā anantarā bhūmiḥ avasthā ajitā tatra viniyogaḥ sthūla viṣaye sa vitarke samādhau vaśīkṛte saṃyamena saṃyamasya avijite nirvitarke viniyogaḥ tasmin api vaśīkṛte sa vicāre viniyogaḥ evam nirvicāre viniyogaḥ iti arthaḥ atas eva sthūla viṣaya samāpatti siddhau satyām purāṇe tad tad āyudha bhūṣaṇa apanayena sūkṣma viṣayaḥ samādhiḥ avatāritaḥ tatas śaṅkha gadā cakra śārṅga ādi rahitam budhaḥ cintayet bhagavat rūpam praśāntam sākṣasūtrakam yadā ca dhāraṇā tasmin avasthānavatī tatas kirīṭa keyūra mukhaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ rahitam smaret tadā eka avayavam devam saḥ aham ca iti punar budhaḥ kuryāt tatas hi aham iti praṇidhāna paraḥ bhavet iti 
TV_3.6.4	 kasmāt punar adharām bhūmim vijitya uttarām vijayate viparyayaḥ kasmāt na bhavati iti atas āha na hi ajita adhara bhūmiḥ iti na hi śilā hradāt gaṅgām prati prasthitaḥ aprāpya megha vanam gaṅgām prāpnoti īśvara prasādāt jita uttara bhūmikasya ca iti kasmāt tad arthasya uttara bhūmi vijayasya pratyāsannasya anyatas eva īśvara praṇidhānāt eva avagata tvāt niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi aviśeṣa ādhāyinaḥ sādhanasya sādhana nyāya atipātāt iti syāt etat āgamataḥ sāmānyatas avagatānām api avāntara bhūmi bhedānām kutas paurvāparya avagatiḥ iti atas āha bhūmeḥ asyāḥ iti jitaḥ pūrvaḥ yogaḥ uttarasya yogasya jñāna pravṛtti adhigama hetuḥ avasthā eva avasthāvān iti abhipretya etat draṣṭavyam 
TV_3.7.1–3.8.2	 trayam antaraṅgam pūrvebhyaḥ kasmāt punar yoga aṅga tva aviśeṣe api saṃyamasya tatra tatra viniyogaḥ na īrareṣām pañcānām iti atas āha trayam antaraṅgam pūrvebhyaḥ tat idam sādhana trayam sādhya samāna viṣaya tvena antaraṅgam na tu evam yama ādayaḥ tasmāt te bahis aṅgāḥ iti arthaḥ tat api bahis aṅgam nirbījasya sādhana trayasya saṃprajñātaḥ eva antaraṅga tvam na tu asaṃprajñāte tasya nirbīja tayā taiḥ saha samāna viṣaya tva abhāvāt teṣu cira niruddheṣu saṃprajñāta parama kāṣṭhā para nāma jñāna prasāda rūpa para vairāgya anantaram utpādāt ca iti āha tat iti tat api bahis aṅgam nirbījasya samāna viṣaya tvam antaraṅga tva prayojakam iha na tu tad anantara bhāvaḥ tasya bahis aṅga īśvara praṇidhāna varti tayā savyabhicāra tvāt iti sthite savyabhicāram api antaraṅga lakṣaṇam tad anantara bhāvi tvam asya na asti tasmāt dūra apeta antaraṅga tā saṃyamasya asaṃprajñātaḥ iti darśayitum tad abhāve bhāvāt iti uktam 
TV_3.9.1–3.9.2^1	 vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāvau nirodha kṣaṇa citta anvayaḥ nirodha pariṇāmaḥ pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt iti atra upayokṣyamāṇa pariṇāma trayam pratipipādayiṣuḥ nirbīja prasaṅgena pṛcchati atha iti vyutthāna saṃprajñātayoḥ cittasya sphuṭatara pariṇāma bheda pracaya anubhavān na praśna avatāraḥ nirodhe tu na anubhūyate pariṇāmaḥ na ca ananubhūyamānaḥ na asti cittasya triguṇa tayā cala tvena guṇānām kṣaṇam api apariṇāmasya asaṃbhavāt iti arthaḥ praśna uttaram sūtram vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāvau nirodha kṣaṇa citta anvayaḥ nirodha pariṇāmaḥ asaṃprajñātam samādhim apekṣya saṃprajñātaḥ vyutthānam nirudhyate anena iti nirodhaḥ jñāna prasādaḥ param vairāgyam tayoḥ vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāvau tatra vyutthāna saṃskārasya abhibhavaḥ nirodha saṃskārasya āvirbhāvaḥ cittasya dharmiṇaḥ nirodha kṣaṇasya nirodha avasarasya dvayoḥ avasthayoḥ anvayaḥ 
TV_3.9.2^2	 na hi cittam dharmi saṃprajñāta avasthāyām asaṃprajñāta avasthāyām ca saṃskāra abhibhava prādurbhāvayoḥ sva rūpeṇa bhidyate iti nanu yathottare kleśāḥ avidyā mūlāḥ avidyā nivṛttau nivartante iti na tu tad nivṛttau pṛthak prayatna antaram āsthīyate evam vyutthāna pratyaya mūlāḥ saṃskārāḥ vyutthāna pratyaya nivṛttau eva nivartante iti tad nivṛttau na nirodha saṃskāraḥ apekṣitavyaḥ iti atas āha vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ iti na kāraṇa mātra nivṛttiḥ kārya nivṛtti hetuḥ mā bhūt kuvinda nivṛttau api paṭasya nivṛttiḥ api tu yat kāraṇa ātmakam yat kāryam tad kāraṇa nivṛttau tad kārya nivṛttiḥ uttare ca kleśāḥ avidyā ātmānaḥ iti uktam atas tad nivṛttau teṣām nivṛttiḥ upapannā na tu evam pratyaya ātmānaḥ saṃskārāḥ cira niruddhe pratyaye saṃprati smaraṇa darśanāt tasmāt pratyaya nivṛttau api tad nivṛttau nirodha saṃskāra pracayaḥ eva upāsanīyaḥ iti arthaḥ sugamam anyat 
TV_3.10.1–3.10.2	 tasya praśānta vāhi tā saṃskārāt sarvathā vyutthāna saṃskāra abhibhave tu balavatā nirodha saṃskāreṇa cittasya kīdṛśaḥ pariṇāmaḥ iti atas āha tasya praśānta vāhi tā saṃskārāt vyutthāna saṃskāra mala rahita nirodha saṃskāra paramparā mātravāhi tā praśānta vāhi tā kasmāt punar saṃskāra pāṭavam apekṣate na tu saṃskāra mātram iti atas āha tad saṃskāra māndyaḥ iti tat iti nirodham parāmṛśati ye tu na abhibhūyate iti paṭhanti te tadā vyutthānam parāmṛśanti 
TV_3.11.1–3.11.2	 sarva artha tā eka agra tayoḥ kṣaya udayau cittasya samādhi pariṇāmaḥ saṃprajñāta samādhi pariṇāma avasthām cittasya darśayati sarva artha tā eka agra tayoḥ kṣaya udayau cittasya samādhi pariṇāmaḥ vikṣipta tā sarva artha tā san na vinaśyati iti kṣayaḥ tirobhāvaḥ na asat utpadyate iti udayaḥ āvirbhāvaḥ sva ātma bhūtayoḥ sarva artha tā eka agra tayoḥ dharmayoḥ yau apāya upajanau sarva artha tāyāḥ apāyaḥ ekāgra tāyā upajanaḥ tayoḥ anugatam cittam samādhīyate pūrva aparībhūta sādhya māna samādhi viśeṣaṇam bhavati iti 
TV_3.12.1–3.12.2	 tatas punar śānta uditau tulya pratyayau cittasya ekāgra tā pariṇāmaḥ tatas punar śānta uditau tulya pratyayau cittasya ekāgra tā pariṇāmaḥ punar samādheḥ pūrva aparībhūtāyāḥ avasthāyāḥ samādhi niṣpattau satyām śānta uditau atīta vartamānau tulyau ca tau pratyayau ca iti tulya pratyayau ekāgra tāyām tu dvayoḥ sādṛśyam samāhita cittasya iti samādhi niṣpattiḥ darśitāḥ tathā eva ekāgram eva avadhim āha ā samādhi bhreṣāt bhraṃśāt iti 
TV_3.13.1–3.13.2^1	 etena bhūta indriyeṣu dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ vyākhyātāḥ prāsaṅgikam ca vakṣyamāṇaupayikam ca bhūta indriya pariṇāmam vibhajate etena bhūta indriyeṣu dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ vyākhyātāḥ vyācaṣṭe etena iti nanu citta pariṇati mātram uktam na tu tad prakārāḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ tat katham teṣām atideśaḥ iti atas āha tatra vyutthāna nirodhayoḥ iti dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā śabdāḥ param na uccāritā na tu dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ na uktāḥ iti saṃkṣepa arthaḥ tathā hi vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ iti atra eva sūtre dharma pariṇāmaḥ uktaḥ imam ca dharma pariṇāmam darśayatā tena eva dharma adhikaraṇaḥ lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ api sūcitaḥ eva iti āha lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ iti 
TV_3.13.2^2	 lakṣyate anena iti lakṣaṇam kāla bhedaḥ tena hi lakṣitam vastu vastu antarebhyaḥ kāla antara yuktebhyaḥ vyavacchidyate iti nirodhaḥ tri lakṣaṇaḥ asya eva vyākhyānam tribhiḥ adhvabhiḥ yuktaḥ adhva śabdaḥ kāla vacanaḥ sa khalu anāgata lakṣaṇam adhvānam prathamam hitvā tat kim adhva vat dharma tvam api atipatati na iti āha dharma tvam anatikrāntaḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇam pratipannaḥ yaḥ eva nirodhaḥ anāgataḥ āsīt saḥ eva saṃprati vartamānaḥ na tu nirodhaḥ anirodhaḥ iti arthaḥ vartamāna tā svarūpa vyākhyānam yatra asya svarūpeṇa sva ucita artha kriyā kāriṇā rūpeṇa abhivyaktiḥ samudācāraḥ eṣaḥ asya prathamam anāgatam adhvānam apekṣya dvitīyaḥ adhvā 
TV_3.13.2^3	 syāt etat anāgatam adhvānam hitvā ced vartamāna tām āpannaḥ tām ca hitvā atīta tām āpatsyate hanta bhoḥ adhvanām utpāda vināśau syātām na ca iṣi ete na hi asataḥ utpādaḥ na api sataḥ vināśaḥ iti atas āha na ca atīta anāgatābhyām sāmānya ātmanā avasthitābhyām viyuktaḥ iti anāgatasya nirodhasya vartam āna tā lakṣaṇam darśayitvā vartamāna vyutthānasya atīta tām tṛtīyam adhvānam āha tathā vyutthānam iti tat kim nirodhaḥ eva anāgataḥ na vyutthānam na iti āha evam punar vyutthānam iti vyutthāna jāti apekṣayā punarbhāvaḥ na vyakti apekṣayā na hi atītam punar bhavati iti svarūpa abhivyaktiḥ artha kriyā kṣamasya āvirbhāvaḥ 
TV_3.13.2^4	 sa ca evaṃlakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ uktaḥ tad jātīyeṣu paunaḥpunyena vartate iti atas āha evam punar iti dharma pariṇāma sūcitam eva avasthā pariṇāmam āha tathā iti dharmāṇām vartamāna adhvanām balavat tva abalavat tve avasthā tasyāḥ pratikṣaṇam tāratamyam pariṇāmaḥ upasaṃharati eṣaḥ iti pariṇāma bhedānām saṃbandhi bhedāt nirdhārayati tatra anubhava anusārāt dharmiṇaḥ iti tat kim eṣa pariṇāmaḥ guṇānām kādācid kaḥ na iti āha evam iti kasmāt punar ayam pariṇāmaḥ sadātanaḥ iti atas āha calam ca iti caḥ hetu arthaḥ vṛttam pracāraḥ etat eva kutas iti atas āha guṇa svābhāvyam iti uktam atra eva purastāt saḥ ayam trividhaḥ api citta pariṇāmaḥ bhūta indriyeṣu sūtrakāreṇa nirdiṣṭaḥ iti āha etena iti 
TV_3.13.2^5	 eṣa dharma pariṇāma bhedaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedam ālakṣya tatra bhūtānām pṛthivī ādīnām dharmiṇām gavādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ vā dharma pariṇāmaḥ dharmāṇām ca atīta anāgata vartamāna rūpa tā lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇa āpannasya gavā ādeḥ bālya kaumāra yauvana vārdhakyam avasthā pariṇāmaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām api nava purātanatā avasthā pariṇāmaḥ evam indriyāṇām api dharmiṇām tad tad nīla ādi ālocanam dharma pariṇāmaḥ dharmasya vartamānatā ādi lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇasya ratna ādi ālocanasya sphuṭa tva asphuṭa tva ādiḥ avasthā pariṇāmaḥ saḥ ayam evaṃvidhaḥ bhūta indriya pariṇāmaḥ dharmiṇaḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthānām bhedam āśritya veditavyaḥ 
TV_3.13.2^6	 abhedam āśritya āha paramārthataḥ tu iti tuśabdaḥ bheda pakṣāt viśinaṣṭi pāramārthika tvam asya jñāpyate na tu anyasya pariṇāma tvam niṣidhyate kasmāt dharmi svarūpa mātraḥ hi iti nanu yadi dharmi vikriyā eva dharmaḥ katham asaṃkara pratyayaḥ loke pariṇāmeṣu iti atas āha dharma dvāra iti dharma śabdena dharma lakṣaṇa avasthāḥ parigṛhyante tad dvāreṇa dharmiṇaḥ eva vikriyā iti ekā ca asaṃkīrṇā ca tad dvārāṇām abhede api dharmiṇaḥ paraspara saṃkarāt nanu dharmāṇām abhinna tve dharmiṇaḥ adhvanām ca bhede dharmiṇaḥ ananya tvena dharmeṇa api iha dharmi vat bhavitavyam iti atas āha tatra dharmasya iti bhāvaḥ saṃsthāna bhedaḥ 
TV_3.13.2^7	 suvarṇa ādeḥ yathā bhājanasya rucaka svastika vya padeśa bhedaḥ bhavati tanmātram anyathā bhavati na tu dravyam suvarṇam asuvarṇa tām upaiti atyanta bheda abhāvāt iti vakṣyamāṇa abhisaṃdhiḥ ekānta vādinam bauddham utthāpayati aparaḥ āha iti dharmāḥ eva hi rucaka ādayaḥ tathā utpannāḥ paramārtha santaḥ na punar suvarṇam nāma kiṃcid ekam anekeṣu anugatam dravyam iti yadi punar nivartamāneṣu api dharmeṣu dravyam anugatam bhavet tatas na citi śakti vat pariṇameta api tu kauṭasthyena eva parivarteta pariṇāma ātmakam rūpam parihāya rūpa antareṇa kauṭasthyena parivartanam parivṛttiḥ 
TV_3.13.2^8	 yathā citi śaktiḥ anyathā anyathā bhāvam bhajamāneṣu api guṇeṣu svarūpāt apracyutā kūṭastha nityā evam suvarṇa ādi api syāt na ca iṣyate tasmāt na dravyam atiriktam dharmebhyaḥ iti pariharati ayam adoṣaḥ iti kasmāt ekānta tā anabhyupagamāt yadi citi śakteḥ iva dravyasya aikāntikīm nityatām abhyupagacchema tatas evam upālabhyemahi na tu aikāntikīm nityatām ātiṣṭhāmahe kim tu tat etat trailokyam na tu dravya mātram vyakteḥ artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ rūpāt apaiti kasmāt nitya tva pratiṣedhāt pramāṇena yadi hi ghaṭaḥ vyakteḥ na apeyāt kapāla śarkarā cūrṇa ādiṣu avasthāsu api vyaktaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti pūrvavat upalabdhi artha kriye kuryāt tasmāt anityam trailokyam 
TV_3.13.2^9	 astu tarhi anityam eva upalabdhi artha kriyā rahita tvena gagana aravinda vat ati tuccha tvāt iti atas āha apetam api asti na atyanta tucchatāḥ yena ekāntataḥ anityam syāt iti arthaḥ kasmāt vināśa pratiṣedhāt pramāṇena tathā hi yat tuccham na tat kadācid api upalabdhi artha kriye karoti yathā gagana aravindam karoti ca etat trailokyam kadācid upalabdhi artha kriye iti tathā utpattimat dravya tva dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā yogi tva ādayaḥ api atyanta tuccha gagana nalina nara viṣāṇa ādi vyāvṛttāḥ sattva hetavaḥ udāhāryāḥ tathā ca dharmī na atyantam nityaḥ yena citi śakti vat kūṭastha nityaḥ syāt kim tu kathaṃcid nityaḥ tathā ca pariṇāmi iti siddham 
TV_3.13.2^10	 etena mṛd piṇḍa ādi avasthāsu kāryāṇām ghaṭa ādīnām anāgatānām sattvam veditavyam syāt etat apetam api ced asti kasmāt pūrvavat na upalabhyate iti atas āha saṃsargāt sva kāraṇa layāt saukṣmyam darśanān arha tvam tatas ca anupalabdhiḥ iti tat evam dharma pariṇāmam samarthya lakṣaṇa pariṇāmam api lakṣaṇānām paraspara anugamanena samarthayate lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ iti ekaikam lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇa antarābhyām samanugatam iti arthaḥ nanu eka lakṣaṇa yoge lakṣaṇa antare na anubhūyete tat katham tad yogaḥ iti atas āha yathā puruṣaḥ iti na hi anubhava abhāvaḥ pramāṇa siddham apalapati tad utpādaḥ eva tatra tad sadbhāve pramāṇam asataḥ utpāda asaṃbhavāt nara viṣāṇa vat iti 
TV_3.13.2^11	 para uktam doṣam utthāpayati atra lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ iti yadā dharmaḥ vartamānaḥ tadā eva yadi atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca tadā trayaḥ api adhvānaḥ saṃkīryeran anukrameṇa ca adhvanām bhāve asat utpāda prasaṅgaḥ iti bhāvaḥ pariharati tasya parihāraḥ iti vartamāna tā eva hi dharmāṇām anubhava siddhā tatas prāc paścāt kāla saṃbandham avagamayati na khalu asat utpadyate na ca sat vinaśyati tat idam āha evam hi na cittam iti krodha uttara kālam hi cittam rāga dharmakam anubhūyate yadā ca rāgaḥ krodha samaye anāgata tvena na āsīt katham asau utpadyeta anutpannaḥ ca katham anubhūyeta iti bhavatu evam tathā api kutas adhvanām asaṃkaraḥ iti pṛcchati kim ca iti 
TV_3.13.2^12	 kim kāraṇam asaṃkare caḥ punar arthe uttaram āha trayāṇām lakṣaṇānām yugapad na asti saṃbhavaḥ kasmin ekasyām citta vṛttau krameṇa tu lakṣaṇānām ekatamasya sva vyañjaka añjanasya bhāvaḥ bhavet saṃbhavet lakṣya adhīna nirūpaṇa tayā lakṣaṇānām lakṣya ākāreṇa tadvat tā atra eva pañcaśikha ācārya saṃmatim āha uktam ca iti etat ca prāk eva vyākhyātam upasaṃharati tasmāt iti āvirbhāva tirobhāva rūpa viruddha dharma saṃsargāt asaṃkaraḥ adhvanām iti dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā rāgasya iti pūrvam krodhasya rāga saṃbandha avagamaḥ darśitaḥ iti idānīm tu viṣaya antara vartinaḥ rāgasya viṣaya antara vartinā rāga antareṇa saṃbandha avagamaḥ iti 
TV_3.13.2^13	 dārṣṭa antikam āha tathā lakṣaṇasya iti iti nanu sati api anekānta abhyupagame abhedaḥ asti iti dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā anya tve tad abhinnasya dharmiṇaḥ api anya tva prasaṅgaḥ saḥ eva ca na iṣyate tad anugama anubhava virodhāt iti atas āha na dharmī tri adhvā yatas tad abhinnāḥ dharmāḥ tri adhvānaḥ dharmāṇām adhvatraya yogam eva sphorayati te lakṣitāḥ abhivyaktāḥ vartamānāḥ iti yāvat alakṣitāḥ anabhivyaktāḥ anāgatāḥ atītāḥ iti yāvat tatra lakṣitāḥ tām tām avasthām balavat tva durbala tva ādikām prāpnuvantaḥ anyatvena pratinirdiśyante avasthā antarataḥ na dravya antarataḥ avasthā śabdena dharma lakṣaṇa avasthāḥ ucyante etat uktam bhavati anubhavaḥ eva hi dharmiṇaḥ dharma ādīnām bheda abhedau vyavasthāpayati 
TV_3.13.2^14	 na hi aikāntike abhede dharma ādīnām dharmiṇaḥ dharmi rūpavat dharma ādi tvam na api aikāntike bhede gavāśva vat dharma ādi tvam sa ca anubhavaḥ anaikāntika tvam avasthāpayan api dharma ādiṣu upajana apāya dharmakeṣu api dharmiṇam ekam anugamayan dharmān ca parasparataḥ vyāvartayan pratyātmam anubhūyate iti tad anusāriṇaḥ vayam na tam ativartya sva icchayā dharma anubhavān vyavasthāpayitum īśmahe iti atra eva laukikam dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā ekā rekhā iti yathā tat eva rekhā svarūpam tad tad sthāna apekṣayā śata ādi tvena vyapadiśyate evam tat eva dharmi rūpam tad tad dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā bhedena anya tvena pratinirdiśyate iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.13.2^15	 dārṣṭa antika artham dṛṣṭānta antaram āha yathā ca eka tve api iti atra antare paroktam doṣam utthāpayati avasthā iti avasthā pariṇāme dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāme kauṭasthya doṣa prasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ dharmi dharma lakṣaṇa avasthānām pṛcchati katham iti uttaram adhvanaḥ vyāpāreṇa iti dadhnaḥ kila yaḥ anāgataḥ adhvā tasya vyāpāraḥ kṣīrasya vartamāna tvam tena vyavahita tvāt dhetoḥ yadā dharmaḥ dadhi lakṣaṇaḥ sva vyāpāram dādhika ādi ārambham kṣīre san api na karoti tadā anāgataḥ yadā karoti tadā vartamānaḥ yadā kṛtvā nivṛttaḥ san eva sva vyāpārāt dādhika ādi ārambhāt tadā atītaḥ iti evam traikālye api sattvāt dharma dharmiṇoḥ lakṣaṇānām avasthānām ca kauṭasthyam prāpnoti 
TV_3.13.2^16–3.13.3	 sarvadā sattā hi nitya tvam caturṇām api ca sarvadā sattve asattve vā na utpādaḥ tāvat mātram ca lakṣaṇam kūṭastha nityatāyāḥ na hi citi śakteḥ api kūṭastha nityāyāḥ kaścid anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti bhāvaḥ pariharati na asau doṣaḥ kasmāt guṇi nitya tve api guṇānām vimardaḥ anyonya abhibhāvya abhibhāvaka tvam tasya vaicitryāt etat uktam bhavati yadi api sarvadā sattvam caturṇām api guṇi guṇānām tathā api guṇa vimarda vaicitryeṇa tad ātma bhūta tad vikāra āvirbhāva tirobhāva bhedena pariṇāma śāli tayā na kauṭasthyam citi śakteḥ tu na sva ātma bhūta vikāra āvirbhāva tirobhāvaḥ iti kauṭasthyam yathā āhuḥ nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ yat svabhāvaḥ na naśayti iti 
TV_3.13.4	 vimarda vaicitryam eva vikāra vaicitrye hetum prakṛtau vikṛtau ca darśayati yathā saṃsthānam pṛthivī ādi pariṇāma lakṣaṇam ādimat dharma mātram vināśi tirobhāvi śabda ādīnām śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandha tanmātrāṇām sva kāryam apekṣya avināśinām atirobhāvinām prakṛtau darśayati evam liṅgam iti tasmin vikāra saṃjñā na tu evam vikāravatī citi śaktiḥ iti bhāvaḥ tat evam parīkṣaka siddhām vikṛtim prakṛtim ca udāhṛtya vikṛtau eva loka siddhāyām guṇa vimarda vaicitryam dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāma vaicitrya hetum udāharati tatra idam udāharaṇam iti na ca ayam niyamaḥ lakṣaṇānām eva avasthā pariṇāmaḥ iti sarveṣām eva dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā bhedānām avasthā śabda vācya tvāt ekaḥ eva avasthā pariṇāmaḥ sarva sādhāraṇaḥ iti āha dharmiṇaḥ api iti vyāpakam pariṇāma lakṣaṇam āha avasthitasya dravyasya iti dharma śabdaḥ āśrita tvena dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā vācakaḥ 
TV_3.14.1–3.14.2^1^1	 śānta udita avyapadeśya dharma anupātī dharmī yasya eṣa trividhaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tam dharmiṇam sūtreṇa lakṣayati tatra śānta udita avyapadeśya dharma anupātī dharmī dharmaḥ asya asti iti dharmī iti na avijñāte dharme sa śakyaḥ jñātum iti dharmam darśayati yogyatā iti dharmiṇaḥ dravyasya mṛd ādeḥ śaktiḥ eva cūrṇa piṇḍa ghaṭa ādi utpatti śaktiḥ eva dharmaḥ teṣām tatra avyakta tvena bhāvaḥ iti yāvat nanu evam avyakta tayā santaḥ te tatas prādurbhavantu udaka āharaṇa ādayaḥ tu taiḥ sva kāraṇāt anāsāditāḥ kutas prāptāḥ iti atas uktam yogya tā avacchinnā iti 
TV_3.14.1–3.14.2^1^2	 yaḥ asau ghaṭa ādīnām utpatti śaktiḥ sa udaka āharaṇa ādi yogya tā avacchinnā tena udaka āharaṇa ādayaḥ api ghaṭa ādibhiḥ sva kāraṇāt eva prāptāḥ iti na akasmikāḥ iti bhāvaḥ athavā ke dharmiṇaḥ iti atra uttaram yogyatā avacchinnāḥ dharmiṇaḥ iti kaḥ dharmaḥ iti atra uttaram śaktiḥ eva dharmaḥ teṣām yogya tā eva dharmaḥ iti arthaḥ atas tadvān dharmī iti siddham bhavati tad sadbhāve pramāṇam āha sa ca phala prasava bheda anumitaḥ ekasya dharmiṇaḥ anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca cūrṇa piṇḍa ghaṭa ādi rūpaḥ iti arthaḥ kārya bheda darśanāt ca bhinnaḥ iti yāvat 
TV_3.14.2^2	 paridṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhaḥ tatra anubhava ārohiṇaḥ vartamānasya mṛd piṇḍasya śānta avi apadeśyābhyām mṛd cūrṇa mṛd ghaṭābhyām bhedam āha tatra vartamānaḥ iti yadi na bhidyeta piṇḍa vat cūrṇa ghaṭayoḥ api tadvat eva sva vyāpāra vyāpti prasaṅgaḥ iti bhāvaḥ avyaktasya tu piṇḍasya na uktam bheda sādhanam saṃbhavati iti āha yadā tu iti kaḥ asau kena bheda sādhanena bhidyeta iti tat evam dharmāṇām bheda sādhanam abhidhāya tam bhedam vibhajate tatra ye khalu iti uditāḥ iti vartamānāḥ iti arthaḥ adhvanām paurvāparyam niyamayati te ca iti codayati kimartham iti kiṃnimittam atītasya anantarāḥ na bhavanti vartamānāḥ hetum āha siddhāntī pūrva paścimatāyāḥ abhāvāt viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇīm anupalabdhim sūcayati anupalambham eva upalambha vaidharmyeṇa darśayati yathā anāgata vartamānayoḥ iti upasaṃharati tat tasmāt anāgataḥ eva samanantaraḥ pūrva tvena bhavati vartamānasya na atītaḥ atītasya vartamānaḥ pūrva tvena samanantaraḥ na avyapadeśyaḥ tasmāt adhvanām yaviṣṭhaḥ atītaḥ iti siddham 
TV_3.14.2^3	 syāt etat anubhūyamāna anubhūta tayā udita atītau śakyau unnetum avyapadeśyāḥ tu punar dharmāḥ avyapadeśya tayā evam śakyā na unnetum iti āśayavān pṛcchati atha avyapadeśyāḥ ke keṣu samīkṣāmahe atra uttaram āha sarvam sarva ātmakam iti yatra uktam iti tat eva upapādayati jala bhūmyoḥ iti jalasya hi rasa rūpa sparśa śabdavataḥ bhūmeḥ ca gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdavatyāḥ pāriṇāmikam vanaspati latā gulma ādiṣu mūla phala prasava pallava ādi gata rasa ādi vaiśvarūpyam dṛṣṭam saḥ ayam anevam ātmikāyāḥ bhūmeḥ anīdṛśasya vā jalasya na pariṇāmaḥ bhavitum arhati upapāditam hi na asat utpadyate iti tathā sthāvarāṇām pāriṇāmikam jaṅgameṣu manuṣya paśu mṛga ādiṣu rasa ādi vaicitryam dṛṣṭam upayuñjānāḥ hi te phala ādīni rūpa ādi bheda saṃpadam āsādayanti evam jaṅgamānām pāriṇāmikam sthāvareṣu dṛṣṭam rudhira avasekāt kila dāḍimī phalāni tāla phala mātrāṇi bhavanti upasaṃharati evam sarvam jala bhūmi ādi sarva rasa ādi ātmakam tatra hetum āha jāti anucchedena jala tva bhūmi tva ādi jāteḥ sarvatra pratyabhijñāyamāna tvena anucchedāt 
TV_3.14.2^4	 nanu sarvam ced sarva ātmakam hanta bhoḥ sarvasya sarvadā sarvatra sarvathā saṃnidhānāt samāna kālam bhāvānām vyaktiḥ prasajyeta na khalu saṃnihita avikala kāraṇam kāryam vilambitum arhati iti atas āha deśa kāla iti yadi api kāraṇam sarvam sarva ātmakam tathā api yaḥ yasya kāryasya deśaḥ yathā kuṅkumasya kāśmīraḥ teṣām sattve api pāñcāla ādiṣu na samudācāraḥ iti na kuṅkumasya pāñcāla ādiṣu abhivyaktiḥ evam nidāghe na prāvṛṣaḥ samudācāraḥ iti na tadā śālīnām evam na mṛgī manuṣyam prasūte na tasyām manuṣya ākāra samudācāraḥ iti evam na apuṇyavān sukha rūpam bhuṅkte na tasmin puṇya nimittasya samudācāraḥ iti 
TV_3.14.2^5	 tasmāt deśa kāla ākāra nimittānām apabandhāt apagamāt na samāna kālam ātmanām bhāvānām abhivyaktiḥ iti tat evam dharmān vibhajya teṣu dharmiṇaḥ anugamam darśayati yaḥ eteṣu iti sāmānyam dharmi rūpam viśeṣaḥ dharmaḥ tad ātmā ubhaya ātmakaḥ iti arthaḥ tat evam anugatam dharmiṇam darśayitvā tam anicchataḥ vaināśikasya kṣaṇikam vijñāna mātram cittam icchataḥ aniṣṭa prasaṅgam uktam smārayati yasya tu iti vastu pratyabhijñānāt ca iti na hi devadattena dṛṣṭam yajñadattaḥ pratyabhijānāti tasmāt yaḥ ca anubhavitā saḥ eva pratyabhijñāta iti 
TV_3.15.1–3.15.2^1	 krama anya tvam pariṇāma anya tve hetuḥ krama anya tvam pariṇāma anya tve hetuḥ kim ekasya dharmiṇaḥ ekaḥ eva dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā lakṣaṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ uta bahavaḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā lakṣaṇāḥ pariṇāmāḥ tatra kim prāptam eka tvāt dharmiṇaḥ ekaḥ eva pariṇāmaḥ na hi eka rūpāt kāraṇāt kārya bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati tasya ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt iti evam prāptaḥ ucyate krama anya tvāt pariṇāma anya tvam ekasyāḥ mṛdaḥ cūrṇa piṇḍa ghaṭa kapāla kaṇā ākārā pariṇati paramparā kramavatī laukika parīkṣakaiḥ adhyakṣam samīkṣyate anyat ca idam cūrṇapiṇḍayoḥ ānantaryam anyat ca piṇḍa ghaṭayoḥ anyat ca ghaṭa kapālayoḥ anyat ca kapāla kaṇayoḥ ekatra parasya anyatra pūrva tvāt saḥ ayam krama bhedaḥ pariṇāmaḥ ekasmin avakalpamānaḥ pariṇāma bhedam āpādayati 
TV_3.15.2^2	 ekaḥ api ca mṛd dharmī krama upanipāti tad tad sahakāri samavadhāna krameṇa kramavatīm pariṇāma paramparām udvahat na enām ākasmikayati iti bhāvaḥ dharma pariṇāma anyatva vat lakṣaṇa pariṇāma anya tve avasthā pariṇāma anya tve ca samānam krama anya tvam hetuḥ iti tat etat bhāṣyeṇa avadyotyate ekasya dharmiṇaḥ iti krama kramavatoḥ abhedam āsthāya sa tasya kramaḥ iti uktam tathā avasthā pariṇāma kramaḥ iti tathā hi kīnāśena koṣṭhāgāre prayatna saṃrakṣitāḥ api hi vrīhayaḥ hāyanaiḥ ati bahubhiḥ pāṇi sparśa mātra viśīryamāṇa avayava saṃsthānāḥ paramāṇu bhāvam anubhavantaḥ dṛśyante na ca ayam abhinavānām akasmāt eva prādurbhavitum arhati tasmāt kṣaṇa paramparā krameṇa sūkṣma sūkṣmatara sūkṣmatamabṛhat bṛhattara bṛhattam ādi krameṇa prāpteṣu viśiṣṭaḥ ayam lakṣyate iti tat idam krama anya tvam dharma dharmi bheda pakṣaḥ eva iti āha te ete iti 
TV_3.15.2^3	 ā vikārebhyaḥ ā ca āliṅgāt āpekṣikaḥ dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ mṛd ādeḥ api tanmātra apekṣayā dharma tvāt iti āha dharmaḥ api iti yadā parama artha dharmiṇī aliṅge abheda upacāra prayogaḥ tad dvāreṇa sāmānādhikaraṇya dvāreṇa dharmī eva dharmaḥ iti yāvat tadā ekaḥ eva pariṇāmaḥ dharmi pariṇāmaḥ eva iti arthaḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthānām dharmi svarūpa abhiniveśāt tat anena dharmiṇaḥ dūra utsāritam kūṭastha nitya tvam iti ukta prāyam dharma pariṇāmam pratipādayan prasaṅgena citta dharmāṇām prakāra bhedam āha cittasya iti paridṛṣṭāḥ pratyakṣāḥ aparidṛṣṭāḥ parokṣāḥ tatra pratyaya ātmakāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ rāga ādayaḥ ca vastu mātrāḥ iti aprakāśa rūpa tām āha syāt etat aparidṛṣṭāḥ ced na santi eva iti atas āha anumānena prāpitaḥ vastu mātreṇa sadbhāvaḥ yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ paścāt mānasādharmyāt āgamaḥ api anumānam 
TV_3.15.2^4	 sapta aparidṛṣṭān kārikayā saṃgṛhṇāti nirodha iti nirodhaḥ vṛttīnām asaṃprajñāta avasthā cittasya āgamataḥ saṃskāra śeṣa bhāvaḥ anumānataḥ ca samadhigamyate dharma grahaṇena puṇya apuṇye upalakṣayati kvacid karma iti pāṭhaḥ tatra api tat janite puṇya apuṇye eva gṛhyete te ca āgamataḥ sukha duḥkha upabhoga darśanāt vā anumānataḥ gamyete saṃskāraḥ tu smṛteḥ anumīyate evam triguṇa tvāt cittasya calam ca guṇa vṛttam iti pratikṣaṇam pariṇāmaḥ anumīyate evam jīvanam prāṇa dhāraṇam prayatna bhedaḥ asaṃviditaḥ cittasya dharmaḥ śvāsa praśvāsābhyām anumīyate evam cetasaḥ ceṣṭā kriyā yathā yathā taiḥ taiḥ indriyaiḥ śarīra pradeśaiḥ vā saṃprayujyate sā api tad saṃyogāt eva anumīyate evam śaktiḥ api udbhūtānām kāryāṇām sūkṣma avasthā cetasaḥ dharma sthūla kārya anubhavāt eva anumīyate iti 
TV_3.16.1–3.16.2	 pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt atīta anāgata jñānam atas param ā pāda parisamāpteḥ saṃyama viṣayaḥ tad vaśīkāra sūcanī vibhūtiḥ ca vaktavyā tatra ukta prakāram pariṇāma trayam eva tāvat prathamam upātta sakala yoga aṅgasya yoginaḥ saṃyama viṣaya tayā upakṣipati pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt atīta anāgata jñānam nanu yatra saṃyamaḥ tatra eva sākṣātkaraṇam tat katham pariṇāma traya saṃyamaḥ atīta anāgatam sākṣātkārayet iti atas āha tena pariṇāma trayam sākṣātkriyamāṇam teṣu pariṇāmeṣu anugate ye atīta anāgate tad viṣayam jñānam saṃpādayati pariṇāma traya sākṣātkaraṇam eva tad antarbhūta atīta anāgata sākṣāt karaṇa ātmakam iti na viṣaya bhedaḥ saṃyama sākṣātkārayoḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.17.1–3.17.3	 śabda artha pratyayānām itaretara adhyāsāt saṃkaraḥ tad pravibhāga saṃyamāt sarva bhūta ruta jñānam ayam aparaḥ saṃyamasya viṣayaḥ upakṣipyate śabda artha pratyayānām itaretara adhyāsāt saṃkaraḥ tad pravibhāga saṃyamāt sarva bhūta ruta jñānam atra vācakam śabdam ācikhyāsuḥ prathamam tāvat vāc vyāpāra viṣayam āha tatra vāc vāc indriyam varṇa vyañjakam aṣṭa sthānam yathā āha aṣṭau sthānāni varṇānām uraḥ kaṇṭhaḥ śiraḥ tathā jihvā mūlam ca dantāḥ ca nāsikā oṣṭhau ca tālu ca iti 
TV_3.17.4^1	 sā vāc varṇeṣu eva yathā loka pratīti siddheṣu arthavatī na ca vācakaḥ iti arthaḥ śrotra vyāpāra viṣayam nirūpayati śrotram punar dhvaneḥ udānasya vāc indriya abhighātinaḥ yaḥ pariṇati bhedaḥ varṇa ātmā tena ākāreṇa pariṇatam tanmātra viṣayam na tu vācaka viṣayam iti arthaḥ yathā āloka pratīti siddhebhyaḥ varṇebhyaḥ vācakam bhinatti padam punar vācakam punar nāda anusaṃhāra buddhi nirgrāhyam yathā pratīti siddhāt nādān varṇān pratyekam gṛhītvā anu paścāt yā saṃharati eka tvam āpādayati gauḥ iti etat ekam padam iti tayā padam gṛhyate 
TV_3.17.4^2	 yadi api prācyaḥ api buddhayaḥ varṇa ākāram padam eva pratyekam gocarayanti tathā api na viśadam prathate carame tu vijñāne tat ati viśadam iti nāda anusaṃhāra buddhi nirgrāhyam uktam yaḥ tu vaijātyāt eka pada anubhavam avijñāya varṇān eva vācakān ātiṣṭhate tam pratyāha varṇāḥ iti te khalu amī varṇāḥ pratyekam vācya viṣayām dhiyam ādadhīran nāgadantakā iva śikyā avalambanam saṃhatāḥ vā grāvāṇaḥ iva piṭhara dhāraṇam na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ ekasmāt artha pratīteḥ anutpatteḥ utpattau vā dvitīya ādīnām anuccāraṇa prasaṅgaḥ niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi viśeṣa an ādhāyinaḥ sādhanasya sādhana nyāya atipātāt 
TV_3.17.4^3	 tasmāt dvitīyaḥ pariśiṣyate saṃbhavati hi grāvṇām saṃhatānām piṭhara dhāraṇam eka samaya bhāvi tvāt varṇānām tu yaugapadya asaṃbhavaḥ atas parasparam anugrāhya anugrāhaka tva ayogāt saṃbhūya api na artha dhiyam ādadhate te pada rūpam ekam asaṃspṛśantaḥ tādātmyena atas eva anupasthāpayanta āvirbhūtāḥ tirobhūtāḥ ayaḥ śalākā kalpāḥ pratyekam apada sva rūpāḥ ucyante yadi punar padam ekam tādātmyena spṛśeyuḥ varṇāḥ tatas na ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha varṇaḥ punar ekaikaḥ pada ātmā sarva abhidhāna śakti pracitaḥ sarvābhiḥ abhidhāna śaktibhiḥ nicitaḥ go gaṇa gaura naga ityādiṣu hi gakāraḥ go tva ādi artha abhidhāyiṣu dṛṣṭaḥ iti tad tad abhidhāna śaktiḥ 
TV_3.17.4^4	 evam soma śociḥ iti ādiṣu īśvara ādi artha abhidhāyiṣu padeṣu ovarṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti saḥ api tad tad abhidhāna śaktiḥ evam sarvatrohanīyam sa ca ekaikaḥ varṇaḥ gakāra ādiḥ sahakāri yat varṇa antaram okāra ādi tat eva pratiyogi pratisaṃbandhi yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt vaiśvarūpyam nānātvam iva āpannaḥ na tu nānātvam āpannas tasya tattvāt eva pūrvaḥ varṇaḥ gakāraḥ uttareṇa okāreṇa gaṇa ādi padebhyaḥ vyāvartya uttaraḥ ca okāraḥ gakāreṇa śocira ādi padebhyaḥ vyāvartya viśeṣe go tva vācake go pada sphoṭe avasthāpitaḥ anusaṃhāra buddhau 
TV_3.17.4^5	 ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ artha pratyayaḥ hi varṇaiḥ niyata krama tayā parasparam asaṃbhavadbhiḥ aśakyaḥ kartum na ca saṃskāra dvāra āgneya ādīnām iva paramā pūrve vā svarge vā janayitavye aniyata kramāṇām api sāhityam artha buddhi upajanane varṇānām iti sāṃpratam vikalpa asaha tvāt sa khalu ayam varṇa anubhava janyaḥ saṃskāraḥ smṛti prasava hetuḥ anyaḥ vā āgneya ādi janyaḥ iva apūrva abhidhānaḥ na tāvat anantaraḥ kalpanā gaurava āpatteḥ saḥ eva tāvat adṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ kalpanīyaḥ tasya ca kramavadbhiḥ varṇa anubhavaiḥ ekasya janya tvam na saṃbhavati iti tad jātīyān eka avāntara saṃskāra kalpanā iti gauravam na ca eṣa jñāpaka hetu aṅgam ajñātaḥ tad aṅga tām anubhavati iti na khalu saṃbandhaḥ artha pratyāyana aṅgam ajñātaḥ aṅga tām upaiti smṛti phala prasava anumitaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ sva kāraṇa anubhava viṣaya niyataḥ na viṣaya antare pratyayam ādhātum utsahate anyathā yat kiṃcid eva ekaikam anubhūya sarvaḥ sarvam jānīyāt iti na ca pratyeka varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra piṇḍa labdha janma smṛti darpaṇa samārohiṇaḥ varṇāḥ samadhigata sahabhāvāḥ vācakāḥ iti sāṃpratam 
TV_3.17.4^6	 krama ākrama viparīta krama anubhūtānām tatra aviśeṣeṇa artha dhī janana prasaṅgāt na ca etat smaraṇa jñānam pūrva anubhava vartinīm para apara tām gocarayitum arhati tasmāt varṇebhyaḥ asaṃbhavan artha pratyayaḥ eka pada anubhavam eva sva nimittam upakalpayati na ca eṣa pade api prasaṅgaḥ tat dhi pratyekam eva prayatna bheda bhinnāḥ dhvanayaḥ vyañjayantaḥ paraspara visadṛśa tad tad pada vyañjaka dhvanibhiḥ tulya sthāna karaṇa niṣpannāḥ sadṛśāḥ santaḥ anyonya visadṛśaiḥ padaiḥ padam ekam sadṛśam āpādayantaḥ pratiyogi bhedena tad tad sādṛśyānām bhedāt tad upadhānāt ekam api anavayavam api sa avayavam iva aneka ātmakam iva avabhāsayanti yathā niyata varṇa parimāṇa saṃsthānam mukham ekam api maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa āt ayaḥ vibhinna varṇa parimāṇa saṃsthānam anekam ādarśayanti na paramārthataḥ sādṛśya upadhāna bheda kalpitāḥ bhāgāḥ eva nirbhāgasya padasya varṇāḥ tena tad buddhiḥ varṇa ātmanā pada bhede sphoṭam abhedam eva nirbhāgam eva sabhedam iva sa bhāgam iva ālambate 
TV_3.17.4^7	 atas gopada sphoṭa bhedasya ekasya gakāra bhāgaḥ gaura ādi pada sphoṭa sādṛśyena na nirdhārayanti sva bhāginam iti okāreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ nirdhārayati evam okāraḥ api bhāgaḥ śocira ādi pada sadṛśa tayā na śaktaḥ nirdhārayitum sva bhāginam go pada sphoṭam iti gakāreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ nirdhārayati asahabhāvinām api ca saṃskāra dvāreṇa asti sahabhāvaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva upapattiḥ na ca bhinna viṣaya tvam saṃskārayoḥ bhāga dvaya viṣayayoḥ anubhavayoḥ tad janmanoḥ ca saṃskārayoḥ eka pada viṣaya tvāt 
TV_3.17.4^8	 kevala bhāga anubhavena padam avyaktam anubhūyate anusaṃhāra dhiyā tu bhāga anubhava yoni saṃskāra labdha janmanā vyaktam iti viśeṣaḥ avyakta anubhavāḥ ca prāñcaḥ saṃskāra ādhāna krameṇa vyaktam anubhavam ādadhānā dṛṣṭā yathā dūrāt vanaspatau asti pratyayāḥ avyaktāḥ vyakta vanaspati pratyaya hetavaḥ na ca iyam vidhā varṇānām artha pratyāyane saṃbhavinī no khalu varṇāḥ pratyekam avyaktam artha pratyayam ādadhati ante vyaktam iti śakyam vaktum pratyakṣa jñānaḥ eva niyamāt vyakta avyakta tvasya varṇa ādheyaḥ tu artha pratyayaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ tat eṣa varṇebhyaḥ jāyamānaḥ sphuṭaḥ eva jāyeta 
TV_3.17.4^9	 na vā jāyeta na tu asphuṭaḥ sphoṭasya tu dhvani vyaṅgyasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ sphuṭa asphuṭa tve kalpyete iti asamānam evam pratyeka varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahita śrotra labdha janmani anusaṃhāra buddhau saṃhatā varṇā eka pada sphoṭa bhāvam āpannāḥ prayatna viśeṣa vyaṅgyatayā prayatna viśeṣasya ca niyata krama apekṣa tayā kramasya anya tve tad abhivyañjaka prayatna viśeṣa abhāvena tad abhivyakti abhāva prasaṅgāt krama anurodhinaḥ artha saṃketena avacchinnāḥ saṃketa avacchedam eva laukikam sa bhāga pada viṣayam darśayanti iyantaḥ dvitrāḥ tricaturāḥ pañcaṣā vai ete sarva abhidhāna śakti parivṛtā gakāra aukāra visarjanīyāḥ sāsnādi mantam artham avadyotayanti iti tat kim idānīm saṃketa anusāreṇa varṇānām eva vācaka tvam tathā ca na padam nāma kiṃcid ekam iti atas āha tat eteṣām iti dhvani nimittaḥ kramaḥ dhvani kramaḥ upasaṃhṛtaḥ dhvani kramaḥ yeṣu te tathā uktāḥ buddhyā nirbhāsyate prakāśyate iti buddhi nirbhāsaḥ saṃketa avacchinnāḥ sthūla darśi loka āśaya anurodhena gakāra aukāra visarjanīyāḥ iti uktam 
TV_3.17.4^10	 gakāra ādīnām api tad bhāga tayā tādātmyena vācaka tvāt prati iti anusārataḥ tu ekam eva padam vācakam iti arthaḥ etat eva spaṣṭayati tat ekam padam loka buddhyā pratīyate iti saṃbandhaḥ kasmāt ekam iti atas āha eka buddhi viṣayaḥ gauḥ iti ekam padam iti eka ākārāyāḥ buddheḥ viṣayaḥ yatas tasmāt ekam tasya vyañjakam āha eka prayatna ākṣiptam iti rasaḥ iti pada vyañjakāt prayatnāt vilakṣaṇaḥ saraḥ iti pada vyañjakaḥ prayatnaḥ sa ca upakramataḥ saraḥ iti pada vyakti lakṣaṇa phala avacchinnaḥ pūrva aparībhūtaḥ ekas tadākṣiptam bhāgānām sādṛśya upadhāna bheda kalpitānām parama artha satām abhāvāt abhāgam 
TV_3.17.4^11	 atas eva pūrva aparībhūta bhāvāt akramam nanu varṇāḥ pūrva aparībhūtāḥ te ca asya bhāgāḥ iti katham akramam abhāgam ca iti atas āha avarṇam na hi asya varṇāḥ bhāgāḥ kim tu sādṛśya upadhāna bhedāt padam eva tena tena ākāreṇa aparamārtha satā prathate na hi maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādi vartīni mukhāni mukhasya paramārtha sataḥ avayavāḥ iti bauddham anusaṃhāra buddhau viditam antya varṇa pratyayasya vyāpāraḥ saṃskāraḥ pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ tena upasthāpitam viṣayīkṛtam 
TV_3.17.4^12	 varṇa anubhava tad tad saṃskārāṇām ca pada viṣaya tvam upapāditam adhastāt syāt etat abhāgam akramam avarṇam ced pada tattvam kasmāt evaṃvidham kadācid na prathate na hi lākṣā rasa avaseka upadhāna āpādi ta aruṇa bhāvaḥ sphaṭika maṇiḥ tad apagame su accha dhavalaḥ na anubhūyate tasmāt pāramārthikāḥ eva varṇāḥ iti atas āha paratra iti pratipipādayiṣayā varṇaiḥ eva abhidhīyamānaiḥ uccāryamāṇaiḥ śrūyamāṇaiḥ ca śrotṛbhiḥ anādiḥ yaḥ ayam vāc vyavahāraḥ vibhakta varṇa pada nibandhanaḥ tad janitā vāsanā sā api anādiḥ eva 
TV_3.17.4^13–3.17.5	 tad anuviddhayā tad vāsitayā loka buddhyā vibhakta varṇa rūṣita pada avagāhinyā siddha vat parama artha vat saṃpratipattyā saṃvādena vṛddhānām padam pratīyate etat uktam bhavati asti kaścid upādhiḥ yaḥ upadheyena saṃyujyate viyujyate ca yathā lākṣā ādiḥ tatra tad viyoge sphaṭikaḥ svābhāvikena su accha dhavalena rūpeṇa prakāśate iti yujyate pada pratyayasya tu prayatna bheda upanīta dhvani bhedāt anyatas anutpādāt tasya ca sadā sādṛśya doṣa rūṣita tayā varṇa ātmanā eva pratyaya janaka tvam iti kutas nirupādhinaḥ padasya prathā yathā āhuḥ dhvanayaḥ sadṛśa ātmānaḥ viparyāsasya hetavaḥ upalambhakam eteṣām viparyāsasya kāraṇam upāya tvāt ca niyataḥ pada darśita darśinām jñānasya eva ca bādheyam loke dhruvam upaplavaḥ iti 
TV_3.17.6^1	 yatas pada ātmā vibhakta varṇa rūṣitaḥ prakāśate atas sthūla darśī lokaḥ varṇān eva padam abhimanyamānaḥ tān eva prakāra bheda bhājaḥ artha bhede saṃketayati iti āha tasya iti tasya padasya ajānataḥ ekasya api saṃketa buddhitaḥ sthūla darśi loka hitāya varṇa ātmanā vibhāgaḥ vibhāgam āha etāvatām na nyūnānām adhikānām vā evaṃjātīyakaḥ nairantarya krama viśeṣaḥ anusaṃhāraḥ ekabuddhi upagrahaḥ ekasya arthasya go tva ādeḥ vācakaḥ iti nanu yadi ekasya arthasya ayam śabdaḥ vācakaḥ iti saṃketaḥ hanta bhoḥ śabda arthayoḥ na itaretara adhyāsaḥ tarhi iti atas āha saṃketaḥ tu iti smṛtau ātmā svarūpam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ na hi kṛtaḥ iti eva saṃketaḥ artham avadhārayati api tu smaryamāṇaḥ 
TV_3.17.6^2	 etat uktam bhavati abhinna ākāraḥ eva saṃkete kathaṃcid bhedam vikalpya ṣaṣṭhī prayuktā iti yaḥ eṣām pravibhāga jñaḥ sa tatra saṃyame bhavati sarva vid sarva bhūta ruta jñaḥ iti tat evam vikalpita varṇa bhāgam ekam anavayavam padam vyutpādya kalpita pada vibhāgam vākyam ekam anavayavam vyutpādayitum āha sarva padeṣu ca asti vākya śaktiḥ ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ para pratyāyanāya śabdaḥ prayujyate tatra tat eva ca param prati pratipādayitavyam yat taiḥ pratipitsitam tat eva taiḥ pratipitsitam yad upādāna ādi gocaraḥ na ca padārtha mātram tat gocaraḥ kim tu vākya arthaḥ iti vākya artha parāḥ eva sarve śabdāḥ tena saḥ eva teṣām arthaḥ 
TV_3.17.6^3	 atas yatra api kevalasya padasya prayogaḥ tatra api pada antareṇa saha ekīkṛtya tatas arthaḥ gamyate na tu kevalāt kasmāt tanmātrasya asāmarthyāt tathā ca vākyam eva tatra tatra vācakam na tu padāni tad bhāga tayā tu teṣām api asti vākya artha vācaka śaktiḥ padārthaḥ iva pada bhāga tayā varṇānām tena yathā varṇaḥ ekaikaḥ sarva padārtha abhidhāna śaktiḥ pracitaḥ evam padam api ekaikam sarva vākya artha abhidhāna śakti pracitam tat idam uktam sarva padeṣu ca asti vākya śaktiḥ vṛkṣaḥ iti ukte asti iti gamyate adhyāhṛta astipada sahitam vṛkṣaḥ iti padam vākya arthe vartate iti tad bhāga tvāt vṛkṣa padam tatra vartate kasmāt punar asti iti gamyate iti atas āha na sattām padārthaḥ vyabhicarati iti 
TV_3.17.6^4	 loke eva hi padānām artha avadhāraṇa upāyaḥ sa ca kevalam padārtham asti arthena abhisamasya sarvatra vākya arthī karoti saḥ ayam avyabhicāraḥ sat tayā padārthasya atas eva śabda vṛtti vidām vyavahāraḥ yatra anyat kriyā padam na asti tatra astiḥ bhavantī paraḥ prayoktavyaḥ iti kriyā bheda avi abhicāri prātipadikam uktvā kriyā bhedam kāraka avyabhicāriṇam darśayati tathā ca pacati iti uktaḥ iti pacati iti ukte hi kāraka mātrasya tad anvaya yogyasya avagamāt anya vyāvṛtti paraḥ tad bhedānām anuvādaḥ tat evam bhedaḥ eva vākya arthaḥ iti tathā anapekṣam api padam vākya arthe vartamānam dṛśyate iti sutarām asti vākya śaktiḥ padānām iti āha dṛṣṭam ca iti 
TV_3.17.6^5	 na ca etāvatā api śrotriya ādi padasya svatantrasya evaṃvidha artha pratyāyanam na yāvat asti ādibhiḥ abhisamāsaḥ asya bhavati tathā ca asya api vākya avayava tvāt kalpita tvam eva iti bhāvaḥ syāt etat padānām eva ced vākya śaktiḥ kṛtam tarhi vākyena tebhyaḥ eva tad artha avasāyāt iti atas āha tatra vākyaḥ iti uktam etat na kevalāt padāt padārthaḥ pratipitsitaḥ pratīyate na yāvat etat pada antareṇa abhisamasyate iti tathā ca vākyāt padāni apoddhṛtya kalpitāni vākya arthāt ca apa uddhṛtya tat eka deśam kārakam vā kriyām vā tad padam prakṛti ādi vibhāga kalpanayā vyākaraṇīyam anvākhyeyam kimartham punar etāvatā kleśena anvākhyāyate iti atas āha anyathā iti 
TV_3.17.6^6	 ghaṭaḥ bhavati bhavati bhikṣām dehi bhavati tiṣṭhati iti nāma ākhyātayoḥ ca sāmyāt evam aśvaḥ tvam aśvaḥ yāti iti evam ajā payaḥ piba ajā payaḥ śatrūn iti nāma ākhyāta sārūpyāt anirjñātam nāma tvena ākhyāta tvena vā anvākhyāna abhāve niṣkṛṣya ajñātam katham kriyāyām kārake vā vyākriyeta tasmāt vākyāt padāni apoddhṛtya vyākhyātavyāni na tu anvākhyānāt eva pāramārthikaḥ vibhāgaḥ padānām iti tat evam śabda rūpam vyutpādya śabda artha pratyayānām saṃketa āpādita saṃkarāṇām asaṃkaram ākhyātum upakramate teṣām śabda artha pratyayānām pravibhāgaḥ tat yathā śvetate prāsādaḥ iti kriyā arthaḥ śabdaḥ 
TV_3.17.6^7	 sphuṭataraḥ hi atra pūrvāparībhūtāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhya rūpāyāḥ siddha rūpaḥ kriyā arthaḥ śvetataḥ iti bhinnaḥ śabdaḥ yatra api śabda arthayoḥ siddha rūpa tvam tatra api arthāt asti śabdasya bhedaḥ iti āha śvetaḥ prāsādaḥ iti kāraka arthaḥ śabdaḥ abhihita tvāt ca kāraka vibhakteḥ abhāvaḥ artham vibhajate kriyākāraka ātmā tad arthaḥ tayoḥ śabdayoḥ arthaḥ kriyā ātmā kāraka ātmā ca pratyayam vibhajate pratyayaḥ ca iti caśabdena tad arthaḥ iti etat padam atra anukṛṣyate tat atra anya padārtha pradhānam saṃbadhyate saḥ eva kriyākāraka ātma arthaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ nanu abhedena pratīteḥ śabda artha pratyayānām saṃkarāt kutas pravibhāgaḥ iti āśayavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti 
TV_3.17.6^8	 uttaram āha saḥ ayam iti abhisaṃbandhāt iti saṃketa upādhiḥ eka ākāra pratyayaḥ na tu tāttvikaḥ iti arthaḥ saṃketasya nimitta tā darśitā saṃketaḥ iti saptamyāḥ parama artham āha yaḥ tu śvetaḥ arthaḥ iti avasthā nava purāṇa tva ādayaḥ saha gataḥ saṃkīrṇaḥ evam ca pravibhāga saṃyamāt yoginaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām paśu mṛga sarīsṛpa vayaḥ prabhṛtīnām yāni rutāni tatra api avyaktam padam tad arthaḥ tad pratyayaḥ ca iti tat iha manuṣya vacana vācya pratyayeṣu kṛtaḥ saṃyamaḥ samāna jātīya tayā teṣu api kṛtaḥ eva iti teṣām rutam tad artha bhedam tat pratyayam ca yogī jānāti iti siddham 
TV_3.18.1–3.18.2^1	 saṃskāra sākṣāt karaṇāt pūrva jāti jñānam saṃskāra sākṣāt karaṇāt pūrva jāti jñānam jñāna jāḥ hi saṃskārāḥ smṛteḥ hetavaḥ avidyā ādi saṃskārāḥ avidyā ādīnām kleśānām hetavaḥ vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga rūpaḥ tasya hetavaḥ dharma adharma rūpāḥ pūrveṣu bhaveṣu abhisaṃskṛtāḥ niṣpāditāḥ sva kāraṇaiḥ yathāsaṃskṛtam vyañjanam kṛtam iti gamyate pariṇāma ceṣṭā nirodha śakti jīvanāni eva dharmāḥ cittasya tadvat aparidṛṣṭāḥ citta dharmāḥ teṣu śruteṣu anumiteṣu sa parikareṣu saṃyamaḥ saṃskārāṇām dvayeṣām sākṣāt kriyāyai samarthaḥ astu tatra saṃyamāt tad sākṣātkāraḥ pūrva jāti sākṣātkāraḥ tu kutas iti atas āha na ca deśa iti nimittam pūrva śarīram indriya ādi ca 
TV_3.18.2^2	 sa anubandha saṃskāra sākṣātkāraḥ eva na antarīyaka tayā jāti ādi sākṣātkāram ākṣipati iti arthaḥ sva saṃskāra saṃyamam parakīyeṣu atidiśati paratra api evam iti atra śraddhā utpāde hetum anubhavataḥ āvaṭyasya jaigīṣavyeṇa saṃvādam upanyasyati atra idam ākhyānam śrūyate iti mahākalpaḥ mahā sargaḥ tanudharaḥ iti nirmāṇa kāya saṃpad uktāḥ bhavyaḥ śobhanaḥ vigalita rajaḥ tamaḥ malaḥ iti arthaḥ pradhāna vaśi tvam aiśvaryam tena hi pradhānam vikṣobhya yasmai yādṛśīm kāya indriya saṃpadam ditsati tasmai tādṛśīm datte svakīyāni ca kāya indriya sahasrāṇi nirmāya antarikṣe divi bhuvi ca yatheccham viharati iti saṃtoṣaḥ hi tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ buddhi sattvasya praśānta tā dharmaḥ 
TV_3.19.1–3.20.2	 pratyayasya para citta jñānam pratyayasya para citta jñānam para pratyayasya cittamātrasya sākṣātkaraṇāt iti na ca tat sa ālambanam tasya aviṣayī bhūta tvāt yathā saṃskāra sākṣātkāraḥ tad anubandha pūrva janma sākṣātkāram ākṣipati evam para citta sākṣātkāraḥ api tad ālambana sākṣātkāram ākṣipet iti prāptaḥ āha na ca tat sa ālambanam tasya aviṣayī bhūta tvāt sa anubandha saṃskāra viṣayaḥ asau saṃyamaḥ ayam tu para citta mātra viṣayaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
TV_3.21.1–3.21.2	 kāya rūpa saṃyamāt tad grāhya śakti stambhe cakṣuṣprakāśa asaṃprayoge antardhānam kāya rūpa saṃyamāt tad grāhya śakti stambhe cakṣuṣprakāśa saṃprayoge antardhānam pañca ātmakaḥ kāyaḥ sa ca rūpavat tayā cākṣuṣaḥ bhavati rūpeṇa hi kāyaḥ ca tad rūpam ca cakṣuḥ grahaṇa karma śaktim anubhavati tatra yadā rūpe saṃyama viśeṣaḥ yoginā kriyate tadā rūpasya grāhya śaktiḥ rūpavat kāya pratyakṣa tā hetuḥ stambhyate tasmāt grāhya śakti stambhe sati antardhānam yoginaḥ tatas parakīya cakṣuḥ janitena prakāśena jñānena asaṃprayogaḥ cakṣuḥ jñāna aviṣaya tvam yoginaḥ kāyasya iti yāvat tasmin kartavye antardhānam kāraṇam iti arthaḥ etena iti kāya śabda sparśa rasa gandha saṃyamāt tad grāhya śakti stambhe śrotra tvac rasana ghrāṇa prakāśa asaṃprayoge antardhānam iti sūtram ūhanīyam 
TV_3.22.1–3.22.2^1	 sa upakramam nirupakramam ca karma tad saṃyamāt aparānta jñānam ariṣṭebhyaḥ vā sa upakramam nirupakramam ca karma tad saṃyamāt aparānta jñānam ariṣṭebhyaḥ vā āyuḥ vipākam ca karma dvividham sa upakramam nirupakramam ca yat khalu aika bhavikam karma jāti āyuḥ bhoga hetuḥ tat āyuḥ vipākam tat ca kiṃcid kāla anapekṣam eva bhoga dānāya prasthitam datta bahu bhogam alpa avaśiṣṭa phalam pravṛtta vyāpāram kevalam tad phalasya sahasā bhoktum ekena śarīreṇa aśakya tvāt vilambate tat idam sa upakramam upakramaḥ vyāpāraḥ tad sahitam iti arthaḥ tat eva tu datta stoka phalam tad kālam apekṣya phala dānāya vyāpriyamāṇam kādācid ka manda vyāpāram nirupakramam 
TV_3.22.2^2	 etat eva nidarśanābhyām viśadayati tatra yathā iti atra eva ati vaiśadyāya nidarśana antaram darśayati yathā vā agniḥ iti para antam mahāpralayam apekṣya aparāntaḥ maraṇam tasmin karmaṇi dharma adharmayoḥ saṃyamāt aparānta jñānam tatas ca yogī sa upakramam ātmanaḥ karma vijñāya bahūn kāyāt nirmāya sahasā phalam bhuktvā sva icchayā mriyate prāsaṅgikam āha ariṣṭebhyaḥ vā ari vat trāsayanti iti ariṣṭāni trividhāni maraṇa cihnāni viparītam vā sarvam māhendra jāla ādi vyatirekeṇa grāma nagara ādi svargam abhimanyate manuṣya lokam eva deva lokam iti 
TV_3.23.1–3.23.2	 maitrī ādiṣu balāni maitrī ādiṣu balāni maitrī ādiṣu saṃyamān maitrī ādi balāni asya bhavanti tatra maitrī bhāvanātaḥ balam yena jīva lokam sukhākaroti tatas sarva hitaḥ bhavati evam karuṇā balāt prāṇinaḥ duḥkhāt duḥkha hetoḥ vā samuddharati evam mudita abalāt jīva lokasya mādhyasthyam ādhatte vakṣyamāṇaupayikam bhāvanā kāraṇa tvam samādheḥ āha bhāvanātaḥ samādhiḥ yaḥ sa saṃyamaḥ yadi api dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi trayam eva saṃyamaḥ na samādhi mātram tathā api samādhi anantaram kārya utpādāt samādheḥ prādhānyāt tatra saṃyamaḥ upacaritaḥ kvacid bhāvanā samādhiḥ iti pāṭhaḥ tatra bhāvanā samādhī samūhasya saṃyamasya avayavau hetū bhavataḥ vīryam prayatnaḥ tena maitrī ādi balavataḥ puṃsaḥ sukhita ādiṣu pareṣām kartavyeṣu prayatnaḥ avandhyaḥ bhavati iti upekṣā audāsīnyam na tatra bhāvanā na api sukha ādi vat bhāvyam kiṃcid asti iti 
TV_3.24.1–3.26.2^1	 baleṣu hasti bala ādīni baleṣu hasti bala ādīni yasya bale saṃyamaḥ tasya balam labhate iti pravṛtti āloka nyāsāt sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa jñānam pravṛtti āloka nyāsāt sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa jñānam sūkṣme vyavahite viprakṛṣṭe vā arthe saṃyamena vinyasya tam adhigacchati bhuvana jñānam sūrye saṃyamāt bhuvana jñānam sūrye saṃyamāt ā dhruva āditas meru pṛṣṭhāt tat evam anena saṃgraha śloka antena saṃkṣepataḥ sapta lokān upanyasya vistareṇa āha tatra avīceḥ iti ghana śabdena pṛthivī ucyate bhūmiḥ sthānam iti arthaḥ ete mahā narakāḥ aneka upanaraka parivārāḥ boddhavyāḥ etān eva nāma antareṇa upasaṃharati mahā iti tasya sūrya pracārāt rātriṃdivam lagnam iva vartate yam eva asya bhāgam sūryaḥ tyajati tatra rātriḥ yam eva bhāgam alaṃkaroti tatra dinam iti sakala jambūdvīpa parimāṇam āha tat etat yojana śata sāhasram kiṃbhūtam yojanānām śata sāhasram iti āha sumeroḥ diśi diśi tad ardhena pañcāśat yojana sahasreṇa vyūḍham saṃkṣiptam yatas asya madhyasthaḥ sumeruḥ samudrāḥ ca sarṣapa rāśi kalpāḥ iti dviguṇāḥ dviguṇāḥ iti saṃbandhaḥ 
TV_3.26.2^2	 yathā sarṣapa rāśiḥ na vrīhi rāśiḥ iva ucchritaḥ na api bhūmi samaḥ tathā samudrāḥ api iti arthaḥ vicitraiḥ śailaiḥ avataṃsaiḥ iva saha vartante iti sa vicitra śaila avataṃsāḥ dvīpāḥ tat etat sarvam sa dvīpa vipinana ganagara nīradhi mālā valayam lokāloka parivṛtam viśvaṃbharā maṇḍalam brahmāṇḍa madhye vyūḍham saṃkṣiptam su pratiṣṭhitam saṃsthānam saṃniveśaḥ yasya tat tathā uktam ye yatra prativasanti tatra tān darśayati tatra pātālaḥ iti sumeroḥ saṃniveśam āha sumeruḥ iti tat evam bhūrlokam sa prakāram uktvā sa prakāram eva antarīkṣa lokam āha graha iti vikṣepaḥ vyāpāraḥ svar lokam ādarśayati māhendra nivāsinaḥ iti devanikāyāḥ deva jātayaḥ 
TV_3.26.2^3	 ṣaṇṇām api deva nikāyānām rūpa utkarṣam āha sarve saṃkalpa siddhāḥ iti saṃkalpa mātrāt eva eṣām viṣayāḥ upanamanti vṛndārakāḥ pūjyāḥ kāma bhoginaḥ maithuna priyāḥ aupapādika dehāḥ pitroḥ saṃyogam antareṇa akasmāt eva divyam śarīram eṣām dharma viśeṣa atisaṃskṛtebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ bhavati iti mahar lokam āha mahati iti mahābhūta vaśinaḥ yat yat etebhyaḥ rocate tat tat eva mahābhūtāni prayacchanti tad icchātaḥ ca mahābhūtāni tena tena saṃsthānena avatiṣṭhante dhyāna āhārāḥ dhyāna mātra tṛptāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ bhavanti janalokam āha prathamaḥ iti ukta krameṇa bhūta indriya vaśinaḥ iti bhūtāni pṛthivī ādīni indriyāṇi śrotra ādīni yathā niyoktum icchanti tathā eva niyujyante 
TV_3.26.2^4	 ukta krama apekṣayā dvitīyam brahmaṇaḥ tapolokam āha dvitīyaḥ iti bhūta indriya prakṛti vaśinaḥ iti prakṛtiḥ pañca tanmātrāṇi tad vaśinaḥ tad icchātaḥ hi tanmātrāṇi eva kāya ākāreṇa pariṇamantaḥ iti āgaminaḥ dviguṇa iti ābhāsvarebhyaḥ dviguṇa āyuṣaḥ mahā bhāsvarāḥ tebhyaḥ api dviguṇa āyuṣaḥ satya mahābhāsvarāḥ iti arthaḥ ūrdhvam iti ūrdhvam satya loke apratihata jñānāḥ avīceḥ tu prabhṛti ā tapolokam sūkṣma vyavahita ādi sarvam vijānanti iti arthaḥ tṛtīyam brahmaṇaḥ satya lokam āha tṛtīyaḥ iti akṛtaḥ bhavanasya gṛhasya nyāsaḥ yaiḥ te tathā uktāḥ ādhāra abhāvāt eva sva pratiṣṭhāḥ sveṣu śarīreṣu pratiṣṭhā yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ pradhāna vaśinaḥ tad icchātaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi pravartante yāvat sarga āyuṣaḥ tathā ca śrūyate 
TV_3.26.3–3.26.4^1	 brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padam iti tat evam caturṇām deva nikāyānām sādhāraṇa dharmān uktvā nāma viśeṣa grahaṇena dharma viśeṣān āha tatra iti acyutāḥ nāma devāḥ sthūla viṣaya dhyāna sukhāḥ tena te tṛpyanti śuddha nivāsāḥ nāma devāḥ sūkṣma viṣaya dhyāna sukhāḥ tena te tṛpyanti satya ābhāḥ nāma devāḥ indriya viṣaya dhyāna sukhāḥ tena te tṛpyanti saṃjñā saṃjñinaḥ nāma devāḥ asmitā mātra dhyāna sukhāḥ tena te tṛpyanti te ete sarve saṃprajñāta samādhim upāsate atha asaṃprajñāta samādhi niṣṭhāḥ videha prakṛti layāḥ kasmāt na loka madhye nyasyante iti atas āha videha prakṛti layāḥ tu iti buddhi vṛttimantaḥ hi darśita viṣayāḥ lokayātrām vahantaḥ lokeṣu vartante
