TV_3.26.4^2	 na ca evam videha prakṛti layāḥ sati api sa adhikāra tvaḥ iti arthaḥ tat etat ā satya lokam ā ca avīceḥ yoginā sākṣātkaraṇīyam sūrya dvāre suṣumnāyām nāḍyām na ca etāvatā api tad sākṣātkāraḥ bhavati iti atas āha evam tāvat anyatra api suṣumnāyāḥ anyatra api yoga upādhyāya upadiṣṭeṣu yāvat idam sarvam jagat dṛṣṭam iti buddhi sattvam hi svabhāvataḥ eva viśva prakāśana samartham tamaḥ malāvṛtam yatra eva rajasā udghāṭyate tat eva prakāśayati sūrya dvāra saṃyama udghāṭitam tu bhuvanam prakāśayati na ca evam anyatra api prasaṅgaḥ tad saṃyamasya tāvat mātra udghāṭana sāmarthyāt iti sarvam avadātam 
TV_3.27–31.1–3.27–31.6	 candre tārā vyūha jñānam dhruve tad gati jñānam nābhi cakre kāya vyūha jñānam kaṇṭha kūpe kṣudh pipāsā nivṛttiḥ kūrma nāḍyām sthairyam candre tārā vyūha jñānam dhruve tad gati jñānam nābhi cakre kāya vyūha jñānam kaṇṭha kūpe kṣudh pipāsā nivṛttiḥ kūrma nāḍyām sthairyam tatra tatra jijñāsāyām yoginaḥ tatra tatra saṃyamaḥ evam kṣudh pipāsā nivṛtti hetuḥ saṃyamaḥ sthairya hetuḥ ca sūtrapadaiḥ upadiṣṭaḥ bhāṣyeṇa ca nigada vyākhyātena vyākhyātaḥ iti na vyākhyātaḥ 
TV_3.32.1–3.33.2	 mūrdha jyotiṣi siddha darśanam mūrdha jyotiṣi siddha darśanam mūrdha śabdena suṣumnā nāḍī lakṣyate tatra saṃyamaḥ iti prātibhāt vā sarvam prātibhāt vā sarvam pratibhohaḥ tad bhavam prātibham prasaṃkhyāna hetu saṃyamavataḥ hi tad prakarṣe prasaṃkhyāna udaya pūrva liṅgam yat ūha jam jñānam tena sarvam vijānāti yogī tat ca prasaṃkhyāna saṃnidhāpanena saṃsārāt tārayati iti tārakam 
TV_3.34.1–3.34.2	 hṛdaye citta saṃvid hṛdaye citta saṃvid hṛdaya padam vyācaṣṭe yat idam asmin brahma pure bṛhat tvāt ātmā brahma tasya puram nilayaḥ tat dhi tatra vijānāti svam iti daharam gartam tat eva puṇḍarīkam adhomukham veśma manasaḥ citta saṃvedana tve hetum āha tatra vijñānam tatra saṃyamāt cittam vijānāti sva vṛtti viśiṣṭam 
TV_3.35.1–3.35.2^1	 sattva puruṣayoḥ atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ parārthāt sva artha saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam sattva puruṣayoḥ atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ parārthāt sva artha saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam yatra prakāśa rūpasya ati svacchasya nitānta abhibhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ tayā viveka khyāti rūpeṇa pariṇatasya buddhi sattvasya ātyantikaḥ caitanyāt asaṃkaraḥ tatra kā eva kathā rajaḥ tamasoḥ jaḍa svabhāvayoḥ iti āśayavān sūtrakāraḥ sattva puruṣayoḥ iti uvāca imam eva abhiprāyam gṛhītvā bhāṣya kāraḥ api āha buddhi sattvam prakhyā śīlam iti na prakhyā śīla mātram api tu viveka khyāti rūpeṇa pariṇatam atas nitānta śuddha prakāśa tayā atyanta sārūpyam caitanyena iti saṃkaraḥ iti atas āha samānā iti sattvena upanibandhanam avinābhāvaḥ saṃbandhaḥ samānam sattva upanibandhanam yayoḥ rajaḥ tamasoḥ te tathā ukte 
TV_3.35.2^2	 vaśīkāraḥ abhibhavaḥ asaṃkaram āha tasmāt ca iti cakāraḥ api arthaḥ na kevalam rajaḥ tamobhyām iti arthaḥ pariṇāminaḥ iti vaidharmyam apariṇāminaḥ puruṣāt uktam pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ śānta ghora mūḍha rūpāyāḥ buddheḥ caitanya bimba udgrāheṇa caitanyasya śānta ādi ākāra adhya āropaḥ candramasaḥ iva svaccha salila pratibimbitasya tad kampāt kampana āropaḥ bhoga hetum āha darśita viṣaya tvāt iti asakṛt vyākhyātam nanu buddhi sattvam astu puruṣa bhinnam bhogaḥ tu puṃsaḥ kutas bhidyate iti atas āha sa bhoga pratyayaḥ bhoga rūpaḥ pratyayaḥ sattvasya atas para artha tvāt dṛśyaḥ bhogyaḥ 
TV_3.35.2^3	 sattvam hi para artham saṃhata tvāt tad dharmaḥ ca bhogaḥ iti saḥ api para arthaḥ yasmai ca parasmai asau tasya bhoktuḥ bhogyaḥ athavā anukūla pratikūla vedanīyaḥ tu sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ bhogaḥ na ca ayam ātmānam eva anukūlayati pratikūlayati vā sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt atas anukūlanīya pratikūlanīya arthaḥ bhogaḥ sa bhoktā ātmā tasya dṛśyaḥ bhogyaḥ iti yaḥ tu tasmāt para arthāt viśiṣṭaḥ iti para arthāt iti pañcamī anya pada adhyāhāreṇa vyākhyātāḥ syāt etat puruṣa viṣayā ced prajñā hanta bhoḥ puruṣaḥ prajñāyāḥ prajñeya iti prajñā antaram eva tatra tatra iti anavasthāpātaḥ iti atas āha na ca puruṣa pratyayena iti 
TV_3.35.2^4	 ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ cityā jaḍaḥ prakāśyate na jaḍena citiḥ puruṣa pratyayaḥ tu acit ātmā katham cit ātmānam prakāśayet cit ātmā tu apara adhīna prakāśaḥ jaḍam prakāśayati iti yuktam buddhi sattva ātmanā iti acit rūpa tādātmyena jaḍa tvam āha buddhi sattva gata puruṣa pratibimba ālambanāt puruṣa ālambanam na tu puruṣa prakāśanāt puruṣa ālambanam buddhi sattvam eva tu tena pratyayena saṃkrānta puruṣa pratibimbam puruṣa= chāyā āpannam caitanyam ālambataḥ iti puruṣa arthaḥ atra eva śrutim udāharati tathā hi uktam īśvareṇa vijñātāram iti na kenacid iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.36.1–3.36.2	 tatas prātibha śrāvaṇa vedanā ādarśa āsvāda vārtāḥ jāyante sa ca sva artha saṃyamaḥ na yāvat pradhānam sva kāryam puruṣa jñānam abhinirvartayati tāvat tasya purastāt yāḥ vibhūtīḥ ādhatte tāḥ sarvāḥ darśayati tatas prātibha śrāvaṇa vedanā ādarśa āsvāda vārtāḥ jāyante tat anena yoga ja dharma anugṛhītānām manaḥ śrotra tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇānām yathāsaṃkhyam prātibha jñāna divya śabda ādi aparokṣa hetu bhāvāḥ uktāḥ śrotra ādīnām pañcānām divya śabda ādi upalambhakānām tān trikyaḥ saṃjñāḥ śrāvaṇa ādyāḥ sugamam bhāṣyam 
TV_3.37.1–3.37.2	 te samādhau upasargāḥ vyutthāne siddhayaḥ kadācid ātma viṣaya saṃyame pravṛttaḥ tad prabhāvāt amūḥ artha antara siddhīḥ adhigamya kṛtārtham anyaḥ saṃyamāt viramet atas āha te samādhau upasargāḥ vyutthāne siddhayaḥ vyutthita cittaḥ hi tāḥ siddhīḥ abhimanyate janma durgataḥ iva draviṇa kaṇikām api draviṇa saṃbhāram yoginā tu samāhita cittena upanatābhyaḥ api tābhyaḥ virantavyam abhisaṃhita tāpa trayā ātyantika upaśama rūpa parama puruṣa arthaḥ sa khalu ayam katham tad pratyanīkāsu siddhiṣu rajyeta iti sūtra bhāṣyayoḥ arthaḥ 
TV_3.38.1–3.38.2	 bandha kāraṇa śaithilyāt pracāra saṃvedanāt ca cittasya para śarīra āveśaḥ tat evam jñāna rūpam aiśvaryam puruṣa darśana antam saṃyama phalam uktvā kriyā rūpam aiśvaryam saṃyama phalam āha bandha kāraṇa śaithilyāt pracāra saṃvedanāt ca cittasya para śarīra āveśaḥ samādhi balāt iti bandha kāraṇa viṣaya saṃyama balāt prādhānyāt samādhi grahaṇam pracarati anena asmin iti pracāraḥ cittasya gamāgama adhvānaḥ nāḍyaḥ tasmin pracāre saṃyamāt tad vedanam tasmāt ca bandha kāraṇa śaithilyāt na tena pratibadhyate apratibaddham api unmārgeṇa gacchan na sva śarīrāt apratyūham niṣkrāmati na ca para śarīram āviśati tasmāt tad pracāraḥ api jñātavyaḥ indriyāṇi ca citta anusārīṇi para śarīre yathā adhiṣṭhānam niviśantaḥ iti 
TV_3.39.1–3.39.3	 udāna jayāt jala paṅka kaṇṭaka ādiṣu asaṅgaḥ utkrāntiḥ ca udāna jayāt jala paṅka kaṇṭaka ādiṣu asaṅgaḥ utkrāntiḥ ca samasta indriya vṛttiḥ jīvanam prāṇa ādi lakṣaṇā prāṇa ādayaḥ lakṣaṇam yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā dvayi indriyāṇām vṛttiḥ bāhya abhyantarī ca bāhyā rūpa ādi ālocana lakṣaṇā ābhyantarī tu jīvanam sā hi prayatna bhedaḥ śarīra upagṛhīta māruta kriyā bheda hetuḥ sarva karaṇa sādhāraṇaḥ yathā āhuḥ sāmānya karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca iti 
TV_3.39.4	 taiḥ asya lakṣaṇīya tvāt tasya prayatnasya kriyā kāryam pañcatayī prāṇaḥ ā nāsikā agrāt ā ca hṛdayāt avasthitaḥ aśita pīta āhāra pariṇati bhedam rasam tatra tatra sthāne samam anurūpam nayan samānaḥ ā hṛdayāt ā ca nābheḥ asya avasthānam mūtra purīṣa garbha ādīnām apanayana hetuḥ apānaḥ ā nābheḥ ā ca pāda talāt asya vṛttiḥ unnayanāt ūrdhvam nayanāt rasa ādīnām udānaḥ ā nāsikā agrāt ā ca śirasaḥ vṛttiḥ asya vyāpī vyānaḥ eṣām uktānām pradhānam prāṇaḥ tad utkrame sarva utkrama śruteḥ prāṇam utkrāmantam anu sarve prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti iti tat evam prāṇa ādīnām kriyā sthāna bhedena bhedam pratipādya sūtra artham avatārayati udāna jayāt iti udāne kṛta saṃyamaḥ tad jayāt jala ādibhiḥ na pratihanyate utkrāntiḥ ca arciḥ ādi mārgeṇa bhavati prāyaṇa kāle tasmāt tām utkrāntim vaśi tvena pratipadyate prāṇa ādi saṃyamāt tat vijaye bhūta jayaḥ etāḥ kriyāḥ sthāna vijaya ādi bhedāt pratipattavyāḥ 
TV_3.40.1–3.41.2^1	 samāna jayāt jvalanam samājanayāt jvalanam tejasaḥ śārīrasya upadhmānam uttejanam śrotra ākāśayoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt divyam śrotram sva artha saṃyamāt anvācaya śiṣṭam śrāvaṇa ādi uktam saṃprati śrāvaṇa ādi arthāt eva saṃyamāt śrāvaṇa ādi bhavati iti āha śrotra ākāśayoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt divyam śrotram saṃyama viṣayam śrotra ākāśayoḥ saṃbandham ādhāra ādheya bhāvam āha sarva śrotrāṇām āhaṃkārikāṇām api ākāśam karṇa śaṣkulī vivaram pratiṣṭhā tad āyatanam śrotram tad upakāra apakārābhyām śrotrasya upakāra apakāra darśanāt śabdānām ca śrotra sahakāriṇām pārthiva ādi śabda grahaṇe kartavye karṇa śaṣkulī suṣira varti śrotram sva āśrayana bhoga tā sā dhāraṇa śabdam apekṣate gandha ādi guṇa sahakāribhiḥ ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ bāhyam pṛthivī ādi varti gandha ādi ālocane kārye dṛṣṭam āhaṃkārikam api ghrāṇrasana tvac cakṣuḥ śrotram bhūta adhiṣṭhānam eva bhūta upakāra apakārābhyām ghrāṇa ādīnām upakāra apakāra darśanāt iti uktam 
TV_3.41.2^2	 tat ca idam śrotram āhaṃkārikam ayaḥ pratimam ayaskānta maṇi kalpena vaktṛ vaktra samutpannena vaktra sthena śabdena ākṛṣṭam sva vṛtti paramparayā vaktṛ vaktram āgatam śabdam ālocayati tathā ca diś deśa varti śabda pratītiḥ prāṇa bhṛt mātrasya na asati bādhake apramāṇīkṛtā bhaviṣyati iti tathā ca pañcaśikhasya vākyam tulya deśa śravaṇānām eka deśa śruti tvam sarveṣām bhavati iti tulya deśāni śravaṇāni śrotrāṇi yeṣām caitra ādīnām te tathā uktāḥ sarveṣām śravaṇāni ākāśa vartīni iti arthaḥ tat ca śrotra adhiṣṭhānam ākāśam śabda guṇa tanmātrāt utpannam śabda guṇakam yena śabdena sahakāriṇā pārthiva ādīn śabdān gṛhṇāti tasmāt sarveṣām eka jātīyā śrutiḥ śabdaḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.41.2^3	 tat anena śrotra adhiṣṭhāna tvam ākāśasya śabda guṇa tvam ca darśitam iti tat ca eka deśa śruti tvam ākāśasya liṅgam sā hi eka jātīyā śabdavyañjikā śrutiḥ yad āśrayā tat eva ākāśa śabda vācyam na hi īdṛśīm śrutim antareṇa śabda vyaktiḥ na ca īdṛśī śrutiḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇaḥ tasya sva ātmani vyaṅgya vyañjaka tva anupapatteḥ iti anāvaraṇam ca ākāśa liṅgam yadi ākāśam na abhaviṣyat anyonya saṃpiṇḍitāni mūrtāni na sūcībhiḥ api abhetsyanta tatas ca sarvaiḥ eva sarvam āvṛtam syāt na ca mūrta dravya abhāva mātrāt eva anāvaraṇam asya abhāvasya bhāva āśrita tvena tad abhāve abhāvāt na ca citi śaktiḥ tad āśrayā bhavitum arhati apariṇāmi tayā avacchedaka tva abhāvāt na ca diś kāla ādayaḥ pṛthivī ādi dravya vyatiriktāḥ santi 
TV_3.41.2^4–3.42.2	 tasmāt tādṛśaḥ pariṇati bhedaḥ nabhasaḥ eva iti sarvam avadātam anāvaraṇe ca ākāśa liṅge siddhe yatra yatra anāvaraṇam tatra tatra sarvatra ākāśam iti sarva gata tvam api ākāśasya siddham iti āha tathā amūrtasya iti śrotra sadbhāve pramāṇam āha śabda grahaṇa iti kriyā hi karaṇa sādhyāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ yathā chidādiḥ vā asya ādi sādhyāḥ tat iha śabda grahaṇa kriyayā api karaṇa sādhyayā bhavitavyam yat ca karaṇam tat ca śrotram iti atha asyāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ eva kasmāt karaṇam na bhavanti iti atas āha badhira ābadhirayoḥ iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām avadhāraṇam upalakṣaṇam ca etat tvac vātayoḥ cakṣuḥ tejasaḥ rasanā udakayoḥ nāsikā pṛthivyoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt divya tvac ādi api ūhanīyam kāya ākāśayoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt laghu tūla samāpatteḥ ca ākāśa gamanam kāya akaśayoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt laghu tūla samāpatteḥ ca ākāśa gamanam kāya ākāśa saṃbandha saṃyamāt vā laghuni vā tūla ādau kṛta saṃyamāt samāpattim cetasaḥ tad sthatad añjana tām labdhvā iti siddhi kramam āha jalaḥ iti 
TV_3.43.1–3.43.2	 bahis akalpitā vṛttiḥ mahāvidehā tatas prakāśa āvaraṇa kṣayaḥ aparam api para śarīra āveśa hetum saṃyamam kleśa karma vipāka kṣaya hetum ca āha bahis akalpitā vṛttiḥ mahāvidehā tatas prakāśa āvaraṇa kṣayaḥ videhām āha śarīrāt iti akalpitāyāḥ mahāvidehāyāḥ yaḥ upāyaḥ tad pradarśanāya kalpitām videhām āha sā yadi iti vṛtti mātram kalpanā jñāna mātram tena mahāvidehām āha yā tu iti upāya upeyate kalpita akalpitayoḥ āha tatra iti kim para śarīra āveśa mātram itas na iti āha tatas ca iti tatas dhāraṇātas mahāvidehāyāḥ manaḥ pravṛtteḥ siddhiḥ kleśaḥ ca karma ca tābhyām vipāka trayam jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ tat etat rajaḥ tamaḥ mūlam vigalita rajaḥ tamasaḥ sattva mātrāt viveka khyāti mātra samutpādāt tat etat vipāka trayam rajaḥ tamaḥ mūla tayā tad ātmakam sat buddhi sattvam āvṛṇoti tad kṣayāt ca nirāvaraṇam yogi cittam yatheccham viharati vijānāti ca iti 
TV_3.44.1–3.44.2	 sthūla svarūpa sūkṣma anvaya arthavattva saṃyamāt bhūta jayaḥ sthūla svarūpa sūkṣma anvaya arthavattva saṃyamāt bhūta jayaḥ sthūlam ca svarūpam ca sūkṣmam ca anvayaḥ ca arthavat tvam ca iti sthūla svarūpa sūkṣma anvaya arthavat tvāni teṣu saṃyamāt tad jayaḥ sthūlam āha tatra iti pārthivāḥ pāthasīyāḥ taijasāḥ vāyavīyāḥ ākāśīyāḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ yathāsaṃbhavam viśeṣāḥ ṣaḍjagāndhāra ādayaḥ śīta uṣṇa ādayaḥ nīla pīta ādayaḥ kaṣāya madhura ādayaḥ surabhi a ādayaḥ ete hi nāma rūpa prayojanaiḥ para sparataḥ bhidyante iti viśeṣāḥ eteṣām pañca pṛthivyām gandha varjam catvāraḥ apsu gandha rasa varjam trayaḥ tejasi gandha rasa rūpa varjam dvau nabhasvati śabdaḥ eva ākāśe te eva īdṛśāḥ viśeṣāḥ saha ākāra ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ sthūla śabdena paribhāṣitāḥ śāstre tatra api pārthivāḥ tāvat dharmāḥ 
TV_3.44.3–3.44.11	 ākāraḥ gauravam raukṣyam varaṇam sthairyam eva ca vṛttiḥ bhedaḥ kṣamā kārṣṇyam kāṭhinyam sarva bhogya tā apām dharmāḥ snehaḥ saukṣmyam prabhā śauklyam mārdavam gauravam ca yat śaityam rakṣā pavitra tvam saṃdhānam ca audakāḥ guṇāḥ taijasāḥ dharmāḥ ūrdhva bhāj pācakam dagdhṛ pāvakam laghu bhāsvaram pradhvaṃsi ojasvi vai tejaḥ pūrvābhyām bhinna lakṣaṇam vāyavīyāḥ dharmāḥ tiryagyānam pavitra tvam ākṣepaḥ nodanam balam calam acchāyatā raukṣyam vāyoḥ dharmāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ ākāśīyāḥ dharmāḥ sarvatas gatiḥ avyūhaḥ aviṣṭambhaḥ ca iti te trayaḥ ākāśa dharmāḥ vyākhyātāḥ pūrva dharma vilakṣaṇāḥ iti 
TV_3.44.12–3.44.13	 te ete ākāra prabhṛtayaḥ dharmāḥ taiḥ saha iti ākāraḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣaḥ go tva ādiḥ dvitīyam rūpam āha dvitīyam rūpam sva sāmānyam mūrtiḥ sāṃsiddhikam kāṭhinyam snehaḥ jalam mṛjā puṣṭi bala ādhāna hetuḥ vahniḥ uṣṇatodarye saurye bhaume ca sarvatra eva tejasi samaveta uṣṇa tā iti sarvam ca etat dharma dharmiṇoḥ abheda vivakṣayā abhidhānam vāyuḥ praṇāmī vahana śīlaḥ tat āha calanena tṛṇa ādīnām śarīrasya aṭanena ca sarvagam vāyu sāmānyam nāmi tvam anumīyate 
TV_3.44.14^1	 sarvatas gatiḥ ākāśaḥ sarvatra śabda upalabdhi darśanāt śrotra āśraya ākāśa guṇena hi śabdena pārthiva ādi śabda upalabdhiḥ iti upapāditam adhastāt etat sva rūpa śabdena uktam asya eva mūrti ādi sāmānyasya śabda ādayaḥ ṣaḍja ādayaḥ uṣṇa tva ādayaḥ śukla tva ādayaḥ kaṣāya tva ādayaḥ surabhi tva ādayaḥ mūrti ādīnām sāmānyānām bhedāḥ sāmānyāni api mūrti ādīni jambīra panasa āmalaka phala ādīni rasa ādi bhedāt parasparam vyāvartante tena eteṣām ete rasa ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ tathā ca uktam eka jāti samanvitānām pratyekam pṛthivī ādīnām ekaikayā jātyā mūrti sneha ādinā samanvitānām eṣām ṣaḍja ādi dharma mātra vyāvṛttiḥ iti tat evam sāmānyam mūrti ādi uktam viśeṣāḥ ca śabda ādayaḥ uktāḥ ye ca āhuḥ sāmānya viśeṣa āśrayaḥ dravyam iti tān pratyāha sāmānya viśeṣa samudāyaḥ atra darśane dravyam ye api tad āśrayaḥ dravyam āsthiṣata taiḥ api tad samudāyaḥ anubhūyamānaḥ na apahnotavyaḥ na ca tad apahnave tayoḥ ādhāraḥ dravyam iti bhavati tasmāt tat eva astu dravyam 
TV_3.44.14^2	 na tu tābhyām tad samudāyāt ca tad ādhāram aparam dravyam upalabhāmahe grāvabhyaḥ grāva samudāyāt iva ca tad ādhāram aparam pṛthagvidham śikharam samūhaḥ dravyam iti uktam tatra samūha mātram dravyam iti bhrama apanuttaye samūha viśeṣaḥ dravyam iti nirdhārayitum samūha prakārān āha dviṣṭhaḥ hi iti yasmāt evam tasmāt na samūha mātram dravyam iti arthaḥ dvābhyām prakārābhyām tiṣṭhati iti dviṣṭhaḥ ekam prakāram āha pratyasta mitā iti pratyastam itaḥ bhedaḥ yeṣām avayavānām te tathā uktāḥ pratyasta mita bhedāḥ avayavāḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ etat uktam bhavati śarīra vṛkṣa yūtha vana śabdebhyaḥ samūhaḥ pratīyamānaḥ apratīta avayava bhedaḥ tad vācaka śabda aprayogāt samūhaḥ ekaḥ avagamyate iti yuta ayuta siddha avayava tvena cetana acetana tvena ca udāharaṇa catuṣṭayam yuta ayutasiddha avayava tvam ca agre vakṣyate dvitīyam prakāram āha śabdena upātta bheda avayava anugataḥ samūhaḥ ubhaye deva manuṣyāḥ iti deva manuṣyāḥ iti hi śabdena ubhaya śabda vācyasya samūhasya bhāgau bhinnau upāttau 
TV_3.44.14^3	 nanu ubhaya śabdāt tāvat avayava bhedaḥ na pratīyate tat katham upātta bheda avayava anugataḥ iti atas āha tābhyām bhāgābhyām eva samūhaḥ abhidhīyate ubhaya śabdena bhāga dvaya vāci śabda sahitena samūhaḥ vācyaḥ vākyasya vākya artha vācaka tvāt iti bhāvaḥ punar dvaividhyam āha sa ca iti bhedena ca abhedena ca vivakṣitaḥ bheda vivakṣitam āha āmrāṇām vanam brāhmaṇānām saṃghaḥ iti bhedaḥ eva ṣaṣṭhī śruteḥ yathā gargāṇām gauḥ iti abheda vivakṣitam āha āmravaṇam brāhmaṇa saṃghaḥ iti āmrāḥ ca te vanam ca iti samūha samūhinoḥ abhedam vivakṣitvā sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti arthaḥ vidha antaram āha sa punar dvividhaḥ yutasiddha avayavaḥ samūhaḥ yuta siddhāḥ pṛthak siddhāḥ sa antarālāḥ avayavāḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ yūtham vanam iti sa antarālāḥ hi tad avayavāḥ vṛkṣāḥ ca gāvaḥ ca ayutasiddha avayavaḥ ca samūhaḥ vṛkṣaḥ gauḥ paramāṇuḥ iti nirantarāḥ hi tad avayavāḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ vā sāsna ādayaḥ vā iti 
TV_3.44.14^4	 tat eteṣu samūheṣu dravya bhūtam samūham nirdhārayati ayutasiddhā iti tat evam prāsaṅgikam dravyam vyutpādya prakṛtam upasaṃharati etat sva rūpam iti uktam iti tṛtīyam rūpam vivakṣuḥ pṛcchati atha iti uttaram āha tanmātram iti tasya ekaḥ avayavaḥ parimāṇa bhedaḥ paramāṇuḥ sāmānyam mūrtiḥ śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ tad ātmā ayutasiddhāḥ nirantarāḥ ye avayavāḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ tad bhedeṣu anugataḥ samudāyaḥ yathā ca paramāṇuḥ sūkṣmam rūpam evam sarva tanmātrāṇi sūkṣmam rūpam iti upasaṃharati etat iti atha bhūtānām caturtham rūpam khyāti kriyā sthiti śīlāḥ guṇāḥ kārya svabhāvam anupatitum anugantum śīlam yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ atas eva anvaya śabdena uktāḥ atha eṣām pañcamam rūpam arthavat tvam vivṛṇoti bhoga iti nanu evam api santu guṇāḥ arthavantaḥ tad kāryāṇām tu kutas arthavat tvam iti atas āha guṇāḥ iti bhautikāḥ go ghaṭa ādayaḥ tat evam saṃyama viṣayam uktvā saṃyamam tad phalam ca āha teṣu iti bhūta prakṛtayaḥ bhūta svabhāvāḥ 
TV_3.45.1–3.45.2^1	 tatas aṇima ādi prādurbhāvaḥ kāya saṃpad tad dharmānabhighātaḥ ca saṃkalpa anuvidhāne bhūtānām kim yoginaḥ sidhyati iti atas āha tatas aṇima ādi prādurbhāvaḥ kāya saṃpad tad dharmānabhighātaḥ ca sthūla saṃyama jayāt catasraḥ siddhayaḥ bhavanti iti āha tatra aṇimā mahān api bhavati aṇuḥ laghimā mahān api laghuḥ bhūtvā iṣīkātūlaḥ iva ākāśe viharati mahima alpaḥ api nāga naga gagana parimāṇaḥ bhavati prāptiḥ sarve bhāvāḥ saṃnihitāḥ bhavanti yoginaḥ tat yathā bhūmiṣṭhaḥ eva aṅguli agreṇa spṛśati candramasam svarūpa saṃyama vijayāt siddhim āha prākāmyam icchā anabhighātaḥ na asya rūpam bhūta svarūpaiḥ mūrti ādibhiḥ hanyate bhūmau unmajjati nimajjati ca yathā udake sūkṣma viṣaya saṃyama jayāt siddhim āha vaśitvam bhūtāni pṛthivī ādīni bhautikāni go ghaṭa ādīni teṣu vaśī svatantraḥ bhavati teṣām tu avaśyaḥ tad kāraṇa tanmātra pṛthivī ādi parama aṇu vaśīkārāt tad kārya vaśīkāra ḥ tena yāni yathā avasthāpayati tāni tathā avatiṣṭhantaḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.45.2^2	 anvaya viṣaya saṃyama jayāt siddhim āha īśitṛ tvam teṣām bhūta bhautikānām vijita mūla prakṛtiḥ san yaḥ prabhava utpādaḥ yaḥ ca api ayaḥ vināśaḥ yaḥ ca vyūhaḥ yathāvat avasthāpanam teṣām īṣṭe arthavat tva saṃyamāt siddhim āha yatra kāmāvasāyi tvam satya saṃkalpa tā vijita guṇa arthavat tvaḥ hi yogī yat yad artha tayā saṃkalpayati tat tasmai prayojanāya kalpate viṣam api amṛta kārye saṃkalpya bhojayan jīvayati iti syāt etat yathā śakti viparyāsam karoti evam padārtha viparyāsam api kasmāt na karoti tathā ca candramasam ādityam kuryāt kuhūm ca sinīvālīm iti atas āha na ca śaktaḥ api iti na khalu ete yatra kāmāvasāyinaḥ tatrabhavataḥ parameśvarasya ājñām atikramitum utsahante śaktayaḥ tu padārthānām jāti deśa kāla avasthā bhedena aniyata svabhāvāḥ iti yujyate tāsu tad icchā anuvidhānam iti etāni aṣṭau aiśvaryāṇi tad dharmānabhighātaḥ iti aṇima ādi prādurbhāvaḥ iti anena eva tad dharma anabhighāta siddhau punar upādānam kāya siddhi vat etat sūtra upabaddha sakala viṣaya saṃyama phalavat tva jñāpanāya sugamam anyat 
TV_3.46.1–3.47.2^1	 rūpa lāvaṇya bala vajra saṃhanana tvāni kāya saṃpad kāya saṃpadam āha rūpa lāvaṇya bala vajra saṃhanana tvāni kāya saṃpad vajrasya iva saṃhananam avayava vyūhaḥ dṛḍhaḥ nibiḍaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ grahaṇa svarūpa asmita anvaya arthavattva saṃyamāt indriya jayaḥ jita bhūtasya yoginaḥ indriya jaya upāyam āha grahaṇa svarūpa asmita anvaya arthavattva saṃyamāt indriya jayaḥ grahaṇam ca svarūpam ca asmitā ca anvayaḥ ca arthavat tvam ca teṣu saṃyamaḥ tasmāt iti arthaḥ gṛhītiḥ grahaṇam tat ca grāhya adhīna nirūpaṇam iti grāhyam darśayati sāmānya viśeṣa ātmā iti grāhyam uktvā grahaṇam āha teṣu iti vṛttiḥ ālocanam viṣaya ākārā pariṇatiḥ iti yāvat ye tu āhuḥ sāmānya mātra gocara indriya vṛttiḥ iti tān pratyāha na ca iti gṛhyate iti grahaṇam na sāmānya mātra gocaram grahaṇam bāhya indriya tantram hi manaḥ bāhye pravartate anyathā andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgāt tat iha yadi na viśeṣa viṣayam indriyam tena asau anālocitaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti katham manasā anuvyavasīyeta 
TV_3.47.2^2	 tasmāt sāmānya viśeṣa viṣayam indriya ālocanam iti tat etat grahaṇam indriyāṇām prathamam rūpam dvitīyam rūpam āha svarūpam punar iti ahaṃkāraḥ hi sattva bhāgena ātmīyena indriyāṇi ajījanat atas yat tatra karaṇa tvam sāmānyam yat ca niyata rūpa ādi viṣaya tvam viśeṣaḥ tat ubhayam api prakāśa ātmakam iti arthaḥ teṣām tṛtīyam rūpam iti ahaṃkāraḥ hi indriyāṇām kāraṇam iti yatra indriyāṇi tatra tena bhavitavyam iti sarva indriya sādhāraṇyāt sāmānyam indriyāṇām iti arthaḥ caturtham rūpam iti guṇānām hi dvairūpyam vyavaseya ātmaka tvam vyavasāya ātmaka tvam ca tatra vyavaseya ātmaka tām grāhyatām āsthāya pañca tanmātrāṇi bhūta bhautikāni nirmimīte vyavasāya ātmaka tvam tu grahaṇa rūpam āsthāya sa ahaṃkārāṇi indriyāṇi iti arthaḥ śeṣam sugamam 
TV_3.48.1–3.48.2	 tatas manojavi tvam vikaraṇa bhāvaḥ pradhāna jayaḥ ca pañca rūpa indriya jayāt siddhīḥ āha tatas manojavi tvam vikaraṇa bhāvaḥ pradhāna jayaḥ ca videhānām indriyāṇām karaṇa bhāvaḥ vikaraṇa bhāvaḥ deśaḥ kāśmīra ādiḥ kālaḥ atīta ādiḥ viṣayaḥ sūkṣma ādiḥ sa anvaya indriya jayāt sarva prakṛti vikāra vaśi tvam pradhāna jayaḥ tāḥ etāḥ siddhayaḥ madhupratīkāḥ iti ucyante yoga śāstra niṣṇātaiḥ syāt etat indriya jayāt indriyāṇi sa viṣayāṇi vaśyāni bhavantu pradhāna ādīnām tad kāraṇānām kim āyātam iti atas āha etāḥ ca iti karaṇānām indriyāṇām pañca rūpāṇi grahaṇa ādīni teṣām jayāt etat uktam bhavati na indriya mātra jayasya etāḥ siddhayaḥ api tu pañca rūpasya tad antargatam ca pradhāna ādi iti 
TV_3.49.1–3.49.2	 sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātrasya sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam sarvajñātṛ tvam ca te ete jñāna kriyā rūpa aiśvarya hetavaḥ saṃyamāḥ sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa ca sva siddhi upasaṃhāra saṃpādita śraddhā dvāreṇa yad arthāḥ tasyāḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyāteḥ avāntara vibhūtīḥ darśayati sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātrasya sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam sarvajñātṛ tvam ca nirdhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ mala tayā vaiśāradyam tatas parā vaśīkāra saṃjñā rajaḥ tamobhyām upaplutam hi citta sattvam avaśyam āsīt tad upaśame tu tad vaśyam yoginaḥ vaśinaḥ tasmin vaśye yoginaḥ sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātra rūpa pratiṣṭhasya sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam etat eva vivṛṇoti sarva ātmānaḥ iti vyavasāya vyavaseya ātmānaḥ jaḍa prakāśa rūpāḥ iti arthaḥ tat anena kriyā aiśvaryam uktam jñāna aiśvaryam āha sarvajñātṛ tvam iti asyāḥ api dvividhāyāḥ siddheḥ vairāgyāya yogi jana prasiddhām saṃjñām āha eṣā viśoka iti kleśāḥ ca bandhanāni ca karmāṇi tāni kṣīṇāni yasya sa tathā 
TV_3.50.1–3.50.2	 tad vairāgyāt api doṣa bīja kṣaye kaivalyam saṃyama antarāṇām puruṣa artha ābhāsa phala tvāt viveka khyāti saṃyama artha tām darśayitum viveka khyāteḥ para vairāgya upajanana dvāreṇa kaivalyam phalam āha tad vairāgyāt api doṣa bīja kṣaye kaivalyam yadā asya yoginaḥ kleśa karma kṣayaḥ evam jñānam bhavati kiṃbhūtam iti āha sattvasya ayam viveka pratyayaḥ dharmaḥ śeṣam tatra tatra vyākhyāta tvāt sugamam 
TV_3.51.1–3.51.2^1	 sthāni upanimantraṇe saṅga smayā karaṇam punar aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt saṃprati kaivalya sādhane pravṛttasya yoginaḥ pratyūha saṃbhave tad nirākaraṇa kāraṇam upadiśati sthāni upanimantraṇe saṅga smayā karaṇam punar aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt sthānāni yeṣām santi te sthāninaḥ mahā indra ādayaḥ taiḥ upanimantraṇam tasmin saṅgaḥ ca smayaḥ ca na kartavyaḥ punar aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt tatra yam devāḥ sthānaiḥ upamantrayante tam yoginam ekam nirdhārayitum yāvantaḥ yoginaḥ saṃbhavanti tāvataḥ eva āha catvāraḥ iti tatra prāthamakalpikasya svarūpam āha tatra abhyāsi iti pravṛtta mātram na punar vaśīkṛtam jyotiḥ jñānam para citta ādi viṣayam yasya sa tathā dvitīyam āha ṛtaṃbhara prajñaḥ iti yatra idam uktam ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā iti sa hi bhūta indriyāṇi jigīṣuḥ tṛtīyam āha bhūta indriya jayī iti tena hi sthūla ādi saṃyamena grahaṇa ādi saṃyamena ca bhūta indriyāṇi jitāni 
TV_3.51.2^2	 tam eva āha sarveṣu bhāviteṣu niṣpāditeṣu bhūta indriya jayāt para citta ādi jñāna ādiṣu kṛta rakṣā bandhaḥ yatas tebhyaḥ na cyavate bhāvanīyeṣu niṣpādanīyeṣu viśoka ādiṣu para vairāgya paryanteṣu kartavya sādhanavān puruṣa prayatnasya sādhana viṣayasya eva sādhya niṣpādaka tvāt caturtham āha caturthaḥ iti tasya hi bhagavataḥ jīvanmuktasya carama dehasya citta pratisargaḥ ekaḥ arthaḥ tat eteṣu yogiṣu upanimantraṇa viṣayam yoginam avadhārayati tatra madhumatīm iti prāthama kalpike tāvat mahā indra ādīnām tad prāpti śaṅkā eva na asti tṛtīyaḥ api taiḥ na upanimantraṇīyaḥ bhūta indriya vaśi tvena eva tad prāpteḥ caturthaḥ api para vairāgya saṃpatteḥ āsaṅga śaṅkā dūra utsāritā eva iti pāriśeṣyāt dvitīyaḥ eva ṛtaṃbhara prajñaḥ tad upanimantraṇa viṣayaḥ iti vaihāyasam ākāśa gāmi akṣayam avināśi ajaram sadā abhinavam smaya karaṇe doṣam āha smayāt ayam iti smayāt susthitaṃmanyaḥ na anitya tām bhāvayiṣyati na tasyām praṇidhāsyati iti arthaḥ sugamam anyat 
TV_3.52.1–3.52.2^1^1	 kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ saṃyamāt viveka jam jñānam uktā kvacid kvacid saṃyamāt sarvajña tā sā ca na niḥśeṣa jña tā api tu prakāra mātra vivakṣayā yathā sarvaiḥ vyañjanaiḥ bhuktam iti atra hi yāvantaḥ vyañjana prakārāḥ taiḥ bhuktam iti gamyate na tu niḥśeṣaiḥ iti asti ca niḥśeṣa vacanaḥ sarva śabdaḥ yathā upanītam annam sarvam aśitam prāśakena iti tatra hi niḥśeṣam iti gamyate tat iha niḥśeṣa jña tā lakṣaṇasya viveka ja jñānasya sādhanam saṃyamam āha kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ saṃyamāt viveka jam jñānam kṣaṇa padārtham nidarśana pūrvakam āha yathā iti 
TV_3.52.1–3.52.2^1^2	 loṣṭasya hi pravibhajyamānasya yasmin avayave alpatva tāratamyam vyavatiṣṭhate saḥ apakarṣa paryantaḥ paramāṇuḥ yathā tathā apakarṣa paryantaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ pūrva apara bhāga vikala kāla kalā iti yāvat tam eva kṣaṇam prakāra antareṇa darśayati yāvatā vā iti paramāṇu mātram deśam atikrāmet iti arthaḥ krama padārtham āha tat pravāha iti tad padena kṣaṇaḥ parāmṛśyate na ca īdṛśaḥ kramaḥ vāstavaḥ kim tu kālpanikaḥ tasya samāhāra rūpasya ayugapad upasthiteṣu vāstava tvena vicāra asaha tvāt iti āha kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ iti 
TV_3.52.2^2	 ayugapad bhā vi kṣaṇa dharma tvāt kramasya kṣaṇa sama āhārasya avāstava tvāt kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ api avāstava tvam samāhārasya naisargika vaitaṇḍika buddhi atiśaya rahitāḥ laukikāḥ pratikṣaṇaḥ eva vyutthita darśanāḥ bhrāntāḥ ye kālam īdṛśam vāstavam abhimanyante iti tat kim kṣaṇaḥ api avāstavaḥ na iti āha kṣaṇaḥ tu vastu patitaḥ vāstavaḥ iti arthaḥ kramasya avalambanam avalambaḥ saḥ asya asti iti krameṇa avalambyate vaikalpikena iti arthaḥ kramasya kṣaṇa avalambana tve hetum āha kramaḥ ca iti kramasya āvāstava tve hetum āha na ca iti caḥ hetu arthe yaḥ tu vaijātyāt sahabhāvam upeyāt tam pratyāha kramaḥ ca na dvayoḥ iti kasmāt asaṃbhavaḥ iti atas āha pūrvasmāt iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti tat kim idānīm śaśa viṣāṇāyamānāḥ eva pūrva uttara kṣaṇāḥ na iti āha ye tu iti anvitāḥ sāmyena samanvāgatāḥ iti arthaḥ upasaṃharati tena iti vartamānasya eva artha kriyāsu sva ucitāsu sāmarthyāt iti 
TV_3.53.1–3.53.2^1	 jāti lakṣaṇa deśaiḥ anyatā anavacchedāt tulyayoḥ tatas pratipattiḥ yadi api etat viveka jam jñānam niḥśeṣa bhāva viṣayam iti agre vakṣyate tathā api ati sūkṣma tvāt prathamam tasya viṣaya viśeṣaḥ upakṣipyate jāti lakṣaṇa deśaiḥ anyatā anavacchedāt tulyayoḥ tatas pratipattiḥ laukikānām jāti bhedaḥ anya tāyāḥ jñāpaka hetuḥ tulyā jātiḥ go tvam tulyaḥ ca deśaḥ pūrva ādiḥ kālākṣī svastimatyoḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ param iti dvayoḥ āmalakayoḥ tulya āmalaka tva jātiḥ vartula ādi lakṣaṇam tulyam deśa bhedaḥ param iti yadā tu yogi jñānam jijñāsunā kenacid pūrva āmalakam anya vyagrasya yoginaḥ jñātuḥ uttara deśa upāvartyate uttara deśam āmalakam tatas apasārya pidhāya vā tadā tulya deśa tve pūrvam etat uttaram etat iti pravibhāga anupapattiḥ prājñasya laukikasya tri pramāṇī nipuṇasya asaṃdigdhena ca tattva jñānena bhavitavyam viveka jajñānavataḥ yoginaḥ saṃdigdha tva anupapatteḥ atas uktam sūtra kṛtā tatas pratipattiḥ 
TV_3.53.2^2	 tatas iti vyācaṣṭe viveka ja jñānāt iti kṣaṇa tad krama saṃyamāt jātam jñānam katham āmalakam tulya jāti lakṣaṇa deśāt āmalaka antarāt vivecayati iti pṛcchati katham iti uttaram āha pūrva āmalaka sahakṣaṇaḥ deśaḥ pūrva āmalakena ekakṣaṇaḥ deśaḥ tena saha nirantara pariṇāmaḥ iti yāvat uttara āmalaka sahakṣaṇāt deśāt uttara āmalaka nirantara pariṇāmāt bhinnaḥ bhavatu deśayoḥ bhedaḥ kim āyātam āmalaka bhedasya iti atas āha te ca āmalake sva deśa kṣaṇa anubhava bhinne sva deśa sahitaḥ yaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tasya āmalakasya kālakalā sva deśena saha auttara adharya rūpa pariṇāma lakṣitā sā sva deśa kṣaṇaḥ tasya anubhavaḥ prāptiḥ vā jñānam vā tena bhinne āmalake yayoḥ āmalakayoḥ pūrva uttarābhyām deśābhyām auttara adharya pariṇāma kṣaṇaḥ āsīt tayoḥ deśa antara auttara adharya pariṇāma kṣaṇa viśiṣṭa tvam anubhavan saṃyamī te bhinne eva pratyeti 
TV_3.53.2^3	 saṃprati tad deśa pariṇāme api pūrva bhinna deśa pariṇāmāt viśiṣṭasya ca etad deśa pariṇāma kṣaṇasya saṃyamataḥ sākṣātkaraṇāt tat idam uktam anya deśa kṣaṇa anubhavaḥ tu tayoḥ anya tve hetuḥ iti anena eva nidarśanena laukika parīkṣaka saṃvāda ādinā paramāṇoḥ api īdṛśasya bhedaḥ yogi īśvara buddhi gamyaḥ śraddheyaḥ iti āha etena iti apare tu varṇayanti varṇanam udāharati yaḥ iti vaiśeṣikāḥ hi nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ iti āhuḥ tathā hi yoginaḥ muktān tulya jāti deśa kālān vyavadhi rahitān parasparataḥ bhedena pratyekam tattvena ca pratipadyante tasmāt asti kaścid antyaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti tathā ca saḥ eva nityānām paramāṇu ādīnām dravyāṇām bhedakaḥ iti tat etat dūṣayati tatra api iti jāti deśa lakṣaṇāni udāhṛtāni 
TV_3.53.2^4	 mūrtiḥ saṃsthānam yathā ekam viśuddha avayava saṃsthāna upapannam apasārya tasmin eva deśe anya vyagrasya draṣṭuḥ kutsita avayava saṃniveśaḥ upāvartyate tadā tasya saṃsthāna bhedena bheda pratyayaḥ śarīram vā mūrtiḥ tad saṃbandhena ātmanām saṃsāriṇām mukta ātmanām vā bhūta careṇa yādṛśa tādṛśena bhedaḥ iti sarvatra bheda pratyayasya anyathā siddheḥ na antya viśeṣa kalpanā vyavadhiḥ bheda kāraṇam yathā kuśa puṣkara dvīpayoḥ deśa svarūpayoḥ iti yatas jāti deśa ādi bhedāḥ loka buddhi gamyāḥ atas uktam kṣaṇa bhedaḥ tu yogi buddhi gamyaḥ eva iti eva kāraḥ kṣaṇa bhedam avadhārayati na yogi buddhi gamya tvam tena bhūta careṇa deha saṃbandhena mukta ātmanām api bhedaḥ yogi buddhi gamyaḥ unneyaḥ iti yasya tu uktāḥ bheda hetavaḥ na santi tasya pradhānasya bhedaḥ na asti iti ācaāryaḥ mene yasmāt ūce kṛtārtham prati naṣṭam api anaṣṭam tad anya sādhāraṇa tvāt iti tat āha mūrtivyavadhi iti ukta bheda hetu upalakṣaṇam etat jagat mūlasya pradhānasya pṛthaktvam bhedaḥ na asti iti arthaḥ 
TV_3.54.1–3.54.2	 tārakam sarva viṣayam sarvathā viṣayam akramam ca iti viveka jam jñānam tat evam viṣaya eka deśam viveka ja jñānasya darśayitvā viveka jam jñānam lakṣayati tārakam sarva viṣayam sarvathā viṣayam akramam ca iti viveka jam jñānam viveka jam jñānam iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ śeṣam lakṣaṇam saṃsāra sāgarāt tārayati iti tārakam pūrvasmāt prātibhāt viśeṣayati sarvathā viṣayam iti paryāyāḥ avāntara viśeṣāḥ atas eva viveka jam jñānam paripūrṇam na asya kvacid kiṃcid kathaṃcid kadācid agocaraḥ iti arthaḥ āstām tāvat jñāna antaram saṃprajñātaḥ api tāvat asya aṃśaḥ tasmāt atas param kim paripūrṇam iti āha asya eva aṃśaḥ yoga pradīpaḥ saṃprajñātaḥ kim upakramaḥ kim avasānaḥ ca asau iti āha madhumatīm iti ṛtaṃbharā prajñā eva madhu moda kāraṇa tvāt yathā uktam prajñā prāsādam āruhya iti tadvatī madhumatī dhiyaḥ avasthā tām upādāya yāvat asya parisamāptiḥ saptadhā prānta bhūmiḥ prajñā atas eva viveka jam jñānam tārakam bhavati tad aṃśasya yoga pradīpasya tāraka tvāt iti 
TV_3.55.1–3.55.3^1	 sattva puruṣayoḥ śuddhi sāmye kaivalyam iti tat evam paramparayā kaivalyasya hetūn sa vibhūtīn saṃyamān uktvā sattva puruṣa anya tā jñānam sākṣāt kaivalya sādhanam iti atra sūtram avatārayati prāptā iti viveka jam jñānam bhavatu mā vā bhūt sattva puruṣa anya tā ākhyātiḥ tu kaivalya prayojikā iti arthaḥ sattva puruṣayoḥ śuddhi sāmye kaivalyam iti itiḥ sūtra samāptau īśvarasya pūrva uktaiḥ saṃyamaiḥ jñāna kriyā śaktimataḥ anīśvarasya vā samanantara uktena saṃyamena viveka ja jñāna bhāginaḥ itarasya vā anutpanna jñānasya na vibhūtiṣu kācid apekṣā asti iti āha na hi iti 
TV_3.55.1–3.55.3^2	 nanu yadi anapekṣitāḥ vibhūtayaḥ kaivalye vyarthaḥ tarhi tāsām upadeśaḥ iti atas āha sattva śuddhi dvāreṇa iti itthaṃbhūta lakṣaṇe tṛtīyā na atyantam ahetavaḥ kaivalye vibhūtayaḥ kim tu na sākṣāt iti arthaḥ jñānam viveka jam upakrāntam yat ca pāramparyeṇa kāraṇam tat aupacārikam na tu mukhyam parama arthaḥ tu khyātiḥ eva mukhyam iti arthaḥ jñānāt iti prasaṃkhyānāt iti arthaḥ atra antaraṅgāṇi aṅgāni pariṇāmāḥ prapañcitāḥ saṃyamāt bhūta saṃyogaḥ tāsu jñānam viveka jam iti 
TV_4.1.1–4.1.2^1	 janma auṣadhi mantra tapaḥ samādhi jāḥ siddhayaḥ tat evam prathama dvitīya tṛtīya pādaiḥ samādhi tad sādhana tad vibhūtayaḥ prādhānyena vyutpāditāḥ itarat tu prāsaṅgikam aupodghātikam ca uktam iha idānīm tad hetukam kaivalyam vyutpādanīyam na ca etat kaivalya bhāgīyam cittam para lokam ca para lokinam vijñāna atiriktam citta karaṇaka sukha ādi ātmaka śabda ādi upabhoktāram ātmānam ca prasaṃkhyāna parama kāṣṭhām ca vinā vyutpādya śakyam vaktum iti tat etat sarvam atra pāde vyutpādanīyam itarat ca prasaṅgāt upodghātāt vā tatra prathamam siddha citteṣu kaivalya bhāgīyam cittam nirdhārayitu kāmaḥ pañcatayīm siddhim āha janma auṣadhi mantra tapaḥ samādhi jāḥ siddhayaḥ vyācaṣṭe deha antaritā iti 
TV_4.1.2^2	 svarga upabhoga bhāgīyāt karmaṇaḥ manuṣya jātīya ācaritāt kutaścid nimittāt labdha paripākāt kvacid deva nikāye jāta mātrasya eva divya deha antaritā siddhiḥ aṇima ādyāḥ bhavati iti oṣadhi siddhim āha asura bhavaneṣu iti manuṣyaḥ hi kutaścid nimittāt asura bhavanam upasaṃprāptaḥ kamanīyābhiḥ asura kanyābhiḥ upanītam rasāyanam upayujya ajarā maraṇa tvam anyāḥ ca siddhīḥ āsādayati iha eva vā rasāyana upayogena yathā māṇḍavyaḥ muniḥ rasa upayogāt vindhyavāsī iti mantra siddhim āha mantraiḥ iti tapaḥ siddhim āha tapasā iti saṃkalpa siddhim āha kāmarūpī iti yat eva kāmayate aṇima ādi tat eka pade asya bhavati iti yatra kāmayate śrotum vā mantum vā tatra tat eva śṛṇoti manute vā iti ādi śabdāt darśana ādayaḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ iti 
TV_4.2.1–4.2.2^1	 jāti antara pariṇāmaḥ prakṛti āpūrāt samādhi jāḥ siddhayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ adhastane pāde atha catasṛṣu siddhiṣu auṣadha ādi sādhanāsu teṣām eva kāya indriyāṇām jāti antara pariṇatiḥ iṣyate sā punar na tāvat upādāna mātrāt na hi tāvat mātram upādānam nyūna adhika divya ādivya bhāve asya bhavati no khalu avilakṣaṇam kāraṇam kārya vailakṣaṇyāya alam māsyāka smika tvam bhūt iti āśaṅkya pūrayitvā sūtram paṭhati tatra kāya indriyāṇām anya jātīya pariṇatānām jātyanta pariṇāmaḥ prakṛti āpūrāt 
TV_4.2.1–4.2.2^2	 manuṣya jāti pariṇatānām kāya indriyāṇām yaḥ deva tiryak jāti pariṇāmaḥ sa khalu prakṛti āpūrāt kāyasya hi prakṛtiḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni indriyāṇām ca prakṛtiḥ asmitā tad avayava anupraveśaḥ āpūraḥ tasmāt bhavati tat idam āha pūrva pariṇāma iti nanu yadi āpūreṇa anugrahaḥ kasmāt punar asau na sadātanaḥ iti atas āha dharma ādi iti tat anena tasya eva śarīrasya bālya kaumāra yauvana vārdhaka ādīni ca nyagrodha dhānāyām nyagrodha taru bhāvaḥ ca vahni kaṇikāyāḥ tṛṇa rāśi niveśitāyāḥ vā prodbhavat jvālā sahasra samāliṅgita gagana maṇḍala tvam ca vyākhyātam 
TV_4.3.1–4.3.2^1	 nimittam aprayojakam prakṛtīnām varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas kṣetrika vat prakṛti āpūrāt iti uktam tatra idam saṃdihyate kim āpūraḥ prakṛtīnām svābhāvikaḥ dharma ādi nimittaḥ vā iti kim prāptam satīṣu api prakṛtiṣu kadācid āpūrāt dharma ādi nimitta śravaṇāt ca tad nimittaḥ eva iti prāptam evam prāptaḥ āha nimittam aprayojakam prakṛtīnām varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas kṣetrika vat satyam dharma ādayaḥ nimittam na tu prayojakāḥ teṣām api prakṛti kārya tvāt na ca kāryam kāraṇam prayojayati tasya tad adhīna utpatti tayā kāraṇa paratantra tvāt 
TV_4.3.1–4.3.2^2	 svatantrasya ca prayojaka tvāt na khalu kulālam antareṇa mṛd daṇḍa cakra salila ādayaḥ utpitsitena utpannena vā ghaṭena prayujyante kim tu svatantreṇa kulālena na ca puruṣa arthaḥ api pravartakaḥ kim tu tad uddeśena īśvaraḥ uddeśyatā mātreṇa puruṣa arthaḥ pravartakaḥ iti ucyate utpitsoḥ tu asya puruṣa arthasya avyaktasya sthiti kāraṇa tvam yuktam na ca etāvatā dharma ādīnām animitta tā pratibandha apanayana mātreṇa kṣetrika vat upapatteḥ īśvarasya api dharma adhiṣṭhāna artham pratibandha apanayaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ veditavyaḥ tat etat nigada vyākhyātena bhāṣyeṇa uktam 
TV_4.4.1–4.4.2	 nirmāṇa cittāni asmitā mātrāt prakṛti āpūreṇa siddhīḥ samarthya siddhi vinirmita nānā kāya varti citta eka tva nānātve vicārayati yadā tu iti tatra nānā manaḥ tve kāyānām praticittam abhiprāya bhedāt eka abhiprāya anurodha ḥ ca paraspara pratisaṃdhānam ca na syātām puruṣa antara vat tasmāt ekam eva cittam pradīpa vat visāritayā bahūn api nirmāṇa kāyān vyāpnoti iti prāptaḥ āha nirmāṇa cittāni asmitā mātrāt yat yāvat jīvat śarīram tat sarvam ekaika asādhāraṇa citta anvitam dṛṣṭam tat yathā caitra maitra ādi śarīram tathā ca nirmāṇakāyāḥ iti siddham teṣām api prātisvikam manaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa āha asmitā mātram iti 
TV_4.5.1–4.5.2	 pravṛtti bhede prayojakam cittam ekam anekeṣām yat uktam aneka citta tvaḥ eka abhiprāya anurodhaḥ ca pratisaṃdhānam ca na syātām iti tatra uttaram sūtram pravṛtti bhede prayojakam cittam ekam anekeṣām abhaviṣyat eṣa doṣaḥ yadi cittam ekam nānā kāya varti manaḥ nāyakam na niramāsyat tad nirmāṇe tu adoṣaḥ na ca ekam gṛhītvā kṛtam prātisvikaiḥ manobhiḥ kṛtam vā nāyaka nirmāṇena nijasya eva manasaḥ nāyaka tvāt iti vācyam pramāṇa siddhasya niyoga paryanuyoga anupapatteḥ iti atra purāṇam bhavati 
TV_4.5.3–4.5.4	 ekaḥ tu prabhu śaktyā vai bahudhā bhavati īśvaraḥ bhūtvā yasmāt tu bahudhā bhavati ekaḥ punar tu saḥ tasmāt ca manasaḥ bhedāḥ jāyante ca ete eva hi ekadhā sa dvidhā ca eva tridhā ca bahudhā punar yogi īśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca prāpnuyāt viṣayān kaiścid kaiścid ugram tapaḥ caret saṃharet ca punar tāni sūryaḥ raśmi gaṇān iva iti tat etena abhiprāyeṇa āha bahūnām cittānām iti 
TV_4.6.1–4.6.2	 tatra dhyāna jam anāśayam tat evam uditeṣu pañcasu siddha citteṣu apavarga bhāgīyam cittam nirdhārayati tatra dhyāna jam anāśayam āśeḥ atas iti āśayāḥ karma vāsanāḥ kleśa vāsanāḥ ca te ete na vidyante yasmin tat anāśayam cittam apavarga bhāgīyam bhavati iti arthaḥ yatas rāga ādi nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ na asti atas na asti puṇya pāpa abhisaṃbandhaḥ kasmāt punā rāga ādi janitā pravṛttiḥ na asti iti atas āha kṣīṇa kleśa tvāt iti dhyāna jasya anāśayasya manaḥ antarebhyaḥ viśeṣam darśayitum itareṣām āśayavat tām āha itareṣām tu iti 
TV_4.7.1–4.7.2	 karma aśukla akṛṣṇam yoginaḥ trividham itareṣām tatra eva ca hetu param sūtram avatārayati yatas iti karma aśukla akṛṣṇam yoginaḥ trividham itareṣām padam sthānam cartuṣu samavetā catuṣpadī yat yāvat bahis sādhana sādhyam tatra sarvatra asti kasyacid pīḍā na hi vrīhi ādi sādhane api karmaṇi para pīḍā na asti avaghāta ādi samaye api pipīlika ādi vadha saṃbhavāt antatas bīja ādi vadhena stamba ādi bheda utpatti pratibandhāt anugrahaḥ ca dakṣiṇa ādinā brāhmaṇa ādeḥ iti śuklā tapaḥ svādhyāya dhyānavatām asaṃnyāsinām śukla tvam upapādayati sā hi iti aśukla akṛṣṇā saṃnyāsinām saṃnyāsinaḥ darśayati kṣīṇa iti karma asaṃbhavāt karma saṃnyāsinaḥ hi na kvacid bahis sādhana sādhye karmaṇi pravṛttāḥ iti na ca eṣām asti kṛṣṇaḥ karma āśayaḥ yoga anuṣṭhān a sādhyasya karma āśaya phalasya īśvare samarpaṇāt na śuklaḥ karma āśayaḥ niratyaya phalaḥ hi śuklaḥ ucyate yasya phalam eva na asti kutas tasya niratyaya phala tvam iti arthaḥ tat evam catuṣṭayīm karma jātim uktvā katamā kasya iti avadhārayati tatra aśuklam iti 
TV_4.8.1–4.8.2	 tatas tad vipāka anuguṇānām eva abhivyaktiḥ vāsanānām karma āśayam vivicya kleśa āśaya gatim āha tatas tad vipāka anuguṇānām eva abhivyaktiḥ vāsanānām yat jātīyasya puṇya jātīyasya apuṇya jātīyasya vā karmaṇaḥ yaḥ vipākaḥ divyaḥ vā nārakaḥ vā jāti āyuḥ bhogaḥ tasya vipākasya anuguṇāḥ tāḥ eva āha yāḥ vāsanāḥ karma vipākam anuśerate anukurvanti divya bhoga janitāḥ hi divya karma vipāka anuguṇāḥ vāsanāḥ na hi manuṣya bhoga vāsanā abhivyaktau divya karma phala upabhoga saṃbhavaḥ tasmāt sva vipāka anuguṇāḥ eva vāsanāḥ karma abhivyañjanīyāḥ iti bhāṣya arthaḥ 
TV_4.9.1–4.9.2^1	 jāti deśa kāla vyavahitānām api ānantaryam smṛti saṃskārayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt syāt etat manuṣyasya prāyaṇa anantaram adhigata mārjāra bhāvasya anantara tayā manuṣya vāsanāyāḥ eva abhivyaktvā bhavitavyam na khalu asti saṃbhavaḥ yat anantara divasa anubhūtam na smaryate vyavahita divasa anubhūtam ca smaryate iti atas āha jāti deśa kāla vyavahitānām api ānantaryam smṛti saṃskārayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt bhavatu vṛṣadaṃśa vāsanāyāḥ jāti ādivya vadhiḥ tathā api tasyāḥ phalatas ānantaryam vṛṣadaṃśa vipākena karmaṇā tasyāḥ eva sva vipāka anuguṇāyāḥ abhivyaktau tad smaraṇa samutpādāt iti āha vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka udayaḥ iti udeti asmāt iti udayaḥ karma āśayaḥ punar ca sva vyañjaka añjanaḥ eva udiyāt abhivyajyeta vipāka ārambha abhimukhaḥ kriyeta iti arthaḥ 
TV_4.9.2^2	 abhisaṃskāra kriyā upādāya gṛhītvā vyajyeta yadi vyajyeta sva vipāka anuguṇāḥ eva vāsanā gṛhītvā vyajyeta iti arthaḥ ānantaryam eva phalatas kāraṇa dvārakam upapādya kārya dvārakam upapādayati kutas ca smṛti iti eka rūpa tā sādṛśyam tat eva āha yathā iti nanu anubhava sa rūpāḥ ced saṃskārāḥ tathā sati anubhavāḥ viśara āravaḥ iti ete api viśara āravaḥ katham cira bhāvine anubhavāya kalperan iti atas āha te ca karma vāsanā anurūpāḥ yathāpūrvam sthāyi kṣaṇika karma nimittam api evam kṣaṇikā anubhava nimittaḥ api saṃskāraḥ sthāyī kiṃcid bheda adhiṣṭhānam ca sārūpyam anyathā bhede tattvena sādṛśya anupapatteḥ iti arthaḥ sugamam anyat 
TV_4.10.1–4.10.2^1	 tāsām anādi tvam ca āśiṣaḥ nitya tvāt syāt etat vyajyeran pūrva pūrvatara janma abhisaṃskṛtāḥ vāsanāḥ yadi pūrva pūrvatara janma sadbhāve pramāṇam syāt tat eva tu na asti na ca jāta mātrasya jantoḥ harṣa śoka darśana mātram pramāṇam bhavitum arhati padma ādi saṃkoca vikāsa vat svābhāvika tvena tad upapatteḥ iti atas āha tāsām anādi tvam ca āśiṣaḥ nitya tvāt tāsām vāsanānām anādi tvam ca na kevalam ānantaryam iti ca arthaḥ āśiṣaḥ nitya tvāt ātma āśiṣaḥ vāsanānām anādi tve nitya tva avi abhicārāt iti nanu svābhāvika tvena api upapatteḥ asiddham āśiṣaḥ nitya tvam iti atas āha yā iyam iti nāstikaḥ pṛcchati kasmāt uttaram jāta mātrasya jantoḥ iti atas eva etasmin janmani ananubhūta maraṇa dharmakasya maraṇam eva dharmaḥ saḥ ananubhūtaḥ yena sa tathā uktaḥ tasya mātuḥ aṅkāt praskhalataḥ kampamānasya māṅgalya cakra ādi lāñchitam tat uraḥ sūtram ati gāḍham pāṇigrāham avalambamānasya bālakasya kampa bheda anumitā dveṣa anuṣakte duḥkhe yā smṛtiḥ tad nimittaḥ maraṇa trāsaḥ katham bhavet iti 
TV_4.10.2^2	 nanu uktam svabhāvāt iti atas āha na ca svābhāvikam vastu nimittam upādatte gṛhṇāti sva utpattau etat uktam bhavati bālakasya īdṛśaḥ dṛśyamānaḥ kampaḥ bhaya nibandhanaḥ īdṛśa kampa tvāt asmad ādi kampa vat bālakasya bhayam dveṣa duḥkha smṛti nimittam bhaya tvāt asmad ādi bhaya vat āgāmi pratyavāya utprekṣā lakṣaṇam ca bhayam na duḥkha smṛti mātrāt bhavati api tu yatas bibheti tasya pratyavāya hetu bhāvam anumāya saṃprati api pratyavāyam bhayam ca vidadhyāt iti śaṅkate tasmāt yat jātīyāt anubhūta carāt dveṣa anuṣaktam duḥkham upapāditam tasya smaraṇāt tad jātīyasya anubhūyamānasya tad duḥkha hetu tvam anumāya tatas bibheti na ca bālakena asmin janmani skhalanasya anyatra duḥkha hetu tvam avagatam na ca tādṛśam duḥkham upalabdham 
TV_4.10.2^3	 tasmāt prāc bhavīyaḥ anubhavaḥ pariśiṣyate tat ca etat evam prayogam ārohati jāta mātrasya bālasya smṛtiḥ pūrva anubhava nibandhanā smṛti tvāt asmad ādi smṛti vat iti na ca padma saṃkoca vikāsau api svābhāvikau na hi svābhāvikam kāraṇa antaram apekṣate vahneḥ auṣṇyam prati api kāraṇa antara apekṣā prasaṅgāt tasmāt āgantukam aruṇa kara saṃparka mātram eva kamalinī vikāsa kāraṇam saṃkoca kāraṇam ca saṃskāraḥ sthiti sthāpakaḥ iti evam smita ādi anumita harṣa ādayaḥ api prāci bhave hetavaḥ veditavyāḥ tat āstām tāvat prakṛtam upasaṃharati tasmāt iti nimittam labdha vipāka kālam karma pratilambhaḥ abhivyaktiḥ prasaṅgataḥ citta parimāṇa vipratipattim nirācikīrṣuḥ vipratipattim āha ghaṭa prāsāda iti deha pradeśa varti kārya darśanāt dehāt bahis sadbhāve cittasya na pramāṇam asti na ca etat aṇu parimāṇam dīrgha śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇa ādau aparyāyeṇa jñāna pañcaka anutpāda prasaṅgāt 
TV_4.10.2^4	 na ca ananubhūyamāna krama kalpanāyām pramāṇam asti na ca ekam aṇu manaḥ nānā deśaiḥ indriyaiḥ aparyāyeṇa saṃbandhum arhati tat pāriśeṣyāt kāya parimāṇam cittam ghaṭa prāsāda varti pradīpa vat saṃkoca vikāśau puttikā hasti dehayoḥ asya utpatsyete śarīra parimāṇam eva ākāraḥ parimāṇam yasya iti apare pratipannāḥ nanu evam katham asya kṣetra bīja saṃyogaḥ na khalu etat anāśrayam mṛta śarīrāt mātṛ pitṛ deha vartinī lohita retasī prāpnoti paratantra tvāt na hi sthāṇu ādiṣu agacchatsu tad chāyā gacchati na ca āgacchati paṭe tad āśrayam citram gacchati tathā ca na saṃsāraḥ syāt iti atas āha tathā ca antara abhāvaḥ saṃsāraḥ ca yuktaḥ iti tathā ca śarīra parimāṇa tve deha antara prāptaye pūrva deha tyāgaḥ deha antara prāptiḥ ca antarā asya ativāhika śarīra saṃyogāt bhavataḥ tena khalu ayam deha antare saṃcaret tathā ca purāṇam 
TV_4.10.3–4.10.4^1	 aṅguṣṭha mātram puruṣam niścakarṣa yamaḥ balāt iti saḥ ayam antara abhāvaḥ atas eva saṃsāraḥ ca yuktaḥ iti tat etat amṛṣyamāṇaḥ sva matam āha vṛttiḥ eva asya vibhunaḥ cittasya saṃkoca vikāsinī iti ācāryaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ pratipede idam atra ākūtam yadi anāśrayam cittam na deha antara saṃcāri katham etat ātivāhikam āśrayate tatra api deha antara kalpanāyām anavasthā na ca asya dehāt niṣkarṣaḥ sa ativāhikasya saṃbhavati niṣkṛṣṭasya cetasaḥ tad saṃbandhāt astu tarhi sūkṣmaśarīram evā sargāt ā ca mahāpralayāt niyatam cittānām adhiṣṭhānam ṣāṣ kauśika śarīram adhyavarti 
TV_4.10.4^2	 tena hi cittam ā satya lokāt ā ca avīceḥ tatra tatra śarīre saṃcarati niṣkarṣaḥ ca asya upapannaḥ ṣāṣ kauśikāt kāyāt tatra hi tad antara abhāvaḥ tasya niyata tvāt na ca asya api sadbhāve pramāṇam asti na khalu etat adhyakṣa gocaraḥ na ca saṃsāraḥ asya anumānam ācārya matena api upapatteḥ āgamaḥ tu puruṣasya niṣkarṣam āha na ca cittam vā sūkṣmaśarīram vā puruṣaḥ kim tu citi śaktiḥ apratisaṃkramāḥ na ca asyāḥ niṣkarṣaḥ saṃbhavati iti aupacārikaḥ vyākhyeyaḥ tathā ca citeḥ cittasya ca tatra tatra vṛtti abhāvaḥ eva niṣkarṣa arthaḥ 
TV_4.10.4^3	 yat ca smṛti itihāsa purāṇeṣu maraṇa anantaram preta śarīra prāptiḥ tad vimokaḥ ca sapiṇḍīkaraṇa ādibhiḥ iti uktam tat anujānīmaḥ ātivāhika tvam tasya na mṛṣyāmahe na ca atra asti kaścid āgamaḥ labdha śarīraḥ eva ca yama puruṣaiḥ api pāśa baddhaḥ nīyate na tu ātivāhika śarīraḥ tasmāt āhaṃkārika tvāt cetasaḥ ahaṃkārasya ca gagana maṇḍala vat trailokya vyāpi tvāt vibhu tvam manasaḥ evam ced asya vṛttiḥ api vibhvīti sarvajña tā āpattiḥ iti atas uktam vṛttiḥ eva asya iti syāt etat citta mātra adhīnāyāḥ vṛtteḥ saṃkoca vikāsau kutas kādācid kau iti atas āha tat ca cittam dharma ādi nimitta apekṣam 
TV_4.10.4^4	 vṛttau nimittam vibhajate nimittam ca iti ādi grahaṇena indriya dhana ādayaḥ gṛhyante śraddhā ādi iti atra api vīrya smṛti ādayaḥ gṛhyante āntara tve saṃmatim ācāryāṇām āha tathā ca uktam vihāraḥ vyāpāraḥ prakṛṣṭam śuklam tayoḥ bāhya abhyantarayoḥ madhye jñāna vairāgye tat janitaḥ dharmaḥ kena bāhya sādhyena dharmeṇa atiśayyete abhibhūyete jñāna vairāgya jau eva dharmau tam abhibhavataḥ bīja bhāvāt apanayate iti arthaḥ atra eva su prasiddham udāharaṇam āha daṇḍaka araṇyam iti 
TV_4.11.1–4.11.2	 hetu phala āśraya ālambanaiḥ saṃgṛhīta tvāt eṣām abhāve tad abhāvaḥ atha etāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ vāsanāḥ ca anādayaḥ ced katham āsām ucchedaḥ na khalu citi śaktiḥ anādiḥ ucchidyate iti atas āha hetu phala āśraya ālambanaiḥ saṃgṛhīta tvāt eṣām abhāve tad abhāvaḥ anādeḥ api samucchedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā anāgata tvasya iti savyabhicāra tvāt asādhanam citi śaktiḥ tu vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt na vinaśyati na tu anādi tvāt uktam ca vāsanānām anādīnām api samucchede kāraṇam sūtreṇa iti anugraha upaghātau api dharma adharma ādi nimittam upalakṣayataḥ tena surā pāna ādayaḥ api saṃgṛhītāḥ bhavanti netrī nāyikā atra eva hetum āha mūlam iti pratyutpanna tā vartam āna tā na tu dharma svarūpa utpādaḥ atra eva hetum āha na hi iti yat abhimukhībhūtam vastu kāminī saṃparka ādi vyāpaka abhāve vyāpyasya abhāvaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
TV_4.12.1–4.12.2^1	 atīta anāgatam svarūpataḥ asti adhva bhedāt dharmāṇām uttara sūtram avatārayitum śaṅkate na asti iti asataḥ iti tu saṃpāta āyātam nidarśanāya vā atīta anāgatam svarūpataḥ asti adhva bhedāt dharmāṇām na asatām utpādaḥ na satām vināśaḥ kim tu satām eva dharmāṇām adhva bheda pariṇāmaḥ eva udaya vyayau iti sūtra arthaḥ anubhūtā prāptā yena vyaktiḥ tat tathā saṃprati vyaktiḥ na asti iti yāvat itas ca traikālye api dharmaḥ san iti āha yadi ca iti na hi asañjñāna viṣayaḥ saṃbhavati iti nirupākhya tvāt viṣaya avabhāsam hi vijñānam na asati viṣaye bhavati traikālya viṣayam ca vijñānam yoginām asmad ādīnām ca vijñānam asati viṣaye na utpannam syāt utpadyate ca tasmāt atīta anāgate sāmānya rūpeṇa samanugate staḥ iti evam anubhavataḥ jñānam viṣaya sattve hetuḥ uktam uddeśya tvāt api anāgatasya viṣaya tvena sattvam eva iti āha kim ca bhoga bhāgīyasya iti 
TV_4.12.2^2	 kuśalaḥ nipuṇaḥ anuṣṭheye api ca yat yat nimittam tat sarvam naimittike sati eva viśeṣam ādhatte yathā kāṇḍalau= aveda adhyāya ādayaḥ na khalu ete kāṇḍalau= ādayaḥ asantam utpādayanti sataḥ eva tu tad prāpti vikārau kurvanti evam kulāla ādayaḥ api sataḥ eva ghaṭasya vartamānī bhāva hetavaḥ iti āha sataḥ ca iti yadi tu vartamāna tva abhāvāt atīta anāgatayoḥ asattvam hanta bho vartamānasya api abhāvaḥ atīta anāgata tva abhāvāt adhva viśiṣṭa tayā tu sattvam trayāṇām api aviśiṣṭam iti abhiprāyeṇa āha dharmī ca iti pratyekam avasthānam pratyavasthitiḥ iti dravyate iti dravye dharmiṇi sārvavibhaktikaḥ tasiḥ yadi atīta anāgatau atīta anāgata tve na staḥ tarhi vartamāna samaye tattva abhāvāt na syātām iti atas āha ekasya ca iti prakṛtam upasaṃharati iti na abhūtvā bhāvaḥ iti 
TV_4.13.1–4.13.3	 te vyakta sūkṣmāḥ guṇa ātmānaḥ syāt etat ayam tu nānā prakāraḥ dharmi dharma avasthā pariṇāma rūpaḥ viśva bheda prapañcaḥ na pradhānāt ekasmāt bhavitum arhati na hi avilakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt kārya bheda saṃbhavaḥ iti atas āha te vyakta sūkṣmāḥ guṇa ātmānaḥ te tri adhvānaḥ dharmāḥ vyaktāḥ ca sūkṣmāḥ ca guṇa ātmānaḥ na traiguṇya atiriktam eṣām asti kāraṇam vaicitryam tu tadā ahita anādi kleśa vāsanā anugatāt vaicitryāt yathā uktam vāyupurāṇe vaiśvarūpyāt pradhānasya pariṇāmaḥ ayam adbhutaḥ iti 
TV_4.13.4	 vyaktānām pṛthivī ādīnām ekādaśa indriyāṇām ca vartamānānām atīta anāgata tvam ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ yathāyogam bhavanti saṃprati viśvasya nitya anitya rūpe vibhajan nitya rūpam āha sarvam idam iti dṛśyamānam saṃniveśaḥ saṃsthāna bhedavān pariṇāmaḥ iti arthaḥ atra eva ṣaṣṭi tantra śāstrasya anuśiṣṭiḥ māyā iva na tu māyā su tucchakam vināśi yathā hi māyā ahnāya eva anyathā bhavati evam vikārāḥ api āvirbhāva tirobhāva dharmāṇaḥ pratikṣaṇam anyathā prakṛtiḥ nitya tayā māyā vidharmiṇī paramārtha iti 
TV_4.14.1–4.14.2^1	 pariṇāma eka tvāt vastu tattvam bhavatu traiguṇyasya ittham pariṇāma vaicitryam ekaḥ tu pariṇāmaḥ pṛthivī iti vā toyam iti vā kutas ātmanaḥ ekatva virodhāt iti āśaṅkya sūtram avatārayati yadā tu sarve guṇāḥ iti pariṇāma eka tvāt vastu tattvam bahūnām api ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā gavā aśva mahiṣa mātaṅgānām rumā nikṣiptānām ekaḥ lavaṇa tva jātīya lakṣaṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ varti taila analānām ca pradīpaḥ iti evam bahu tve api guṇānām pariṇāma eka tvam tatas tanmātra bhūta bhautikānām pratyekam tattvam eka tvam grahaṇa ātmakānām sattva pradhāna tayā prakāśa ātmanām ahaṃkāra avāntara kāryāṇām karaṇa bhāvena ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ śrotram indriyam 
TV_4.14.2^2	 teṣām eva guṇānām tamaḥ pradhāna tayā jaḍa tvena grāhya ātmakānām śabda tanmātra bhāvena ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ śabdaḥ viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda tanmātram viṣayaḥ iti jaḍa tvam āha na tu tanmātrasya śrotra viṣaya tva saṃbhavaḥ iti śeṣam sugamam atha vijñāna vādinam vaināśikam utthāpayati na asti arthaḥ vijñāna visahacaraḥ iti yadi hi bhūta bhautikāni vijñāna mātrāt bhinnāni bhaveyuḥ tatas tad utpatti kāraṇam īdṛśam pradhānam kalpyeta na tu tāni vijñāna atiriktāni santi paramārthataḥ tat katham pradhāna kalpanam katham ca grahaṇānām indriyāṇām ahaṃkāra vikārāṇām kalpanā iti 
TV_4.14.2^3	 tathā hi jaḍasya arthasya svayam aprakāśa tvāt na asti arthaḥ vijñāna visahacaraḥ sāhacaryam saṃbandhaḥ tad abhāvaḥ visahacara tvam viḥ abhāva arthaḥ vijñāna asaṃbandhaḥ na asti vyavahāra yogyaḥ iti arthaḥ asti tu jñānam artha visahacaram tasya svayaṃprakāśa tvena sva gocara astitāvyavahāre kartavye jaḍam artham pratyapekṣā bhāvāt tat anena vedya tva saha upalambha niyamau sūcitau vijñāna vādinā tau ca evam prayogam ārohataḥ yat vedyate yena vedanena tat tatas na bhidyate yathā jñānasya ātmā 
TV_4.14.2^4–4.14.3	 vedyante ca bhūtabhautikāni iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ niṣedhya bheda viruddhena abhedena vyāptam vedya tvam dṛśyamānam sva vyāpakam abhedam upasthāpayat tad viruddham bhedam pratikṣipati iti tathā yat yena niyata saha upalambham tat tatas na bhidyate yathā ekasmāt candrāt dvitīyaḥ candraḥ niyata saha upalambhaḥ ca arthaḥ jñānena iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ niṣedhya bheda vyāpakān iyama viruddhaḥ niyamaḥ aniyamam nivartayan tad vyāptam bhedam pratikṣipati iti syāt etat arthaḥ ced na bhinnaḥ jñānāt katham bhinna vat pratibhāsate iti atas āha kalpitam iti yathā āhuḥ vaināśikāḥ saha upalambha niyamāt abhedaḥ nīla tad dhiyoḥ bhedaḥ ca bhrānti vijñānaiḥ dṛśyaḥ indau iva advaye iti 
TV_4.14.4^1	 kalpita tvam viśadayati jñāna parikalpanā iti nirākaroti te iti te katham śraddheya vacanāḥ syuḥ iti saṃbandhaḥ pratijñānam upasthitam pratyupasthitam katham tathā iti yathā yathā avabhāsate idaṃkāra āspada tvena tathā tathā svayam upasthitam na tu kalpanā upakalpitam vijñāna viṣaya tā āpannam sva māhātmyena iti vijñāna kāraṇa tvam arthasya darśayati yasmāt arthena svakīyayā grāhya śaktyā vijñānam ajani tasmāt arthasya grāhakam tat evaṃbhūtam vastu katham apramāṇa ātmakena vikalpa vijñāna balena vikalpasya aprāmāṇika tvāt tat balasya api tad ātmanaḥ apramāṇa ātmaka tvam tena vastu svarūpam utsṛjya upaplutam kṛtvā 
TV_4.14.4^2	 upagṛhya iti kvacid pāṭhaḥ tatra api saḥ eva arthaḥ tat eva apalapantaḥ śraddhātavya vacanāḥ syuḥ iti idam atra ākūtam saha upalambha niyamaḥ ca vedya tvam ca hetū saṃdigdha vyatireka tayā na aikāntikau tathā hi jñāna ākārasya bhūta bhautika ādeḥ yat etat bāhya tvam sthūla tvam ca bhāsete na te jñāne saṃbhavataḥ tathā hi nānā deśa vyāpitā sthaulyam vicchinna deśa tā ca bāhya tvam na ca eka vijñānasya nānā deśa vyāpitā vicchinna deśa tā ca upapadyate tad deśa tva ātad deśa tva lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsargasya ekatra asaṃbhavāt saṃbhave vā trailokyasya ekatva prasaṅgāt 
TV_4.14.4^3	 atas eva astu vijñāna bhedaḥ iti ced hanta bhoḥ parama sūkṣma gocarāṇām pratyayānām paraspara vārtā anabhijñānām sva gocara mātra jāgarūkāṇām kutastyaḥ ayam sthūla avabhāsaḥ na ca vikalpa gocaraḥ abhilāpaḥ saṃsarga abhāvāt viśada pratibhāsa tvāt ca na ca sthūlam ālocitam yatas tad upādhikasya viśadatā bhavet tad pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ na ca avikalpa vat vikalpaḥ api su a ākāra mātra gocaraḥ tasya ca asthūla tvāt na sthūla gocaraḥ bhavitum arhati tasmāt bāhye ca pratyaye sthūlasya bāhyasya ca asaṃbhavāt alīkam etat āsthātavyam na ca alīkam vijñānāt abhinnam vijñānasya tadvat tucchatva prasaṅgāt 
TV_4.14.4^4	 tathā ca vedya tvasya abheda vyāpya tva abhāvāt kutas bheda pratipakṣa tvam saha upalambha niyamaḥ ca sat asatoḥ iva vijñāna sthaulyayoḥ satoḥ api svabhāvāt vā kutaścid pratibandhāt vā upapatsyate tasmāt anaikāntika tvāt etau hetvābhāsau vikalpa mātram eva bāhya abhāve prasuvāte na ca pratyakṣa māhātmyam vikalpa mātreṇa apodyate tasmāt sādhu uktam katham apramāṇa ātmakena vikalpa jñāna balena iti etena pratyaya tvam api svapna ādi pratyaya dṛṣṭāntena nirālambana tva sādhanam apāstam prameya vikalpaḥ tu avayavi vyavasthāpanena pratyuktaḥ vistaraḥ tu nyāya kaṇikāyām anusaraṇīyaḥ iti tat iha kṛtam vistareṇa iti 
TV_4.15.1–4.15.2^1	 vastu sāmye citta bhedāt tayoḥ vibhaktaḥ panthāḥ tat evam utsūtram bhāṣya kṛt vijñāna atirikta sthāpane yuktim uktvā sautrīm yuktim avatārayati kutas ca etat iti vastu sāmye citta bhedāt tayoḥ vibhaktaḥ panthāḥ yat nānātve yasya ekatvam tat tatas atyantam bhidyate yathā caitrasya jñānam ekam bhinnebhyaḥ deva datta viṣṇu mitra maitra pratyayebhyaḥ bhidyate jñāna nānā tve api ca arthaḥ na bhidyate iti bhavati vijñānebhyaḥ anyaḥ abhedaḥ ca arthasya jñāna bhede api pramātṝṇām paraspara pratisaṃdhānāt avasīyate asti hi rakta dviṣṭa vimūḍha madhya sthānām ekasyām yoṣiti pratīyamānāyām pratisaṃdhānam yā tvayā dṛśyate sā eva mayā api iti 
TV_4.15.2^2	 tasmāt vastu sāmye citta bhedāt jñāna bhedāt tayoḥ artha jñānayoḥ vibhaktaḥ panthāḥ svarūpa bheda upāyaḥ sukha jñānam kāntāyām kāntasya sapatnīnām duḥkha jñānam caitrasya tu tām avindataḥ mūḍha jñānam viṣādaḥ syāt etat yaḥ ekasya cittena parikalpitaḥ kāminī lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ tena eva anyeṣām api cittam uparajyate iti sādhāraṇam upapadyate iti atas āha na ca anyā iti tathā sati ekasmin nīla jñānavati sarve eva nīla jñānavantaḥ syuḥ iti nanu artha vādinām api ekaḥ arthaḥ katham sukha ādi bheda bhinna vijñāna hetuḥ 
TV_4.15.2^3	 na hi avilakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt kārya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ iti atas āha sāṃkhya pakṣaḥ iti ekasya eva bāhyasya vastunaḥ traiguṇya pariṇāmasya trairūpyam upapannam evam api sarveṣām aviśeṣeṇa sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam vijñānam syāt iti atas āha dharma ādi nimitta apekṣam rajaḥ sahitam sattvam dharma apekṣam sukha jñānam janayati sattvam eva tu vigalita rajaskam vidyā apekṣam mādhyasthya jñānam iti te ca dharma ādayaḥ na sarve sarvatra puruṣe santi kim tu kaścid kvacid iti upapannā vyavasthā iti atra kecid āhuḥ prāvādukā jñāna saha bhūḥ eva arthaḥ bhogya tvāt sukha ādi vat iti 
TV_4.15.2^4	 etat uktam bhavati bhavatu arthaḥ jñānāt vyatiriktaḥ tathā api asau jaḍa tvāt na jñānam antareṇa śakyaḥ pratipattum jñānena tu bhāsanīyaḥ tathā ca jñāna samayaḥ eva asti na anyadā pramāṇa abhāvāt iti tat etat utsūtram tāvat dūṣayati bhāṣya kāraḥ te etayā dvāra iti vastu khalu sarva citta sādhāraṇam aneka kṣaṇa paramparohyamānam pariṇāma ātmakam anubhūyate laukika parīkṣakaiḥ tat ced vijñānena saha bhavet nūnam evaṃvidham evam ced idam aṃśasya upari kaḥ ayam anurodhaḥ yena saḥ api na apahnūyeta iti arthaḥ 
TV_4.16.1–4.16.2^1	 na ca ekacitta tantram vastu tat apramāṇakam tadā kim syāt mā vā bhūt idaṃaṃśasya apahnavaḥ jñāna saha bhūḥ eva astu arthaḥ tatra api āha na ca ekacitta tantram vastu tat apramāṇakam tadā kim syāt yat dhi ghaṭa grāhi cittam tat yadā paṭa dravya vyagra tayā na ghaṭe vartate yat vā viveka viṣayam āsīt tat eva ca nirodham samāpadyate tadā ghaṭa jñānasya vā viveka jñānasya vā abhāvāt vivekaḥ vā ghaṭaḥ vā jñāna bheda mātra jīvanaḥ tad nāśāt naṣṭaḥ eva syāt iti āha ekacittā iti kim tat syāt na syāt iti arthaḥ saṃbadhyamānam ca cittena tat vastu vivekaḥ vā ghaṭaḥ vā kutas utpadyeta niyata kāraṇa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi bhāvāni hi kāryāṇi na sva kāraṇam ativartya kāraṇa antarāt bhavitum īśate 
TV_4.16.2^2	 mā bhūt akāraṇa tve teṣām kādācitka tva vyāghātaḥ na ca tat jñāna kāraṇa tvam eva tad kāraṇa tvam iti yuktam āśāmodakasya modakasya ca upayujyamānasya rasa vīrya vipāka ādi sāmya prasaṅgāt tasmāt sādhu uktam saṃbadhyamānam vā punar cittena iti api ca yaḥ yaḥ arvāc bhāgaḥ sa sarvaḥ madhya para bhāga vyāptaḥ jñāna adhīne sadbhāve tu asya ananubhūyamāna tvāt madhya para bhāgau na staḥ iti vyāpaka abhāvāt arvāc bhāgaḥ api na syāt iti artha abhāvāt kutas jñāna sahabhūḥ arthaḥ iti āha ye ca asya iti anupasthitāḥ ajñātāḥ upasaṃharati tasmāt iti sugamam śeṣam 
TV_4.17.1–4.17.2^1	 tad uparāga apekṣi tvāt cittasya vastu jñāta ajñātam syāt etat arthaḥ ced svatantraḥ sa ca jaḍa svabhāvaḥ iti na kadācid prakāśeta prakāśane vā jaḍa tvam api asya apagatam iti bhāvaḥ api apagacchet na jātu svabhāvam apahāya bhāvaḥ vartitum arhati na ca indriya ādi ādheyaḥ jaḍa svabhāvasya arthasya dharmaḥ prakāśate iti sāṃpratam artha dharma tve nīlatva ādi vat sarva puruṣa sādhāraṇaḥ iti ekaḥ śāstra arthaḥ iti sarve eva vidvāṃsaḥ prasajyeran na jālmaḥ kaścid asti na ca atīta anāgatayoḥ dharmaḥ pratyutpannaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt svatantraḥ arthaḥ upalambha viṣayaḥ iti manoratha mātram etat iti atas āha tad uparāga apekṣi tvāt cittasya vastu jñāta ajñātam 
TV_4.17.2^2	 jaḍa svabhāvaḥ api arthaḥ indriya praṇāḍikayā cittam uparañjayati tat evaṃbhūtam citta darpaṇam upasaṃkrānta pratibimbā citi śaktiḥ cittam artha uparaktam cetayamāna artham anubhavati na tu arthe kiṃcid prākaṭī ādikam ādhatte na api asaṃbaddhā cittena tad pratibimba saṃkrānteḥ ukta tvāt iti yadi api ca sarva gata tvāt cittasya ca indriyasya ca ahaṃkārikasya viṣaye na asti saṃbandhaḥ tathā api yatra śarīre vṛttimat cittam tena saha saṃbandhaḥ viṣayāṇām iti ayaskānta maṇi kalpāḥ iti uktam ayaḥ sadharmakam cittam iti indriya praṇāḍikayā abhisaṃbandhya uparañjayanti atas eva cittam pariṇāmi iti āha vastunaḥ iti 
TV_4.18.1–4.18.2	 sadā jñātāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ tad prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvāt tat evam citta vyatirekiṇam artham avasthāpya tebhyaḥ pariṇati dharmakebhyaḥ vyatiriktam ātmānam ādarśayitum tad vaidharmyam apariṇāmi tvam asya vaktum pūrayitvā sūtram paṭhati yasya tu tat eva cittam viṣayaḥ tasya sadā jñātāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ tad prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvāt kṣipta mūḍha vikṣiptā ekāgra tā avasthitam cittam ā nirodhāt sarvadā puruṣeṇa anubhūyate vṛttimat tat kasya hetoḥ yatas puruṣaḥ apariṇāmī pariṇāmi tve citta vat puruṣaḥ api jñāta ajñāta viṣayaḥ bhavet jñāta viṣayaḥ eva tu ayam tasmāt apariṇāmī tatas ca pariṇāmibhyaḥ atiricyate iti tat etat āha yadi citta vat iti sadā jñāta tvam tu manasaḥ sa vṛttikasya tasya yaḥ prabhuḥ svāmī bhoktā iti yāvat tasya prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvam anumāpayati tathā ca apariṇāminaḥ tasya puruṣasya pariṇāminaḥ cittāt bhedaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_4.19.1–4.19.2^1^1	 na tat su ābhāsam dṛśya tvāt atra vaināśikam utthāpayati syāt āśaṅka iti ayam arthaḥ syāt etat evam yadi cittam ātmanaḥ viṣayaḥ syāt api tu sva prakāśam etat viṣaya ābhāsam pūrva cittam pratītya samutpannam tat kutas puruṣasya sadā ajñāta viṣaya tvam kutastarām vā apariṇāmi tayā pariṇāminaḥ cittāt bhedaḥ iti na tat su ābhāsam dṛśya tvāt bhavet etat evam yadi sva saṃvedanam cittam syāt na tu etat asti tat dhi pariṇāmi tayā nīla ādi vat anubhava vyāpyam yat ca anubhava vyāpyam na tat su ābhāsam bhavitum arhati sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt 
TV_4.19.1–4.19.2^1^2	 na hi tat eva kriyā ca karma kārakam ca na hi pākaḥ pacyate chidā vā chidyate puruṣaḥ tu apariṇāmī na anubhava karmā iti na asmin svayaṃprakāśa tā na yujyate apara adhīna prakāśa tā hi asya svayaṃprakāśa tā na anubhava karmatā tasmāt dṛśya tvāt darśana karma cittam na su a ābhāsam ātma prakāśa pratibimba tayā eva cittasya tad vṛtti viṣayāḥ prakāśante iti bhāvaḥ nanu dṛśyaḥ agniḥ svayaṃprakāśaḥ ca na hi yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ agninā vyajyante evam agniḥ agni antareṇa iti atas āha na ca agniḥ atra iti 
TV_4.19.2^2	 kasmāt na hi iti mā nāma agniḥ agni antarāt prakāśiṣṭa vijñānāt tu prakāśate iti na svayam prakāśate iti na vyabhicāraḥ iti arthaḥ prakāśaḥ ca ayam iti ayam iti puruṣa svabhāvāt prakāśāt vyavacchinatti kriyā rūpaḥ prakāśaḥ iti yāvat etat uktam bhavati yā yā kriyā sā sā sarvā kartṛ karaṇa karma saṃbandhena dṛṣṭāḥ yathā pākaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ caitra agni taṇḍula saṃbandhena yathā vā prakāśanam tathā ca prakāśaḥ api kriyā iti tayā api tathā bhavitavyam saṃbandhaḥ ca bheda āśrayaḥ nābhede saṃbhavati iti arthaḥ kim ca su ābhāsam cittam iti agrāhyam eva kasyacid iti śabda arthaḥ syāt etat mā bhūt grāhyam cittam na hi grahaṇasya akāraṇasya avyāpakasya ca nivṛttau citta nivṛttiḥ iti atas āha sva buddhi iti buddhiḥ cittam pracārāḥ vyāpārāḥ sattvāḥ prāṇinaḥ cittasya vṛtti bhedāḥ krodha lobha ādayaḥ sva āśrayeṇa cittena sva viṣayeṇa ca saha pratyātmam anubhūyamānāḥ cittasya agrāhyatām vighaṭayanti iti arthaḥ sva buddhi pracāra pratisaṃvedanam eva viśadayati kruddhaḥ aham iti 
TV_4.20.1–4.20.4	 eka samaye ca ubhaya anavadhāraṇam eka samaye ca ubhaya anavadhāraṇam su ābhāsam viṣaya ābhāsam cittam iti bruvāṇaḥ na tāvat yena eva vyāpāreṇa ātmānam avadhārayati tena eva viṣayam api iti vaktum arhati na hi avilakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ kārya bhedāya paryāptaḥ tasmāt vyāpāra bhedaḥ aṅgīkartavyaḥ na ca vaināśikānām utpatti bheda atiriktaḥ asti vyāpāraḥ na ca ekasyāḥ eva utpatteḥ avilakṣaṇāyāḥ kārya vailakṣaṇya saṃbhavaḥ tasya ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt na ca ekasya utpatti dvaya saṃbhavaḥ tasmāt arthasya ca jñāna rūpasya ca avadhāraṇam na ekasmin samayaḥ iti tat etat bhāṣyeṇa ucyate na ca ekasmin kṣaṇaḥ iti tathā ca uktam vaināśikaiḥ bhūtiḥ yeṣām kriyā sā eva kārakam sā eva ca ucyate iti tasmāt dṛśya tvam etat cittasya sadātanam svābhāsa tvam apanayat draṣṭāram ca draṣṭuḥ apariṇāmi tvam ca darśayati iti siddham 
TV_4.21.1–4.21.2	 citta antara dṛśye buddhi buddheḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ smṛti saṃkaraḥ ca punar vaināaśikam utthāpayati syāt matiḥ mā bhūt dṛśya tvena sva saṃvedanam evam api ātmā na sidhyati sva saṃtāna vartinā carama cid ta kṣaṇena svarasa niruddha sva janaka citta kṣaṇa grahaṇāt iti arthaḥ samam ca tad jñāna tvena anantaram ca avyavahita tvena samanantaram tena citta antara dṛśye buddhi buddheḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ smṛti saṃkaraḥ ca buddhiḥ iti cittam iti arthaḥ na agṛhītā caramā buddhiḥ pūrva buddhi grahaṇa samarthāḥ na hi buddhyā saṃbaddhā pūrva buddhiḥ buddhāḥ bhavitum arhati na hi agṛhīta daṇḍaḥ daṇḍinam avagantum arhati tasmāt anavasthā iti vijñāna vedanā saṃjñā rūpa saṃskārāḥ skandhāḥ sāṃkhya yoga ādayaḥ pravādāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca yogāḥ ca te eva ādayaḥ yeṣām vaiśeṣika ādi pravādānām te sāṃkhya yoga ādayaḥ pravādāḥ sugamam anyat 
TV_4.22.1–4.22.2^1	 citeḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ tad ākāra āpattau sva buddhi saṃvedanam syāt etat yadi cittam na su ābhāsam na api citta antara vedyam ātmanā api katham bhokṣyate cittam na khalu ātmanaḥ svayaṃprakāśasya api asti kācid kriyā na ca tām antareṇa kartā na ca asaṃbaddhaḥ cittena karmaṇā tasya bhoktā ati prasaṅgāt iti āśayavān pṛcchati katham iti sūtreṇa uttaram āha citeḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ tad ākāra āpattau sva buddhi saṃvedanam yat tat avocat vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra iti tat itas samutthitam citeḥ sva buddhi saṃvedanam buddheḥ tad ākāra āpattau citi pratibimba ādhāra tayā tad rūpa tā āpattau satyām 
TV_4.22.2^2	 yathā hi candramasaḥ kriyām antareṇa api saṃkrānta candra pratibimbam amalam jalam acalam calam iva ālavālam arālam iva candramasam avabhāsayati evam vinā api citi vyāpāram upasaṃkrānta citi pratibimbam cittam sva gatayā kriyayā kriyāvatīm asaṃgatām api saṃgatām citi śaktim avabhāsayat bhogya bhāvam āsādayat bhoktṛ bhāvam āpādayati tasyāḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ bhāṣyam api etat artham asakṛt tatra tatra vyākhyātam iti na vyākhyātam atra buddhi vṛtti aviśiṣṭa tve jñāna vṛtteḥ āgamam udāharati tathā ca uktam na pātālam iti śāśvatasya śivasya brahmaṇaḥ viśuddha svabhāvasya citi= chāyā āpannām manaḥ vṛttim eva citi= chāyā āpanna tvāt citeḥ api aviśiṣṭām guhām vedayante tasyām eva guhāyām tat guhyam brahma tad apanaye tu svayaṃprakāśam anāvaraṇam anupasargam pradyotate carama dehasya bhagavataḥ iti 
TV_4.23.1–4.23.2^1	 draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam cittam sarva artham tat evam dṛśya tvena cittasya pariṇāminaḥ tad atiriktaḥ pumān apariṇati dharma upapāditaḥ saṃprati loka pratyakṣam api atra pramāṇayati atas ca etat iti avaśyam ca etat iti arthaḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam cittam sarva artham yathā hi nīla ādi anuraktam cittam nīla ādi artham pratyakṣeṇa eva avasthāpayati evam draṣṭṛ= chāyā āpattyā tat anuraktam cittam draṣṭāram api pratyakṣeṇa avasthāpayati asti hi tri ākāram jñānam nīlam aham saṃprati emi iti tasmāt jñeya vat tad jñātā api pratyakṣa siddhaḥ api na vivicya avasthāpitaḥ yathā jale candramasaḥ bimbam na tu etāvatā tat apratyakṣam na ca asya jala gata tve tat apramāṇam iti candra rūpe api apramāṇam bhavitum arhati 
TV_4.23.2^2–4.23.3	 tasmāt citta pratibimba tayā caitanya gocarā api citta vṛttiḥ na caitanya agocara iti tat idam sarva artha tvam cittasya iti tat etat āha manaḥ hi iti na kevalam tad ākāra āpattyā mantavyena arthena uparaktam manaḥ api tu svayam ca iti cakāraḥ bhinnakramaḥ puruṣeṇa iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ tad chāyā āpattiḥ puruṣasya vṛttiḥ iyam ca caitanya= chāyā āpattiḥ cittasya vaināśikaiḥ abhyupetavyāḥ katham anyathā citte caitanyam ete āropayām babhūvuḥ iti āha tat anena iti kecid vaināśikāḥ bāhya artha vādinaḥ apare vijñāna mātra vādinaḥ nanu yadi cittam eva draṣṭṛ ākāram dṛśya ākāram ca anubhūyate hanta cittāt abhinnau eva āstām draṣṭṛ dṛśyau yathā āhuḥ abhinnaḥ api hi buddhi ātmā viparyāsita darśanaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvitti bhedavān iva lakṣyate iti 
TV_4.23.4	 tat katham ete anukampanīyāḥ iti atas āha samādhi prajñāyām iti te khalu uktābhiḥ upapattibhiḥ citta atiriktam puruṣam abhyupagamya api aṣṭāṅga yoga upadeśena samādhi prajñāyām ātma gocarāyām avatārya bodhayitavyāḥ tat yathā samādhi prajñāyām prajñeyaḥ arthaḥ ātmā pratibimbībhūtaḥ anyaḥ kasmāt tasya ātmanaḥ ālambanībhūta tvāt atha cittāt abhinnam eva kasmāt na ālambanam bhavati iti yadi yukti bodhitaḥ api vaiyātyāt vadet tatra hetum āha sa ced ātma rūpaḥ arthaḥ cittamātram syāt na tu tatas vyatiriktaḥ tatas katham prajñayā eva prajñā rūpam avadhāryeta sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt upasaṃharati tasmāt iti samīcīna upadeśena anukampitāḥ bhavanti iti āha evam iti jātitaḥ svabhāvataḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_4.24.1–4.24.2^1	 tat asaṃkhyeya vāsanābhiḥ citram api para artham saṃhatyakāri tvāt citta atirikta ātma sadbhāve hetu antaram avatārayati kutas ca iti tat asaṃkhyeya vāsanābhiḥ citram api para artham saṃhatyakāri tvāt yadi api asaṃkhyeyāḥ karma vāsanāḥ kleśa vāsanāḥ ca cittam eva adhiśerate na tu puruṣam tathā ca vāsanā adhīnāḥ vipākāḥ citta āśraya tayā cittasya bhoktṛtām āvahanti bhoktuḥ arthe ca bhogyam iti sarvam citta artham prāptam tathā api tat cittam asaṃkhyeya vāsanā vicitram api para artham kasmāt saṃhatyakāri tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ vyācaṣṭe tat etat iti syāt etat cittam saṃhatya api kariṣyati sva artham ca bhaviṣyati kaḥ khalu virodhaḥ iti yadi kaścid brūyāt tam pratyāha saṃhatyakāriṇā iti sukha cittam iti bhogam upalakṣayati tena duḥkha cittam api draṣṭavyam 
TV_4.24.2^2	 jñānam iti apavargaḥ uktaḥ etat uktam bhavati sukha duḥkhe citte pratikūla anukūla ātmake na ātmani saṃbhavataḥ sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt na ca anyaḥ api saṃhatyakārī sākṣāt paramparayā vā sukha duḥkhe vidadhānaḥ tābhyām anukūlanīyaḥ pratikūlanīyaḥ vā tasmāt yaḥ sākṣāt paramparayā vā na sukha duḥkhayoḥ vyāpriyate saḥ eva ābhyām anukūlanīyaḥ pratikūlanīyaḥ vā sa ca nitya udāsīnaḥ puruṣaḥ evam apavṛjyate yena jñānena tasya api jñeya tantra tvāt sva ātmani ca vṛtti virodhāt na jñāna artha tvam na bāhya viṣayāt asmāt apavarga saṃbhavaḥ videha prakṛti layānām apavarga asaṃbhavāt tasmāt tad jñānam api puruṣa artham eva na tat sva artham na api para mātra artham saṃhata para artha tve ca anavasthā prasaṅgāt asaṃhata para artha siddhiḥ iti 
TV_4.25.1–4.25.2^1	 viśeṣa darśinaḥ ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivṛttiḥ tat evam kaivalya mūla bījam yukti mayam ātma darśanam uktvā tad upadeśa adhikṛtam puruṣam anadhikṛta puruṣa antarāt vyāvṛttam āha viśeṣa darśinaḥ ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivṛttiḥ yasya ātma bhāve bhāvanā asti tasya aṣṭāṅga yoga upadeśāt anutiṣṭhataḥ yuñjānasya tad paripākāt citta sattva puruṣayoḥ viśeṣa darśanāt ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivartate yasya ātma bhāva bhāvanā eva na asti nāstikasya tasya upadeśān adhikṛtasya apariniścita ātma tatpara loka bhāvasya na upadeśaḥ na viśeṣa darśanam na ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivṛttiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu ātma bhāva bhāvanāyāḥ citta vartinyāḥ kutas avagamaḥ iti atas āha yathā prāvṛṣi iti 
TV_4.25.2^2	 prāc bhavīyam tattva darśana bījam apavarga bhāgīyam yat karma aṣṭāṅga yoga anuṣṭhānam tat eka deśa anuṣṭhānam vā tad abhinirvartitam asti iti anumīyate tasya ca ātma bhāva bhāvanā avaśyam eva svābhāvikī vastu abhyāsam vinā api pravartate anadhikāriṇam āgaminām vacanena darśayati yasya abhāvāt idam iti pūrva pakṣaḥ na asti karma phalam para lokinaḥ abhāvāt para loka abhāvaḥ iti tatra ruciḥ aruciḥ ca nirṇaye pañcaviṃśati tattva viṣaye ātma bhāva bhāvanā prāk vyākhyātāḥ viśeṣa darśinaḥ parāmarśam āha cittasya eva iti tasya viśeṣa darśana kuśalasya ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivartate iti 
TV_4.26.1–4.27.2	 tadā viveka nimnam kaivalya prāgbhāram cittam atha viśeṣa darśinaḥ kīdṛśam cittam iti atas āha tadā viveka nimnam kaivalya prāgbhāram cittam nigada vyākhyātam tad chidreṣu pratyaya antarāṇi saṃskārebhyaḥ syāt etat viśeṣa darśanam ced viveka niṣṭham na jātu cittam vyutthitam syāt dṛśyate ca asya bhikṣām aṭatas vyutthitam iti atas āha tad chidreṣu pratyaya antarāṇi saṃskārebhyaḥ pratyaya iti pratīyate yena sa pratyayaḥ citta sattvam tasmāt vivekaḥ citeḥ tena nimnasya jānāmi iti sākṣāt mokṣaḥ vivicya darśitaḥ na jānāmi iti mohaḥ tad mūlau ahaṃkāra mamakārau aham asmi iti vā mama iti vā darśitau kṣīyamāṇāni ca tāni bījāni ca iti samāsaḥ pūrva saṃskārebhyaḥ vyutthāna saṃskārebhyaḥ 
TV_4.28.1–4.28.2	 hānam eṣām kleśa vat uktam syāt etat sati api viveka vijñāne vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ yadi pratyaya antarāṇi prasuvate kaḥ tarhi hāna hetuḥ eteṣām yatas pratyaya antarāṇi na punar prasuvīran iti atas āha hānam eṣām kleśa vat uktam aparipakva viveka jñānasya akṣīyamāṇāḥ vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ pratyaya antaram prasuvate na tu paripakva viveka jñānasya kṣīṇāḥ pratyaya antarāṇi prasotum arhanti yathā viveka= chidra samutpannāḥ api kleśāḥ na saṃskāra antaram prasuvate tat kasya hetoḥ tat ete kleśāḥ viveka jñāna vahni dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ iti evam vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ api iti atha vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ viveka jñāna saṃskāraiḥ niroddhavyāḥ viveka saṃskārāḥ ca nirodha saṃskāraiḥ nirodha saṃskārāṇām tu abāhya viṣaya tvam darśitam nirodha upāyaḥ prāyas cintanīyaḥ iti atas āha jñāna saṃskārāḥ tu iti para vairāgya saṃskārāḥ iti arthaḥ 
TV_4.29.1–4.29.2	 prasaṃkhyāne api akusīdasya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharma meghaḥ samādhiḥ tat evam sūtra kāraḥ vyutthāna nirodha upāyam prasaṃkhyānam uktvā prasaṃkhyāna nirodha upāyam āha prasaṃkhyāne api akusīdasya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharma meghaḥ samādhiḥ tatas prasaṃkhyānāt na kiṃcid sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tva ādi prārthayate pratyuta tatra api kliśnāti pariṇāmi tva doṣa darśanena viraktaḥ sarvathā viveka khyātiḥ eva bhavati etat eva vivṛṇoti tatra api iti yadā vyutthāna pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ tadā na ayam brāhmaṇaḥ sarvathā viveka khyātiḥ yatas tasya na pratyaya antarāṇi bhavanti tatas sarvathā viveka khyātiḥ iti tadā asya dharma meghaḥ samādhiḥ bhavati etat uktam bhavati prasaṃkhyāne viraktaḥ tad nirodham icchan dharma megham samādhim upāsīta tad upāsane ca sarvathā viveka khyātiḥ bhavati tathā ca tam niroddhum pārayati iti 
TV_4.30.1–4.30.2	 tatas kleśa karma nivṛttiḥ tasya ca prayojanam āha tatas kleśa karma nivṛttiḥ kasmāt punar jīvan eva vidvān vimuktaḥ bhavati uttaram yasmāt iti kleśa karma vāsanā iddhaḥ kila karma āśayaḥ jāti ādi nidānam na ca asati nidāne nidānī bhavitum arhati yathā aha atra bhagavān akṣapādaḥ vīta rāga janma adarśanāt iti 
TV_4.31.1–4.31.2^1	 tadā sarva āvaraṇa mala apetasya jñānasya ānantyāt jñeyam alpam atha evam dharma meghe sati kīdṛśam cittam iti atas āha tadā sarva āvaraṇa mala apetasya jñānasya ānantyāt jñeyam alpam āvriyate citta sattvam ebhiḥ iti āvaraṇāni malāḥ kleśa karmāṇi sarve ca te āvaraṇa malāḥ ca iti sarva āvaraṇa mala as tebhyaḥ apetasya citta sattvasya jñānasya jñāyate anena iti anayā vyutpatti ānantyāt aparimeya tvāt jñeyam alpam yathā hi śaradi ghana paṭala m uktasya caṇḍa arciṣaḥ paritas pradyotamānasya prakāśa ānantyāt prakāśyāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ alpāḥ prakāśante evam apagata rajaḥ tamasaḥ citta sattvasya prakāśa ānantyāt alpam prakāśyam iti tat etat āha sarvaiḥ iti etat eva vyatireka mukhena sphorayati āvarakeṇa tamasā abhibhūtam iti 
TV_4.31.2^2	 kriyā śīlena rajasā pravartitam atas eva udghāṭitam pradeśāt apanītam tamaḥ iti arthaḥ atas eva sarvān dharmān jñeyān mehati varṣati prakāśanena iti dharma meghaḥ iti ucyate nanu ayam astu dharma meghaḥ samādhiḥ sa vāsana kleśa karma āśaya praśama hetuḥ atha sati api asmin kasmāt na jāyate punar jantuḥ iti atas āha yatra idam uktam iti kāraṇa samucchedāt api ced kāryam kriyate hanta bho maṇi vedha ādayaḥ andha ādibhyaḥ bhaveyuḥ pratyakṣāḥ tathā ca anupapanna artha tāyām ābhāṇakaḥ laukikaḥ upapanna arthaḥ syāt avidhyat andhaḥ maṇim iti āvayat grathitavān pratyamuñcat pinaddhavān abhyapūjayat stutavān iti 
TV_4.32.1–4.32.2	 tatas kṛtārthānām pariṇāma krama samāptiḥ guṇānām nanu dharma meghasya parā kāṣṭhā jñāna prasāda mātram param vairāgyam sa mūla ghātam apahantu vyutthāna samādhi saṃskārān sa kleśa karma āśayān guṇāḥ tu svatas eva vikāra karaṇa śīlāḥ kasmāt tādṛśam api puruṣam prati deha indriya ādīn na ārabhante iti atas āha tatas kṛtārthānām pariṇāma krama samāptiḥ guṇānām śīlam idam guṇānām yat amī yam prati kṛtārthāḥ tam prati na pravartante iti bhāvaḥ 
TV_4.33.1–4.33.2^1	 kṣaṇa pratiyogī pariṇāma apara anta nirgrāhyaḥ kramaḥ atra antare pariṇāma kramam pṛcchati atha kaḥ ayam iti kṣaṇa pratiyogī pariṇāma apara anta nirgrāhyaḥ kramaḥ pariṇāma kramaḥ kṣaṇa pratiyogī kṣaṇaḥ pratisaṃbandhī yasya sa tathā uktaḥ kṣaṇa pracaya āśrayaḥ iti arthaḥ na jātu kramaḥ kramavantam antareṇa śakyaḥ nirūpayitum na ca ekasya eva kṣaṇasya kramaḥ tasmāt kṣaṇa pracaya āśrayaḥ pariśiṣyate tat idam āha kṣaṇa anantaryā iti pariṇāma krame pramāṇam āha pariṇāmasya iti navasya hi vastrasya prayatna saṃrakṣitasya api cireṇa purāṇa tā dṛśyate saḥ ayam pariṇāmasya apara antaḥ paryavasānam tena hi pariṇāmasya kramaḥ tatas prāk api purāṇa tāyāḥ sūkṣma sūkṣmatara sūkṣmatama sthūla sthūlatara sthūlatama tva ādīnām paurvāparyam anumīyate etat eva vyatireka mukhena darśayati na hi iti ananubhūtaḥ aprāptaḥ krama kṣaṇaḥ yayā sā tathā uktā nanu eṣa kramaḥ pradhānasya na saṃbhavati tasya nitya tvāt iti atas āha nityeṣu ca iti bahuvacanena sarva nitya vyāpitām kramasya pratijānīte 
TV_4.33.2^2	 tatra nityānām prakāra bhedam darśayitvā nitya vyāpitām kramasya upapādayati dvayī iti nanu kūṭastham svabhāvāt apracyutam astu nityam pariṇāmi sadā eva svarūpāt cyavamānam katham nityam iti atas āha yasmin iti dharma lakṣaṇa avasthānām udaya vyaya dharma tvam dharmiṇaḥ tu tattvāt avighātaḥ eva iti atha kim pariṇāma apara anta nirgrāhya tā sarvatra kramasya na iti āha tatra guṇa dharmeṣu buddhi ādiṣu iti yatas labdha paryavasānaḥ dharmāṇām vināśāt pradhānasya tu pariṇāma kramaḥ na labdha paryavasānaḥ nanu pradhānasya dharma rūpeṇa pariṇāmāt astu pariṇāma kramaḥ puruṣasya tu apariṇāminaḥ kutas pariṇāma kramaḥ iti atas āha kūṭasthā iti tatra baddhānām citta avyatireka abhimānāt tad pariṇāmena pariṇāma adhyāsaḥ muktānām ca asti kriyām upādāya avāstavaḥ api pariṇāmaḥ moha kalpitaḥ śabdasya puraḥsara tayā tad pṛṣṭhaḥ vikalpaḥ asti kriyām upādattaḥ iti guṇeṣu alabdha paryavasānaḥ pariṇāma kramaḥ iti uktam tat asahamānaḥ pṛcchati atha iti sthityā iti mahāpralaya avasthāyām gatyā iti sṛṣṭau 
TV_4.33.2^3	 etat uktam bhavati yadi ānantyāt na pariṇāma samāptiḥ saṃsārasya hanta bhoḥ katham mahāpralaya samaye sarveṣām ātmanām sahasā samucchidyeta katham ca sṛṣṭi ādau sahasā utpadyeta saṃsāraḥ tasmāt ekaikasya ātmanaḥ mukti krameṇa sarveṣām vimokṣāt ucchedaḥ sarveṣām saṃsārasya krameṇa iti pradhāna pariṇāma krama parisamāptiḥ evam ca pradhānasya api anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca apūrva sattva prādurbhāvaḥ iṣyate yena ānantyam syāt tathā sati anādi tva vyāhateḥ sakala śāstra artha bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ iti bhāvaḥ uttaram āha avacanīyam anuttara arham etat 
TV_4.33.2^4	 ekāntataḥ etasya avacanīya tām darśayitum ekānta vacanīyam praśnam darśayati asti praśnaḥ iti sarvaḥ jātaḥ mariṣyati iti praśna uttaram om bho iti satyam bho iti arthaḥ avibhajya vacanīyam uktvā pravibhajya vacanīyam praśnam āha atha sarve iti vibhajya vacanīyatām āha vibhajya iti vibhajya vacanīyam eva praśna antaram vispaṣṭa artham āha tathā manuṣya iti ayam tu avacanīyaḥ ekāntataḥ na hi sāmānyena kuśala akuśala puruṣa saṃsārasya antavat tvam anantavat tvam vā śakyam ekāntataḥ vaktum 
TV_4.33.2^5	 yathā prāṇa bhṛt mātrasya śreyaḥ tvam aśreyaḥ tvam vā na ekāntataḥ śakyam avadhārayitum yathā jāta mātrasya maraṇam ekāntataḥ vibhajya punar śakya avadhāraṇam iti āha kuśalasya iti ayam abhisaṃdhiḥ krameṇa mokṣe sarveṣām mokṣāt saṃsāra ucchedaḥ iti anumānam tat ca āgama siddha mokṣa āśrayam tathā ca abhyupagata mokṣa pratipādaka āgama pramāṇa bhāvaḥ katham tam eva āgamam pradhāna vikāra nityatāyām apramāṇīkuryāt tasmāt āgama bādhita viṣayam etat anumānam na pramāṇam śrūyate hi śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇeṣu sarga pratisarga paramparāyāḥ anādi tvam ananta tvam ca iti api ca sarveṣām eva ātmanām saṃsārasya na tāvat yugapad ucchedaḥ saṃbhavī na hi paṇḍita rūpāṇām api aneka janma paramparā abhyāsa pariśrama sādhyāḥ viveka khyāti pratiṣṭhā kim punar prāṇa bhṛt mātrasya sthāvara jaṅgama ādeḥ ekadā akasmāt bhavitum arhati na ca kāraṇa ayaugapadye kārya yaugapadyam yujyate krameṇa tu viveka khyātau asaṃkhyeyānām krameṇa muktau na saṃsāra ucchedaḥ ananta tvāt jantūnām asaṃkhyeya tvāt iti sarvam avadātam 
TV_4.34.1–4.34.2	 puruṣa artha śūnyānām guṇānām pratiprasavaḥ kaivalyam svarūpa pratiṣṭhā vā citi śaktiḥ iti kaivalya rūpa avadhāraṇa parasya sūtrasya avāntara saṃgatim āha guṇa adhikārā iti puruṣa artha śūnyānām guṇānām pratiprasavaḥ kaivalyam svarūpa pratiṣṭhā vā citi śaktiḥ iti kṛta karaṇīya tayā puruṣa artha śūnyānām yaḥ pratiprasavaḥ sva kāraṇe pradhāne layaḥ teṣām kārya kāraṇa ātmakānām guṇānām vyutthāna samādhi nirodha saṃskārāḥ manasi līyante manaḥ asmitāyām asmitā liṅge liṅgam aliṅgaḥ iti yaḥ ayam guṇānām kārya kāraṇa ātmakānām pratisargaḥ tat kaivalyam yam kaṃcid puruṣam prati pradhānasya mokṣaḥ svarūpa pratiṣṭhā vā puruṣasya mokṣaḥ iti āha svarūpa iti asti hi mahāpralaye api svarūpa pratiṣṭhā citi śaktiḥ na ca asau mokṣaḥ iti atas āha punar iti sautraḥ iti śabdaḥ śāstra parisamāptau 
TV_4.34.3	 mukti arha cittam para loka meya jña siddhaye dharma ghanaḥ samādhiḥ dvayī ca muktiḥ pratipāditā asmin pāde prasaṅgāt api ca anyat uktam nidānam tāpānām uditam atha tāpāḥ ca kathitāḥ saha aṅgaiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ vihitam iha yoga dvayam api kṛtaḥ mukteḥ adhvā guṇa puruṣa bhedaḥ sphuṭataraḥ viviktam kaivalyam parigalita tāpā citiḥ asau
